// --- CONFIGURATION ---

// Watchlist from Config tab — reads ALL column pairs (A/B, C/D, E/F, etc.)
// Odd columns = section headers, even columns = tickers
// Same ticker in multiple sections = shows up multiple times on Watchlist tab
function getWatchlist() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let configSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Config');
  if (!configSheet) {
    configSheet = ss.insertSheet('Config');
    configSheet.getRange('A1').setValue('Section');
    configSheet.getRange('B1').setValue('Ticker');
    configSheet.getRange('D1').setValue('Section');
    configSheet.getRange('E1').setValue('Ticker');
    configSheet.getRange('G1').setValue('Section');
    configSheet.getRange('H1').setValue('Ticker');
    configSheet.getRange('A2').setValue('WATCHING');
    configSheet.getRange('B3').setValue('AVGO');
    configSheet.getRange('B4').setValue('TSM');
    configSheet.getRange('D2').setValue('SECTOR ETFs');
    configSheet.getRange('E3').setValue('XLK');
    configSheet.getRange('E4').setValue('SOXX');
    configSheet.getRange('E5').setValue('SMH');
    configSheet.setColumnWidth(3, 20);
    configSheet.setColumnWidth(6, 20);
    configSheet.setColumnWidth(9, 20);
    return [
      {symbol: 'AVGO', section: 'WATCHING'},
      {symbol: 'TSM', section: 'WATCHING'},
      {symbol: 'XLK', section: 'SECTOR ETFs'},
      {symbol: 'SOXX', section: 'SECTOR ETFs'},
      {symbol: 'SMH', section: 'SECTOR ETFs'}
    ];
  }

  const lastCol = configSheet.getLastColumn();
  const lastRow = configSheet.getLastRow();
  
  const results = [];
  
  // ── 1. Read Config tab (all sections EXCEPT My Positions) ──
  if (lastRow >= 2 && lastCol >= 2) {
    const data = configSheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, lastCol).getValues();
    const HEADER_WORDS = new Set(['TICKER', 'SECTION', 'NAME', 'SYMBOL', '']);

    for (let grp = 0; grp < lastCol; grp += 3) {
      let currentSection = 'UNSORTED';
      for (let row = 0; row < data.length; row++) {
        const sectionCol = String(data[row][grp] || '').trim();
        const tickerCol = grp + 1 < lastCol ? String(data[row][grp + 1] || '').trim().toUpperCase() : '';
        if (sectionCol !== '' && sectionCol !== 'undefined') {
          currentSection = sectionCol;
        }
        if (tickerCol !== '' && tickerCol !== 'undefined' && !HEADER_WORDS.has(tickerCol)) {
          // Skip MY POSITIONS and PAPER TRADES from Config — they come from APIs
          if (currentSection.toUpperCase() !== 'MY POSITIONS' && currentSection.toUpperCase() !== 'PAPER TRADES') {
            results.push({ symbol: tickerCol, section: currentSection });
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }
  
  // ── 2. Read My Positions from TradeStation-powered tab ──
  // Separate live positions from paper trades into distinct sections
  var posTickers = getMyPositionTickers();
  var paperTickers = getPaperPositionTickers();
  var paperSet = {};
  for (var pi = 0; pi < paperTickers.length; pi++) {
    paperSet[paperTickers[pi]] = true;
  }
  for (var i = 0; i < posTickers.length; i++) {
    if (paperSet[posTickers[i]]) {
      results.push({ symbol: posTickers[i], section: 'PAPER TRADES' });
    } else {
      results.push({ symbol: posTickers[i], section: 'MY POSITIONS' });
    }
  }

  // ── 3. Read Dynamic tab (rotating overflow tickers) ──
  try {
    var dynItems = _readDynamic(ss);
    for (var di = 0; di < dynItems.length; di++) {
      // Avoid duplicates with Config tickers
      var isDupe = false;
      for (var ri = 0; ri < results.length; ri++) {
        if (results[ri].symbol === dynItems[di].symbol) { isDupe = true; break; }
      }
      if (!isDupe) {
        results.push({ symbol: dynItems[di].symbol, section: 'DYNAMIC', dynamicSource: dynItems[di].source, dynamicReason: dynItems[di].reason });
      }
    }
  } catch(de) { Logger.log('Dynamic merge error: ' + de.message); }

  return results;
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// DYNAMIC WATCHLIST — 75 rotating tickers from gap scan, earnings, Arete, RVOL alerts
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

var DYNAMIC_TAB = 'Dynamic';
var DYNAMIC_MAX = 75;
// S&P 500 + some Russell 1000 components for gap scan (broad universe, quote-only)
// This is a curated subset — not ALL 1000, just the most tradeable
var GAP_SCAN_UNIVERSE = [
  // Top 100 by avg volume that aren't in a typical Config watchlist
  // Populated from Config at runtime by _getGapScanUniverse()
];

function _getDynamicSheet(ss) {
  var sh = ss.getSheetByName(DYNAMIC_TAB);
  if (!sh) {
    sh = ss.insertSheet(DYNAMIC_TAB);
    sh.getRange('A1:G1').setValues([['Symbol', 'Source', 'Added', 'Reason', 'LastConf', 'Grade', 'Keep']]);
    sh.setFrozenRows(1);
    sh.setColumnWidth(4, 250);
    Logger.log('Created Dynamic tab');
  }
  return sh;
}

function _readDynamic(ss) {
  var sh = _getDynamicSheet(ss);
  if (sh.getLastRow() <= 1) return [];
  var vals = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 7).getValues();
  var items = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < vals.length; i++) {
    var sym = String(vals[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!sym || !/^[A-Z]{1,5}$/.test(sym)) continue;
    items.push({
      symbol: sym,
      source: String(vals[i][1] || ''),
      added: String(vals[i][2] || ''),
      reason: String(vals[i][3] || ''),
      lastConf: parseFloat(vals[i][4]) || 0,
      grade: String(vals[i][5] || ''),
      keep: String(vals[i][6] || '').toUpperCase() === 'Y'
    });
  }
  return items;
}

function _writeDynamic(ss, items) {
  var sh = _getDynamicSheet(ss);
  // Clear old data
  if (sh.getLastRow() > 1) sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 7).clearContent();
  if (!items.length) return;
  var rows = items.slice(0, DYNAMIC_MAX).map(function(it) {
    return [it.symbol, it.source, it.added, it.reason, it.lastConf || '', it.grade || '', it.keep ? 'Y' : ''];
  });
  sh.getRange(2, 1, rows.length, 7).setValues(rows);
}

// Populate Dynamic tab — called at pre-market and on each full scan
function populateDynamic(ss, configSymbolSet, earningsMap) {
  var existing = _readDynamic(ss);
  var existingSet = {};
  for (var ei = 0; ei < existing.length; ei++) existingSet[existing[ei].symbol] = existing[ei];
  
  var today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  var tmrw = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(Date.now() + 86400000), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  var newItems = [];
  
  // ── Source 1: Gap scan (pre-market) ──
  // Only run if we have less than DYNAMIC_MAX tickers
  if (existing.length < DYNAMIC_MAX) {
    try {
      // Get a broad quote batch for gap detection
      // Use the S&P 500 ETF components via a curated list
      var gapCandidates = _runGapScan(configSymbolSet);
      for (var gi = 0; gi < gapCandidates.length && existing.length + newItems.length < DYNAMIC_MAX; gi++) {
        var gc = gapCandidates[gi];
        if (!configSymbolSet[gc.symbol] && !existingSet[gc.symbol]) {
          newItems.push({
            symbol: gc.symbol, source: 'GAP', added: today,
            reason: 'Gap ' + (gc.gap > 0 ? '+' : '') + gc.gap.toFixed(1) + '%, RVOL ' + gc.rvol.toFixed(1),
            lastConf: 0, grade: '', keep: false
          });
          existingSet[gc.symbol] = true;
        }
      }
    } catch(ge) { Logger.log('Dynamic gap scan error: ' + ge.message); }
  }
  
  // ── Source 2: Earnings this week ──
  if (earningsMap) {
    var earnSyms = Object.keys(earningsMap);
    for (var ek = 0; ek < earnSyms.length && existing.length + newItems.length < DYNAMIC_MAX; ek++) {
      var es = earnSyms[ek];
      var earn = earningsMap[es];
      if (!configSymbolSet[es] && !existingSet[es] && earn.date) {
        var ed = String(earn.date);
        if (ed === today || ed === tmrw) {
          newItems.push({
            symbol: es, source: 'EARNINGS', added: today,
            reason: 'Reports ' + ed + ' ' + (earn.time || ''),
            lastConf: 0, grade: '', keep: false
          });
          existingSet[es] = true;
        }
      }
    }
  }
  
  // ── Source 3: Arete email tickers ──
  try {
    var areteRaw = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('ARETE_GMAIL_CACHE') || '';
    if (areteRaw) {
      var areteMatches = areteRaw.match(/\$([A-Z]{1,5})\b/g) || [];
      // Also match standalone tickers (less reliable, so only if they look like tickers)
      var standaloneMatches = areteRaw.match(/\b([A-Z]{2,5})\b/g) || [];
      var allMatches = new Set();
      for (var am = 0; am < areteMatches.length; am++) allMatches.add(areteMatches[am].replace('$', ''));
      // Only add standalone if they're in a known ticker universe (avoid false positives like THE, FOR, etc.)
      var commonWords = new Set(['THE','FOR','AND','BUT','NOT','YOU','ARE','HAS','WAS','CAN','ALL','DAY','NEW','NOW',
        'ONE','TWO','OUR','OUT','HOW','WHY','GET','SET','BIG','LOW','TOP','RUN','PUT','BUY','ANY','MAY','ITS',
        'PRE','POST','NEXT','LAST','THIS','THAT','WITH','FROM','BEEN','WILL','HAVE','MORE','LESS','EACH','MUCH',
        'ALSO','JUST','SOME','THAN','THEN','WELL','VERY','ONLY','INTO','OVER','SUCH','BACK','LONG','SHORT',
        'HIGH','OPEN','CLOSE','ABOVE','BELOW','AFTER','BEFORE','ABOUT','TODAY','WEEK','YEAR','HOLD','SELL','STOP']);
      for (var sm2 = 0; sm2 < standaloneMatches.length; sm2++) {
        var st = standaloneMatches[sm2];
        if (!commonWords.has(st) && st.length >= 2) allMatches.add(st);
      }
      allMatches.forEach(function(tk) {
        if (!configSymbolSet[tk] && !existingSet[tk] && existing.length + newItems.length < DYNAMIC_MAX) {
          newItems.push({
            symbol: tk, source: 'ARETE', added: today,
            reason: 'Mentioned in Arete email ' + today,
            lastConf: 0, grade: '', keep: false
          });
          existingSet[tk] = true;
        }
      });
    }
  } catch(ae) { Logger.log('Dynamic Arete parse error: ' + ae.message); }
  
  // Merge: keep existing + add new
  var merged = existing.concat(newItems);
  _writeDynamic(ss, merged);
  Logger.log('Dynamic watchlist: ' + existing.length + ' existing + ' + newItems.length + ' new = ' + merged.length + ' total');
  return merged;
}

// Intraday RVOL alert — called during full scans to add surprise movers
function _addDynamicRVOLAlerts(ss, quoteMap, configSymbolSet) {
  var existing = _readDynamic(ss);
  var existingSet = {};
  for (var i = 0; i < existing.length; i++) existingSet[existing[i].symbol] = true;
  
  var today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  var todayAdds = 0;
  for (var j = 0; j < existing.length; j++) {
    if (existing[j].source === 'RVOL_ALERT' && existing[j].added === today) todayAdds++;
  }
  if (todayAdds >= 10) return; // Max 10 intraday RVOL adds per day
  
  var newItems = [];
  var syms = Object.keys(quoteMap);
  for (var k = 0; k < syms.length; k++) {
    var sym = syms[k];
    if (configSymbolSet[sym] || existingSet[sym]) continue;
    if (sym.charAt(0) === '$' || sym.charAt(0) === '@') continue;
    var q = quoteMap[sym];
    if (!q) continue;
    var rvol = getRvolTOD(parseInt(q.Volume || 0), parseInt(q.PreviousVolume || 1));
    var chg = Math.abs(parseFloat(q.NetChangePct || 0));
    if (rvol >= 3 && chg >= 3 && existing.length + newItems.length < DYNAMIC_MAX && todayAdds + newItems.length < 10) {
      newItems.push({
        symbol: sym, source: 'RVOL_ALERT', added: today,
        reason: 'RVOL ' + rvol.toFixed(1) + ', ' + (parseFloat(q.NetChangePct) > 0 ? '+' : '') + parseFloat(q.NetChangePct).toFixed(1) + '%',
        lastConf: 0, grade: '', keep: false
      });
      existingSet[sym] = true;
    }
  }
  
  if (newItems.length > 0) {
    var merged = existing.concat(newItems);
    _writeDynamic(ss, merged);
    Logger.log('Dynamic RVOL alerts: added ' + newItems.length + ' tickers');
  }
}

// Gap scan: fetch broad universe quotes, filter for gaps
function _runGapScan(configSymbolSet) {
  try {
    // Use a curated broad list stored in ScriptProperties (set via menu)
    var rawList = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('GAP_SCAN_UNIVERSE') || '';
    if (!rawList) return [];
    var symbols = rawList.split(',').map(function(s) { return s.trim(); }).filter(function(s) { return s && !configSymbolSet[s]; });
    if (!symbols.length) return [];
    
    // Batch quote — 1 UrlFetch regardless of count
    var quotes = tsQuotes(symbols);
    var candidates = [];
    for (var i = 0; i < quotes.length; i++) {
      var q = quotes[i];
      var prevClose = parseFloat(q.PreviousClose || 0);
      var open = parseFloat(q.Open || 0);
      var last = parseFloat(q.Last || 0);
      if (!prevClose || !last) continue;
      var gap = ((open - prevClose) / prevClose) * 100;
      var rvol = getRvolTOD(parseInt(q.Volume || 0), parseInt(q.PreviousVolume || 1));
      if (Math.abs(gap) >= 3.0 && rvol >= 2.0) {
        candidates.push({ symbol: q.Symbol, gap: gap, rvol: rvol, last: last });
      }
    }
    candidates.sort(function(a, b) { return Math.abs(b.gap) - Math.abs(a.gap); });
    return candidates.slice(0, 20); // Top 20 gappers
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('Gap scan error: ' + e.message);
    return [];
  }
}

// EOD cleanup: remove transient tickers, keep positions + flagged
function setupGapScanUniverse() {
  // S&P 500 + NASDAQ 100 components NOT typically in Config watchlists
  // These are the broad universe for pre-market gap scanning (1 batch quote = 1 UrlFetch)
  var defaultUniverse = 'ABT,AFRM,ALB,ALGN,AMGN,AMT,APD,ASAN,AXP,BEAM,BIIB,BILL,BKNG,BKR,BMY,BSX,C,CCI,CFLT,CHTR,CI,CL,CMCSA,CME,CMI,COF,COP,CRSP,CSX,DASH,DD,DG,DHR,DKNG,DLR,DLTR,DOCU,DOW,DVN,DXCM,ECL,EDIT,EL,ELV,EMR,ENPH,EOG,ETN,EXPE,F,FCX,FDX,FSLR,FSR,GE,GILD,GM,GOLD,GRAB,HAL,HLT,HON,HUBS,HUM,ICE,IDXX,ILMN,INTU,ISRG,ITW,KO,LCID,LIN,LULU,LVS,LYFT,LYV,MAR,MCD,MCHP,MCO,MDT,MELI,MGM,MMC,MMM,MNDY,MNST,MPC,MPWR,MRK,MRNA,MSCI,MTCH,NEM,NKE,NSC,NTLA,NU,NXPI,O,OKTA,ON,PARA,PATH,PCOR,PENN,PEP,PG,PH,PINS,PLD,PNC,PSA,PSX,PXD,PYPL,RBLX,REGN,ROK,ROKU,ROST,RUN,SBUX,SCHW,SE,SEDG,SNAP,SOFI,SPG,SPGI,STLA,STM,SWKS,SYK,T,TEAM,TFC,TJX,TMO,TMUS,TTD,TWLO,TXN,U,UNP,UPS,UPST,USB,VEEV,VLO,VRTX,VZ,WBD,WDAY,WELL,WFC,WOLF,WYNN,ZM,ZTS';
  
  // Auto-exclude any that are already in Config
  var configTickers = {};
  try {
    var wl = getWatchlist();
    for (var i = 0; i < wl.length; i++) {
      if (wl[i].section !== 'DYNAMIC') configTickers[wl[i].symbol] = true;
    }
  } catch(e) {}
  
  var filtered = defaultUniverse.split(',').filter(function(t) { return !configTickers[t.trim()]; });
  var universe = filtered.join(',');
  
  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('GAP_SCAN_UNIVERSE', universe);
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Gap Scan Universe set: ' + filtered.length + ' tickers (excluded ' + (defaultUniverse.split(',').length - filtered.length) + ' already in Config).\n\nThese will be scanned for 3%+ gaps at pre-market. Cost: 1 UrlFetch per scan.');
}

function cleanupDynamic(ss) {
  var items = _readDynamic(ss);
  var positionTickers = new Set();
  try {
    var posTks = getMyPositionTickers();
    for (var p = 0; p < posTks.length; p++) positionTickers.add(posTks[p]);
  } catch(e) {}
  
  var kept = items.filter(function(it) {
    if (it.keep) return true; // Manually pinned
    if (positionTickers.has(it.symbol)) return true; // Open position
    return false; // Remove
  });
  
  var removed = items.length - kept.length;
  _writeDynamic(ss, kept);
  Logger.log('Dynamic EOD cleanup: removed ' + removed + ', kept ' + kept.length);
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// CONF_PEAK_5D — Dynamic low-signal deprioritization
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

function _updateConfPeaks(confluenceMap) {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var peakRaw = props.getProperty('CONF_PEAK_5D');
  var peaks = {};
  try { if (peakRaw) peaks = JSON.parse(peakRaw); } catch(e) { peaks = {}; }
  
  var syms = Object.keys(confluenceMap);
  for (var i = 0; i < syms.length; i++) {
    var sym = syms[i];
    var conf = confluenceMap[sym] ? (confluenceMap[sym].totalConfluence || 0) : 0;
    var existing = peaks[sym] || 0;
    if (conf > existing) peaks[sym] = conf;
  }
  
  props.setProperty('CONF_PEAK_5D', JSON.stringify(peaks));
}

function _getConfPeaks() {
  var peakRaw = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('CONF_PEAK_5D');
  try { return peakRaw ? JSON.parse(peakRaw) : {}; } catch(e) { return {}; }
}

// Called daily at EOD to age the peaks (decay toward 0 over 5 days)
function _decayConfPeaks() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var peakRaw = props.getProperty('CONF_PEAK_5D');
  var peaks = {};
  try { if (peakRaw) peaks = JSON.parse(peakRaw); } catch(e) { return; }
  
  var newPeaks = {};
  var syms = Object.keys(peaks);
  for (var i = 0; i < syms.length; i++) {
    var decayed = peaks[syms[i]] * 0.85; // Decay 15% per day
    if (decayed >= 10) newPeaks[syms[i]] = Math.round(decayed * 10) / 10; // Drop below 10 entirely
  }
  props.setProperty('CONF_PEAK_5D', JSON.stringify(newPeaks));
  Logger.log('CONF_PEAK_5D decay: ' + syms.length + ' → ' + Object.keys(newPeaks).length + ' tickers');
}

// ==================== WATCHLIST DOC SYNC (replaces syncPMWatchlist) ====================
// Syncs ALL data Claude needs for MBUs into one Google Doc:
//   1. Market data (gameplan, breadth, benchmarks, futures, sectors, internals, ratios, commodities, inverse ETFs)
//   2. Economic Calendar (today + rest of week with impact/forecast/actual/affected tickers)
//   3. Watchlist sections (My Positions [from TS API], Arete Swing, DT Carry Overs, Watching)
//   4. Arete Changes (flagged NEW/UPDATE tickers)
//
// Called from:
//   - syncAll() on hourly trigger (same as before)
//   - End of main scanner refresh during market hours (for live market data)
//
// Replaces: syncPMWatchlist()

const WATCHLIST_DOC_ID = '10hefkh0-6rpwb2LSMnDjMFEgI_rtxESwdNadGF-EhqY';

function syncWatchlistDoc(areteFlags) {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var watchlist = getWatchlist();
  
  // ── 1. Read Market tab data ──
  var marketSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Market');
  var marketRows = [];
  var ecoRows = [];
  
  if (marketSheet) {
    var mktLastRow = marketSheet.getLastRow();
    var mktLastCol = marketSheet.getLastColumn();
    
    // Cols A-D: Market data (breadth, benchmarks, futures, sectors, etc.)
    if (mktLastRow > 0 && mktLastCol >= 4) {
      marketRows = marketSheet.getRange(1, 1, mktLastRow, 4).getValues();
    }
    
    // Cols F-M: Economic Calendar (8 columns starting at col 6)
    if (mktLastRow > 0 && mktLastCol >= 13) {
      ecoRows = marketSheet.getRange(1, 6, mktLastRow, 8).getValues();
    } else if (mktLastRow > 0 && mktLastCol >= 6) {
      var ecoCols = Math.min(mktLastCol - 5, 8);
      ecoRows = marketSheet.getRange(1, 6, mktLastRow, ecoCols).getValues();
    }
  }
  
  // ── 2. Build watchlist sections ──
  var sections = {
    'MY POSITIONS': [],
    'PAPER TRADES': [],
    'ARETE WATCHING': [],
    'ARETE SWING': [],
    'DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS': [],
    'WATCHING': []
  };
  var sectionKeys = Object.keys(sections);
  
  watchlist.forEach(function(item) {
    var sec = item.section.toUpperCase();
    if (sec === 'MY POSITIONS') {
      sections['MY POSITIONS'].push(item.symbol);
    } else if (sec === 'PAPER TRADES') {
      sections['PAPER TRADES'].push(item.symbol);
    } else if (sec === 'ARETE WATCHING') {
      sections['ARETE WATCHING'].push(item.symbol);
    } else if (sec === 'ARETE SWING' || sec === 'SWING TRADES') {
      sections['ARETE SWING'].push(item.symbol);
    } else if (sec === 'DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS' || sec === 'DAYTRADE CARRY OVERS' || sec === 'DT CARRY OVERS') {
      sections['DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS'].push(item.symbol);
    } else if (sec === 'WATCHING') {
      sections['WATCHING'].push(item.symbol);
    }
  });
  
  // ── 3. Build flag/label/note/date/price lookups from areteFlags ──
  var flagLookup = {}, labelLookup = {}, noteLookup = {}, dateLookup = {}, priceLookup = {};
  if (areteFlags) {
    ['ARETE SWING', 'DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS'].forEach(function(sec) {
      if (areteFlags[sec]) {
        areteFlags[sec].forEach(function(item) {
          var key = sec + '::' + item.ticker;
          if (item.flag && item.flag !== '') flagLookup[key] = item.flag;
          if (item.label && item.label !== item.ticker) labelLookup[key] = item.label;
          if (item.note && item.note !== '') noteLookup[key] = item.note;
          if (item.entryDate && item.entryDate !== '') dateLookup[key] = item.entryDate;
          if (item.entryPrice && item.entryPrice !== '') priceLookup[key] = item.entryPrice;
        });
      }
    });
  }
  
  // ── 4. Open or create doc ──
  var doc;
  if (WATCHLIST_DOC_ID && WATCHLIST_DOC_ID !== '') {
    try {
      doc = DocumentApp.openById(WATCHLIST_DOC_ID);
    } catch(e) {
      Logger.log('Could not open doc ' + WATCHLIST_DOC_ID + ': ' + e);
      doc = DocumentApp.create('Watchlist Doc');
      Logger.log('Created new doc: ' + doc.getId());
      Logger.log('UPDATE WATCHLIST_DOC_ID in script to: ' + doc.getId());
    }
  } else {
    doc = DocumentApp.create('Watchlist Doc');
    Logger.log('Created new Watchlist Doc: ' + doc.getId());
    Logger.log('UPDATE WATCHLIST_DOC_ID in script to: ' + doc.getId());
  }
  
  // ── 5. Clear and rebuild ──
  var body = doc.getBody();
  body.appendParagraph('');
  while (body.getNumChildren() > 1) {
    body.removeChild(body.getChild(0));
  }
  body.getChild(0).asParagraph().setText('V9 Watchlist Doc');
  body.getChild(0).asParagraph().setHeading(DocumentApp.ParagraphHeading.HEADING1);
  
  body.appendParagraph('Auto-synced: ' + new Date().toLocaleString('en-US', {timeZone: 'America/Phoenix'}))
      .setItalic(true).setFontSize(9);
  
  
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // SECTION A: WATCHLIST (My Positions, Arete, DT Carry, Watching)
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  body.appendParagraph('WATCHLIST').setHeading(DocumentApp.ParagraphHeading.HEADING1);
  
  var changes = [];
  
  sectionKeys.forEach(function(sec) {
    body.appendParagraph(sec).setHeading(DocumentApp.ParagraphHeading.HEADING2);
    if (sections[sec].length > 0) {
      sections[sec].forEach(function(ticker) {
        var key = sec + '::' + ticker;
        var flag       = flagLookup[key] || '';
        var note       = noteLookup[key] || '';
        var entryDate  = dateLookup[key] || '';
        var entryPrice = priceLookup[key] || '';
        var displayName = labelLookup[key] || ticker;
        
        var parts = [displayName];
        if (entryDate !== '')  parts.push(entryDate);
        if (entryPrice !== '') parts.push(entryPrice);
        if (flag !== '') {
          parts.push('\u{1F195} ' + flag);
          changes.push({ ticker: displayName, flag: flag, section: sec, note: note });
        }
        if (note !== '') parts.push(note);
        
        var item = body.appendListItem(parts.join(' \u2014 '))
            .setGlyphType(DocumentApp.GlyphType.BULLET);
        var tvUrl = 'https://www.tradingview.com/chart/?symbol=' + ticker;
        item.editAsText().setLinkUrl(0, displayName.length - 1, tvUrl);
      });
    } else {
      body.appendParagraph('(none)').setItalic(true);
    }
  });
  
  // Arete Changes
  if (changes.length > 0) {
    body.appendParagraph('').setSpacingAfter(6);
    body.appendParagraph('ARETE CHANGES').setHeading(DocumentApp.ParagraphHeading.HEADING2);
    changes.forEach(function(c) {
      var emoji = c.flag === 'NEW' ? '\u{1F7E2}' : '\u{1F7E1}';
      var line = emoji + ' ' + c.ticker + ' \u2014 ' + c.flag + ' (' + c.section + ')';
      if (c.note && c.note !== '') line += ': ' + c.note;
      body.appendListItem(line).setGlyphType(DocumentApp.GlyphType.BULLET);
    });
  }
  
  
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // SECTION B: MARKET DATA (from Market tab cols A-D)
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  if (marketRows.length > 0) {
    body.appendParagraph('MARKET DATA').setHeading(DocumentApp.ParagraphHeading.HEADING1);
    
    var SECTION_HEADERS = [
      'GAMEPLAN', 'BENCHMARKS', 'FUTURES', 'BREADTH DETAIL', 'INTERNALS',
      'INTERMARKET RATIOS', 'COMMODITIES', 'GROWTH SECTORS', 'DEFENSIVE SECTORS',
      'INVERSE ETFs (GP-D)'
    ];
    
    var currentMktSection = '';
    var pendingRows = [];
    var pendingHeaders = [];
    
    for (var mi = 0; mi < marketRows.length; mi++) {
      var mColA = String(marketRows[mi][0] || '').trim();
      var mColB = String(marketRows[mi][1] || '').trim();
      var mColC = String(marketRows[mi][2] || '').trim();
      var mColD = String(marketRows[mi][3] || '').trim();
      
      // Skip scanner title and blank spacer rows
      if (mColA === 'V9 CONFLUENCE SCANNER') continue;
      if (mColA === '' && mColB === '' && mColC === '' && mColD === '') {
        if (pendingRows.length > 0) {
          _writeMarketSection(body, currentMktSection, pendingHeaders, pendingRows);
          pendingRows = [];
          pendingHeaders = [];
        }
        continue;
      }
      
      // Check if this is a section header
      var isMktHeader = false;
      for (var si = 0; si < SECTION_HEADERS.length; si++) {
        if (mColA === SECTION_HEADERS[si]) { isMktHeader = true; break; }
      }
      
      if (isMktHeader) {
        if (pendingRows.length > 0) {
          _writeMarketSection(body, currentMktSection, pendingHeaders, pendingRows);
          pendingRows = [];
        }
        currentMktSection = mColA;
        pendingHeaders = [mColA, mColB, mColC, mColD];
        continue;
      }
      
      // Data row
      if (mColA !== '' || mColB !== '') {
        pendingRows.push([mColA, mColB, mColC, mColD]);
      }
    }
    
    // Flush last section
    if (pendingRows.length > 0) {
      _writeMarketSection(body, currentMktSection, pendingHeaders, pendingRows);
    }
  }
  
  
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // SECTION C: ECONOMIC CALENDAR (from Market tab cols F-M)
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  if (ecoRows.length > 1) {
    body.appendParagraph('ECONOMIC CALENDAR').setHeading(DocumentApp.ParagraphHeading.HEADING1);
    
    for (var ei = 1; ei < ecoRows.length; ei++) {
      var eRow    = ecoRows[ei];
      var eTitle  = String(eRow[0] || '').trim();
      var eTime   = String(eRow[1] || '').trim();
      var eImpact = String(eRow[2] || '').trim();
      var ePrev   = String(eRow[3] || '').trim();
      var eFcst   = String(eRow[4] || '').trim();
      var eActual = String(eRow[5] || '').trim();
      var eTvChart = eRow.length > 6 ? String(eRow[6] || '').trim() : '';
      var eTickers = eRow.length > 7 ? String(eRow[7] || '').trim() : '';
      
      if (eTitle === '' && eTime === '') continue;
      
      // Day separator rows (── TODAY ──, ── FRIDAY ──, etc.)
      if (eTitle.indexOf('\u2500') >= 0 || eTitle.indexOf('──') >= 0) {
        body.appendParagraph(eTitle).setHeading(DocumentApp.ParagraphHeading.HEADING3);
        continue;
      }
      
      // Impact emoji prefix
      var ePrefix = '';
      if (eImpact === 'High') ePrefix = '\u{1F534} ';      // 🔴
      else if (eImpact === 'Medium') ePrefix = '\u{1F7E1} '; // 🟡
      
      // Build compact line: Title — Time — Prev/Fcst/Act — Tickers
      var eParts = [ePrefix + eTitle];
      if (eTime !== '') eParts.push(eTime);
      
      var eDataStr = '';
      if (ePrev !== '')   eDataStr += 'Prev: ' + ePrev;
      if (eFcst !== '')   eDataStr += (eDataStr ? ' | ' : '') + 'Fcst: ' + eFcst;
      if (eActual !== '') eDataStr += (eDataStr ? ' | ' : '') + 'Act: ' + eActual;
      if (eDataStr !== '') eParts.push(eDataStr);
      
      if (eTickers !== '') eParts.push('\u2192 ' + eTickers); // →
      
      body.appendListItem(eParts.join(' \u2014 '))
          .setGlyphType(DocumentApp.GlyphType.BULLET);
    }
  }
  doc.saveAndClose();
  Logger.log('Watchlist Doc synced: ' + marketRows.length + ' market rows, ' +
             Math.max(0, ecoRows.length - 1) + ' eco events, ' +
             sections['MY POSITIONS'].length + ' positions, ' +
             sections['ARETE WATCHING'].length + ' arete watching, ' +
             sections['ARETE SWING'].length + ' arete swing, ' +
             sections['DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS'].length + ' dt carry, ' +
             sections['WATCHING'].length + ' watching, ' +
             changes.length + ' changes flagged');
}

// ── Helper: Write one Market tab section as a table in the doc ──
function _writeMarketSection(body, sectionName, headers, rows) {
  if (rows.length === 0) return;
  
  body.appendParagraph(sectionName).setHeading(DocumentApp.ParagraphHeading.HEADING2);
  
  // Compact inline format for Gameplan (1-2 rows)
  if (sectionName === 'GAMEPLAN') {
    for (var gi = 0; gi < rows.length; gi++) {
      body.appendParagraph(rows[gi].filter(function(v) { return v !== ''; }).join(' \u00B7 '))
          .setBold(true).setFontSize(11);
    }
    return;
  }
  
  // Table format for everything else
  var hasHeader = (headers && headers.length > 0 && String(headers[1] || '') !== '');
  var table = body.appendTable();
  
  if (hasHeader) {
    var hRow = table.appendTableRow();
    for (var hc = 0; hc < 4; hc++) {
      var hCell = hRow.appendTableCell(String(headers[hc] || ''));
      hCell.editAsText().setBold(true).setFontSize(9);
    }
  }
  
  for (var ri = 0; ri < rows.length; ri++) {
    var dRow = table.appendTableRow();
    for (var dc = 0; dc < 4; dc++) {
      var val = String(rows[ri][dc] || '');
      // Format date objects that come through as raw timestamps
      if (val.indexOf('GMT') >= 0 || (val.indexOf('T') >= 0 && val.indexOf(':') >= 0 && val.length > 15)) {
        try {
          var d = new Date(val);
          if (!isNaN(d.getTime())) {
            val = (d.getMonth()+1) + '/' + d.getDate() + ' ' + d.getHours() + ':' + (d.getMinutes() < 10 ? '0' : '') + d.getMinutes();
          }
        } catch(e) {}
      }
      dRow.appendTableCell(val).editAsText().setFontSize(9);
    }
  }
  
  // Remove the phantom empty first row that appendTable() creates
  if (table.getNumRows() > 0) {
    var firstRow = table.getRow(0);
    if (firstRow.getNumCells() === 1 && firstRow.getCell(0).getText().trim() === '') {
      table.removeRow(0);
    }
  }
}

// ==================== ARETE TRADES TAB to CONFIG SYNC ====================
// Reads "ARETE TRADES" tab, pulls SWING TRADES and DAYTRADE CARRY OVERS
// sections, strips annotations like "(short)", writes tickers to Config col D/E
// under ARETE SWING and DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS headers.
// Returns flag data (NEW/UPDATE) for use by syncWatchlistDoc.
// Run on same hourly trigger as syncWatchlistDoc (call from wrapper).

function syncAreteToConfig() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const areteSheet = ss.getSheetByName('ARETE TRADES');
  if (!areteSheet) {
    Logger.log('syncAreteToConfig: No "ARETE TRADES" tab found — skipping');
    return { 'ARETE SWING': [], 'DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS': [] };
  }
  
  const configSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Config');
  if (!configSheet) {
    Logger.log('syncAreteToConfig: No "Config" tab found — skipping');
    return { 'ARETE SWING': [], 'DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS': [] };
  }
  
  // --- Read ARETE TRADES tab ---
  // Col A = section headers OR flags (NEW/UPDATE), Col B = tickers, Col K = notes
  const areteLast = areteSheet.getLastRow();
  if (areteLast < 2) return { 'ARETE SWING': [], 'DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS': [] };
  const areteData = areteSheet.getRange(1, 1, areteLast, 11).getValues(); // A through K
  
  // Source section names on ARETE TRADES tab to target section names on Config
  const SOURCE_TO_TARGET = {
    'SWING TRADES': 'ARETE SWING',
    'DAYTRADE CARRY OVERS': 'DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS',
    'DAYTRADE CARRYOVERS': 'DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS',
    'DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS': 'DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS',
    'DT CARRY OVERS': 'DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS'
  };
  
  // Flags that indicate a ticker change (not a section header)
  const FLAG_WORDS = new Set(['NEW', 'UPDATE', 'UPDATED', 'REMOVED', 'CLOSED']);
  
  // Words/patterns to ignore (sub-headers, descriptions, legends)
  const IGNORE_PATTERNS = ['(', 'LEGEND', 'LAST UPDATED', 'STOCK TICKER'];
  
  // Store tickers with flags: {ticker, flag}
  const targetTickers = {
    'ARETE SWING': [],
    'DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS': []
  };
  
  let currentSection = '';
  
  // Helper: check if colA starts with any known source section name
  function matchSection(text) {
    var keys = Object.keys(SOURCE_TO_TARGET);
    for (var k = 0; k < keys.length; k++) {
      if (text === keys[k] || text.indexOf(keys[k]) === 0) {
        return SOURCE_TO_TARGET[keys[k]];
      }
    }
    return null;
  }
  
  // Helper: should this row be ignored (sub-headers, descriptions)?
  function shouldIgnore(text) {
    for (var p = 0; p < IGNORE_PATTERNS.length; p++) {
      if (text.indexOf(IGNORE_PATTERNS[p]) === 0 || text.indexOf(IGNORE_PATTERNS[p]) >= 0) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
  
  for (let i = 0; i < areteData.length; i++) {
    const colA = String(areteData[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    const colB = String(areteData[i][1] || '').trim();
    
    // Skip empty rows and ignorable rows (sub-headers, legends)
    if (colA === '' && colB === '') continue;
    if (shouldIgnore(colA)) continue;
    
    // Check if this row is a section header
    var matched = matchSection(colA);
    if (matched) {
      currentSection = matched;
    } else if (colA !== '' && !FLAG_WORDS.has(colA)) {
      // Some other section header (OPTIONS, SPECIAL SITUATIONS, etc.) — stop capturing
      if (currentSection !== '') {
        currentSection = '';
      }
    }
    
    // Capture ticker if we're in a target section
    if (currentSection !== '' && colB !== '') {
      // Clean ticker for Config (strip annotations)
      let ticker = colB.replace(/\s*\(.*?\)\s*/g, '').trim().toUpperCase();
      // Display label for doc (preserve annotations like "short")
      let label = ticker;
      var annoMatch = colB.match(/\(([^)]+)\)/);
      if (annoMatch) {
        label = ticker + ' (' + annoMatch[1].trim().toLowerCase() + ')';
      }
      // Determine flag
      let flag = '';
      if (FLAG_WORDS.has(colA)) {
        flag = colA;
      }
      // Col C = entry date (index 2), Col D = entry price (index 3), Col K = notes (index 10)
      let entryDateRaw = areteData[i][2];
      let entryDate = '';
      if (entryDateRaw instanceof Date) {
        entryDate = (entryDateRaw.getMonth() + 1) + '/' + entryDateRaw.getDate();
      } else if (entryDateRaw) {
        entryDate = String(entryDateRaw).trim();
      }
      let entryPriceRaw = areteData[i][3];
      let entryPrice = '';
      if (typeof entryPriceRaw === 'number' && entryPriceRaw > 0) {
        entryPrice = '$' + entryPriceRaw.toFixed(2);
      } else if (entryPriceRaw) {
        let parsed = String(entryPriceRaw).trim();
        if (parsed !== '' && parsed !== '0') entryPrice = parsed;
      }
      let note = String(areteData[i][10] || '').trim();
      // Skip header-like words
      if (ticker && ticker !== 'STOCK TICKER' && ticker !== 'TICKER' && ticker !== '') {
        targetTickers[currentSection].push({ 
          ticker: ticker, label: label, flag: flag, 
          entryDate: entryDate, entryPrice: entryPrice, note: note 
        });
      }
    }
  }
  
  // --- Write to Config tab col D/E (tickers only, no flags) ---
  const configLast = configSheet.getLastRow();
  const configLastCol = configSheet.getLastColumn();
  const colD = 4;
  const colE = 5;
  
  let configColD = [];
  if (configLast >= 1 && configLastCol >= colD) {
    configColD = configSheet.getRange(1, colD, configLast, 1).getValues().map(function(r) {
      return String(r[0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    });
  }
  
  const targetSections = ['ARETE SWING', 'DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS'];
  
  const sectionRows = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < configColD.length; i++) {
    if (configColD[i] !== '') {
      sectionRows.push({name: configColD[i], row0: i});
    }
  }
  
  // Process each target section - work bottom-up to avoid row shifts
  for (let t = targetSections.length - 1; t >= 0; t--) {
    const secName = targetSections[t];
    const items = targetTickers[secName];
    
    let headerIdx = -1;
    for (let s = 0; s < sectionRows.length; s++) {
      if (sectionRows[s].name === secName) {
        headerIdx = sectionRows[s].row0;
        break;
      }
    }
    
    if (headerIdx === -1) {
      const appendRow = configLast + 1 + (t * 2);
      configSheet.getRange(appendRow, colD).setValue(secName);
      for (let i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
        configSheet.getRange(appendRow + 1 + i, colE).setValue(items[i].ticker);
      }
      Logger.log('syncAreteToConfig: Appended ' + secName + ' with ' + items.length + ' tickers');
    } else {
      let nextHeaderRow0 = configColD.length;
      for (let s = 0; s < sectionRows.length; s++) {
        if (sectionRows[s].row0 > headerIdx) {
          nextHeaderRow0 = sectionRows[s].row0;
          break;
        }
      }
      
      const startClearRow = headerIdx + 2;
      const endClearRow = nextHeaderRow0 + 1;
      
      if (endClearRow > startClearRow) {
        const clearCount = endClearRow - startClearRow;
        // Only clear col E (tickers) — do NOT clear col D (section headers)
        configSheet.getRange(startClearRow, colE, clearCount, 1).clearContent();
      }
      
      for (let i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
        configSheet.getRange(startClearRow + i, colE).setValue(items[i].ticker);
      }
      
      Logger.log('syncAreteToConfig: Updated ' + secName + ' — ' + items.length + ' tickers');
    }
  }
  
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  Logger.log('syncAreteToConfig: Complete');
  
  // Return flag data for syncWatchlistDoc to use in the doc
  return targetTickers;
}

// ==================== COMBINED SYNC WRAPPER ====================
// Call this from the hourly trigger — runs Arete mirror first, then PM doc sync
// Passes Arete flag data through to the doc writer.

function syncAll() {
  const areteFlags = syncAreteToConfig();  // Mirror ARETE TRADES tab to Config, get flags
  syncWatchlistDoc(areteFlags);            // Config + Market tab + Econ Calendar to Watchlist Doc
}

// Breadth symbols
const BREADTH_SYMBOLS = ['$TICK', '$ADD', '$ADQD', '$VOLD', '$VOLQD', '$VIX'];

// Sector ETFs
const GROWTH_SECTORS = ['XLK', 'SOXX', 'SMH', 'XLY', 'XLF', 'XLI', 'XLC', 'IWM'];
const DEFENSIVE_SECTORS = ['XLU', 'XLP', 'XLV', 'XLE', 'XLB'];

// Sector ETF → description + biggest names
const SECTOR_INFO = {
  'XLK':  'Technology | AAPL, MSFT, NVDA, AVGO',
  'SOXX': 'Semiconductors | NVDA, AVGO, AMD, QCOM',
  'SMH':  'Semis (VanEck) | TSM, NVDA, AVGO, ASML',
  'XLY':  'Consumer Disc | AMZN, TSLA, HD, MCD',
  'XLF':  'Financials | BRK.B, JPM, V, MA',
  'XLI':  'Industrials | GE, CAT, UNP, RTX',

// How many 5-min bars to pull for RSI/EMA (14-period RSI needs ~20 bars)
const BARS_BACK = 30;

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// RVOL TIME-OF-DAY (Per-Ticker Volume Profile)
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// _VolProfile tab: 10-day rolling average of cumulative volume at each 5-min slot
// _VolToday tab: today's cumulative volume snapshots (merged into profile at EOD)
// Zero extra UrlFetch — reads quote.Volume already fetched

var VOLP_DAYS = 10;        // Rolling average window
var VOLP_OUTLIER_CAP = 2;  // Cap outlier days at 2x average (prevents earnings distortion)

// ── Read profile for a ticker at a given slot ──
var _volProfileCache = null; // {ticker: {slot: avgVol}}
var _volProfileDate = '';

function _loadVolProfile(ss) {
  if (_volProfileCache && _volProfileDate === Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd')) {
    return _volProfileCache;
  }
  _volProfileCache = {};
  var sh = ss.getSheetByName('_VolProfile');
  if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() <= 1 || sh.getLastColumn() <= 1) return _volProfileCache;
  var data = sh.getDataRange().getValues();
  var header = data[0];
  for (var r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    var slot = parseInt(data[r][0]) || 0;
    if (!slot) continue;
    for (var c = 1; c < header.length; c++) {
      var tk = String(header[c]).trim();
      if (!tk) continue;
      var vol = parseFloat(data[r][c]) || 0;
      if (vol > 0) {
        if (!_volProfileCache[tk]) _volProfileCache[tk] = {};
        _volProfileCache[tk][slot] = vol;
      }
    }
  }
  _volProfileDate = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  return _volProfileCache;
}

// ── Get RVOL-TOD for a ticker ──
// Returns adjusted RVOL based on per-ticker volume profile
// Falls back to generic curve if no profile data
function getRvolTOD(volume, prevDayVolume, ticker, ss) {
  if (!prevDayVolume || prevDayVolume <= 0) return volume > 0 ? 1.0 : 0;
  var now = new Date();
  var azH = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'H'), 10);
  var azM = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'm'), 10);
  var azMin = azH * 60 + azM;
  var slot = Math.floor(azMin / 5) * 5;
  var _rOff = _getMarketOffset();
  if (slot < (450 - _rOff)) slot = 450 - _rOff;
  if (slot > (840 - _rOff)) return prevDayVolume > 0 ? volume / prevDayVolume : 1.0; // AH: raw RVOL

  // Try per-ticker profile first
  if (ticker && ss) {
    var profile = _loadVolProfile(ss);
    var tkProfile = profile[ticker];
    if (tkProfile && tkProfile[slot] && tkProfile[slot] > 0) {
      return volume / tkProfile[slot];
    }
  }

  // Fallback: generic market-wide curve
  var pct = _genericVolPct(slot);
  if (pct <= 0) return 1.0;
  var expected = prevDayVolume * pct;
  return expected > 0 ? (volume / expected) : 1.0;
}

// Generic fallback curve (market-wide U-shape)
function _genericVolPct(slot) {
  // First 30min: ~25% of volume. Midday: gradual. Last 30min: ~15%
  var elapsed = slot - (450 - _rOff); // minutes since market open
  var total = (840 - _rOff) - (450 - _rOff);    // total minutes
  if (elapsed <= 0) return 0.01;
  if (elapsed >= total) return 1.0;
  // U-shape model: heavier at open and close
  var t = elapsed / total; // 0 to 1
  // Open-heavy curve: y = 0.4*sqrt(t) + 0.6*t (front-loads volume)
  return Math.min(1.0, 0.4 * Math.sqrt(t) + 0.6 * t);
}

// ── Update today's volume snapshot ──
function _updateVolToday(ss, azHour, azMinute) {
  var azMin = azHour * 60 + azMinute;
  if (azMin < SPARK_START || azMin > SPARK_END) return;
  if (azMinute % SPARK_INTERVAL > 1 && azMinute % SPARK_INTERVAL < (SPARK_INTERVAL - 1)) return;
  var slotIdx = Math.round((azMin - SPARK_START) / SPARK_INTERVAL);
  if (slotIdx < 0 || slotIdx >= SPARK_SLOTS) return;

  var wlSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
  if (!wlSheet) return;
  var wlData = wlSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  var startRow = -1;
  for (var i = 0; i < wlData.length; i++) {
    if (String(wlData[i][3]).trim() === 'Ticker') { startRow = i + 1; break; }
  }
  if (startRow < 0) return;

  // Collect tickers + cumulative volume (from quote data in Watchlist)
  var tickers = [], volumes = {};
  for (var i = startRow; i < wlData.length; i++) {
    var tk = String(wlData[i][3] || '').trim();
    if (!tk || !/^[A-Z]{1,5}$/.test(tk)) continue;
    // Volume is in the Watchlist's volume column (index 36)
    var vol = parseInt(wlData[i][36]) || 0;
    if (vol > 0 && tickers.indexOf(tk) < 0) {
      tickers.push(tk);
      volumes[tk] = vol;
    }
  }
  if (!tickers.length) return;
  tickers.sort();

  var vtSheet = ss.getSheetByName('_VolToday');
  var today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd');

  if (!vtSheet) {
    vtSheet = ss.insertSheet('_VolToday');
  }

  // New day → clear and rebuild
  var dateCell = String(vtSheet.getRange(1, 1).getValue());
  if (dateCell !== today) {
    vtSheet.clearContents();
    var header = ['slot'];
    for (var t = 0; t < tickers.length; t++) header.push(tickers[t]);
    vtSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, header.length).setValues([header]);
    vtSheet.getRange(1, 1).setValue(today);
    var slots = [];
    for (var s = 0; s < SPARK_SLOTS; s++) slots.push([SPARK_START + s * SPARK_INTERVAL]);
    vtSheet.getRange(2, 1, SPARK_SLOTS, 1).setValues(slots);
  }

  // Read header for column mapping
  var headerRow = vtSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, vtSheet.getLastColumn() || 1).getValues()[0];
  var colMap = {};
  for (var c = 1; c < headerRow.length; c++) colMap[String(headerRow[c]).trim()] = c + 1;

  // Add new tickers
  var lastCol = headerRow.length;
  var newTickers = [];
  for (var t = 0; t < tickers.length; t++) {
    if (!colMap[tickers[t]]) {
      lastCol++;
      colMap[tickers[t]] = lastCol;
      newTickers.push(tickers[t]);
    }
  }
  if (newTickers.length) vtSheet.getRange(1, headerRow.length + 1, 1, newTickers.length).setValues([newTickers]);

  // Write volumes for this slot
  var row = slotIdx + 2;
  for (var t = 0; t < tickers.length; t++) {
    var col = colMap[tickers[t]];
    if (col && volumes[tickers[t]]) vtSheet.getRange(row, col).setValue(volumes[tickers[t]]);
  }
}

// ── EOD: Merge today into rolling profile ──
function _mergeVolProfile(ss) {
  var vtSheet = ss.getSheetByName('_VolToday');
  if (!vtSheet || vtSheet.getLastRow() <= 1) return;

  var vpSheet = ss.getSheetByName('_VolProfile');
  if (!vpSheet) vpSheet = ss.insertSheet('_VolProfile');

  var todayData = vtSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  var todayHeader = todayData[0];

  // Read existing profile
  var profileData = vpSheet.getLastRow() > 0 ? vpSheet.getDataRange().getValues() : [];
  var profileHeader = profileData.length ? profileData[0] : ['slot'];

  // Build profile map: {ticker: {slot: avgVol}}
  var profileMap = {};
  var profileColMap = {};
  for (var c = 1; c < profileHeader.length; c++) {
    var tk = String(profileHeader[c]).trim();
    if (tk) { profileColMap[tk] = c; profileMap[tk] = {}; }
  }
  for (var r = 1; r < profileData.length; r++) {
    var slot = parseInt(profileData[r][0]) || 0;
    for (var c = 1; c < profileHeader.length; c++) {
      var tk = String(profileHeader[c]).trim();
      var val = parseFloat(profileData[r][c]) || 0;
      if (tk && val > 0) profileMap[tk][slot] = val;
    }
  }

  // Read count (how many days have been merged)
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var dayCount = parseInt(props.getProperty('VOLP_DAY_COUNT') || '0');
  dayCount = Math.min(dayCount, VOLP_DAYS - 1); // Cap at window-1 so new day has weight

  // Merge today's data using exponential moving average
  // New avg = (old_avg × dayCount + today) / (dayCount + 1)
  // With outlier cap: if today > 2x old_avg, cap at 2x
  for (var c = 1; c < todayHeader.length; c++) {
    var tk = String(todayHeader[c]).trim();
    if (!tk) continue;
    if (!profileMap[tk]) profileMap[tk] = {};
    for (var r = 1; r < todayData.length; r++) {
      var slot = parseInt(todayData[r][0]) || 0;
      var todayVol = parseFloat(todayData[r][c]) || 0;
      if (!slot || !todayVol) continue;
      var oldAvg = profileMap[tk][slot] || 0;
      if (oldAvg > 0 && todayVol > oldAvg * VOLP_OUTLIER_CAP) {
        todayVol = oldAvg * VOLP_OUTLIER_CAP; // Cap outlier
      }
      if (dayCount > 0 && oldAvg > 0) {
        profileMap[tk][slot] = (oldAvg * dayCount + todayVol) / (dayCount + 1);
      } else {
        profileMap[tk][slot] = todayVol;
      }
    }
  }

  // Write merged profile back
  var allTickers = Object.keys(profileMap).sort();
  var newHeader = ['slot'];
  for (var t = 0; t < allTickers.length; t++) newHeader.push(allTickers[t]);

  var rows = [newHeader];
  for (var s = 0; s < SPARK_SLOTS; s++) {
    var slot = SPARK_START + s * SPARK_INTERVAL;
    var row = [slot];
    for (var t = 0; t < allTickers.length; t++) {
      row.push(Math.round(profileMap[allTickers[t]][slot] || 0));
    }
    rows.push(row);
  }

  vpSheet.clearContents();
  vpSheet.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length).setValues(rows);

  props.setProperty('VOLP_DAY_COUNT', Math.min(dayCount + 1, VOLP_DAYS).toString());
  Logger.log('VolProfile merged: ' + allTickers.length + ' tickers, day ' + (dayCount + 1) + '/' + VOLP_DAYS);
}

// VOLD/VOLDQ scaling divisors (TV-to-TradeStation normalization)
const VOLD_DIVISOR = 470;
const VOLDQ_DIVISOR = 1000;

// --- PHASE-BASED REFRESH SCHEDULE ---
// Controls which tickers get 5-min bars on each refresh to manage UrlFetch quota.
// Quotes (price/vol/change) always run for ALL tickers — bars are the expensive part.
//
// Phase 1: PRE-MARKET   7:00-7:30 AZ  — 1 full scan (1st refresh), then >=20 + Watchlist Doc
// Phase 2: MARKET OPEN  7:30-8:30 AZ  — >=20 + Watchlist Doc, 1 full scan at 30 min mark
// Phase 3: CORE SESSION 8:30-2:00 AZ  — >=22 + Watchlist Doc, full scan every 30 min
// Phase 4: AFTER-HOURS  2:00-4:00 AZ  — Watchlist Doc only
//
// Estimated daily budget: ~10,600 fetches (53% of 20K limit)

function _buildPhaseConfig() {
  var off = _getMarketOffset();
  return {
    PRE_MARKET:   { start: 390 - off, end: 450 - off, threshold: 20, fullInterval: 0, pmWatch: true },
    MARKET_OPEN:  { start: 450 - off, end: 510 - off, threshold: 20, fullInterval: 6, pmWatch: true },
    CORE_SESSION: { start: 510 - off, end: 840 - off, threshold: 22, fullInterval: 12, pmWatch: true },
    AFTER_HOURS:  { start: 840 - off, end: 960 - off, threshold: 99, fullInterval: 0, pmWatch: true }
  };
}
var PHASE_CONFIG = _buildPhaseConfig();
const _PC_INIT = {  // reference — actual from _buildPhaseConfig()
};

// AH smart filter: only these get bars after 2pm
function _getAHBarsTickers(ss) {
  var keep = new Set();
  // Open positions
  try {
    var posSheet = ss.getSheetByName('My Positions');
    if (posSheet && posSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var pv = posSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      for (var i = 1; i < pv.length; i++) {
        var tk = String(pv[i][1] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        if (tk && /^[A-Z]{1,5}$/.test(tk)) keep.add(tk);
      }
    }
  } catch(e) {}
  // Earnings today/tomorrow
  try {
    var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var earnRaw = props.getProperty('EARNINGS_THIS_WEEK');
    if (earnRaw) {
      var earns = JSON.parse(earnRaw);
      var today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
      var tmrw = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(Date.now() + 86400000), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
      for (var ei = 0; ei < earns.length; ei++) {
        var ed = earns[ei].date || '';
        if (ed === today || ed === tmrw) keep.add((earns[ei].symbol || '').toUpperCase());
      }
    }
  } catch(e) {}
  // Manual AH watch (comma-separated in ScriptProperty)
  try {
    var manual = (PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('AH_WATCH_TICKERS') || '').split(',');
    for (var mi = 0; mi < manual.length; mi++) {
      var mt = manual[mi].trim().toUpperCase();
      if (mt) keep.add(mt);
    }
  } catch(e) {}
  return keep;
}

const SCANNER_TIMEZONE = 'America/Phoenix'; // Arizona time (no DST)

// ── Dynamic ET↔AZ offset: detects EDT vs EST automatically ──
// AZ is always UTC-7. During EST (Nov-Mar): 2h behind ET, market 7:30-2:00 AZ.
// During EDT (Mar-Nov): 3h behind ET, market 6:30-1:00 AZ.
// Returns 60 during EDT, 0 during EST. Subtract from all EST-based AZ minutes.
var _cachedOffset = null;
function _etDstOffset() {
  var now = new Date();
  var azH = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, 'America/Phoenix', 'H'), 10);
  var etH = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, 'America/New_York', 'H'), 10);
  var diff = ((etH - azH) + 24) % 24;
  return diff >= 3 ? 60 : 0;
}
function _getMarketOffset() {
  if (_cachedOffset === null) _cachedOffset = _etDstOffset();
  return _cachedOffset;
}
function _resetMarketOffset() { _cachedOffset = null; }
function _marketOpenAZ()  { return 450 - _getMarketOffset(); }
function _marketCloseAZ() { return 840 - _getMarketOffset(); }

// --- URLFETCH QUOTA TRACKING (Rolling 24-Hour Window) ---
// Google's 20K UrlFetch quota resets on a ROLLING 24-hour basis, not at midnight.
// We track hourly buckets: each hour's count is stored as "QUOTA_HH=count".
// To get the rolling 24h total, we sum all buckets from the last 24 hours.
// Buckets older than 25 hours are pruned on each write.

const URLFETCH_QUOTA_LIMIT = 20000;  // Google Workspace limit

function _getQuotaBucketKey(date) {
  // Key format: "QUOTA_2026-02-19_14" (date + hour)
  return 'QUOTA_' + Utilities.formatDate(date, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd_HH');
}

function _getRolling24hCount() {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const now = new Date();
  let total = 0;
  const bucketKeys = [];
  
  // Check each of the last 24 hours
  for (let h = 0; h < 24; h++) {
    const bucketTime = new Date(now.getTime() - h * 3600000);
    const key = _getQuotaBucketKey(bucketTime);
    bucketKeys.push(key);
    const val = parseInt(props.getProperty(key) || '0');
    total += val;
  }
  
  return { count: total, bucketKeys: bucketKeys };
}

function _addQuotaCount(n, label) {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  const now = new Date();
  const key = _getQuotaBucketKey(now);
  
  // Increment current hour bucket (total)
  const current = parseInt(props.getProperty(key) || '0');
  props.setProperty(key, (current + n).toString());
  
  // Increment category subtotal for this hour
  // Categories: quotes, bars, market, bridge, claude, news, positions, other
  var cat = 'other';
  if (label.indexOf('quotes') === 0) cat = 'quotes';
  else if (label.indexOf('bars') === 0) cat = 'bars';
  else if (label.indexOf('market-') === 0) cat = 'market';
  else if (label.indexOf('bridge') === 0 || label.indexOf('pulse') === 0) cat = 'bridge';
  else if (label.indexOf('claude') === 0) cat = 'claude';
  else if (label.indexOf('finnhub') === 0 || label.indexOf('rss') === 0) cat = 'news';
  else if (label.indexOf('ts-') === 0 || label.indexOf('alpaca') === 0 || label.indexOf('position') === 0) cat = 'positions';
  var catKey = key + '_' + cat;
  var catCur = parseInt(props.getProperty(catKey) || '0');
  props.setProperty(catKey, (catCur + n).toString());
  
  // Update rolling log (last 20 entries for debugging)
  const log = props.getProperty('QUOTA_LOG') || '';
  const time = Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'HH:mm:ss');
  const rolling = _getRolling24hCount();
  const entry = time + ' +' + n + ' ' + label + ' (24h=' + rolling.count + ')';
  const lines = log ? log.split('|') : [];
  lines.push(entry);
  if (lines.length > 30) lines.splice(0, lines.length - 30);
  props.setProperty('QUOTA_LOG', lines.join('|'));
  
  // Prune old buckets (>25 hours) to avoid property buildup
  if (now.getMinutes() === 0) {
    _pruneOldBuckets(props, now);
  }
  
  return rolling.count;
}

function _pruneOldBuckets(props, now) {
  const allProps = props.getProperties();
  // Keep 5 days (120 hours) of buckets for dashboard history chart.
  // Since bucket keys use Arizona time and we compare against Arizona "now",
  // we just regenerate the 25 valid keys and delete anything else with QUOTA_2 prefix.
  const validKeys = new Set();
  for (let h = 0; h < 121; h++) {
    validKeys.add(_getQuotaBucketKey(new Date(now.getTime() - h * 3600000)));
  }
  validKeys.add('QUOTA_LOG');  // preserve the log
  
  for (const key in allProps) {
    if (key.startsWith('QUOTA_') && !validKeys.has(key)) {
      props.deleteProperty(key);
    }
    if (key.startsWith('APICOST_') || key.startsWith('APITOK_')) {
      var matchDate = key.substring(key.indexOf('_') + 1);
      var matchQuota = 'QUOTA_' + matchDate;
      if (!validKeys.has(matchQuota)) props.deleteProperty(key);
    }
  }
}

// Wrapped UrlFetchApp calls that auto-track quota
function trackedFetch(url, options, label) {
  _addQuotaCount(1, label || 'fetch');
  return UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
}

function trackedFetchAll(requests, label) {
  _addQuotaCount(requests.length, (label || 'fetchAll') + '×' + requests.length);
  return UrlFetchApp.fetchAll(requests);
}


// --- SCANNER ON/OFF SWITCHES ---
// Two independent toggles via ScriptProperties:
//   SCANNER_ENABLED  — controls 5-min partial refresh cycle (ON/OFF)
//   FULLSCAN_ENABLED — controls periodic 30-min full scans (ON/OFF)
// When scanner is OFF, the 5-min trigger still fires but updateSheet() exits immediately.
// When full scan is OFF, periodic fulls are skipped but partials still run.

function isScannerEnabled() {
  return PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('SCANNER_ENABLED') !== 'OFF';
}

function isFullScanEnabled() {
  return PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('FULLSCAN_ENABLED') !== 'OFF';
}

function isMarketRefreshEnabled() {
  return PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('MARKET_REFRESH_ENABLED') !== 'OFF';
}

function startScanner() {
  // Create trigger if none exists, AND enable
  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('SCANNER_ENABLED', 'ON');
  
  const triggers = ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers();
  let hasUpdateTrigger = false;
  for (const trigger of triggers) {
    if (trigger.getHandlerFunction() === 'updateSheet') {
      hasUpdateTrigger = true;
      break;
    }
  }
  if (!hasUpdateTrigger) {
    ScriptApp.newTrigger('updateSheet')
      .timeBased()
      .everyMinutes(5)
      .create();
  }
  
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('✅ Scanner ON — 5-min partial refresh running.');
}

function stopScanner() {
  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('SCANNER_ENABLED', 'OFF');
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('🛑 Scanner OFF — trigger still exists but updateSheet() will skip.\nUse "Start Scanner" to re-enable.');
}

function startFullScan() {
  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('FULLSCAN_ENABLED', 'ON');
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('✅ Periodic full scans ON — every 30 min during OPEN/CORE phases.');
}

function stopFullScan() {
  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('FULLSCAN_ENABLED', 'OFF');
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('🛑 Periodic full scans OFF — only partials will run.\nManual "Full Scan Now" still works.');
}

function startMarketRefresh() {
  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('MARKET_REFRESH_ENABLED', 'ON');
  
  const triggers = ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers();
  let hasMarketTrigger = false;
  for (const trigger of triggers) {
    if (trigger.getHandlerFunction() === 'updateMarketTab') {
      hasMarketTrigger = true;
      break;
    }
  }
  if (!hasMarketTrigger) {
    ScriptApp.newTrigger('updateMarketTab')
      .timeBased()
      .everyMinutes(1)
      .create();
  }
  
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('✅ Market tab 1-min refresh ON — ~1 fetch/min, ~420/day.');
}

function stopMarketRefresh() {
  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('MARKET_REFRESH_ENABLED', 'OFF');
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('🛑 Market tab 1-min refresh OFF — trigger still exists but updateMarketTab() will skip.');
}

function removeTrigger() {
  // Nuclear option — removes ALL triggers and disables everything
  const triggers = ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers();
  let removed = 0;
  for (const trigger of triggers) {
    var fn = trigger.getHandlerFunction();
    if (fn === 'updateSheet' || fn === 'updateMarketTab' || fn === 'weekendPulse') {
      ScriptApp.deleteTrigger(trigger);
      removed++;
    }
  }
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  props.setProperty('SCANNER_ENABLED', 'OFF');
  props.setProperty('FULLSCAN_ENABLED', 'OFF');
  props.setProperty('MARKET_REFRESH_ENABLED', 'OFF');
  props.setProperty('WEEKEND_PULSE_ENABLED', 'OFF');
  props.setProperty('PULSE_MODE', 'false');
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('🗑️ All triggers removed (' + removed + ' deleted) — scanner + full scans + market refresh + weekend pulse disabled.');
}

function showQuotaStatus() {
  const rolling = _getRolling24hCount();
  const log = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('QUOTA_LOG') || '(none)';
  const scannerOn = isScannerEnabled();
  const fullOn = isFullScanEnabled();
  const lines = log.split('|').join('\n');
  const pct = (rolling.count / URLFETCH_QUOTA_LIMIT * 100).toFixed(1);
  
  // Current phase (using reliable Utilities.formatDate for AZ timezone)
  var now = new Date();
  var _azH = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'H'), 10);
  var _azM = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'm'), 10);
  var azMin = _azH * 60 + _azM;
  var phase = 'OFF-HOURS';
  if (azMin >= PHASE_CONFIG.PRE_MARKET.start && azMin < PHASE_CONFIG.PRE_MARKET.end) phase = 'PRE-MARKET (>=20 + PMW)';
  else if (azMin >= PHASE_CONFIG.MARKET_OPEN.start && azMin < PHASE_CONFIG.MARKET_OPEN.end) phase = 'MARKET OPEN (>=20 + PMW, full/30m)';
  else if (azMin >= PHASE_CONFIG.CORE_SESSION.start && azMin < PHASE_CONFIG.CORE_SESSION.end) phase = 'CORE SESSION (>=22 + PMW, full/30m)';
  else if (azMin >= PHASE_CONFIG.AFTER_HOURS.start && azMin < PHASE_CONFIG.AFTER_HOURS.end) phase = 'AFTER-HOURS (PMW only)';
  
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(
    'QUOTA STATUS (Rolling 24h)\n' +
    '━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━\n' +
    'UrlFetch calls (24h): ' + rolling.count.toLocaleString() + ' / ' + URLFETCH_QUOTA_LIMIT.toLocaleString() + ' (' + pct + '%)\n' +
    '1-min Market: ' + (isMarketRefreshEnabled() ? '✅ ON' : '🛑 OFF') + '\n' +
    '5-min Scanner: ' + (scannerOn ? '✅ ON' : '🛑 OFF') + '\n' +
    '30-min Full Scan: ' + (fullOn ? '✅ ON' : '🛑 OFF') + '\n' +
    'Phase: ' + phase + ' (' + _azH + ':' + (_azM < 10 ? '0' : '') + _azM + ' AZ)\n\n' +
    'Recent log:\n' + lines
  );
}

// --- AUTH HELPERS ---

function getScriptProperties() {
  return PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
}

function getAccessToken() {
  const props = getScriptProperties();
  const tokenExpiry = props.getProperty('TOKEN_EXPIRY');
  const now = new Date().getTime();

  if (tokenExpiry && now < (parseInt(tokenExpiry) - 60000)) {
    return props.getProperty('ACCESS_TOKEN');
  }

  return refreshAccessToken();
}

function refreshAccessToken() {
  const props = getScriptProperties();
  const clientId = props.getProperty('CLIENT_ID');
  const clientSecret = props.getProperty('CLIENT_SECRET');
  const refreshToken = props.getProperty('REFRESH_TOKEN');

  const response = trackedFetch('https://signin.tradestation.com/oauth/token', {
    method: 'post',
    contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded',
    payload: {
      grant_type: 'refresh_token',
      client_id: clientId,
      client_secret: clientSecret,
      refresh_token: refreshToken
    },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  }, 'token-refresh');

  const data = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());

  if (data.access_token) {
    props.setProperty('ACCESS_TOKEN', data.access_token);
    props.setProperty('TOKEN_EXPIRY', String(new Date().getTime() + (data.expires_in * 1000)));
    return data.access_token;
  } else {
    Logger.log('Token refresh failed: ' + response.getContentText());
    throw new Error('Failed to refresh access token');
  }
}

// --- API HELPERS ---

function tsQuotes(symbols) {
  if (!symbols || symbols.length === 0) return [];
  const token = getAccessToken();
  const symbolStr = symbols.join(',');
  const url = 'https://api.tradestation.com/v3/marketdata/quotes/' + symbolStr;

  const response = trackedFetch(url, {
    headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  }, 'quotes-' + symbols.length);

  const code = response.getResponseCode();
  const text = response.getContentText();
  if (code !== 200) {
    Logger.log('tsQuotes HTTP ' + code + ' for ' + symbols.length + ' symbols | body: ' + text.substring(0, 300));
    return [];
  }
  if (!text || text.trim() === '') return [];

  try {
    const data = JSON.parse(text);
    return data.Quotes || [];
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Quote parse error: ' + e.message + ' | Response: ' + text.substring(0, 200));
    return [];
  }
}

function tsBars(symbol, interval, unit, barsBack) {
  const token = getAccessToken();
  const url = 'https://api.tradestation.com/v3/marketdata/barcharts/' + symbol
    + '?interval=' + interval + '&unit=' + unit + '&barsback=' + barsBack;

  const response = trackedFetch(url, {
    headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  }, 'bars-' + symbol);

  const text = response.getContentText();
  if (!text || text.trim() === '') return [];

  try {
    const data = JSON.parse(text);
    return data.Bars || [];
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Bars parse error for ' + symbol + ': ' + e.message + ' | Response: ' + text.substring(0, 200));
    return [];
  }
}

// --- TECHNICAL CALCULATIONS ---

function calcRSI(bars, period) {
  if (bars.length < period + 1) return 50;

  let gains = 0, losses = 0;

  for (let i = 1; i <= period; i++) {
    const change = parseFloat(bars[i].Close) - parseFloat(bars[i-1].Close);
    if (change > 0) gains += change;
    else losses += Math.abs(change);
  }

  let avgGain = gains / period;
  let avgLoss = losses / period;

  for (let i = period + 1; i < bars.length; i++) {
    const change = parseFloat(bars[i].Close) - parseFloat(bars[i-1].Close);
    if (change > 0) {
      avgGain = (avgGain * (period - 1) + change) / period;
      avgLoss = (avgLoss * (period - 1)) / period;
    } else {
      avgGain = (avgGain * (period - 1)) / period;
      avgLoss = (avgLoss * (period - 1) + Math.abs(change)) / period;
    }
  }

  if (avgLoss === 0) return 100;
  const rs = avgGain / avgLoss;
  return 100 - (100 / (1 + rs));
}

function calcEMA(bars, period, field) {
  if (bars.length < period) return parseFloat(bars[bars.length - 1][field || 'Close']);

  const multiplier = 2 / (period + 1);
  let ema = 0;

  for (let i = 0; i < period; i++) {
    ema += parseFloat(bars[i][field || 'Close']);
  }
  ema = ema / period;

  for (let i = period; i < bars.length; i++) {
    const price = parseFloat(bars[i][field || 'Close']);
    ema = (price - ema) * multiplier + ema;
  }

  return ema;
}

function calcVWAP(bars) {
  let cumVolPrice = 0;
  let cumVol = 0;

  for (const bar of bars) {
    const typical = (parseFloat(bar.High) + parseFloat(bar.Low) + parseFloat(bar.Close)) / 3;
    const vol = parseInt(bar.TotalVolume);
    cumVolPrice += typical * vol;
    cumVol += vol;
  }

  return cumVol > 0 ? cumVolPrice / cumVol : 0;
}

function calcATR(bars, period) {
  if (bars.length < 2) return 0;

  const trs = [];

  for (let i = 1; i < bars.length; i++) {
    const high = parseFloat(bars[i].High);
    const low = parseFloat(bars[i].Low);
    const prevClose = parseFloat(bars[i-1].Close);
    const tr = Math.max(high - low, Math.abs(high - prevClose), Math.abs(low - prevClose));
    trs.push(tr);
  }

  const start = Math.max(0, trs.length - period);
  let sum = 0;
  for (let i = start; i < trs.length; i++) sum += trs[i];
  return sum / Math.min(period, trs.length - start);
}

// --- BREADTH SCORING ---

function scoreBreadth(breadthQuotes) {
  const q = {};
  for (const quote of breadthQuotes) {
    q[quote.Symbol] = quote;
  }

  let score = 0;

  const tick = parseFloat((q['$TICK'] || {}).Last || 0);
  if (tick >= 700) score += 2;
  else if (tick >= 300) score += 1;
  else if (tick <= -700) score -= 2;
  else if (tick <= -300) score -= 1;

  const add = parseFloat((q['$ADD'] || {}).Last || 0);
  if (add >= 1000) score += 2;
  else if (add >= 400) score += 1;
  else if (add <= -1000) score -= 2;
  else if (add <= -400) score -= 1;

  const adqd = parseFloat((q['$ADQD'] || {}).Last || 0);
  if (adqd >= 1000) score += 2;
  else if (adqd >= 500) score += 1;
  else if (adqd <= -1000) score -= 2;
  else if (adqd <= -500) score -= 1;

  const vold = parseFloat((q['$VOLD'] || {}).Last || 0) / VOLD_DIVISOR;
  if (vold >= 700000) score += 2;
  else if (vold >= 150000) score += 1;
  else if (vold <= -700000) score -= 2;
  else if (vold <= -150000) score -= 1;

  const volqd = parseFloat((q['$VOLQD'] || {}).Last || 0) / VOLDQ_DIVISOR;
  if (volqd >= 3500000) score += 2;
  else if (volqd >= 1500000) score += 1;
  else if (volqd <= -3500000) score -= 2;
  else if (volqd <= -1500000) score -= 1;

  const vix = parseFloat((q['$VIX'] || {}).Last || 20);
  if (vix < 15) score += 1;
  else if (vix <= 18) score += 0.5;

  return { score, tick, add, adqd, vold, volqd, vix };
}

// --- SECTOR SCORING ---

function scoreSectors(sectorQuotes) {
  let growthGreen = 0;
  let defGreen = 0;
  const sectorData = {};

  for (const q of sectorQuotes) {
    const pct = parseFloat(q.NetChangePct || 0);
    sectorData[q.Symbol] = pct;

    if (GROWTH_SECTORS.includes(q.Symbol) && pct > 0) growthGreen++;
    if (DEFENSIVE_SECTORS.includes(q.Symbol) && pct > 0) defGreen++;
  }

  let sectorPts = 0;
  if (growthGreen >= 7) sectorPts = 1.5;
  else if (growthGreen === 6) sectorPts = 1.25;
  else if (growthGreen === 5) sectorPts = 1.0;
  else if (growthGreen === 4) sectorPts = 0.75;
  else if (growthGreen === 3) sectorPts = 0.5;
  else if (growthGreen === 2) sectorPts = 0.25;

  if (defGreen >= 4 && growthGreen <= 2) sectorPts -= 0.5;
  if (defGreen >= 3 && growthGreen >= 6) sectorPts += 0.5;

  let leader = '', lagger = '', leaderPct = -999, laggerPct = 999;
  for (const sym of [...GROWTH_SECTORS, ...DEFENSIVE_SECTORS]) {
    const pct = sectorData[sym] || 0;
    if (pct > leaderPct) { leaderPct = pct; leader = sym; }
    if (pct < laggerPct) { laggerPct = pct; lagger = sym; }
  }

  return { sectorPts, growthGreen, defGreen, leader, lagger, leaderPct, laggerPct, sectorData };
}

// --- GAMEPLAN ---

function getGameplan(totalScore) {
  const adjPct = ((totalScore + 10) / 29) * 100;

  let gp, action, sizing;
  if (totalScore >= 9.5) {
    gp = 'A'; action = 'HUNT MODE'; sizing = '$15-20K';
  } else if (totalScore >= 3) {
    gp = 'B'; action = 'SNIPER MODE'; sizing = '$8-12K';
  } else if (totalScore >= -3) {
    gp = 'C'; action = 'SELECTIVE — CHECK SUB-MODE'; sizing = '$0–$6K (sub-mode dependent)';
  } else {
    gp = 'D'; action = 'SHORT MODE'; sizing = '$8-12K inverse';
  }

  return { gp, action, sizing, adjPct: adjPct.toFixed(1) };
}

// --- TRAJECTORY & GP SUB-MODE ---
// Analyzes breadth history to classify trajectory as Improving/Stable/Fading.
// Combined with GP letter to produce sub-mode labels like A-Cooling, C-Recovery, etc.
// Returns { trajectory, subMode, label, sizingAdj }

function classifyTrajectory(breadthHistory) {
  if (!breadthHistory || breadthHistory.length < 3) {
    return { trajectory: 'Stable', confidence: 'low' };
  }
  
  // Use last 6 readings (or all if fewer)
  var recent = breadthHistory.slice(-Math.min(6, breadthHistory.length));
  var oldest = recent[0].v;
  var newest = recent[recent.length - 1].v;
  var delta = newest - oldest;
  
  // Calculate slope: average change per reading
  var totalChange = 0;
  for (var i = 1; i < recent.length; i++) {
    totalChange += (recent[i].v - recent[i - 1].v);
  }
  var avgChange = totalChange / (recent.length - 1);
  
  // Calculate volatility (are readings bouncy or smooth?)
  var reversals = 0;
  for (var i = 2; i < recent.length; i++) {
    var prev = recent[i - 1].v - recent[i - 2].v;
    var curr = recent[i].v - recent[i - 1].v;
    if ((prev > 0 && curr < 0) || (prev < 0 && curr > 0)) reversals++;
  }
  var isChoppy = reversals >= Math.floor((recent.length - 2) * 0.6);
  
  // Classify
  var trajectory, confidence;
  if (isChoppy && Math.abs(delta) < 2.0) {
    trajectory = 'Choppy';
    confidence = 'medium';
  } else if (delta >= 2.0 || avgChange >= 0.4) {
    trajectory = 'Improving';
    confidence = Math.abs(delta) >= 3.0 ? 'high' : 'medium';
  } else if (delta <= -2.0 || avgChange <= -0.4) {
    trajectory = 'Fading';
    confidence = Math.abs(delta) >= 3.0 ? 'high' : 'medium';
  } else {
    trajectory = 'Stable';
    confidence = 'medium';
  }
  
  return { trajectory: trajectory, confidence: confidence, delta: delta.toFixed(1), avgChange: avgChange.toFixed(2) };
}

function getGPSubMode(gpLetter, trajectoryResult) {
  var traj = trajectoryResult.trajectory;
  
  // Sub-mode label mapping
  var modeMap = {
    'A-Improving':  { label: 'A-Surge',         sizingAdj: 'full',    desc: 'Screaming. All setups, lean in.' },
    'A-Stable':     { label: 'A-Steady',         sizingAdj: 'full',    desc: 'Strong and holding.' },
    'A-Fading':     { label: 'A-Cooling',        sizingAdj: 'reduce',  desc: 'Losing steam. Tighten stops, no new max-size.' },
    'A-Choppy':     { label: 'A-Choppy',         sizingAdj: 'caution', desc: 'Strong but erratic. Standard size, watch closely.' },
    'B-Improving':  { label: 'B-Building',       sizingAdj: 'standard', desc: 'Approaching A. Start positioning.' },
    'B-Stable':     { label: 'B-Steady',         sizingAdj: 'standard', desc: 'Solid. High confluence setups.' },
    'B-Fading':     { label: 'B-Weakening',      sizingAdj: 'reduce',  desc: 'Heading toward C. Reduce new entries.' },
    'B-Choppy':     { label: 'B-Choppy',         sizingAdj: 'caution', desc: 'Positive but noisy. Be selective.' },
    'C-Improving':  { label: 'C-Recovery',       sizingAdj: 'small',   desc: 'Getting better. Tier 1-2, select setups.' },
    'C-Stable':     { label: 'C-Flat',           sizingAdj: 'bench',   desc: 'Going nowhere. Very selective or bench.' },
    'C-Fading':     { label: 'C-Deteriorating',  sizingAdj: 'bench',   desc: 'Heading toward D. Shorts only or sit out.' },
    'C-Choppy':     { label: 'C-Choppy',         sizingAdj: 'bench',   desc: 'Directionless noise. Bench.' },
    'D-Improving':  { label: 'D-Bottoming',      sizingAdj: 'reduce',  desc: 'Worst may be over. Reduce inverse size, trail stops.' },
    'D-Stable':     { label: 'D-Persistent',     sizingAdj: 'inverse', desc: 'Staying ugly. Inverse ETFs or sit out.' },
    'D-Fading':     { label: 'D-Capitulation',   sizingAdj: 'inverse', desc: 'Getting worse. Max inverse or full sit-out.' },
    'D-Choppy':     { label: 'D-Choppy',         sizingAdj: 'reduce',  desc: 'Ugly and erratic. Reduced inverse or sit out.' }
  };
  
  var key = gpLetter + '-' + traj;
  var mode = modeMap[key] || { label: gpLetter + '-' + traj, sizingAdj: 'standard', desc: '' };
  
  return {
    subMode: mode.label,
    sizingAdj: mode.sizingAdj,
    desc: mode.desc,
    trajectory: traj,
    confidence: trajectoryResult.confidence,
    delta: trajectoryResult.delta,
    avgChange: trajectoryResult.avgChange
  };
}

// --- NEWS CATALYST LOOKUP (for confluence scoring) ---
// Reads cached news (Finnhub + RSS) from ScriptProperties and builds
// a Set of tickers that have news today. Called once per refresh cycle,
// result passed into calcConfluence for each ticker.

function buildNewsCatalystSet() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var tickerSet = {};
  
  // Company name → ticker map (matches getNewsTags in dashboard)
  var companyMap = {
    "apple":"AAPL","microsoft":"MSFT","google":"GOOG","alphabet":"GOOG","amazon":"AMZN",
    "meta":"META","facebook":"META","nvidia":"NVDA","tesla":"TSLA","netflix":"NFLX",
    "amd":"AMD","intel":"INTC","broadcom":"AVGO","qualcomm":"QCOM","tsmc":"TSM",
    "asml":"ASML","micron":"MU","palantir":"PLTR","salesforce":"CRM","adobe":"ADBE",
    "coinbase":"COIN","jpmorgan":"JPM","goldman":"GS","morgan stanley":"MS",
    "bank of america":"BAC","wells fargo":"WFC","citigroup":"C","disney":"DIS",
    "boeing":"BA","caterpillar":"CAT","exxon":"XOM","chevron":"CVX",
    "walmart":"WMT","costco":"COST","home depot":"HD","target":"TGT",
    "uber":"UBER","airbnb":"ABNB","spotify":"SPOT","snap":"SNAP",
    "crowdstrike":"CRWD","snowflake":"SNOW","datadog":"DDOG","shopify":"SHOP",
    "arm holdings":"ARM","super micro":"SMCI","supermicro":"SMCI",
    "eli lilly":"LLY","novo nordisk":"NVO","unitedhealth":"UNH",
    "berkshire":"BRK.B","warren buffett":"BRK.B"
  };
  var skip = {"THE":1,"AND":1,"FOR":1,"ARE":1,"BUT":1,"NOT":1,"YOU":1,"ALL":1,"CAN":1,"HAS":1,"HER":1,"WAS":1,"ONE":1,"OUR":1,"OUT":1,"NEW":1,"NOW":1,"WAY":1,"MAY":1,"SAY":1,"SHE":1,"TWO":1,"HOW":1,"ITS":1,"LET":1,"PUT":1,"TOO":1,"USE":1,"CEO":1,"IPO":1,"GDP":1,"CPI":1,"PPI":1,"PCE":1,"FED":1,"SEC":1,"USA":1,"NYSE":1,"ETF":1,"DOJ":1,"FTC":1,"NATO":1,"OPEC":1,"IMF":1,"WHO":1,"FBI":1};
  
  function extractTickers(headline, related) {
    var tickers = [];
    var seen = {};
    // Related field
    if (related) {
      var rel = related.split(',');
      for (var r = 0; r < rel.length; r++) {
        var tk = rel[r].trim().toUpperCase();
        if (tk && tk.length >= 1 && tk.length <= 5 && !seen[tk]) { seen[tk] = 1; tickers.push(tk); }
      }
    }
    // $TICKER patterns
    var dm = headline.match(/\$([A-Z]{1,5})/g);
    if (dm) {
      for (var d = 0; d < dm.length; d++) {
        var tk = dm[d].replace('$', '');
        if (!seen[tk]) { seen[tk] = 1; tickers.push(tk); }
      }
    }
    // Uppercase words (3-5 chars)
    var words = headline.split(/[^A-Za-z]+/);
    for (var w = 0; w < words.length; w++) {
      var wd = words[w];
      if (wd.length >= 2 && wd.length <= 5 && wd === wd.toUpperCase() && /^[A-Z]+$/.test(wd) && !skip[wd] && !seen[wd]) {
        seen[wd] = 1; tickers.push(wd);
      }
    }
    // Company names
    var lower = headline.toLowerCase();
    var keys = Object.keys(companyMap);
    for (var c = 0; c < keys.length; c++) {
      if (lower.indexOf(keys[c]) >= 0) {
        var tk = companyMap[keys[c]];
        if (!seen[tk]) { seen[tk] = 1; tickers.push(tk); }
      }
    }
    return tickers;
  }
  
  // Parse both news caches
  var allNews = [];
  try {
    var fhRaw = props.getProperty('NEWS_CACHE');
    if (fhRaw) allNews = allNews.concat(JSON.parse(fhRaw));
  } catch(e) {}
  try {
    var rssRaw = props.getProperty('RSS_NEWS_CACHE');
    if (rssRaw) allNews = allNews.concat(JSON.parse(rssRaw));
  } catch(e) {}
  
  // Only consider news from last 12 hours
  var cutoff = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000) - (12 * 3600);
  for (var i = 0; i < allNews.length; i++) {
    if (allNews[i].time && allNews[i].time < cutoff) continue;
    var tickers = extractTickers(allNews[i].headline || '', allNews[i].related || '');
    for (var t = 0; t < tickers.length; t++) {
      tickerSet[tickers[t]] = 1;
    }
  }
  
  Logger.log('News catalyst set: ' + Object.keys(tickerSet).length + ' tickers with news today');
  return tickerSet;
}

// --- CONFLUENCE SCORING (per ticker) ---

function calcConfluence(quote, bars, spyQuote, breadthScore, vix, newsCatalystSet) {
  const last = parseFloat(quote.Last);
  const vwap = parseFloat(quote.VWAP || 0);
  const bid = parseFloat(quote.Bid || 0);
  const ask = parseFloat(quote.Ask || 0);
  const volume = parseInt(quote.Volume || 0);
  const prevVolume = parseInt(quote.PreviousVolume || 1);
  const prevClose = parseFloat(quote.PreviousClose || last);
  const open = parseFloat(quote.Open || last);
  const high = parseFloat(quote.High || last);
  const low = parseFloat(quote.Low || last);
  const netPct = parseFloat(quote.NetChangePct || 0);
  const spyPct = parseFloat(spyQuote.NetChangePct || 0);

  const rsi5m = calcRSI(bars, 14);
  const ema9 = calcEMA(bars, 9);
  const ema20 = calcEMA(bars, 20);
  const ema50 = calcEMA(bars, 50);
  const atr = calcATR(bars, 14);
  const calcedVwap = vwap > 0 ? vwap : calcVWAP(bars);

  const rvolRaw = prevVolume > 0 ? volume / prevVolume : 1;
  const rvol = getRvolTOD(volume, prevVolume, quote.Symbol, null); // Per-ticker RVOL-TOD (global cache)
  const relStr = netPct - spyPct;
  const gapPct = prevClose > 0 ? ((open - prevClose) / prevClose) * 100 : 0;

  const orHigh = bars.length > 0 ? parseFloat(bars[0].High) : high;
  const orLow = bars.length > 0 ? parseFloat(bars[0].Low) : low;

  const spread = ask - bid;
  const spreadPct = last > 0 ? (spread / last) * 100 : 999;
