  // 1. Market Context (0-5) — rebalanced v90.5: C days get 2-2.5 not 1-2
  let marketCtx = 0;
  if (breadthScore >= 9.5) marketCtx = 5;
  else if (breadthScore >= 6) marketCtx = 4;
  else if (breadthScore >= 3) marketCtx = 3;
  else if (breadthScore >= 0) marketCtx = 2.5;
  else if (breadthScore >= -3) marketCtx = 2;
  else marketCtx = 1;

  // 2. Price Structure (0-5)
  let priceStr = 0;
  if (last > calcedVwap) priceStr += 1.5;
  if (last > ema9) priceStr += 1;
  if (last > ema20) priceStr += 1;
  if (ema9 > ema20) priceStr += 0.5;
  if (last > orHigh) priceStr += 1;
  else if (last > orLow) priceStr += 0.5;
  priceStr = Math.min(5, priceStr);

  // 3. Momentum (0-5)
  let momentum = 0;
  if (rsi5m >= 40 && rsi5m <= 60) momentum += 3;
  else if (rsi5m >= 55 && rsi5m <= 75) momentum += 2.5;
  else if (rsi5m >= 30 && rsi5m <= 40) momentum += 1.5;
  else if (rsi5m > 75) momentum += 0.5;
  else if (rsi5m < 30) momentum += 1;
  if (last > ema9 && ema9 > ema20) momentum += 2;
  else if (last > ema9) momentum += 1;
  momentum = Math.min(5, momentum);

  // 4. Volume (0-5)
  let volScore = 0;
  if (rvol >= 3.0) volScore = 5;
  else if (rvol >= 2.0) volScore = 4;
  else if (rvol >= 1.5) volScore = 3;
  else if (rvol >= 1.0) volScore = 2;
  else if (rvol >= 0.75) volScore = 1;

  // 5. Key Level Proximity (0-5)
  let levelProx = 0;
  const vwapDist = calcedVwap > 0 ? Math.abs(last - calcedVwap) / calcedVwap * 100 : 999;
  const orHighDist = orHigh > 0 ? Math.abs(last - orHigh) / orHigh * 100 : 999;
  if (vwapDist < 0.3) levelProx += 2.5;
  else if (vwapDist < 0.5) levelProx += 1.5;
  else if (vwapDist < 1.0) levelProx += 0.5;
  if (orHighDist < 0.3) levelProx += 2.5;
  else if (orHighDist < 0.5) levelProx += 1.5;
  levelProx = Math.min(5, levelProx);

  // 6. Execution Quality (0-5)
  let execQual = 0;
  if (spreadPct < 0.03) execQual += 2.5;
  else if (spreadPct < 0.05) execQual += 2;
  else if (spreadPct < 0.1) execQual += 1;
  if (volume > 5000000) execQual += 1.5;
  else if (volume > 1000000) execQual += 1;
  else if (volume > 500000) execQual += 0.5;
  const now = new Date();
  const etHour = now.getUTCHours() - 5;
  if ((etHour >= 9 && etHour < 11) || (etHour >= 15 && etHour < 16)) execQual += 1;
  execQual = Math.min(5, execQual);

  const coreTotal = marketCtx + priceStr + momentum + volScore + levelProx + execQual;

  // ATR Multiple (+2 to -2)
  let atrMod = 0;
  const dayRange = high - low;
  const atrMult = atr > 0 ? dayRange / atr : 1;
  if (atrMult <= 0.5) atrMod = 2;
  else if (atrMult <= 1.0) atrMod = 1;
  else if (atrMult <= 1.5) atrMod = 0;
  else if (atrMult <= 2.5) atrMod = -1;
  else atrMod = -2;

  // Gap Analysis (+2 to -2)
  let gapMod = 0;
  const absGap = Math.abs(gapPct);
  if (absGap < 0.5 && last > open) gapMod = 2;
  else if (absGap < 1.0) gapMod = 1;
  else if (absGap < 2.0) gapMod = 0;
  else if (absGap < 3.0) gapMod = -1;
  else gapMod = -2;

  // Relative Strength (+2 to -2)
  let rsMod = 0;
  if (relStr >= 3) rsMod = 2;
  else if (relStr >= 1.5) rsMod = 1;
  else if (relStr >= -1.5) rsMod = 0;
  else if (relStr >= -3) rsMod = -1;
  else rsMod = -2;

  // News/Catalyst modifier (+2 to -2) — auto-scored from cached news
  const sym = quote.Symbol || '';
  let newsMod = 0;
  if (newsCatalystSet && newsCatalystSet[sym]) {
    // Has news today — score based on RVOL (high volume + news = strong catalyst)
    if (rvol >= 2.0) newsMod = 2;
    else if (rvol >= 1.0) newsMod = 1;
    else newsMod = 0;  // News but no volume reaction = meh
  }

  const modTotal = atrMod + gapMod + rsMod + newsMod;
  const totalConfluence = Math.max(0, Math.min(38, coreTotal + modTotal));

  let quality;
  if (totalConfluence >= 28) quality = 'A+';
  else if (totalConfluence >= 24) quality = 'Solid';
  else if (totalConfluence >= 20) quality = 'Playbook';
  else if (totalConfluence >= 16) quality = 'Watch';
  else quality = 'Skip';

  let setup = '';
  var setupScore = 0, setup2 = '', setup2Score = 0;

  // ── Setup Scoring Engine (v91) — scores ALL setups independently, picks best ──
  function _setupScore(name, match, rv, minRV, cf, minCf, bonus) {
    if (!match) return 0;
    var s = 10;
    if (minRV > 0 && rv >= minRV) s += Math.min((rv - minRV) / minRV * 5, 5);
    else if (minRV > 0 && rv < minRV) return 0;
    if (cf >= minCf) s += Math.min((cf - minCf) / 4, 5);
    else return 0;
    s += Math.min(bonus || 0, 10);
    return Math.round(s * 10) / 10;
  }

  var _scores = {};
  var _conf = totalConfluence;

  _scores['BigDogBounce'] = _setupScore('BDB', belowVwap && isConsolidating && consolidationBars >= 6, rvol, 2, _conf, 16, (consolidationBars - 6) * 0.5 + (rvol >= 3 ? 2 : 0));
  _scores['BigDog'] = _setupScore('BD', aboveVwap && isConsolidating && consolidationMinutes >= 45, rvol, 3, _conf, 20, (consolidationMinutes - 45) / 15 + (rvol >= 4 ? 2 : 0));
  _scores['OpeningDrive'] = _setupScore('OD', bars.length <= 2 && absGapPct >= 3.0, rvol, 2, _conf, 16, (absGapPct - 3) * 1.5 + (rvol >= 4 ? 2 : 0));
  _scores['GapGo'] = _setupScore('GG', absGapPct >= 3.0 && aboveVwap && gapPct >= 3.0, rvol, 2, _conf, 18, (absGapPct - 3) + (rvol >= 3 ? 2 : 0));
  _scores['OR-Break'] = _setupScore('OR', isORBreakout && aboveVwap && rsi5m < 75, rvol, 1.5, _conf, 20, (rvol >= 2.5 ? 2 : 0) + (rsi5m >= 50 && rsi5m <= 65 ? 2 : 0));
  _scores['DailyBreakout'] = _setupScore('DB', near52High && aboveVwap, rvol, 3, _conf, 22, (rvol >= 4 ? 2 : 0) + (pct52 >= 95 ? 3 : pct52 >= 90 ? 1 : 0));
  _scores['Failed-BD'] = _setupScore('FBD', last > orLow && orLow > 0 && aboveVwap && low < orLow, rvol, 1, _conf, 18, (vwapDist < 0.5 ? 2 : 0) + (rvol >= 2 ? 2 : 0) + (emaStackBull ? 1 : 0));
  _scores['ReturnPullback'] = _setupScore('RP', isVWAPReclaim && vwapDist < 0.5, rvol, 1, _conf, 16, (0.5 - vwapDist) * 4 + (emaStackBull ? 2 : 0));
  _scores['VWAP-Hold'] = _setupScore('VH', aboveVwap && vwapDist < 0.5 && emaStackBull && rsi5m >= 40 && rsi5m <= 60, rvol, 1, _conf, 18, (0.5 - vwapDist) * 4 + (rsi5m >= 45 && rsi5m <= 55 ? 2 : 0));
  _scores['Pullback-EMA'] = _setupScore('PE', nearEma20 && emaStackBull && rsi5m >= 35 && rsi5m <= 55, rvol, 1, _conf, 16, (nearEma9 ? 3 : 0) + (rsi5m >= 40 && rsi5m <= 50 ? 2 : 0));
  _scores['Momentum'] = _setupScore('MO', aboveVwap && last > ema9 && emaStackBull && rsi5m >= 55 && rsi5m <= 75 && relStr >= 1, rvol, 1.5, _conf, 22, (relStr - 1) * 2 + (rvol >= 2.5 ? 2 : 0));
  _scores['SecondDay'] = _setupScore('SD', absGapPct >= 2.0 && bars.length >= 3 && vwapDist < 1.5, rvol, 1.5, _conf, 20, (absGapPct - 2) + (vwapDist < 0.5 ? 2 : 0));
  _scores['Scalping'] = _setupScore('SC', rvol >= 1.5 && spreadPct < 0.1, rvol, 1.5, _conf, 16, (spreadPct < 0.05 ? 2 : 0) + (rvol >= 2.5 ? 2 : 0));

  var _ranked = Object.keys(_scores).filter(function(k) { return _scores[k] > 0; }).sort(function(a, b) { return _scores[b] - _scores[a]; });
  setup = _ranked.length > 0 ? _ranked[0] : '';
  setupScore = _ranked.length > 0 ? _scores[_ranked[0]] : 0;
  setup2 = _ranked.length > 1 ? _ranked[1] : '';
  setup2Score = _ranked.length > 1 ? _scores[_ranked[1]] : 0;

  const vwapFlag = last > calcedVwap ? 'PASS' : (last > calcedVwap * 0.995 ? 'WARN' : 'FAIL');
  const rsFlag = relStr >= 1 ? 'PASS' : (relStr >= -1 ? 'WARN' : 'FAIL');
  const rsiFlag = (rsi5m >= 35 && rsi5m <= 75) ? 'PASS' : ((rsi5m >= 25 && rsi5m <= 80) ? 'WARN' : 'FAIL');
  const rvolFlag = rvol >= 1.5 ? 'PASS' : (rvol >= 1.0 ? 'WARN' : 'FAIL');

  // Additional fields
  const ema50DistPct = ema50 > 0 ? ((last - ema50) / ema50) * 100 : 0;
  const high52 = parseFloat(quote.High52Week || quote.High52WeekPrice || 0);
  const low52 = parseFloat(quote.Low52Week || quote.Low52WeekPrice || 0);
  const range52 = high52 - low52;
  const pct52 = range52 > 0 ? ((last - low52) / range52) * 100 : 0;
  const yestHigh = parseFloat(quote.PreviousHigh || quote.YesterdayHigh || 0);
  const yestLow = parseFloat(quote.PreviousLow || quote.YesterdayLow || 0);
  const yestClose = prevClose;
  const avgVol = parseInt(quote.AverageVolume || quote.AvgVolume || prevVolume || 0);

  // --- SETUP-SPECIFIC FLAGS (v90.5) ---
  // These enable future playbook checklist matching on the dashboard
  
  // Consolidation detection: check if recent bars are in a tight range
  let isConsolidating = false;
  let consolidationBars = 0;
  if (bars.length >= 6 && atr > 0) {
    // Look at the last N bars and check if price range is tight relative to ATR
    for (let cb = Math.max(0, bars.length - 30); cb < bars.length; cb++) {
      const barHigh = parseFloat(bars[cb].High || 0);
      const barLow = parseFloat(bars[cb].Low || 0);
      const barRange = barHigh - barLow;
      if (barRange <= atr * 0.3) {
        consolidationBars++;
      } else {
        consolidationBars = 0; // Reset on wide bar
      }
    }
    isConsolidating = consolidationBars >= 4; // 4+ tight bars in a row = consolidating
  }
  const consolidationMinutes = consolidationBars * 5; // Each bar = 5 min
  
  // Gap play: significant gap with volume
  const absGapPct = Math.abs(gapPct);
  const isGapPlay = absGapPct >= 3.0 && rvol >= 3.0;
  
  // VWAP reclaim: was below VWAP, now above (price crossed up through VWAP)
  let isVWAPReclaim = false;
  if (last > calcedVwap && calcedVwap > 0 && bars.length >= 3) {
    // Check if any of last 3 bars had low below VWAP
    for (let vb = Math.max(0, bars.length - 3); vb < bars.length; vb++) {
      if (parseFloat(bars[vb].Low || 0) < calcedVwap) { isVWAPReclaim = true; break; }
    }
  }
  
  // OR breakout: just broke above Opening Range high with volume
  const isORBreakout = last > orHigh && orHigh > 0 && rvol >= 1.5;
  
  // Near 52-week high: within 3% of high
  const near52High = high52 > 0 && last >= high52 * 0.97;

  return {
    last, vwap: calcedVwap, bid, ask, spread, spreadPct,
    rsi5m: rsi5m.toFixed(1), ema9: ema9.toFixed(2), ema20: ema20.toFixed(2),
    atr: atr.toFixed(2), rvol: rvol.toFixed(2),
    relStr: relStr.toFixed(2), gapPct: gapPct.toFixed(2), netPct: netPct.toFixed(2),
    orHigh: orHigh.toFixed(2), orLow: orLow.toFixed(2),
    volume, prevVolume,
    marketCtx, priceStr: priceStr.toFixed(1), momentum: momentum.toFixed(1),
    volScore, levelProx: levelProx.toFixed(1), execQual: execQual.toFixed(1),
    coreTotal: coreTotal.toFixed(1),
    atrMod, gapMod, rsMod, newsMod, modTotal,
    totalConfluence, quality, setup, setupScore, setup2, setup2Score,
    vwapFlag, rsFlag, rsiFlag, rvolFlag,
    ema50: ema50.toFixed(2), ema50DistPct: ema50DistPct.toFixed(2),
    high52, low52, pct52: pct52.toFixed(1),
    yestHigh: yestHigh.toFixed(2), yestLow: yestLow.toFixed(2), yestClose: yestClose.toFixed(2),
    avgVol,
    hasCatalyst: !!(newsCatalystSet && newsCatalystSet[sym]),
    isConsolidating, consolidationMinutes, isGapPlay, isVWAPReclaim, isORBreakout, near52High
  };
}

// --- GOOGLE FINANCE DAILY CACHE ---
// Fetches ONLY marketcap, high52, low52, name via GOOGLEFINANCE formulas.
// Runs ONCE per day (first refresh), then reads from cache for all subsequent refreshes.
// Name is cached permanently (never changes). MarketCap/52wk refresh daily.

function getDailyGFCache(ss, symbols) {
  const CACHE_SHEET = '_GFDaily';
  let cacheSheet = ss.getSheetByName(CACHE_SHEET);

  const today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), 'America/Phoenix', 'yyyy-MM-dd');

  // --- Check if cache is fresh (same day) ---
  if (cacheSheet) {
    const stamp = String(cacheSheet.getRange(1, 1).getValue()).trim();
    if (stamp === today) {
      // Cache is fresh — read and return
      const data = cacheSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      const cached = {};
      for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
        const sym = String(data[i][0]).trim().toUpperCase();
        if (!sym) continue;
        cached[sym] = {
          marketcap: parseFloat(data[i][1]) || 0,
          high52: parseFloat(data[i][2]) || 0,
          low52: parseFloat(data[i][3]) || 0,
          name: String(data[i][4] || '').trim()
        };
      }
      Logger.log('GF daily cache: loaded ' + Object.keys(cached).length + ' entries from ' + today);
      return cached;
    }
  }

  // --- Cache is stale or missing — refresh via GOOGLEFINANCE formulas ---
  Logger.log('GF daily cache: refreshing for ' + symbols.length + ' symbols...');

  const FORMULA_SHEET = '_GFFormulas';
  let formulaSheet = ss.getSheetByName(FORMULA_SHEET);
  if (!formulaSheet) {
    formulaSheet = ss.insertSheet(FORMULA_SHEET);
    formulaSheet.hideSheet();
  }
  formulaSheet.clear();

  // Filter out breadth/futures symbols that GOOGLEFINANCE can't handle
  const gfSymbols = symbols.filter(s => !s.startsWith('$') && !s.startsWith('@') && s.indexOf('/') < 0);

  const formulas = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < gfSymbols.length; i++) {
    const sym = gfSymbols[i];
    formulas.push([
      sym,
      '=IFERROR(GOOGLEFINANCE("' + sym + '","marketcap"),0)',
      '=IFERROR(GOOGLEFINANCE("' + sym + '","high52"),0)',
      '=IFERROR(GOOGLEFINANCE("' + sym + '","low52"),0)',
      '=IFERROR(GOOGLEFINANCE("' + sym + '","name"),"")'
    ]);
  }

  if (formulas.length > 0) {
    formulaSheet.getRange(1, 1, formulas.length, 5).setValues(formulas);
  }

  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  Utilities.sleep(3000);

  const values = formulaSheet.getRange(1, 1, formulas.length, 5).getValues();

  const cached = {};
  for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
    const sym = String(values[i][0]).trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!sym) continue;
    cached[sym] = {
      marketcap: parseFloat(values[i][1]) || 0,
      high52: parseFloat(values[i][2]) || 0,
      low52: parseFloat(values[i][3]) || 0,
      name: String(values[i][4] || '').trim()
    };
  }

  formulaSheet.clear();

  if (!cacheSheet) {
    cacheSheet = ss.insertSheet(CACHE_SHEET);
    cacheSheet.hideSheet();
  }
  cacheSheet.clear();
  const rows = [[today, 'MarketCap', 'High52', 'Low52', 'Name']];
  for (const sym of Object.keys(cached)) {
    rows.push([sym, cached[sym].marketcap, cached[sym].high52, cached[sym].low52, cached[sym].name]);
  }
  cacheSheet.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, 5).setValues(rows);

  Logger.log('GF daily cache: saved ' + (rows.length - 1) + ' entries for ' + today);
  return cached;
}

// --- CONFLUENCE SCORE CACHE (for partial refresh) ---

function readConfluenceCache(ss) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName('_ConfluenceCache');
  if (!sheet) return {};
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (data.length < 2) return {};
  const cache = {};
  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    const sym = String(data[i][0]).trim();
    if (!sym) continue;
    try {
      cache[sym] = JSON.parse(data[i][4]);
    } catch (e) {
      cache[sym] = { totalConfluence: parseFloat(data[i][1]) || 0, quality: data[i][2] || '', setup: data[i][3] || '' };
    }
  }
  return cache;
}

function writeConfluenceCache(ss, confluenceMap) {
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName('_ConfluenceCache');
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet('_ConfluenceCache');
    sheet.hideSheet();
  }
  const existing = readConfluenceCache(ss);
  for (const sym of Object.keys(confluenceMap)) {
    if (confluenceMap[sym]) existing[sym] = confluenceMap[sym];
  }
  const rows = [['Symbol', 'Score', 'Quality', 'Setup', 'JSON']];
  for (const sym of Object.keys(existing)) {
    const c = existing[sym];
    rows.push([sym, c.totalConfluence || 0, c.quality || '', (c.setup ? c.setup + '|' + (c.setupScore||0) + (c.setup2 ? '|' + c.setup2 + '|' + (c.setup2Score||0) : '') : ''), JSON.stringify(c)]);
  }
  sheet.clearContents();
  if (rows.length > 0) {
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, 5).setValues(rows);
  }
}

function getRefreshMode(ss) {
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  
  // Check for manual full scan trigger
  const forceFull = props.getProperty('FORCE_FULL_SCAN') === 'true';
  if (forceFull) {
    props.deleteProperty('FORCE_FULL_SCAN');
    // Reset all phase counters since we just did a full scan
    props.setProperty('PHASE_COUNTER_MARKETOPEN', '0');
    props.setProperty('PHASE_COUNTER_CORESESSION', '0');
    return { 
      mode: 'full', 
      phase: 'MANUAL',
      threshold: 0,
      pmWatch: true,
      reason: 'MANUAL — forced full scan (counters reset)' 
    };
  }
  
  const now = new Date();
  const _azH2 = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'H'), 10);
  const _azM2 = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'm'), 10);
  const azMinutes = _azH2 * 60 + _azM2;
  
  // Determine current phase
  let phase = null;
  let phaseName = '';
  if (azMinutes >= PHASE_CONFIG.PRE_MARKET.start && azMinutes < PHASE_CONFIG.PRE_MARKET.end) {
    phase = PHASE_CONFIG.PRE_MARKET; phaseName = 'PRE-MARKET';
  } else if (azMinutes >= PHASE_CONFIG.MARKET_OPEN.start && azMinutes < PHASE_CONFIG.MARKET_OPEN.end) {
    phase = PHASE_CONFIG.MARKET_OPEN; phaseName = 'MARKET OPEN';
  } else if (azMinutes >= PHASE_CONFIG.CORE_SESSION.start && azMinutes < PHASE_CONFIG.CORE_SESSION.end) {
    phase = PHASE_CONFIG.CORE_SESSION; phaseName = 'CORE SESSION';
  } else if (azMinutes >= PHASE_CONFIG.AFTER_HOURS.start && azMinutes < PHASE_CONFIG.AFTER_HOURS.end) {
    phase = PHASE_CONFIG.AFTER_HOURS; phaseName = 'AFTER-HOURS';
  } else {
    // Outside all phases — shouldn't reach here due to market hours gate, but safe fallback
    phase = PHASE_CONFIG.AFTER_HOURS; phaseName = 'OFF-HOURS';
  }
  
  // Check if confluence cache exists (first run of day needs full)
  const cacheSheet = ss.getSheetByName('_ConfluenceCache');
  if (!cacheSheet || cacheSheet.getLastRow() < 2) {
    return { 
      mode: 'full', 
      phase: phaseName,
      threshold: phase.threshold,
      pmWatch: phase.pmWatch,
      reason: phaseName + ' — no cache, initial full scan' 
    };
  }
  
  // Full scan logic: check counter for phases with fullInterval > 0
  if (phase.fullInterval > 0) {
    const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    // Use phase-specific counter so phase transitions don't reset each other
    const counterKey = 'PHASE_COUNTER_' + phaseName.replace(/[^A-Z]/g, '');
    let counter = parseInt(props.getProperty(counterKey) || '0');
    counter++;
    
    if (counter >= phase.fullInterval && isFullScanEnabled()) {
      props.setProperty(counterKey, '0');
      return { 
        mode: 'full', 
        phase: phaseName,
        threshold: phase.threshold,
        pmWatch: phase.pmWatch,
        reason: phaseName + ' — periodic full scan (every ' + (phase.fullInterval * 5) + ' min)' 
      };
    } else {
      if (counter >= phase.fullInterval) {
        // Full scan was due but disabled — reset counter, stay partial
        props.setProperty(counterKey, '0');
      } else {
        props.setProperty(counterKey, counter.toString());
      }
      return { 
        mode: 'partial', 
        phase: phaseName,
        threshold: phase.threshold,
        pmWatch: phase.pmWatch,
        reason: phaseName + ' — partial ' + counter + '/' + phase.fullInterval + ' (bars for >=' + phase.threshold + ' + PM Watchlist)' + (!isFullScanEnabled() ? ' [full scans OFF]' : '')
      };
    }
  }
  
  // Phases with fullInterval = 0: PRE-MARKET (1 full first refresh only) and AFTER-HOURS (never full)
  if (phaseName === 'PRE-MARKET') {
    const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    const pmDone = props.getProperty('PM_FULL_DONE');
    const today = Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    
    if (pmDone !== today) {
      // First pre-market refresh of the day — do full scan
      props.setProperty('PM_FULL_DONE', today);
      return { 
        mode: 'full', 
        phase: phaseName,
        threshold: phase.threshold,
        pmWatch: phase.pmWatch,
        reason: phaseName + ' — first refresh, full scan to catch movers' 
      };
    }
  }
  
  // Default: partial scan for this phase
  return { 
    mode: 'partial', 
    phase: phaseName,
    threshold: phase.threshold,
    pmWatch: phase.pmWatch,
    reason: phaseName + ' — partial (bars for >=' + phase.threshold + (phase.pmWatch ? ' + PM Watchlist' : '') + ')' 
  };
}

// --- MAIN UPDATE FUNCTION ---

// Manual trigger — runs current phase logic, bypasses market hours check
function forceUpdateSheet() {
  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('FORCE_UPDATE', 'true');
  updateSheet();
}

// Manual trigger — forces full 424-ticker scan, resets 30-min full counter, bypasses market hours
function forceFullScan() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  props.setProperty('FORCE_UPDATE', 'true');
  props.setProperty('FORCE_FULL_SCAN', 'true');
  updateSheet();
}

function updateSheet() {
  _resetMarketOffset(); // Recalculate ET DST offset each cycle
  PHASE_CONFIG = _buildPhaseConfig(); // Rebuild phase gates
  const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  
  // Clear Weekend Pulse mode — main scanner is taking over
  props.setProperty('PULSE_MODE', 'false');
  
  // --- FORCE FLAG CHECK (must come before all gates) ---
  const forceUpdate = props.getProperty('FORCE_UPDATE') === 'true';
  if (forceUpdate) {
    props.deleteProperty('FORCE_UPDATE');
  }
  
  // --- TIME & DAY CONTEXT (using reliable Utilities.formatDate for AZ timezone) ---
  const _now = new Date();
  const azHour = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(_now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'H'), 10);
  const azMin  = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(_now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'm'), 10);
  const azTime = azHour * 60 + azMin;          // minutes since midnight
  const azDow  = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(_now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'u'), 10); // 1=Mon...7=Sun
  const isWeekend = (azDow >= 6);              // 6=Sat, 7=Sun
  const MARKET_START = 6 * 60 + 30;            // 6:30 AM AZ
  const MARKET_END   = 16 * 60;                // 4:00 PM AZ
  
  // --- WEEKEND GATE (absolute — no fetches on Sat/Sun, period) ---
  if (!forceUpdate && isWeekend) {
    Logger.log('Weekend (' + ['Mon','Tue','Wed','Thu','Fri','Sat','Sun'][azDow - 1] + ') — skipping. Use "Update Now" to force.');
    return;
  }
  
  // --- AUTO-ENABLE ON WEEKDAY MARKET OPEN ---
  // If we auto-disabled yesterday (or Friday), re-enable when market window starts.
  // This runs BEFORE the ON/OFF gate so it can flip the switch back on.
  // Does NOT override manual stops (only fires when AUTO_DISABLED flag is set).
  if (!forceUpdate && !isWeekend && azTime >= MARKET_START && azTime <= MARKET_END) {
    if (props.getProperty('AUTO_DISABLED') === 'true' && !isScannerEnabled()) {
      props.setProperty('SCANNER_ENABLED', 'ON');
      props.setProperty('FULLSCAN_ENABLED', 'ON');
      props.setProperty('MARKET_REFRESH_ENABLED', 'ON');
      props.deleteProperty('AUTO_DISABLED');
      // Force prune stale quota buckets so rolling count is accurate after gap
      _pruneOldBuckets(props, new Date());
      Logger.log('☀️ Auto-enabled scanner — weekday market hours started. Stale quota buckets pruned.');
    }
  }
  
  // --- ON/OFF SWITCH CHECK (bypassed by manual Update Now / Full Scan Now) ---
  if (!forceUpdate && !isScannerEnabled()) {
    Logger.log('Scanner is OFF — skipping updateSheet(). Use V9 Scanner > Start Scanner to re-enable.');
    return;
  }
  
  // --- MARKET HOURS CHECK ---
  // Outside trading window: auto-disable to prevent quota burn overnight.
  // Manual "Update Now" bypasses this (sets FORCE_UPDATE flag).
  if (!forceUpdate && (azTime < MARKET_START || azTime > MARKET_END)) {
    // First tick past MARKET_END today? Auto-disable everything.
    if (azTime > MARKET_END && props.getProperty('AUTO_DISABLED') !== 'true') {
      props.setProperty('SCANNER_ENABLED', 'OFF');
      props.setProperty('FULLSCAN_ENABLED', 'OFF');
      props.setProperty('MARKET_REFRESH_ENABLED', 'OFF');
      props.setProperty('AUTO_DISABLED', 'true');
      Logger.log('🌙 Auto-disabled scanner — market closed (' + azHour + ':' + (azMin < 10 ? '0' : '') + azMin + ' AZ). Will auto-enable next weekday at ' + Math.floor(MARKET_START/60) + ':' + (MARKET_START%60 < 10 ? '0' : '') + (MARKET_START%60) + '.');
    } else {
      Logger.log('Outside trading window (' + azHour + ':' + (azMin < 10 ? '0' : '') + azMin + ' AZ) — skipping. Use "Update Now" to force.');
    }
    return;
  }
  
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  // ==================== REFRESH MY POSITIONS (TradeStation API) ====================
  // Runs every scanner tick (5 min) — refreshMyPositions has its own error handling
  try { refreshMyPositions(); } catch(e) { Logger.log('Position refresh skipped: ' + e.message); }
  
  // ── Trade Management: refresh account equity (BOD on first run of day) ──
  try {
    var _todayStr = Utilities.formatDate(_now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    var _lastEquityDate = props.getProperty('TM_LAST_EQUITY_DATE') || '';
    var _setBOD = (_lastEquityDate !== _todayStr);
    refreshAccountEquity(_setBOD);
    if (_setBOD) props.setProperty('TM_LAST_EQUITY_DATE', _todayStr);
    // Sync trades from brokers every tick during market hours
    try { syncTrades(); } catch(e) { Logger.log('updateSheet: syncTrades error: ' + e.message); }
  } catch(e) { Logger.log('Account equity refresh skipped: ' + e.message); }

  // ==================== BREADTH & MARKET TAB ====================
  let breadthSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Market');
  if (!breadthSheet) {
    breadthSheet = ss.insertSheet('Market');
  }

  // Collect ALL symbols needed for market tab
  const ratioSymbols = [];
  for (const rp of RATIO_PAIRS) {
    if (!ratioSymbols.includes(rp[1])) ratioSymbols.push(rp[1]);
    if (!ratioSymbols.includes(rp[2])) ratioSymbols.push(rp[2]);
  }

  const coreSymbols = [
    ...BREADTH_SYMBOLS, ...GROWTH_SECTORS, ...DEFENSIVE_SECTORS,
    BENCHMARK, ...INVERSE_ETFS, ...ratioSymbols, ...BENCHMARKS.map(i => i[0]),
    ...INTERNALS.map(i => i[0]),
    ...COMMODITIES.map(i => i[0]),
    ...FUTURES.map(i => i[0])
  ];
  const uniqueCore = [...new Set(coreSymbols)];
  const coreQuotes = tsQuotes(uniqueCore);

  const mktMap = {};
  for (const q of coreQuotes) mktMap[q.Symbol] = q;

  const marketQuotes = Object.values(mktMap);

  const breadthQuotes = marketQuotes.filter(q => BREADTH_SYMBOLS.includes(q.Symbol));
  const sectorQuotes = marketQuotes.filter(q => [...GROWTH_SECTORS, ...DEFENSIVE_SECTORS].includes(q.Symbol));
  const spyQuote = mktMap[BENCHMARK] || {};
  const inverseQuotes = marketQuotes.filter(q => INVERSE_ETFS.includes(q.Symbol));

  const breadth = scoreBreadth(breadthQuotes);
  const sectors = scoreSectors(sectorQuotes);
  const totalBreadth = breadth.score + sectors.sectorPts;
  const gameplan = getGameplan(totalBreadth);

  // Build Market sheet data
  const marketData = [
    ['V9 CONFLUENCE SCANNER', '', '', new Date()],
    ['', '', '', ''],
    ['GAMEPLAN', 'Score', 'Adj %', 'Action'],
    ['GP-' + gameplan.gp, totalBreadth.toFixed(1), gameplan.adjPct + '%', gameplan.action + ' | ' + gameplan.sizing],
    ['', '', '', ''],
    ['BENCHMARKS', 'Last', 'Change %', 'Description'],
  ];

  for (const item of BENCHMARKS) {
    const sym = item[0];
    const q = mktMap[sym];
    if (q) {
      const pct = parseFloat(q.NetChangePct || 0);
      marketData.push([sym, q.Last, pct.toFixed(2) + '%', item[1]]);
    } else {
      marketData.push([sym, 'N/A', '', item[1]]);
    }
  }

  marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
  marketData.push(['FUTURES', 'Last', 'Change %', 'Description']);

  for (const item of FUTURES) {
    const sym = item[0];
    const q = mktMap[sym];
    if (q) {
      const pct = parseFloat(q.NetChangePct || 0);
      marketData.push([sym, q.Last, pct.toFixed(2) + '%', item[1]]);
    } else {
      marketData.push([sym, 'N/A', '', item[1]]);
    }
  }

  marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
  marketData.push(['BREADTH DETAIL', 'Value', 'Points', 'Description']);
  marketData.push(['$TICK', breadth.tick, '', 'NYSE tick — net upticks vs downticks, >+700 strong buying']);
  marketData.push(['$ADD', breadth.add, '', 'NYSE A/D — advancing vs declining issues, >+1000 broad strength']);
  marketData.push(['$ADQD', breadth.adqd, '', 'NASDAQ A/D — tech/growth breadth, >+1000 strong']);
  marketData.push(['$VOLD (scaled)', breadth.vold.toFixed(0), '', 'NYSE up/down volume — confirms breadth with volume']);
  marketData.push(['$VOLQD (scaled)', breadth.volqd.toFixed(0), '', 'NASDAQ up/down volume — tech volume confirmation']);
  marketData.push(['$VIX', breadth.vix.toFixed(2), '', 'Fear gauge — <15 complacent, 15-18 normal, >25 elevated']);
  marketData.push(['Breadth Score', breadth.score, 'Sector Pts', sectors.sectorPts]);
  marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);

  if (INTERNALS.length > 0) {
    marketData.push(['INTERNALS', 'Value', '', 'Description']);
    for (const item of INTERNALS) {
      const sym = item[0];
      const desc = item[1];
      const q = mktMap[sym];
      marketData.push([sym, q ? q.Last : 'N/A', '', desc]);
    }
    const addVal = parseFloat(breadth.add) || 0;
    const adqdVal = parseFloat(breadth.adqd) || 0;
    const addRatio = adqdVal !== 0 ? (addVal / adqdVal).toFixed(3) : 'N/A';
    marketData.push(['ADD/ADQD', addRatio, '', 'NYSE vs NASDAQ breadth — >1 NYSE leading, <1 NASDAQ leading, divergence = narrow leadership']);
    marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
  }

  if (RATIO_PAIRS.length > 0) {
    marketData.push(['INTERMARKET RATIOS', 'Ratio', 'Chg%', 'What It Tells You']);
    for (const rp of RATIO_PAIRS) {
      const numQ = mktMap[rp[1]];
      const denQ = mktMap[rp[2]];

      if (numQ && denQ) {
        const numLast = parseFloat(numQ.Last || 0);
        const denLast = parseFloat(denQ.Last || 1);
        const numPrev = parseFloat(numQ.PreviousClose || numLast);
        const denPrev = parseFloat(denQ.PreviousClose || denLast);

        const ratio = denLast > 0 ? (numLast / denLast) : 0;
        const prevRatio = denPrev > 0 ? (numPrev / denPrev) : 0;
        const ratioPctChg = prevRatio > 0 ? ((ratio - prevRatio) / prevRatio * 100) : 0;

        marketData.push([rp[0], ratio.toFixed(4), ratioPctChg.toFixed(2) + '%', rp[3] || '']);
      } else {
        marketData.push([rp[0], 'N/A', '', rp[3] || '']);
      }
    }
    marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
  }

  marketData.push(['COMMODITIES', 'Last', 'Change %', 'What It Tells You']);
  for (const item of COMMODITIES) {
    const sym = item[0];
    const desc = item[1];
    const q = mktMap[sym];
    if (q) {
      const pct = parseFloat(q.NetChangePct || 0);
      marketData.push([sym, q.Last, pct.toFixed(2) + '%', desc]);
    } else {
      marketData.push([sym, 'N/A', '', desc]);
    }
  }
  marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);

  marketData.push(['GROWTH SECTORS', 'Change %', '', sectors.growthGreen + '/8 growth green']);
  for (const sym of GROWTH_SECTORS) {
    const pct = sectors.sectorData[sym] || 0;
    marketData.push([sym, pct.toFixed(2) + '%', pct > 0 ? 'UP' : 'DN', SECTOR_INFO[sym] || '']);
  }

  marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
  marketData.push(['DEFENSIVE SECTORS', 'Change %', '', sectors.defGreen + '/5 green']);

  for (const sym of DEFENSIVE_SECTORS) {
    const pct = sectors.sectorData[sym] || 0;
    marketData.push([sym, pct.toFixed(2) + '%', pct > 0 ? 'UP' : 'DN', SECTOR_INFO[sym] || '']);
  }

  marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
  marketData.push(['Leader', sectors.leader, sectors.leaderPct.toFixed(2) + '%', '']);
  marketData.push(['Lagger', sectors.lagger, sectors.laggerPct.toFixed(2) + '%', '']);

  marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
  marketData.push(['INVERSE ETFs (GP-D)', 'Last', 'Change %', '']);
  for (const q of inverseQuotes) {
    marketData.push([q.Symbol, q.Last, (parseFloat(q.NetChangePct || 0)).toFixed(2) + '%', '']);
  }

  breadthSheet.clearContents();
  breadthSheet.clearFormats();
  breadthSheet.getRange(1, 1, marketData.length, 4).setValues(marketData);
  formatMarketTab(breadthSheet, marketData.length, gameplan.gp);

  // ==================== ECONOMIC CALENDAR (Market tab cols F-M) ====================
  try {
    var ecoEvents = fetchEconomicCalendar();
    if (ecoEvents.length > 0) {
      // Clear rows 1-2 in eco calendar columns (blank — aligned with GP banner rows)
      breadthSheet.getRange(1, 6, 2, 8).clearContent().setBackground(null).setFontColor(null).setFontWeight('normal');

      var ecoData = [['ECONOMIC CALENDAR', 'Time (AZ)', 'Impact', 'Previous', 'Forecast', 'Actual', 'TV Chart', 'Tickers']];
      for (var i = 0; i < ecoEvents.length; i++) {
        var e = ecoEvents[i];
        ecoData.push([e.title, e.time, e.impact, e.previous, e.forecast, e.actual, e.tvTicker || '', e.tickers || '']);
      }
      breadthSheet.getRange(3, 6, ecoData.length, 8).setValues(ecoData);

      breadthSheet.getRange(3, 6, 1, 8).setBackground('#1a1a2e').setFontColor('#ffffff').setFontWeight('bold');

      // Clear any previous eco calendar formatting below header
      if (ecoEvents.length > 0) {
        breadthSheet.getRange(4, 6, ecoEvents.length, 8).setBackground(null).setFontColor(null).setFontWeight('normal');
      }

      for (var i = 0; i < ecoEvents.length; i++) {
        var row = i + 4;
        var ev = ecoEvents[i];
        var impact = ev.impact;
        var fullRow = breadthSheet.getRange(row, 6, 1, 8);
        
        // Day separator rows (── TODAY ──, ── MONDAY ──, etc.)
        if (ev.isSeparator) {
          fullRow.setBackground('#1a1a2e').setFontColor('#ffffff').setFontWeight('bold');
          continue; // skip all other formatting for separator rows
        }
        
        // High impact: highlight FULL row pink + bold
        if (impact === 'High') {
          fullRow.setBackground('#ffc7ce').setFontColor('#9c0006').setFontWeight('bold');
        }
        // Medium impact: just the Impact cell gets yellow
        else if (impact === 'Medium') {
          breadthSheet.getRange(row, 8).setBackground('#ffeb9c').setFontColor('#9c6500').setFontWeight('bold');
        }
        // Holiday
        else if (impact === 'Holiday') {
          fullRow.setBackground('#d0e2f7').setFontColor('#1a1a2e').setFontWeight('bold');
        }

        // Actual vs Forecast coloring
        if (ev.actual && ev.forecast) {
          var actualNum = parseFloat(String(ev.actual).replace(/[^0-9.\-]/g, ''));
          var forecastNum = parseFloat(String(ev.forecast).replace(/[^0-9.\-]/g, ''));
          var actualCell = breadthSheet.getRange(row, 11);
          if (!isNaN(actualNum) && !isNaN(forecastNum)) {
            if (actualNum > forecastNum) {
              actualCell.setFontColor('#1b5e20').setFontWeight('bold');
            } else if (actualNum < forecastNum) {
              actualCell.setFontColor('#b71c1c').setFontWeight('bold');
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Economic calendar error: ' + e.message);
  }

  // ==================== WATCHLIST TAB ====================
  let watchSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
  if (!watchSheet) {
    watchSheet = ss.insertSheet('Watchlist');
  }

  // ── Populate Dynamic watchlist (pre-market + ongoing) ──
  var _configSymSetPre = {};
  try {
    var preWl = getWatchlist();
    for (var pw = 0; pw < preWl.length; pw++) {
      if (preWl[pw].section !== 'DYNAMIC') _configSymSetPre[preWl[pw].symbol] = true;
    }
    // earningsMap not available yet, pass null — earnings will be added on first full scan
    populateDynamic(ss, _configSymSetPre, null);
  } catch(dpe) { Logger.log('Dynamic pre-populate: ' + dpe.message); }

  const watchlistItems = getWatchlist();
  const uniqueSymbols = [...new Set(watchlistItems.map(w => w.symbol))];
  
  // Build config symbol set (excludes Dynamic tickers)
  const _configSymSet = {};
  for (const item of watchlistItems) {
    if (item.section !== 'DYNAMIC') _configSymSet[item.symbol] = true;
  }

  // ==================== TRADESTATION QUOTES ====================
  const tsWatchQuotes = tsQuotes(uniqueSymbols);
  Logger.log('TradeStation quotes: ' + tsWatchQuotes.length + '/' + uniqueSymbols.length + ' tickers');

  // ==================== GOOGLE FINANCE DAILY CACHE ====================
  const gfDaily = getDailyGFCache(ss, uniqueSymbols);
  Logger.log('GF daily cache: ' + Object.keys(gfDaily).length + ' entries');

  const quoteMap = {};
  for (const q of tsWatchQuotes) {
    const sym = q.Symbol;
    const gf = gfDaily[sym] || {};
    quoteMap[sym] = {
      Symbol: sym,
      Last: parseFloat(q.Last || 0),
      Bid: parseFloat(q.Bid || q.Last || 0),
      Ask: parseFloat(q.Ask || q.Last || 0),
      Volume: parseInt(q.Volume || 0),
      PreviousVolume: parseInt(q.PreviousVolume || 1),
      PreviousClose: parseFloat(q.PreviousClose || q.Last || 0),
      Open: parseFloat(q.Open || q.Last || 0),
      High: parseFloat(q.High || q.Last || 0),
      Low: parseFloat(q.Low || q.Last || 0),
      NetChangePct: parseFloat(q.NetChangePct || 0),
      High52Week: gf.high52 || 0,
      Low52Week: gf.low52 || 0,
      MarketCap: gf.marketcap || 0,
      AverageVolume: parseInt(q.PreviousVolume || 0),
      Name: gf.name || '',
      VWAP: parseFloat(q.VWAP || 0)
    };
  }

  // ==================== PHASE-BASED REFRESH LOGIC ====================
  const refreshMode = getRefreshMode(ss);
  Logger.log('Refresh mode: ' + refreshMode.phase + ' | ' + refreshMode.mode + ' — ' + refreshMode.reason);

  const cachedConfluence = (refreshMode.mode === 'partial') ? readConfluenceCache(ss) : {};

  let barsSymbols;
  if (refreshMode.mode === 'full') {
    barsSymbols = uniqueSymbols;
  } else {
    // Build PM Watchlist ticker set for always-include
    const pmWatchTickers = new Set();
    if (refreshMode.pmWatch) {
      for (const item of watchlistItems) {
        if (PM_WATCHLIST_SECTIONS.has(item.section.toUpperCase())) {
          pmWatchTickers.add(item.symbol);
        }
      }
    }

    // ── Smart AH: only positions + earnings + flagged after 2pm ──
    const isAH = refreshMode.phase === 'AFTER-HOURS' || (refreshMode.threshold >= 99);
    const ahTickers = isAH ? _getAHBarsTickers(ss) : null;

    // ── Hot Sector Boost: drop threshold for sectors with strong moves ──
    const hotSectors = new Set();
    const sectorETFs = {
      'XLK':'Software','SOXX':'Semis','SMH':'Semis','XLY':'Cons Disc','XLF':'Financials',
      'XLI':'Industrials','XLC':'Comm Svcs','IWM':'Small Cap','XLU':'Utilities',
      'XLP':'Staples','XLV':'Healthcare','XLE':'Energy','XLB':'Materials'
    };
    for (const etf of Object.keys(sectorETFs)) {
      const eq = quoteMap[etf];
      if (eq) {
        const chg = Math.abs(parseFloat(eq.NetChangePct || 0));
        const rv = getRvolTOD(parseInt(eq.Volume || 0), parseInt(eq.PreviousVolume || 1));
        if (chg >= 1.5 && rv >= 1.5) {
          hotSectors.add(sectorETFs[etf]);
          Logger.log('🔥 Hot sector: ' + sectorETFs[etf] + ' (' + etf + ' ' + chg.toFixed(1) + '%, RVOL ' + rv.toFixed(1) + ')');
        }
      }
    }
    // Persist for dashboard
    if (hotSectors.size > 0) {
      PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('HOT_SECTORS', JSON.stringify(Array.from(hotSectors)));
    } else {
      PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().deleteProperty('HOT_SECTORS');
    }

    // ── Low-signal deprioritization: skip bars for tickers cold for 5 days ──
    const confPeaks = _getConfPeaks();

    barsSymbols = uniqueSymbols.filter(sym => {
      // AH mode: only specific tickers
      if (isAH) return ahTickers && ahTickers.has(sym);
      // Always include PM Watchlist tickers
      if (pmWatchTickers.has(sym)) return true;
      // Hot sector boost: drop threshold to 15
      if (hotSectors.size > 0) {
        const sec = typeof _SEC !== 'undefined' ? _SEC[sym] : (typeof getSector === 'function' ? getSector(sym) : '');
        if (sec && hotSectors.has(sec)) {
          const cached = cachedConfluence[sym];
          if (cached && (cached.totalConfluence || 0) >= 15) return true;
        }
      }
      // Low-signal deprioritize: if 5-day peak < 16 AND not in PM watch, skip
      if (confPeaks[sym] !== undefined && confPeaks[sym] < 16 && !pmWatchTickers.has(sym)) return false;
      // Normal: cached confluence meets phase threshold
      const cached = cachedConfluence[sym];
      return cached && (cached.totalConfluence || 0) >= refreshMode.threshold;
    });
    Logger.log('Partial: ' + barsSymbols.length + '/' + uniqueSymbols.length + ' tickers (>=' + refreshMode.threshold + ' confluence + ' + pmWatchTickers.size + ' PM Watch' + (hotSectors.size ? ' + 🔥' + Array.from(hotSectors).join(',') : '') + (isAH ? ' · AH smart: ' + (ahTickers ? ahTickers.size : 0) : '') + ')');
  }

  // ==================== TRADESTATION BARS ====================
  const barsMap = {};
  const token = getAccessToken();
  const BARS_BATCH = 25;
  let barsSuccess = 0, barsFail = 0;
  for (let b = 0; b < barsSymbols.length; b += BARS_BATCH) {
    const batch = barsSymbols.slice(b, b + BARS_BATCH);
    const barsRequests = batch.map(sym => ({
      url: 'https://api.tradestation.com/v3/marketdata/barcharts/' + sym
        + '?interval=5&unit=Minute&barsback=' + BARS_BACK,
      headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token },
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    }));

    const barsResponses = trackedFetchAll(barsRequests, 'bars-batch');
    for (let i = 0; i < batch.length; i++) {
      try {
        const code = barsResponses[i].getResponseCode();
        const text = barsResponses[i].getContentText();
        if (code === 200 && text && text.trim()) {
          const data = JSON.parse(text);
          barsMap[batch[i]] = data.Bars || [];
          if ((data.Bars || []).length > 0) barsSuccess++;
          else barsFail++;
        } else {
          if (code !== 200) Logger.log('Bars HTTP ' + code + ' for ' + batch[i] + ': ' + text.substring(0, 200));
          barsMap[batch[i]] = [];
          barsFail++;
        }
      } catch (e) {
        Logger.log('Bars parse error for ' + batch[i] + ': ' + e.message);
        barsMap[batch[i]] = [];
        barsFail++;
      }
    }
    if (b + BARS_BATCH < barsSymbols.length) Utilities.sleep(2000);
  }
  Logger.log('Bars fetched: ' + barsSuccess + ' success, ' + barsFail + ' empty/failed out of ' + barsSymbols.length + ' (' + refreshMode.mode + ' mode)');

  const confluenceMap = {};
  // Pre-load per-ticker volume profile for RVOL-TOD
  try { _loadVolProfile(ss); } catch(vlp) { Logger.log('VolProfile load: ' + vlp.message); }
  const newsCatalystSet = buildNewsCatalystSet();
  for (const sym of uniqueSymbols) {
    const quote = quoteMap[sym];
    if (!quote) continue;

    if (barsMap[sym] !== undefined) {
      try {
        confluenceMap[sym] = calcConfluence(quote, barsMap[sym] || [], spyQuote, totalBreadth, breadth.vix, newsCatalystSet);
      } catch (e) {
        Logger.log('Confluence error for ' + sym + ': ' + e.message);
        confluenceMap[sym] = cachedConfluence[sym] || null;
      }
    } else if (cachedConfluence[sym]) {
      const cached = cachedConfluence[sym];
      cached.last = quote.Last;
      cached.netPct = quote.NetChangePct ? parseFloat(quote.NetChangePct).toFixed(2) : (cached.netPct || '0.00');
      cached.bid = quote.Bid;
      cached.ask = quote.Ask;
      cached.volume = quote.Volume;
      cached.spreadPct = (quote.Ask && quote.Bid && quote.Last) ? ((quote.Ask - quote.Bid) / quote.Last * 100) : (cached.spreadPct || 0);
      confluenceMap[sym] = cached;
    } else {
      confluenceMap[sym] = null;
    }
  }

  try {
    writeConfluenceCache(ss, confluenceMap);
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Confluence cache write failed (non-fatal): ' + e.message);
  }

  // ── Update CONF_PEAK_5D for low-signal deprioritization ──
  try { _updateConfPeaks(confluenceMap); } catch(cp) { Logger.log('ConfPeak update: ' + cp.message); }

  // ── Dynamic: add RVOL alerts on full scans + refresh earnings-based tickers ──
  if (refreshMode.mode === 'full') {
    try { _addDynamicRVOLAlerts(ss, quoteMap, _configSymSet); } catch(dr) { Logger.log('Dynamic RVOL: ' + dr.message); }
    try {
      var earnMap = getCachedEarnings(ss, uniqueSymbols);
      populateDynamic(ss, _configSymSet, earnMap);
    } catch(dp) { Logger.log('Dynamic earnings refresh: ' + dp.message); }
  }

  // --- IN PLAY TODAY: Surface tickers meeting opportunity criteria ---
  // Scans all scored tickers for: high RVOL, big gap, catalyst, or strong confluence
  // These get flagged for the dashboard regardless of Config section placement
  const inPlayToday = [];
  const positionTickers = new Set();
  try {
    var ptRaw = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('MY_POSITION_TICKERS');
    if (ptRaw) JSON.parse(ptRaw).forEach(function(t) { positionTickers.add(t); });
  } catch(e) {}
  
  for (const sym of uniqueSymbols) {
    const c = confluenceMap[sym];
    if (!c) continue;
    
    const absGap = Math.abs(parseFloat(c.gapPct) || 0);
    const rvolVal = parseFloat(c.rvol) || 0;
    const confVal = c.totalConfluence || 0;
    const hasCat = c.hasCatalyst || false;
    
    // Qualify as "In Play" if ANY of these fire:
    var reasons = [];
    if (absGap >= 3.0) reasons.push('GAP ' + (parseFloat(c.gapPct) >= 0 ? '+' : '') + c.gapPct + '%');
    if (rvolVal >= 3.0) reasons.push('RVOL ' + c.rvol + 'x');
    if (hasCat) reasons.push('CATALYST');
    if (hasCat && rvolVal >= 2.0) reasons.push('NEWS+VOL');
    
    if (reasons.length > 0) {
      inPlayToday.push({
        symbol: sym,
        reasons: reasons,
        confluence: confVal,
        quality: c.quality,
        setup: c.setup,
        rvol: c.rvol,
        gapPct: c.gapPct,
        relStr: c.relStr,
        netPct: c.netPct,
        last: c.last,
        hasCatalyst: hasCat,
        isPosition: positionTickers.has(sym)
      });
    }
  }
  // Sort by confluence descending
  inPlayToday.sort(function(a, b) { return b.confluence - a.confluence; });
  // Persist for dashboard
  try {
    PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('IN_PLAY_TODAY', JSON.stringify(inPlayToday.slice(0, 25)));
    Logger.log('In Play Today: ' + inPlayToday.length + ' tickers qualified');
  } catch(e) {}

  const refreshSummary = refreshMode.mode === 'full'
    ? 'FULL (' + barsSymbols.length + ' bars)'
    : refreshMode.phase + ' PARTIAL (' + barsSymbols.length + '/' + uniqueSymbols.length + ' bars, >=' + refreshMode.threshold + ' + PM Watchlist)';
  Logger.log('Refresh complete: ' + refreshSummary);

  // --- Finnhub Earnings Dates ---
  let earningsMap = {};
  try {
    earningsMap = getCachedEarnings(ss, uniqueSymbols);
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Earnings cache read failed (non-fatal): ' + e.message);
  }

  // --- Finnhub Sector Data ---
  let sectorMap = {};
  try {
    sectorMap = getCachedSectors(ss, uniqueSymbols);
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Sector cache read failed (non-fatal): ' + e.message);
  }

  // Headers
  const headers = [
    'Section', 'Sector', 'Name', 'Ticker', 'Last', 'Chg%',
    'Confluence', 'Quality', 'Setup',
    'Mkt', 'Price', 'Mom', 'Vol', 'Level', 'Exec',
    'ATR Mod', 'Gap Mod', 'RS Mod', 'News Mod',
    'VWAP Flag', 'RS Flag', 'RSI Flag', 'RVOL Flag',
    'VWAP', 'RelStr%', 'RSI(5m)', 'RVOL',
    'EMA9', 'EMA20', 'ATR', 'Gap%', 'OR Hi', 'OR Lo',
    'Bid', 'Ask', 'Spread%', 'Volume',
    'Yest Hi', 'Yest Lo', 'Yest Close',
    '52w Hi', '52w Lo', '52w %',
    'EMA50', 'EMA50 Dist%',
    'AvgVol',
    'Earnings', 'Mkt Cap',
    'Notes'
  ];

  const rows = [headers];

  // --- Read persisted notes from Config tab ---
  const notesMap = {};
  const configSheetNotes = ss.getSheetByName('Config');
  if (configSheetNotes) {
    const notesRange = configSheetNotes.getRange('F1:G500');
    const notesData = notesRange.getValues();
    for (var n = 0; n < notesData.length; n++) {
      if (notesData[n][0] && notesData[n][1]) {
        notesMap[String(notesData[n][0]).trim().toUpperCase()] = String(notesData[n][1]);
      }
    }
  }

  // Build a Set of symbols that got fresh data this cycle for Watchlist filtering
  const refreshedSymbols = new Set(barsSymbols);

  for (const item of watchlistItems) {
    // Only show tickers that got fresh data this cycle
    if (!refreshedSymbols.has(item.symbol)) continue;
    
    const c = confluenceMap[item.symbol];
    const earn = earningsMap[item.symbol] || {};
    const gf = gfDaily[item.symbol] || {};
    const q = quoteMap[item.symbol] || {};
    const mktCap = q.MarketCap ? formatMarketCap(parseFloat(q.MarketCap)) : (gf.marketcap ? formatMarketCap(gf.marketcap) : '');
    const tickerName = q.Name || gf.name || '';
    const sector = sectorMap[item.symbol] || getSector(item.symbol) || '';
    if (c) {
      rows.push([
        item.section, sector, tickerName, item.symbol, c.last, c.netPct,
        c.totalConfluence, c.quality, (c.setup ? c.setup + '|' + (c.setupScore||0) + (c.setup2 ? '|' + c.setup2 + '|' + (c.setup2Score||0) : '') : '-'),
        c.marketCtx, c.priceStr, c.momentum, c.volScore, c.levelProx, c.execQual,
        c.atrMod, c.gapMod, c.rsMod, c.newsMod,
        c.vwapFlag, c.rsFlag, c.rsiFlag, c.rvolFlag,
        c.vwap.toFixed(2), c.relStr, c.rsi5m, c.rvol,
        c.ema9, c.ema20, c.atr, c.gapPct, c.orHigh, c.orLow,
        c.bid, c.ask, c.spreadPct.toFixed(3) + '%', c.volume,
        c.yestHigh, c.yestLow, c.yestClose,
        c.high52 || '', c.low52 || '', c.pct52,
        c.ema50, c.ema50DistPct,
        c.avgVol || '',
        earn.display || '', mktCap,
        notesMap[item.symbol.toUpperCase()] || ''
      ]);
    } else {
      const fallbackPrice = q.Last || '';
      const fallbackChg = q.NetChangePct ? parseFloat(q.NetChangePct).toFixed(2) : '';
      const fallbackVol = q.Volume || '';
      const fallbackMktCap = gf.marketcap ? formatMarketCap(gf.marketcap) : '';
      const fallbackH52 = gf.high52 || '';
      const fallbackL52 = gf.low52 || '';
      const fallback52Pct = (gf.high52 && gf.low52 && gf.high52 > gf.low52 && q.Last) ? (((q.Last - gf.low52) / (gf.high52 - gf.low52)) * 100).toFixed(1) : '';
      rows.push([item.section, sector, tickerName, item.symbol, fallbackPrice, fallbackChg,
        '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '',
        '', '', '', '',
        '', '', '', '',
        '', '', '', '',
        '', '', '', '', '', '',
        '', '', '', fallbackVol,
        '', '', '',
        fallbackH52, fallbackL52, fallback52Pct,
        '', '',
        q.AverageVolume || '',
        earn.display || '', fallbackMktCap,
        notesMap[item.symbol.toUpperCase()] || ''
      ]);
    }
  }

  watchSheet.clearContents();
  watchSheet.clearFormats();

  const gpRow = new Array(headers.length).fill('');
  gpRow[0] = 'GP-' + gameplan.gp + '  |  ' + gameplan.action + '  |  Score: ' + totalBreadth.toFixed(1) + ' (' + gameplan.adjPct + '%)  |  Sizing: ' + gameplan.sizing + '  |  Growth: ' + sectors.growthGreen + '/8  |  Defensive: ' + sectors.defGreen + '/5  |  ' + refreshSummary + '  |  Showing: ' + (rows.length - 1) + '/' + uniqueSymbols.length + '  |  Updated: ' + new Date().toLocaleTimeString() + '  |  Next: ' + new Date(Date.now() + 5 * 60000).toLocaleTimeString();

  const groupRow = new Array(headers.length).fill('');
  groupRow[0] = 'IDENTITY + PRICE';
  groupRow[6] = 'CONFLUENCE';
  groupRow[9] = 'CORE SCORES (0-5)';
  groupRow[15] = 'MODIFIERS (±2)';
  groupRow[19] = 'FLAGS';
  groupRow[23] = 'TECHNICALS';
  groupRow[33] = 'EXECUTION';
  groupRow[37] = 'REFERENCE';
  groupRow[46] = 'EARNINGS / NOTES';

  const allRows = [gpRow, groupRow, ...rows];
  watchSheet.getRange(1, 1, allRows.length, headers.length).setValues(allRows);

  watchSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).merge();

  const merges = [
    [2, 1, 1, 6], [2, 7, 1, 9], [2, 10, 1, 15], [2, 16, 1, 19],
    [2, 20, 1, 23], [2, 24, 1, 33], [2, 34, 1, 37], [2, 38, 1, 46], [2, 47, 1, 49],
  ];
  for (const m of merges) {
    watchSheet.getRange(m[0], m[1], 1, m[3] - m[1] + 1).merge()
      .setHorizontalAlignment('center');
  }
  var groupEnds = [6, 9, 15, 19, 23, 33, 37, 46, 49];
  for (var g = 0; g < groupEnds.length - 1; g++) {
    watchSheet.getRange(2, groupEnds[g], 2, 1)
      .setBorder(null, null, null, true, null, null, '#ffffff', SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID_THICK);
    watchSheet.getRange(2, groupEnds[g] + 1, 2, 1)
      .setBorder(null, true, null, null, null, null, '#ffffff', SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID_THICK);
  }

  if (rows.length > 1) {
    watchSheet.getRange(4, 1, rows.length - 1, headers.length).sort({column: 7, ascending: false});
  }

  watchSheet.getRange(rows.length + 4, 1).setValue('Last Updated: ' + new Date().toLocaleString());

  // ==================== FORMATTING ====================
  formatWatchlist(watchSheet, rows.length + 2, headers.length, 4);

  var existingFilter = watchSheet.getFilter();
  if (existingFilter) {
    var filterRange = existingFilter.getRange();
    if (filterRange.getNumRows() !== rows.length || filterRange.getNumColumns() !== headers.length) {
      existingFilter.remove();
      watchSheet.getRange(3, 1, rows.length, headers.length).createFilter();
    }
  } else {
    watchSheet.getRange(3, 1, rows.length, headers.length).createFilter();
  }

  // ==================== MY POSITIONS VIEW ====================
  buildPositionScannerView(ss, rows, headers, gameplan, totalBreadth, sectors);

  // ==================== PRE-MARKET TAB ====================
  try {
    buildPreMarketTab(ss, watchlistItems, gfDaily, quoteMap, earningsMap, spyQuote);
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Pre-Market tab error (non-fatal): ' + e.message);
  }

  // ==================== WATCHLIST DOC SYNC ====================
  // Sync live market data + econ calendar + watchlist tickers to Google Doc
  // so Claude can pull it for any MBU timing
  try {
    syncWatchlistDoc();  // no areteFlags needed here — hourly syncAll() handles those
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('Watchlist Doc sync error (non-fatal): ' + e.message);
  }

  Logger.log('Sheet updated successfully at ' + new Date());
  
  try {
    PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('lastUpdateTime', Date.now().toString());
  } catch (e) {}
  
  // Record breadth & GP history for charts
  try {
    var histProps = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var histKey = 'BREADTH_GP_HISTORY';
    var histRaw = histProps.getProperty(histKey) || '[]';
    var hist = JSON.parse(histRaw);
    var nowUtc = new Date();
    var azToday = new Date(nowUtc.getTime() - 7 * 3600000);
    var azDateStr = azToday.getFullYear() + '-' + String(azToday.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0') + '-' + String(azToday.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
    if (hist.length > 0 && hist[0].d !== azDateStr) hist = [];
    hist.push({ d: azDateStr, t: Date.now(), v: parseFloat(totalBreadth.toFixed(1)), gp: gameplan.gp });
    if (hist.length > 500) hist = hist.slice(hist.length - 500);
    histProps.setProperty(histKey, JSON.stringify(hist));
    
    // Calculate trajectory and GP sub-mode from breadth history
    var trajResult = classifyTrajectory(hist);
    var subModeResult = getGPSubMode(gameplan.gp, trajResult);
    histProps.setProperty('GP_TRAJECTORY', JSON.stringify(trajResult));
    histProps.setProperty('GP_SUB_MODE', JSON.stringify(subModeResult));
    Logger.log('GP Sub-Mode: ' + subModeResult.subMode + ' (' + trajResult.trajectory + ', delta=' + trajResult.delta + ')');
    
    // ── Cache internals history for dashboard sparklines (every cycle) ──
    try {
      var _ihRaw = histProps.getProperty('INTERNALS_HIST') || '[]';
      var _ih = JSON.parse(_ihRaw);
      if (_ih.length > 0 && _ih[0].d !== azDateStr) _ih = [];
      _ih.push({
        d: azDateStr, t: Date.now(),
        tick: parseFloat(breadth.tick) || 0,
        add: parseFloat(breadth.add) || 0,
        adqd: parseFloat(breadth.adqd) || 0,
        vold: parseFloat(breadth.vold) || 0,
        volqd: parseFloat(breadth.volqd) || 0
      });
      if (_ih.length > 200) _ih = _ih.slice(_ih.length - 200);
      histProps.setProperty('INTERNALS_HIST', JSON.stringify(_ih));
    } catch(ihErr) { Logger.log('IntHist: ' + ihErr.message); }
    
    // ── BREADTH ALERT ENGINE ──
    try {
      _checkBreadthAlerts(hist, totalBreadth, breadth, sectors, sectorQuotes, breadthQuotes);
    } catch(alertErr) {
      Logger.log('BreadthAlert error: ' + alertErr.message);
    }
    
  } catch(e) {}
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// BREADTH ALERT ENGINE
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
var BREADTH_ALERT_IMMEDIATE = 1.5;
var BREADTH_ALERT_SUSTAINED = 2.5;
var BREADTH_ALERT_COOLDOWN = 900000;

function _checkBreadthAlerts(hist, currentScore, breadth, sectors, sectorQuotes, breadthQuotes) {
  if (!hist || hist.length < 2) return;
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var lastAlertTime = parseInt(props.getProperty('BREADTH_ALERT_LAST') || '0');
  if (Date.now() - lastAlertTime < BREADTH_ALERT_COOLDOWN) return;
  
  var prev = hist[hist.length - 2];
  var immDelta = currentScore - prev.v;
  var sustDelta = 0;
  if (hist.length >= 4) sustDelta = currentScore - hist[hist.length - 4].v;
  
  var triggered = false, alertType = '', delta = 0;
  if (Math.abs(immDelta) >= BREADTH_ALERT_IMMEDIATE) { triggered = true; alertType = 'IMMEDIATE'; delta = immDelta; }
  else if (Math.abs(sustDelta) >= BREADTH_ALERT_SUSTAINED) { triggered = true; alertType = 'SUSTAINED'; delta = sustDelta; }
  if (!triggered) return;
  
  var direction = delta > 0 ? 'SURGE' : 'DROP';
  var causes = [];
  
  // 1. Sector flips and big movers
  var prevSectorData = null;
  try { var ps = props.getProperty('PREV_SECTOR_STATE'); if (ps) prevSectorData = JSON.parse(ps); } catch(e) {}
  if (sectors.sectorData && prevSectorData) {
    for (var si = 0; si < sectors.sectorData.length; si++) {
      var sd = sectors.sectorData[si]; var prevSd = null;
      for (var pi = 0; pi < prevSectorData.length; pi++) { if (prevSectorData[pi].sym === sd.sym) { prevSd = prevSectorData[pi]; break; } }
      if (prevSd) {
        var chgNow = parseFloat(sd.chg) || 0, chgPrev = parseFloat(prevSd.chg) || 0;
        if (Math.abs(chgNow - chgPrev) >= 0.3) causes.push({ type: 'SECTOR', sym: sd.sym, delta: chgNow - chgPrev, now: chgNow });
        if ((chgPrev > 0 && chgNow < 0) || (chgPrev < 0 && chgNow > 0)) causes.push({ type: 'SECTOR_FLIP', sym: sd.sym, from: chgPrev, to: chgNow });
      }
    }
  }
  if (sectors.sectorData) { props.setProperty('PREV_SECTOR_STATE', JSON.stringify(sectors.sectorData.map(function(sd) { return { sym: sd.sym, chg: sd.chg }; }))); }
  
  // 2. VIX
  var prevVix = parseFloat(props.getProperty('PREV_VIX') || '0'), curVix = breadth.vix || 0;
  if (prevVix > 0 && Math.abs(curVix - prevVix) >= 0.5) causes.push({ type: 'VIX', from: prevVix, to: curVix, delta: curVix - prevVix });
  props.setProperty('PREV_VIX', String(curVix));
  
  // 3. Internals
  var prevInternals = null;
  try { var pi2 = props.getProperty('PREV_INTERNALS'); if (pi2) prevInternals = JSON.parse(pi2); } catch(e) {}
  var internals = { tick: breadth.tick, add: breadth.add, adqd: breadth.adqd, vold: breadth.vold, volqd: breadth.volqd };
  if (prevInternals) {
    var intNames = { tick: '$TICK', add: '$ADD', adqd: '$ADQD', vold: '$VOLD', volqd: '$VOLQD' };
    for (var k in internals) {
      var cur = parseFloat(internals[k]) || 0, prv = parseFloat(prevInternals[k]) || 0;
      var pctC = prv !== 0 ? ((cur - prv) / Math.abs(prv) * 100) : 0;
      if (Math.abs(pctC) >= 20) causes.push({ type: 'INTERNAL', name: intNames[k], from: prv, to: cur, pctChg: pctC });
    }
  }
  props.setProperty('PREV_INTERNALS', JSON.stringify(internals));
  
  // 4. Growth/Defensive shift
  var prevGrowth = parseInt(props.getProperty('PREV_GROWTH_GREEN') || '-1');
  var prevDef = parseInt(props.getProperty('PREV_DEF_GREEN') || '-1');
  if (prevGrowth >= 0) {
    if (Math.abs(sectors.growthGreen - prevGrowth) >= 2) causes.push({ type: 'GROWTH_SHIFT', from: prevGrowth, to: sectors.growthGreen });
    if (Math.abs(sectors.defGreen - prevDef) >= 2) causes.push({ type: 'DEF_SHIFT', from: prevDef, to: sectors.defGreen });
  }
  props.setProperty('PREV_GROWTH_GREEN', String(sectors.growthGreen));
  props.setProperty('PREV_DEF_GREEN', String(sectors.defGreen));
  
  // 5. Top movers
  var topMovers = [];
  if (sectorQuotes) {
    for (var qi = 0; qi < sectorQuotes.length; qi++) {
      var pct = parseFloat(sectorQuotes[qi].NetChangePct || 0);
      if (Math.abs(pct) >= 1.5) topMovers.push({ sym: sectorQuotes[qi].Symbol, chg: pct });
    }
  }
  topMovers.sort(function(a, b) { return Math.abs(b.chg) - Math.abs(a.chg); });
  if (topMovers.length > 3) topMovers = topMovers.slice(0, 3);
  
  // Build alert
  var alert = {
    type: alertType, direction: direction,
    delta: Math.round(delta * 10) / 10, score: Math.round(currentScore * 10) / 10,
    prevScore: Math.round((currentScore - delta) * 10) / 10,
    timestamp: Date.now(),
    timeAZ: Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'h:mm a'),
    causes: causes, topMovers: topMovers, summary: '', recentNews: []
  };
  
  // Summary text
  var sum = direction + ' ' + (delta > 0 ? '+' : '') + alert.delta + ' to ' + alert.score + ' (' + alertType + '). ';
  var parts = [];
  for (var ci = 0; ci < causes.length; ci++) {
    var c = causes[ci];
    if (c.type === 'SECTOR_FLIP') parts.push(c.sym + ' flipped ' + (c.to > 0 ? 'green' : 'red'));
    else if (c.type === 'SECTOR') parts.push(c.sym + ' ' + (c.delta > 0 ? '+' : '') + c.delta.toFixed(1) + '%');
    else if (c.type === 'VIX') parts.push('VIX ' + (c.delta > 0 ? '+' : '') + c.delta.toFixed(1) + ' to ' + c.to.toFixed(1));
    else if (c.type === 'INTERNAL') parts.push(c.name + ' ' + (c.pctChg > 0 ? '+' : '') + c.pctChg.toFixed(0) + '%');
    else if (c.type === 'GROWTH_SHIFT') parts.push('Growth ' + c.from + ' to ' + c.to + '/8');
    else if (c.type === 'DEF_SHIFT') parts.push('Defensive ' + c.from + ' to ' + c.to + '/5');
  }
  if (topMovers.length > 0) parts.push('Movers: ' + topMovers.map(function(m) { return m.sym + ' ' + (m.chg > 0 ? '+' : '') + m.chg.toFixed(1) + '%'; }).join(', '));
  alert.summary = sum + parts.join(' | ');
  
  // Optional: 1 news fetch
  try {
    var fhKey = getFinnhubKey();
    if (fhKey) {
      var newsResp = trackedFetch('https://finnhub.io/api/v1/news?category=general&token=' + fhKey, { muteHttpExceptions: true }, 'breadth-alert-news');
      if (newsResp.getResponseCode() === 200) {
        var newsItems = JSON.parse(newsResp.getContentText());
        var cutoff = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000) - 1800;
        for (var ni = 0; ni < newsItems.length && alert.recentNews.length < 3; ni++) {
          if (newsItems[ni].datetime >= cutoff && newsItems[ni].headline) alert.recentNews.push({ headline: newsItems[ni].headline, source: newsItems[ni].source || '' });
        }
      }
    }
  } catch(ne) {}
  
  // Store
  var alerts = [];
  try { var ar = props.getProperty('BREADTH_ALERTS'); if (ar) alerts = JSON.parse(ar); } catch(e) {}
  alerts.push(alert);
  if (alerts.length > 20) alerts = alerts.slice(alerts.length - 20);
  props.setProperty('BREADTH_ALERTS', JSON.stringify(alerts));
  props.setProperty('BREADTH_ALERT_LAST', String(Date.now()));
  Logger.log('BREADTH ALERT: ' + alert.summary);
}

function formatMarketCap(mc) {
  if (!mc || mc === 0) return '';
  if (mc >= 1e12) return (mc / 1e12).toFixed(1) + 'T';
  if (mc >= 1e9) return (mc / 1e9).toFixed(1) + 'B';
  if (mc >= 1e6) return (mc / 1e6).toFixed(0) + 'M';
  return mc.toFixed(0);
}

// --- NOTES PERSISTENCE ---

function onEdit(e) {
  const sheet = e.range.getSheet();
  if (sheet.getName() !== 'Watchlist') return;
  
  const row = e.range.getRow();
  const col = e.range.getColumn();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();
  
  if (col !== lastCol || row < 4) return;
  
  const ticker = sheet.getRange(row, 4).getValue();
  const note = e.range.getValue();
  
  if (!ticker) return;
  
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const config = ss.getSheetByName('Config');
  if (!config) return;
  
  const notesRange = config.getRange('F1:G500');
  const notesData = notesRange.getValues();
  
  var found = false;
  for (var i = 0; i < notesData.length; i++) {
    if (String(notesData[i][0]).trim().toUpperCase() === String(ticker).trim().toUpperCase()) {
      config.getRange(i + 1, 7).setValue(note);
      found = true;
      break;
    }
  }
  
  if (!found) {
    for (var i = 0; i < notesData.length; i++) {
      if (!notesData[i][0]) {
        config.getRange(i + 1, 6).setValue(ticker);
        config.getRange(i + 1, 7).setValue(note);
        break;
      }
    }
  }
}

// --- FINNHUB EARNINGS & SECTOR DATA ---

const FINNHUB_KEY_PROP = 'finnhub_api_key';

function getFinnhubKey() {
  return PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty(FINNHUB_KEY_PROP) || '';
}

// ==================== SECTOR CACHE (PERMANENT) ====================

function getCachedSectors(ss, symbols) {
  const CACHE_SHEET = '_SectorCache';
  let cacheSheet = ss.getSheetByName(CACHE_SHEET);
  
  const cached = {};
  if (cacheSheet) {
    const data = cacheSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (data[i][0]) {
        cached[String(data[i][0]).toUpperCase()] = String(data[i][1] || '');
      }
    }
  }
  
  const missing = symbols.filter(s => 
    !s.startsWith('$') && !s.startsWith('@') && s.indexOf('/') < 0 && !cached[s]
  );
  
  if (missing.length === 0) {
    Logger.log('Sector cache: ' + Object.keys(cached).length + ' entries, 0 missing');
    return cached;
  }
  
  // Safety: only fetch missing sectors once per session to avoid repeated fetches if cache write fails
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var sectorFetchDone = props.getProperty('SECTOR_FETCH_DONE');
  var today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), 'America/Phoenix', 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  if (sectorFetchDone === today && missing.length > 10) {
    Logger.log('Sector cache: already attempted fetch today (flag), ' + missing.length + ' still missing — skipping');
    return cached;
  }
  
  Logger.log('Sector cache: fetching ' + missing.length + ' new tickers...');
  const key = getFinnhubKey();
  if (!key) {
    Logger.log('No Finnhub API key — skipping sector fetch');
    return cached;
  }
  
  const BATCH = 50;
  for (let b = 0; b < missing.length; b += BATCH) {
    const batch = missing.slice(b, b + BATCH);
    const requests = batch.map(sym => ({
      url: 'https://finnhub.io/api/v1/stock/profile2?symbol=' + sym + '&token=' + key,
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    }));
    
    const responses = trackedFetchAll(requests, 'finnhub-sectors');
    for (let i = 0; i < batch.length; i++) {
      try {
        const code = responses[i].getResponseCode();
        if (code === 200) {
          const data = JSON.parse(responses[i].getContentText());
          cached[batch[i]] = data.finnhubIndustry || '';
        } else if (code === 429) {
          Logger.log('Sector fetch: rate limited at batch ' + b + ', will continue next refresh');
          break;
        }
      } catch (e) { /* skip */ }
    }
    if (b + BATCH < missing.length) Utilities.sleep(3000);
  }
  
  if (!cacheSheet) {
    cacheSheet = ss.insertSheet(CACHE_SHEET);
    cacheSheet.hideSheet();
  }
  cacheSheet.clear();
  const rows = [['Symbol', 'Sector']];
  for (const sym of Object.keys(cached)) {
    rows.push([sym, cached[sym]]);
  }
  cacheSheet.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, 2).setValues(rows);
  Logger.log('Sector cache: saved ' + (rows.length - 1) + ' entries');
  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('SECTOR_FETCH_DONE', today);
  
  return cached;
}

// ==================== EARNINGS CACHE (DAILY) ====================

function getCachedEarnings(ss, symbols) {
  const CACHE_SHEET = '_EarningsCache';
  let cacheSheet = ss.getSheetByName(CACHE_SHEET);
  
  const today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), 'America/Phoenix', 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  let cached = {};
  
  if (cacheSheet) {
    const stamp = cacheSheet.getRange(1, 1).getValue();
    if (String(stamp) === today) {
      const data = cacheSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (data[i][0]) {
          cached[String(data[i][0])] = {
            date: String(data[i][1] || ''),
            display: String(data[i][2] || ''),
            daysUntil: parseInt(data[i][3]) || 999
          };
        }
      }
      Logger.log('Earnings cache: loaded ' + Object.keys(cached).length + ' entries from ' + today);
      return cached;
    }
  }
  
  // Safety: only fetch once per day even if cache sheet write fails
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var earnFetchDone = props.getProperty('EARN_FETCH_DONE');
  if (earnFetchDone === today) {
    Logger.log('Earnings cache: already fetched today (flag), skipping re-fetch');
    return cached;
  }
  
  Logger.log('Earnings cache: refreshing for ' + symbols.length + ' symbols...');
  const key = getFinnhubKey();
  if (!key) {
    Logger.log('No Finnhub API key — skipping earnings fetch');
    return cached;
  }
  
  const now = new Date();
  const todayStr = Utilities.formatDate(now, 'America/New_York', 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const filteredSyms = symbols.filter(s => !s.startsWith('$') && !s.startsWith('@') && s.indexOf('/') < 0);
  
  const BATCH = 50;
  for (let b = 0; b < filteredSyms.length; b += BATCH) {
    const batch = filteredSyms.slice(b, b + BATCH);
    const requests = batch.map(sym => ({
      url: 'https://finnhub.io/api/v1/calendar/earnings?symbol=' + sym + '&from=' + todayStr + '&to=2027-01-01&token=' + key,
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    }));
    
    const responses = trackedFetchAll(requests, 'finnhub-earnings');
    for (let i = 0; i < batch.length; i++) {
      try {
        const code = responses[i].getResponseCode();
        if (code !== 200) continue;
        const data = JSON.parse(responses[i].getContentText());
        
        if (data.earningsCalendar && data.earningsCalendar.length > 0) {
          var next = data.earningsCalendar[0];
          var earnDate = next.date || '';
          if (earnDate) {
            var earnDateObj = new Date(earnDate + 'T00:00:00');
            var diffMs = earnDateObj.getTime() - now.getTime();
            var diffDays = Math.ceil(diffMs / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
            
            var daysUntil = '';
            if (diffDays === 0) daysUntil = 'TODAY';
            else if (diffDays === 1) daysUntil = 'TOMORROW';
            else if (diffDays < 0) daysUntil = '';
            else daysUntil = diffDays + 'd';
            
            var timing = '';
            if (next.hour === 'bmo') timing = ' BMO';
            else if (next.hour === 'amc') timing = ' AMC';
            
            cached[batch[i]] = {
              date: earnDate,
              display: daysUntil ? earnDate + timing + ' (' + daysUntil + ')' : '',
              daysUntil: diffDays
            };
          }
        }
      } catch (e) { /* skip */ }
    }
    if (b + BATCH < filteredSyms.length) Utilities.sleep(3000);
  }
  
  if (!cacheSheet) {
    cacheSheet = ss.insertSheet(CACHE_SHEET);
    cacheSheet.hideSheet();
  }
  cacheSheet.clear();
  const rows = [[today, 'date', 'display', 'daysUntil']];
  for (const sym of Object.keys(cached)) {
    rows.push([sym, cached[sym].date || '', cached[sym].display || '', cached[sym].daysUntil || 999]);
  }
  if (rows.length > 1) {
    cacheSheet.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, 4).setValues(rows);
  }
  Logger.log('Earnings cache: saved ' + (rows.length - 1) + ' entries');
  props.setProperty('EARN_FETCH_DONE', today);
  
  return cached;
}

// --- PER-REFRESH FORMATTING ---

function formatWatchlist(sheet, numRows, numCols, dataStartRow) {
  if (!dataStartRow) dataStartRow = 4;
  var dataRows = numRows - (dataStartRow - 1);
  if (dataRows < 1) return;

  if (dataStartRow === 4) {
    var gpCell = sheet.getRange(1, 1);
    var gpText = String(gpCell.getValue());
    var gpBg = '#1a1a2e'; var gpFont = '#ffffff';
    if (gpText.indexOf('GP-A') >= 0) { gpBg = '#00C853'; gpFont = '#ffffff'; }
    else if (gpText.indexOf('GP-B') >= 0) { gpBg = '#2196F3'; gpFont = '#ffffff'; }
    else if (gpText.indexOf('GP-C') >= 0) { gpBg = '#FF9800'; gpFont = '#000000'; }
    else if (gpText.indexOf('GP-D') >= 0) { gpBg = '#F44336'; gpFont = '#ffffff'; }
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, numCols).setBackground(gpBg).setFontColor(gpFont)
      .setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(12).setHorizontalAlignment('left').setVerticalAlignment('middle');

    sheet.getRange(2, 1, 1, numCols).setBackground('#2a2a4a').setFontColor('#ffffff').setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(10)
      .setHorizontalAlignment('center').setVerticalAlignment('middle');

    sheet.getRange(3, 1, 1, numCols).setBackground('#1a1a2e').setFontColor('#ffffff').setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(9);
    sheet.setFrozenRows(3);
  } else {
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, numCols).setBackground('#2a2a4a').setFontColor('#ffffff').setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(10)
      .setHorizontalAlignment('center').setVerticalAlignment('middle');
    sheet.getRange(2, 1, 1, numCols).setBackground('#1a1a2e').setFontColor('#ffffff').setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(9);
    sheet.setFrozenRows(2);
  }

  sheet.getRange(dataStartRow, 1, dataRows, numCols).setFontSize(9);

  var sectionVals = sheet.getRange(dataStartRow, 1, dataRows, 1).getValues();
  for (var i = 0; i < sectionVals.length; i++) {
    var sec = String(sectionVals[i][0]).trim().toUpperCase();
    var row = i + dataStartRow;
    if (sec === 'MY POSITIONS') {
      sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, numCols).setBackground('#d0e2f7').setFontWeight('bold');
    } else if (sec === 'ARETE' || sec === 'ARETE RESEARCH') {
      sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, numCols).setBackground('#d4edda').setFontWeight('bold');
    } else if (sec === 'WATCHING') {
      sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, numCols).setBackground('#fde8d0').setFontWeight('bold');
    }
  }

  var sectorPerfMap = {};
  var mktSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('Market');
  if (mktSheet) {
    var mktData = mktSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    for (var m = 0; m < mktData.length; m++) {
      var mSym = String(mktData[m][0]);
      var mChgStr = String(mktData[m][2]);
      if (mChgStr.indexOf('%') >= 0) {
        sectorPerfMap[mSym] = parseFloat(mChgStr);
      }
    }
  }
  
  var sectorRange = sheet.getRange(dataStartRow, 2, dataRows, 1);
  var sectorVals2 = sectorRange.getValues();
  var sectorBgs = [], sectorFonts = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < sectorVals2.length; i++) {
    var sectorSym = String(sectorVals2[i][0]).trim();
    var sPerf = sectorPerfMap[sectorSym] || 0;
    if (sPerf > 0.3) { sectorBgs.push(['#c6efce']); sectorFonts.push(['#006100']); }
    else if (sPerf < -0.3) { sectorBgs.push(['#ffc7ce']); sectorFonts.push(['#9c0006']); }
    else { sectorBgs.push([null]); sectorFonts.push(['#666666']); }
  }
  sectorRange.setBackgrounds(sectorBgs).setFontColors(sectorFonts);

  var confRange = sheet.getRange(dataStartRow, 7, dataRows, 1);
  var confVals = confRange.getValues();
  var confBgs = [], confFonts = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < confVals.length; i++) {
    var v = parseFloat(confVals[i][0]) || 0;
    if (v >= 28) { confBgs.push(['#c6efce']); confFonts.push(['#006100']); }
    else if (v >= 24) { confBgs.push(['#d5f5d5']); confFonts.push(['#006100']); }
    else if (v >= 20) { confBgs.push(['#ffeb9c']); confFonts.push(['#9c6500']); }
    else { confBgs.push(['#ffc7ce']); confFonts.push(['#9c0006']); }
  }
  confRange.setBackgrounds(confBgs).setFontColors(confFonts).setFontWeight('bold');

  sheet.getRange(dataStartRow, 8, dataRows, 1).setBackgrounds(confBgs).setFontColors(confFonts).setFontWeight('bold');

  colorBySign(sheet, dataStartRow, 6, dataRows);
  colorBySign(sheet, dataStartRow, 25, dataRows);

  var flagCols = [20, 21, 22, 23];
  for (var f = 0; f < flagCols.length; f++) {
    var range = sheet.getRange(dataStartRow, flagCols[f], dataRows, 1);
    var vals = range.getValues();
    var bgs = [], fonts = [];
    for (var i = 0; i < vals.length; i++) {
      var val = String(vals[i][0]).toUpperCase();
      if (val === 'PASS') { bgs.push(['#c6efce']); fonts.push(['#006100']); }
      else if (val === 'WARN') { bgs.push(['#ffeb9c']); fonts.push(['#9c6500']); }
      else { bgs.push(['#ffc7ce']); fonts.push(['#9c0006']); }
    }
    range.setBackgrounds(bgs).setFontColors(fonts).setFontWeight('bold');
  }

  var totalCols = sheet.getLastColumn() || numCols;
  var earnVals = sheet.getRange(dataStartRow, 47, dataRows, 1).getValues();
  for (var i = 0; i < earnVals.length; i++) {
    var ev = String(earnVals[i][0]);
    var row = i + dataStartRow;
    var rowRange = sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, totalCols);
    var earnCell = sheet.getRange(row, 47);

    if (ev.indexOf('TODAY') >= 0) {
      rowRange.setBackground('#fff0f0');
      earnCell.setBackground('#ffc7ce').setFontColor('#9c0006').setFontWeight('bold');
    } else if (ev.indexOf('TOMORROW') >= 0) {
      rowRange.setBackground('#fff8ee');
      earnCell.setBackground('#ffeb9c').setFontColor('#9c6500').setFontWeight('bold');
    } else if (ev.match(/\((\d+)d\)/)) {
      var days = parseInt(ev.match(/\((\d+)d\)/)[1]);
      if (days <= 7) {
        rowRange.setBackground('#fffdf0');
        earnCell.setBackground('#fff2cc').setFontColor('#7f6000').setFontWeight('bold');
      }
    }
  }
}

function colorBySign(sheet, startRow, col, numRows) {
  var range = sheet.getRange(startRow, col, numRows, 1);
  var vals = range.getValues();
  var bgs = [], fonts = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < vals.length; i++) {
    var v = parseFloat(vals[i][0]) || 0;
    if (v > 0) { bgs.push(['#c6efce']); fonts.push(['#006100']); }
    else if (v < 0) { bgs.push(['#ffc7ce']); fonts.push(['#9c0006']); }
    else { bgs.push(['#ffffff']); fonts.push(['#000000']); }
  }
  range.setBackgrounds(bgs).setFontColors(fonts);
}

// --- SETUP & TRIGGER ---

function setupCredentials() {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();

  const clientId = ui.prompt('Enter your TradeStation API Key (client_id):').getResponseText();
  const clientSecret = ui.prompt('Enter your TradeStation Secret:').getResponseText();
  const refreshToken = ui.prompt('Enter your Refresh Token:').getResponseText();

  const props = getScriptProperties();
  props.setProperty('CLIENT_ID', clientId);
  props.setProperty('CLIENT_SECRET', clientSecret);
  props.setProperty('REFRESH_TOKEN', refreshToken);

  ui.alert('Credentials saved securely! You can now run updateSheet() or set up a trigger.');
}

function setupFinnhub() {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const key = ui.prompt('Enter your Finnhub API key (free at finnhub.io):').getResponseText();
  if (key) {
    PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty(FINNHUB_KEY_PROP, key.trim());
    ui.alert('Finnhub API key saved! Earnings dates will appear on next refresh.');
  }
}

// Legacy alias — redirects to startScanner
function createTrigger() {
  startScanner();
}

// --- MENU ---

function refreshEarnings() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const cacheSheet = ss.getSheetByName('_EarningsCache');
  if (cacheSheet) cacheSheet.clear();
  const watchlistItems = getWatchlist();
  const uniqueSymbols = [...new Set(watchlistItems.map(w => w.symbol))];
  getCachedEarnings(ss, uniqueSymbols);
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Earnings cache refreshed for ' + uniqueSymbols.length + ' symbols.');
}

function refreshSectors() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const cacheSheet = ss.getSheetByName('_SectorCache');
  if (cacheSheet) {
    ss.deleteSheet(cacheSheet);
  }
  const watchlistItems = getWatchlist();
  const uniqueSymbols = [...new Set(watchlistItems.map(w => w.symbol))];
  getCachedSectors(ss, uniqueSymbols);
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Sector cache refreshed for ' + uniqueSymbols.length + ' symbols.');
}

function clearNewsCache() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  props.deleteProperty('NEWS_CACHE');
  props.deleteProperty('NEWS_CACHE_TIME');
  props.deleteProperty('IC_NEWS_CACHE');
