  props.deleteProperty('IC_NEWS_CACHE_TIME');
  props.deleteProperty('RSS_NEWS_CACHE');
  props.deleteProperty('RSS_NEWS_CACHE_TIME');
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('News cache cleared (Finnhub + IC + CNBC + Yahoo)! Reopen sidebar to see fresh headlines.');
}

// ==================== IC SLUGS (Investing.com Ticker-to-Path Map) ====================
// Maintains IC Slugs tab with ticker -> investing.com URL path mappings
// Used by MBU for dual-link format: ticker->TradingView, 📊->Investing.com app
// Run resolveNewICSlugs() after adding new tickers to Config

function clearDashboardCaches() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  props.deleteProperty('EARNINGS_WEEK_CACHE');
  props.deleteProperty('EARNINGS_WEEK_TS');
  props.deleteProperty('IC_SLUGS_CACHE');
  props.deleteProperty('EARNINGS_CACHE');
  Logger.log('Cleared: EARNINGS_WEEK_CACHE, EARNINGS_WEEK_TS, IC_SLUGS_CACHE, EARNINGS_CACHE');
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Dashboard caches cleared. Next refresh will pull fresh data.');
}

function resolveNewICSlugs() {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var slugSheet = ss.getSheetByName('IC Slugs');
  
  if (!slugSheet) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Create "IC Slugs" tab first with Ticker | Path headers, then import the CSV.');
    return;
  }
  
  var watchlist = getWatchlist();
  var configTickers = [];
  var seen = {};
  for (var i = 0; i < watchlist.length; i++) {
    var sym = watchlist[i].symbol.toUpperCase().trim();
    if (sym && sym.length <= 6 && /^[A-Z.]+$/.test(sym) && !seen[sym]) {
      configTickers.push(sym);
      seen[sym] = true;
    }
  }
  
  var slugData = slugSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  var existingSlugs = {};
  for (var i = 1; i < slugData.length; i++) {
    existingSlugs[String(slugData[i][0]).trim().toUpperCase()] = true;
  }
  
  var missing = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < configTickers.length; i++) {
    if (!existingSlugs[configTickers[i]]) {
      missing.push(configTickers[i]);
    }
  }
  
  if (missing.length === 0) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('All Config tickers already have IC slugs! (' + Object.keys(existingSlugs).length + ' total)');
    return;
  }
  
  Logger.log('Resolving ' + missing.length + ' new IC slugs: ' + missing.join(', '));
  
  var resolved = [];
  var failed = [];
  
  for (var i = 0; i < missing.length; i++) {
    var slug = _resolveICSlug(missing[i]);
    if (slug) {
      resolved.push([missing[i], slug]);
    } else {
      failed.push(missing[i]);
    }
    Utilities.sleep(500);
  }
  
  if (resolved.length > 0) {
    var startRow = slugSheet.getLastRow() + 1;
    slugSheet.getRange(startRow, 1, resolved.length, 2).setValues(resolved);
    if (slugSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      slugSheet.getRange(2, 1, slugSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 2).sort(1);
    }
  }
  
  var msg = 'Resolved: ' + resolved.length + ' new tickers';
  if (failed.length > 0) {
    msg += '\nFailed (' + failed.length + '): ' + failed.join(', ');
    msg += '\nFailed tickers will use fallback /search/?q=TICKER in MBU';
  }
  Logger.log(msg);
  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().deleteProperty('IC_SLUGS_CACHE'); // Force dashboard to re-read
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(msg);
}

function resolveOneTicker(ticker) {
  ticker = ticker.toUpperCase().trim();
  var slug = _resolveICSlug(ticker);
  
  if (slug) {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var slugSheet = ss.getSheetByName('IC Slugs');
    if (slugSheet) {
      slugSheet.appendRow([ticker, slug]);
      if (slugSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
        slugSheet.getRange(2, 1, slugSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 2).sort(1);
      }
    }
    Logger.log(ticker + ' -> ' + slug);
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(ticker + ' resolved: ' + slug);
    return slug;
  } else {
    Logger.log(ticker + ': not found on Investing.com');
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(ticker + ': not found. Will use fallback URL.');
    return null;
  }
}

function _resolveICSlug(ticker) {
  try {
    var url = 'https://api.investing.com/api/search/v2/search?q=' + encodeURIComponent(ticker);
    var response = trackedFetch(url, {
      headers: {
        'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0',
        'Accept': 'application/json',
        'Origin': 'https://www.investing.com',
        'Referer': 'https://www.investing.com/',
      },
      muteHttpExceptions: true,
    }, 'ic-slug-' + ticker);
    
    if (response.getResponseCode() !== 200) {
      Logger.log(ticker + ': HTTP ' + response.getResponseCode());
      return null;
    }
    
    var data = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
    var quotes = data.quotes || [];
    if (quotes.length === 0) return null;
    
    var US_EXCHANGES = ['NASDAQ', 'NYSE', 'AMEX', 'ARCA', 'BATS', 'NYSEARCA'];
    
    // Pass 1: exact ticker on US exchange
    for (var q = 0; q < quotes.length; q++) {
      if (quotes[q].symbol && quotes[q].symbol.toUpperCase() === ticker && quotes[q].url) {
        var ex = (quotes[q].exchange || '').toUpperCase();
        for (var e = 0; e < US_EXCHANGES.length; e++) {
          if (ex.indexOf(US_EXCHANGES[e]) >= 0) return quotes[q].url;
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Pass 2: exact ticker any exchange
    for (var q = 0; q < quotes.length; q++) {
      if (quotes[q].symbol && quotes[q].symbol.toUpperCase() === ticker && quotes[q].url) {
        return quotes[q].url;
      }
    }
    
    // Pass 3: first equities/etfs result
    for (var q = 0; q < quotes.length; q++) {
      if (quotes[q].url && (quotes[q].url.indexOf('/equities/') >= 0 || quotes[q].url.indexOf('/etfs/') >= 0)) {
        return quotes[q].url;
      }
    }
    
    return null;
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log(ticker + ': Error - ' + e.message);
    return null;
  }
}

// ==================== END IC SLUGS ====================

// Open sidebar docked in spreadsheet
function showSidebar() {
  var html = HtmlService.createHtmlOutput(getTimerHtml())
  .setTitle('V9 Scanner');
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showSidebar(html);
}

// Open sidebar in a new browser window via deployed web app URL
function openSidebarNewWindow() {
  var url = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('WEBAPP_URL') || '';
  if (url) {
    var html = HtmlService.createHtmlOutput(
      '<script>window.open("' + url + '", "_blank"); google.script.host.close();</script>'
    ).setWidth(10).setHeight(10);
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModelessDialog(html, 'Opening...');
  } else {
    // Prompt user to paste URL right here
    var ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
    var resp = ui.prompt('Set Web App URL',
      'Paste your deployed Web App URL below.\n\n' +
      'To get it: Deploy > Manage Deployments > copy the URL.\n' +
      'It starts with https://script.google.com/macros/...',
      ui.ButtonSet.OK_CANCEL);
    if (resp.getSelectedButton() === ui.Button.OK && resp.getResponseText().trim()) {
      var newUrl = resp.getResponseText().trim();
      PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('WEBAPP_URL', newUrl);
      // Now open it
      var html = HtmlService.createHtmlOutput(
        '<script>window.open("' + newUrl + '", "_blank"); google.script.host.close();</script>'
      ).setWidth(10).setHeight(10);
      SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModelessDialog(html, 'Opening...');
    }
  }
}

var INTERVAL=5*60;var remaining=INTERVAL;var knownUpdate=null;var readNews={};var lastGP=null;var breadthHistory=[];var gpHistory=[];
var gpColors={A:"#00C853",B:"#2196F3",C:"#FF9800",D:"#F44336"};

function flashGP(letter){
  var banner=document.getElementById("gpBanner");
  banner.style.background=GP_BG[letter]||"transparent";
  banner.classList.remove("gp-flash");
  void banner.offsetWidth;

function updateGPHistory(letter){
  if(!letter)return;
  renderGPTimeline();
}

function renderGPTimeline(){
  var el=document.getElementById("gpTimelineSection");
  if(gpHistory.length<1){el.innerHTML="";return}
  var W=270,H=44,PAD_L=8,PAD_R=8,BAR_TOP=4,BAR_H=16,LABEL_Y=38;
  var plotW=W-PAD_L-PAD_R;
  var now=Date.now();
  
  // Build 7am-2pm AZ window (AZ = UTC-7, no DST)
  var d=new Date();
  var utcMid=Date.UTC(d.getUTCFullYear(),d.getUTCMonth(),d.getUTCDate(),0,0,0);
  var tMin=utcMid+14*3600000; // 7am AZ = 14:00 UTC
  var tMax=utcMid+21*3600000; // 2pm AZ = 21:00 UTC
  if(now>tMax)tMax=now;
  var tRange=tMax-tMin||1;
  
  function xPos(t){var v=PAD_L+(t-tMin)/tRange*plotW;return Math.max(PAD_L,Math.min(W-PAD_R,v))}
  
  var GP_FILL={A:"#00C853",B:"#2196F3",C:"#FF9800",D:"#F44336"};
  
  // Draw colored blocks for each GP period
  var blocks="";
  for(var i=0;i<gpHistory.length;i++){
    var x1=xPos(gpHistory[i].t);
    var x2=(i<gpHistory.length-1)?xPos(gpHistory[i+1].t):xPos(tMax);
    var w=x2-x1;
    if(w<1)w=1;
    blocks+='<rect x="'+x1.toFixed(1)+'" y="'+BAR_TOP+'" width="'+w.toFixed(1)+'" height="'+BAR_H+'" fill="'+GP_FILL[gpHistory[i].gp]+'" rx="2"/>';
    // Label inside block if wide enough
    if(w>20){
      var tx=x1+w/2;
      blocks+='<text x="'+tx.toFixed(1)+'" y="'+(BAR_TOP+BAR_H/2+4)+'" fill="#fff" font-size="9" font-weight="bold" text-anchor="middle">'+gpHistory[i].gp+'</text>';
    }
  }
  
  // Time axis - hardcoded AZ trading hours
  var timeSvg="";
  var azHours=[{h:7,l:"7a"},{h:8,l:"8a"},{h:9,l:"9a"},{h:10,l:"10a"},{h:11,l:"11a"},{h:12,l:"12p"},{h:13,l:"1p"},{h:14,l:"2p"}];
  for(var hi=0;hi<azHours.length;hi++){
    var hMs=utcMid+(azHours[hi].h+7)*3600000;
    var tx=xPos(hMs);
    if(tx>PAD_L+5&&tx<W-PAD_R-5){
      timeSvg+='<line x1="'+tx.toFixed(1)+'" y1="'+(BAR_TOP+BAR_H)+'" x2="'+tx.toFixed(1)+'" y2="'+(BAR_TOP+BAR_H+4)+'" stroke="#444" stroke-width="0.5"/>';
      timeSvg+='<text x="'+tx.toFixed(1)+'" y="'+LABEL_Y+'" fill="#666" font-size="8" text-anchor="middle">'+azHours[hi].l+'</text>';
    }
  }
  
  // Current time marker
  var nowX=xPos(tMax);
  var markerSvg='<line x1="'+nowX.toFixed(1)+'" y1="'+(BAR_TOP-2)+'" x2="'+nowX.toFixed(1)+'" y2="'+(BAR_TOP+BAR_H+2)+'" stroke="#fff" stroke-width="1.5" opacity="0.7"/>';
  
  // Duration label for current GP
  var currentDur="";
  if(gpHistory.length>0){
    var lastEntry=gpHistory[gpHistory.length-1];
    var durMin=Math.floor((now-lastEntry.t)/60000);
    if(durMin<60)currentDur=durMin+"m";
    else currentDur=Math.floor(durMin/60)+"h "+Math.floor(durMin%60)+"m";
  }
  
  var svg='<svg width="'+W+'" height="'+H+'" viewBox="0 0 '+W+' '+H+'" style="display:block">'
    +blocks+timeSvg+markerSvg
    +'</svg>';
  
  var lastLetter=gpHistory[gpHistory.length-1].gp;
  el.innerHTML='<div class="spark-hdr"><span>\\u{1F3AF} GAMEPLAN</span><span class="spark-val" style="color:'+(GP_FILL[lastLetter]||"#fff")+'">GP-'+lastLetter+' <span style="color:#888;font-size:11px">'+currentDur+'</span></span></div>'+svg;
}

function updateSparkline(score){
  renderSparkline();
}

function renderSparkline(){
  var el=document.getElementById("sparklineSection");
  if(breadthHistory.length<2){el.innerHTML="";return}
  var W=270,H=100,PAD_L=28,PAD_R=8,PAD_T=12,PAD_B=22;
  var plotW=W-PAD_L-PAD_R,plotH=H-PAD_T-PAD_B;
  var vals=breadthHistory.map(function(p){return p.v});
  var mn=Math.min.apply(null,vals);
  var mx=Math.max.apply(null,vals);
  mn=Math.min(mn,-5);mx=Math.max(mx,12);
  var range=mx-mn||1;
  
  // Always show 7am-2pm AZ (AZ = UTC-7, no DST)
  var today=new Date();
  var utcMid=Date.UTC(today.getUTCFullYear(),today.getUTCMonth(),today.getUTCDate(),0,0,0);
  var tMin=utcMid+14*3600000; // 7am AZ = 14:00 UTC
  var tMax=utcMid+21*3600000; // 2pm AZ = 21:00 UTC
  if(Date.now()>tMax)tMax=Date.now();
  var tRange=tMax-tMin||1;
  
  function xPos(t){return PAD_L+(t-tMin)/tRange*plotW}
  function yPos(v){return PAD_T+plotH-(v-mn)/range*plotH}
  
  // GP zone backgrounds
  var zones=[
    {min:9.5,max:mx,color:"rgba(0,200,83,0.08)"},
    {min:3,max:9.5,color:"rgba(33,150,243,0.08)"},
    {min:-3,max:3,color:"rgba(255,152,0,0.08)"},
    {min:mn,max:-3,color:"rgba(244,67,54,0.08)"}
  ];
  var zoneSvg="";
  for(var z=0;z<zones.length;z++){
    var zt=yPos(zones[z].max);
    var zb=yPos(zones[z].min);
    if(zb>zt){
      zoneSvg+='<rect x="'+PAD_L+'" y="'+zt.toFixed(1)+'" width="'+plotW+'" height="'+(zb-zt).toFixed(1)+'" fill="'+zones[z].color+'"/>';
    }
  }
  
  // GP threshold lines with labels
  var thresholds=[{v:9.5,c:"#00C853",l:"A 9.5"},{v:3,c:"#2196F3",l:"B 3"},{v:0,c:"#666",l:"0"},{v:-3,c:"#F44336",l:"D -3"}];
  var threshSvg="";
  for(var t=0;t<thresholds.length;t++){
    var ty=yPos(thresholds[t].v);
    if(ty>=PAD_T&&ty<=PAD_T+plotH){
      threshSvg+='<line x1="'+PAD_L+'" y1="'+ty.toFixed(1)+'" x2="'+(W-PAD_R)+'" y2="'+ty.toFixed(1)+'" stroke="'+thresholds[t].c+'" stroke-width="0.5" stroke-dasharray="3,2" opacity="0.5"/>';
      threshSvg+='<text x="'+(PAD_L-3)+'" y="'+(ty+3).toFixed(1)+'" fill="'+thresholds[t].c+'" font-size="8" text-anchor="end" opacity="0.7">'+thresholds[t].l+'</text>';
    }
  }
  
  // Score axis (left) - min and max
  var axisSvg='<text x="'+(PAD_L-3)+'" y="'+(PAD_T+5)+'" fill="#666" font-size="8" text-anchor="end">'+mx.toFixed(0)+'</text>';
  axisSvg+='<text x="'+(PAD_L-3)+'" y="'+(PAD_T+plotH)+'" fill="#666" font-size="8" text-anchor="end">'+mn.toFixed(0)+'</text>';
  
  // Time axis - hardcoded AZ trading hours
  var timeSvg="";
  var azHours=[{h:7,l:"7a"},{h:8,l:"8a"},{h:9,l:"9a"},{h:10,l:"10a"},{h:11,l:"11a"},{h:12,l:"12p"},{h:13,l:"1p"},{h:14,l:"2p"}];
  for(var hi=0;hi<azHours.length;hi++){
    var hMs=utcMid+(azHours[hi].h+7)*3600000;
    var tx=xPos(hMs);
    if(tx>PAD_L+5&&tx<W-PAD_R-5){
      timeSvg+='<line x1="'+tx.toFixed(1)+'" y1="'+(PAD_T+plotH)+'" x2="'+tx.toFixed(1)+'" y2="'+(PAD_T+plotH+4)+'" stroke="#444" stroke-width="0.5"/>';
      timeSvg+='<text x="'+tx.toFixed(1)+'" y="'+(PAD_T+plotH+14)+'" fill="#666" font-size="8" text-anchor="middle">'+azHours[hi].l+'</text>';
    }
  }
  
  // Build colored line segments (color based on GP zone at each point)
  function gpColor(v){return v>=9.5?"#00C853":v>=3?"#2196F3":v>=-3?"#FF9800":"#F44336"}
  var pathSvg="";
  for(var i=1;i<breadthHistory.length;i++){
    var x1=xPos(breadthHistory[i-1].t).toFixed(1);
    var y1=yPos(breadthHistory[i-1].v).toFixed(1);
    var x2=xPos(breadthHistory[i].t).toFixed(1);
    var y2=yPos(breadthHistory[i].v).toFixed(1);
    var segColor=gpColor(breadthHistory[i].v);
    pathSvg+='<line x1="'+x1+'" y1="'+y1+'" x2="'+x2+'" y2="'+y2+'" stroke="'+segColor+'" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round"/>';
  }
  
  // Current value dot + glow
  var lastV=vals[vals.length-1];
  var dotColor=gpColor(lastV);
  var dotX=xPos(tMax).toFixed(1);
  var dotY=yPos(lastV).toFixed(1);
  var dotSvg='<circle cx="'+dotX+'" cy="'+dotY+'" r="5" fill="'+dotColor+'" opacity="0.3"/>';
  dotSvg+='<circle cx="'+dotX+'" cy="'+dotY+'" r="3" fill="'+dotColor+'"/>';
  
  // Plot border
  var borderSvg='<rect x="'+PAD_L+'" y="'+PAD_T+'" width="'+plotW+'" height="'+plotH+'" fill="none" stroke="#333" stroke-width="0.5"/>';
  
  var svg='<svg width="'+W+'" height="'+H+'" viewBox="0 0 '+W+' '+H+'" style="display:block">'
    +zoneSvg+borderSvg+threshSvg+axisSvg+timeSvg+pathSvg+dotSvg
    +'</svg>';
  
  var scoreColor=gpColor(lastV);
  var arrow=breadthHistory.length>=3?(lastV>breadthHistory[breadthHistory.length-3].v?"\\u25B2":"\\u25BC"):"";
  var arrowColor=arrow==="\\u25B2"?"#4caf50":"#F44336";
  
  el.innerHTML='<div class="spark-hdr"><span>\\u{1F4C8} BREADTH</span><span class="spark-val" style="color:'+scoreColor+'">'+lastV.toFixed(1)+' <span style="color:'+arrowColor+';font-size:11px">'+arrow+'</span></span></div>'+svg;
}

function renderHeatmap(sectorData){
  var el=document.getElementById("heatmapSection");
  if(!sectorData||sectorData.length===0){el.innerHTML="";return}
  var growth=[],defense=[];
  for(var i=0;i<sectorData.length;i++){
    if(sectorData[i].type==='D')defense.push(sectorData[i]);
    else growth.push(sectorData[i]);
  }
  function makeBoxes(arr){
    var h='';
    for(var i=0;i<arr.length;i++){
      var val=parseFloat(arr[i].chg)||0;
      var bg,fg;
      if(val>=1){bg="#00C853";fg="#000"}
      else if(val>0){bg="#2E7D32";fg="#fff"}
      else if(val===0){bg="#333";fg="#888"}
      else if(val>=-1){bg="#c62828";fg="#fff"}
      else{bg="#b71c1c";fg="#fff"}
      h+='<span class="heat-box" style="background:'+bg+';color:'+fg+'" title="'+arr[i].name+": "+(val>=0?"+":"")+val.toFixed(2)+'%">'+arr[i].sym+'<br>'+(val>=0?"+":"")+val.toFixed(1)+'%</span>';
    }
    return h;
  }
  var h='<div class="sec-hdr" style="border-left-color:#E040FB">\\u{1F5FA} SECTOR MAP</div>';
  h+='<div style="font-size:9px;color:#888;margin:2px 0 1px 8px">GROWTH</div><div class="heatmap">'+makeBoxes(growth)+'</div>';
  h+='<div style="font-size:9px;color:#888;margin:4px 0 1px 8px">DEFENSIVE</div><div class="heatmap">'+makeBoxes(defense)+'</div>';
  el.innerHTML=h;
}

function chgClass(s){
  if(!s)return"flat";
  var n=parseFloat(String(s).replace('%',''));
  if(isNaN(n))return"flat";
  return n>0?"pos":n<0?"neg":"flat";
}

function fmtChg(s){
  if(!s)return"";
  var str=String(s);
  var hasPercent=str.indexOf('%')>=0;
  var n=parseFloat(str.replace('%',''));
  if(isNaN(n))return s;
  // If Sheets stripped %, value will be tiny decimal like 0.0042 instead of 0.42
  if(!hasPercent&&Math.abs(n)<0.5&&n!==0) n=n*100;
  var pct=n.toFixed(2)+"%";
  return n>0?"+"+pct:pct;
}

function fmtBreadth(sym,val){
  // Color-code breadth values
  var n=parseFloat(val);
  if(isNaN(n))return'<span class="breadth-val flat">'+val+'</span>';
  var cls="flat";
  if(sym==="$TICK"){cls=n>300?"pos":n<-300?"neg":"flat"}
  else if(sym==="$ADD"||sym==="$ADQD"){cls=n>500?"pos":n<-500?"neg":"flat"}
  else if(sym.indexOf("VOLD")>=0||sym.indexOf("VOLQD")>=0){cls=n>0?"pos":n<0?"neg":"flat"}
  else if(sym==="$VIX"){cls=n<18?"pos":n>25?"neg":"flat"}
  return'<span class="breadth-val '+cls+'">'+val+'</span>';
}

function renderAiBrief(brief){
  var el=document.getElementById("aiBriefSection");
  if(!brief){el.innerHTML="";return}
  var h='<div class="ai-hdr">\\u{1F9E0} CATALYST BRIEF</div>';
  h+='<div class="ai-brief">'+brief.replace(/</g,"&lt;").replace(/>/g,"&gt;")+'</div>';
  el.innerHTML=h;
}

var NEWS_SOURCE_BLACKLIST={"marketwatch":1};

function getNewsTags(headline, related){
  var tags=[];
  for(var t=0;t<NEWS_TAGS.length;t++){
    if(NEWS_TAGS[t].rx.test(headline)){
      tags.push(NEWS_TAGS[t]);
    }
  }
  var tickers=[];
  var seen={};
  var companyMap={
    "apple":"AAPL","microsoft":"MSFT","google":"GOOG","alphabet":"GOOG","amazon":"AMZN",
    "meta":"META","facebook":"META","nvidia":"NVDA","tesla":"TSLA","netflix":"NFLX",
    "amd":"AMD","intel":"INTC","broadcom":"AVGO","qualcomm":"QCOM","tsmc":"TSM",
    "asml":"ASML","micron":"MU","palantir":"PLTR","salesforce":"CRM","adobe":"ADBE",
    "coinbase":"COIN","jpmorgan":"JPM","goldman":"GS","morgan stanley":"MS",
    "bank of america":"BAC","wells fargo":"WFC","citigroup":"C","disney":"DIS",
    "boeing":"BA","caterpillar":"CAT","exxon":"XOM","chevron":"CVX",
    "walmart":"WMT","costco":"COST","home depot":"HD","target":"TGT",
    "uber":"UBER","airbnb":"ABNB","spotify":"SPOT","snap":"SNAP",
    "crowdstrike":"CRWD","snowflake":"SNOW","datadog":"DDOG","shopify":"SHOP",
    "arm holdings":"ARM","super micro":"SMCI","supermicro":"SMCI",
    "eli lilly":"LLY","novo nordisk":"NVO","unitedhealth":"UNH",
    "berkshire":"BRK.B","warren buffett":"BRK.B"
  };
  if(related){
    var rel=related.split(",");
    for(var r=0;r<rel.length;r++){
      var tk=rel[r].trim().toUpperCase();
      if(tk&&tk.length>=1&&tk.length<=5&&!seen[tk]){seen[tk]=1;tickers.push(tk)}
    }
  }
  // Find $TICKER patterns
  var dRx=new RegExp("\\\\$([A-Z]{1,5})","g");
  var dm=headline.match(dRx);
  if(dm){
    for(var d=0;d<dm.length;d++){
      var tk=dm[d].replace("$","");
      if(!seen[tk]){seen[tk]=1;tickers.push(tk)}
    }
  }
  // Find uppercase tickers (3-5 chars to reduce false positives)
  var skip={"THE":1,"AND":1,"FOR":1,"ARE":1,"BUT":1,"NOT":1,"YOU":1,"ALL":1,"CAN":1,"HAS":1,"HER":1,"WAS":1,"ONE":1,"OUR":1,"OUT":1,"NEW":1,"NOW":1,"WAY":1,"MAY":1,"SAY":1,"SHE":1,"TWO":1,"HOW":1,"ITS":1,"LET":1,"PUT":1,"TOO":1,"USE":1,"CEO":1,"IPO":1,"GDP":1,"CPI":1,"PPI":1,"PCE":1,"FED":1,"SEC":1,"USA":1,"NYSE":1,"ETF":1,"DOJ":1,"FTC":1,"NATO":1,"OPEC":1,"IMF":1,"WHO":1,"FBI":1};
  var words=headline.split(/[^A-Za-z]+/);
  for(var w=0;w<words.length;w++){
    var wd=words[w];
    if(wd.length>=2&&wd.length<=5&&wd===wd.toUpperCase()&&/^[A-Z]+$/.test(wd)&&!skip[wd]&&!seen[wd]){
      seen[wd]=1;tickers.push(wd);
    }
  }
  // Check company names
  var lower=headline.toLowerCase();
  var keys=Object.keys(companyMap);
  for(var c=0;c<keys.length;c++){
    if(lower.indexOf(keys[c])>=0){
      var tk=companyMap[keys[c]];
      if(!seen[tk]){seen[tk]=1;tickers.push(tk)}
    }
  }
  return{tags:tags,tickers:tickers};
}

var _positionTickers=[];
function renderNews(news){
  var el=document.getElementById("newsSection");
  if(!news||news.length===0){
    el.innerHTML='<div class="news-hdr">\\u{1F4F0} NEWS</div><div style="padding:8px;color:#666;font-size:12px">No recent headlines</div>';
    return;
  }
  var posItems=[];
  var mktItems=[];
  for(var i=0;i<news.length;i++){
    var n=news[i];
    var ago="";
    if(n.time){
      var mins=Math.floor((Date.now()/1000-n.time)/60);
      if(mins<1)ago="just now";
      else if(mins<60)ago=mins+"m ago";
      else{var hrs=Math.floor(mins/60);ago=hrs+"h "+Math.floor(mins%60)+"m ago";}
    }
    var safeUrl=n.url.replace(/"/g,"&quot;");
    var result=getNewsTags(n.headline, n.related);
    var tags=result.tags;
    var tickers=result.tickers;
    if(tags.length===0) continue;
    if(NEWS_SOURCE_BLACKLIST[(n.source||"").toLowerCase()]) continue;
    var isStale=n.time?(Math.floor(Date.now()/1000-n.time)>10800):false;
    if(isStale) continue;
    var tagHtml="";
    if(tags.length>0||tickers.length>0){
      tagHtml='<div class="news-tags">';
      for(var t=0;t<tags.length;t++){
        tagHtml+='<span class="news-tag" style="background:'+tags[t].bg+';color:'+tags[t].fg+'">'+tags[t].label+'</span>';
      }
      for(var k=0;k<tickers.length&&k<5;k++){
        tagHtml+='<span class="news-tag" style="background:#1a1a2e;color:#4caf50;border:1px solid #4caf50">$'+tickers[k]+'</span>';
      }
      tagHtml+='</div>';
    }
    // Check if headline relates to a My Positions ticker
    var isPosition=false;
    for(var p=0;p<_positionTickers.length;p++){
      var pt=_positionTickers[p];
      if(!pt)continue;
      for(var tk=0;tk<tickers.length;tk++){
        if(tickers[tk]===pt){isPosition=true;break;}
      }
      if(isPosition)break;
      // Also check headline for ticker mention
      var ptRx=new RegExp('(^|[\\s(])'+pt+'([\\s).,!?:;]|$)','i');
      if(ptRx.test(n.headline)){isPosition=true;break;}
    }
    var badgeColors={"IC":"#FF6D00","FH":"#1565C0","CN":"#00838F","YF":"#6A1B9A"};
    var badgeLabel=n.feed||"FH";
    var badgeBg=badgeColors[badgeLabel]||"#555";
    var feedBadge='<span style="background:'+badgeBg+';color:#fff;font-size:8px;padding:1px 4px;border-radius:2px;margin-right:4px;font-weight:bold">'+badgeLabel+'</span>';
    var itemObj={html:'',url:safeUrl};
    var ih='<div class="news-item'+(isPosition?' pos-news':'')+'" data-url="'+safeUrl+'">';
    ih+='<span class="news-hl">'+n.headline+'</span>';
    ih+='<div class="news-meta">'+feedBadge+'<span class="news-src">'+n.source+'</span><span class="news-time">'+ago+'</span></div>';
    ih+=tagHtml;
    ih+='</div>';
    itemObj.html=ih;
    if(isPosition){posItems.push(itemObj);}else{mktItems.push(itemObj);}
  }
  var h='';
  if(posItems.length>0){
    h+='<div class="news-hdr" style="color:#4caf50">\\u{1F4CC} MY POSITIONS ('+posItems.length+')</div>';
    for(var pi=0;pi<posItems.length;pi++) h+=posItems[pi].html;
  }
  h+='<div class="news-hdr">\\u{1F4F0} MARKET NEWS'+(mktItems.length>0?' ('+mktItems.length+')':'')+'</div>';
  for(var mi=0;mi<mktItems.length;mi++) h+=mktItems[mi].html;
  el.innerHTML=h;
  var items=el.querySelectorAll(".news-item");
  for(var j=0;j<items.length;j++){
    if(readNews[items[j].getAttribute("data-url")])items[j].classList.add("read");
    items[j].addEventListener("click",function(){
      var u=this.getAttribute("data-url");
      if(u){window.open(u,"_blank");this.classList.add("read");readNews[u]=1}
    });
  }
}

function renderMarket(m,breadthScore,sectorPts,leader,lagger){
  if(!m)return;
  var el=document.getElementById("marketData");
  var h="";
  
  var order=["BENCHMARKS","FUTURES","BREADTH DETAIL","INTERNALS","GROWTH SECTORS","DEFENSIVE SECTORS","INTERMARKET RATIOS","COMMODITIES","INVERSE ETFs (GP-D)"];
  for(var s=0;s<order.length;s++){
    var sec=order[s];
    var items=m[sec];
    if(!items||items.length===0)continue;
    h+='<div class="sec-hdr">'+sec+'</div>';
    for(var i=0;i<items.length;i++){
      var it=items[i];
      if(sec==="BREADTH DETAIL"){
        h+='<div class="mkt-row"><span class="sym">'+it.sym+'</span>'+fmtBreadth(it.sym,it.val)+'</div>';
      } else if(sec==="INTERNALS"){
        h+='<div class="mkt-row"><span class="sym">'+it.sym+'</span>'+fmtBreadth(it.sym,it.val)+'</div>';
      } else if(sec==="GROWTH SECTORS"||sec==="DEFENSIVE SECTORS"){
        // Sectors: val may be "0.42%" or 0.0042 (Sheets strips %)
        var rawVal=String(it.val);
        var pctN;
        if(rawVal.indexOf('%')>=0){
          pctN=parseFloat(rawVal.replace('%',''));
        } else {
          pctN=parseFloat(rawVal);
          // If Sheets converted "0.42%" to 0.0042, it'll be tiny — multiply back
          if(!isNaN(pctN)&&Math.abs(pctN)<1&&rawVal.indexOf('.')==1) pctN=pctN*100;
        }
        var sCls=isNaN(pctN)?"flat":pctN>0?"pos":pctN<0?"neg":"flat";
        var sDisp=isNaN(pctN)?rawVal:pctN.toFixed(2)+"%";
        var udCls=it.chg==="UP"?"pos":it.chg==="DN"?"neg":"flat";
        h+='<div class="mkt-row"><span class="sym">'+it.sym+'</span><span class="mkt-val '+sCls+'">'+sDisp+'</span><span class="mkt-chg '+udCls+'">'+it.chg+'</span></div>';
      } else if(sec==="INTERMARKET RATIOS"){
        var cls=chgClass(it.chg);
        var chgDisplay=fmtChg(it.chg);
        h+='<div class="mkt-row"><span class="sym">'+it.sym+'</span><span class="mkt-val" style="font-size:11px">'+it.val+'</span><span class="mkt-chg '+cls+'">'+chgDisplay+'</span></div>';
      } else {
        var cls=chgClass(it.chg);
        var chgDisplay=fmtChg(it.chg);
        h+='<div class="mkt-row"><span class="sym">'+it.sym+'</span><span class="mkt-val">'+it.val+'</span><span class="mkt-chg '+cls+'">'+chgDisplay+'</span></div>';
      }
    }
    if(sec==="BREADTH DETAIL"&&(breadthScore!==undefined)){
      var scoreN=parseFloat(breadthScore)||0;
      var scoreCls=scoreN>=9.5?"pos":scoreN>=3?"":"flat";
      if(scoreN<=-3)scoreCls="neg";
      else if(scoreN<3)scoreCls="neg";
      h+='<div class="mkt-row score-row"><span class="sym" style="color:#fff">BREADTH</span><span class="mkt-chg '+scoreCls+'">'+breadthScore+'</span><span class="sym" style="color:#fff">SECTOR</span><span class="mkt-chg">'+sectorPts+'</span></div>';
    }
    if(sec==="DEFENSIVE SECTORS"&&leader){
      h+='<div class="summary"><span class="pos">\\u25B2 '+leader+'</span> &nbsp; <span class="neg">\\u25BC '+lagger+'</span></div>';
    }
  }
  el.innerHTML=h;
}

function poll(){
  google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(function(r){
    if(!r)return;
    var el=document.getElementById("countdown");
    if(!r.enabled){
      el.textContent="--:--";el.style.color="#666";remaining=0;
    } else if(r.updated){
      if(knownUpdate!==r.updated){knownUpdate=r.updated;remaining=INTERVAL}
      else{var e=Math.floor((Date.now()-parseInt(r.updated,10))/1000);if(e<600){remaining=Math.max(0,INTERVAL-e)}else{remaining=0}}
    }
    if(r.gpLetter){
      var g=document.getElementById("gp");g.textContent="GP-"+r.gpLetter;g.style.color=gpColors[r.gpLetter]||"#fff";
      var banner=document.getElementById("gpBanner");banner.style.background=GP_BG[r.gpLetter]||"transparent";
      if(lastGP&&lastGP!==r.gpLetter)flashGP(r.gpLetter);
      lastGP=r.gpLetter;
      updateGPHistory(r.gpLetter);
    }
    var p=document.getElementById("phase");
    var ph=r.phase||"OFF";
    p.textContent=phaseLabels[ph]||ph;
    p.style.background=phaseColors[ph]||"#333";
    p.style.color="#fff";
    var s5=document.getElementById("s5");
    s5.textContent=r.enabled?"ON":"OFF";
    s5.style.color=r.enabled?"#4caf50":"#F44336";
    var s1=document.getElementById("s1");
    s1.textContent=r.marketEnabled?"ON":"OFF";
    s1.style.color=r.marketEnabled?"#4caf50":"#F44336";
    var s30=document.getElementById("s30");
    var f=document.getElementById("fullscan");
    if(r.fullEnabled){
      s30.textContent="ON";s30.style.color="#4caf50";
      if(r.fullScanIn>0){f.textContent="\\u27F3"+r.fullScanIn+"m";f.style.color="#2196F3"}
      else if(r.fullScanIn===0){f.textContent="\\u27F3NOW";f.style.color="#00C853"}
      else{f.textContent=""}
    }else{
      s30.textContent="OFF";s30.style.color="#F44336";f.textContent="";
    }
    var q=document.getElementById("quota");
    var c=r.quotaCount||0;
    q.textContent="\\u{1F4E1} "+(c>999?(c/1000).toFixed(1)+"K":c)+" / 20K";
    q.style.color=c>16000?"#F44336":c>12000?"#FF9800":"#00BCD4";
    // Load persisted history from server (replaces in-memory only)
    if(r.history&&r.history.length>0){
      breadthHistory=[];gpHistory=[];var lastGpEntry=null;
      for(var hi=0;hi<r.history.length;hi++){
        var pt=r.history[hi];
        breadthHistory.push({t:pt.t,v:pt.v});
        if(!lastGpEntry||lastGpEntry.gp!==pt.gp){
          gpHistory.push({t:pt.t,gp:pt.gp});
          lastGpEntry=pt;
        }
      }
    }
    if(r.breadthScore!==undefined)updateSparkline(r.breadthScore);
    try{renderHeatmap(r.sectorHeatmap)}catch(e){}
    try{renderAiBrief(r.aiBrief)}catch(e){document.getElementById("aiBriefSection").innerHTML='<div style="color:red;font-size:10px">Brief error: '+e.message+'</div>'}
    try{if(r.positionTickers)_positionTickers=r.positionTickers}catch(e){}
    try{renderNews(r.news)}catch(e){document.getElementById("newsSection").innerHTML='<div style="color:red;font-size:10px">News error: '+e.message+'</div>'}
    try{renderMarket(r.market,r.breadthScore,r.sectorPts,r.leader,r.lagger)}catch(e){document.getElementById("marketData").innerHTML='<div style="color:red;font-size:10px">Market error: '+e.message+'</div>'}
  }).getTimerState();
}
poll();
setInterval(function(){
  var el=document.getElementById("countdown");
  if(!el)return;
  if(remaining<=0){el.textContent="\\u27F3";el.style.color="#2196F3";return}
  var m=Math.floor(remaining/60);var s=remaining%60;
  el.textContent=m+":"+(s<10?"0":"")+s;
  if(remaining<=10)el.style.color="#F44336";
  else if(remaining<=30)el.style.color="#FF9800";
  else el.style.color="#4caf50";
  remaining--;
},1000);
setInterval(poll,3000);
</script>
  `;
}

function doGet(e) {
  var mode = (e && e.parameter && e.parameter.mode) ? e.parameter.mode : 'html';
  
  if (mode === 'json') {
    // Return pure JSON — must use ContentService (no HtmlService in this path)
    var data = getTimerState();
    return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(data))
      .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
  }
  
  if (mode === 'dashboard') {
    // Return full dashboard data including Claude narrative
    var data = getDashboardData();
    return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(data))
      .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
  }
  
  if (mode === 'pretrade') {
    var sym = (e.parameter.symbol || '').toUpperCase();
    var data = getPreTradeData(sym);
    return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(data))
      .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
  }
  
  if (mode === 'scorecard') {
    var scParams = {
      symbol: e.parameter.symbol || '',
      side: e.parameter.side || 'LONG',
      setupType: e.parameter.setup || 'Momentum',
      stop: e.parameter.stop || '0',
      target: e.parameter.target || '0',
      accountId: e.parameter.account || ''
    };
    var scResult = evaluateScorecard(scParams);
    var szResult = computePositionSize({
      gameplan: scResult.gameplan || 'C',
      currentPrice: parseFloat(e.parameter.price || '0'),
      stop: parseFloat(e.parameter.stop || '0'),
      target: parseFloat(e.parameter.target || '0'),
      ivr: parseFloat(e.parameter.ivr || '0'),
      beta: parseFloat(e.parameter.beta || '1'),
      side: e.parameter.side || 'LONG',
      accountId: e.parameter.account || '',
      setupType: e.parameter.setup || 'Momentum',
      spyEM: parseFloat(e.parameter.spyem || '0')
    });
    var combined = { scorecard: scResult, sizing: szResult };
    return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(combined))
      .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
  }
  
  if (mode === 'activesetups') {
    var setups = getActiveSetups();
    return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify({ setups: setups, count: setups.length }))
      .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
  }
  
  if (mode === 'debug') {
    var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var debug = {
      narrative: props.getProperty('DASHBOARD_NARRATIVE') || '(empty)',
      timestamp: props.getProperty('DASHBOARD_TIMESTAMP') || '(empty)',
      session: props.getProperty('DASHBOARD_SESSION') || '(empty)',
      narrativeLength: (props.getProperty('DASHBOARD_NARRATIVE') || '').length
    };
    return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(debug, null, 2))
      .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
  }
  
  // Default: serve full sidebar HTML
  var html = HtmlService.createHtmlOutput(getTimerHtml())
    .setTitle('V9 Scanner Dashboard')
    .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
  return html;
}

// Dedicated JSON endpoint via POST (avoids Apps Script HTML wrapping issue)
function doPost(e) {
  // Check for trade management actions
  try {
    var body = e && e.postData ? JSON.parse(e.postData.contents) : {};
    if (body.action === 'plantrade') {
      var result = logPlannedTrade(body);
      return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(result))
        .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
    }
  } catch(ex) {}
  
  var data = getTimerState();
  return ContentService.createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(data))
    .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
}

// ==================== 1-MIN MARKET TAB REFRESH ====================
// Standalone function on its own 1-min trigger.
// Only fetches core market symbols (~40) and writes Market tab.
// Does NOT touch Watchlist, earnings, sectors, or Pre-Market tabs.
// Cost: ~1 UrlFetch per minute (~420/day).

function updateMarketTab() {
  // Check if enabled
  if (!isMarketRefreshEnabled()) return;
  
  // Market hours + weekend gate (using reliable Utilities.formatDate for AZ timezone)
  var now = new Date();
  var azHour = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'H'), 10);
  var azMinute = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'm'), 10);
  var azDow = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'u'), 10); // 1=Mon...7=Sun
  var azMin = azHour * 60 + azMinute;
  
  // Weekend — skip entirely (zero cost)
  if (azDow >= 6) return; // 6=Sat, 7=Sun
  
  // Only run during market-relevant hours (PRE_MARKET through AFTER_HOURS)
  if (azMin < PHASE_CONFIG.PRE_MARKET.start || azMin >= PHASE_CONFIG.AFTER_HOURS.end) return;
  
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var breadthSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Market');
  if (!breadthSheet) {
    breadthSheet = ss.insertSheet('Market');
  }
  
  // Collect all core symbols needed for Market tab
  var ratioSymbols = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < RATIO_PAIRS.length; i++) {
    if (ratioSymbols.indexOf(RATIO_PAIRS[i][1]) < 0) ratioSymbols.push(RATIO_PAIRS[i][1]);
    if (ratioSymbols.indexOf(RATIO_PAIRS[i][2]) < 0) ratioSymbols.push(RATIO_PAIRS[i][2]);
  }
  
  var coreSymbols = [].concat(
    BREADTH_SYMBOLS, GROWTH_SECTORS, DEFENSIVE_SECTORS,
    [BENCHMARK], INVERSE_ETFS, ratioSymbols,
    BENCHMARKS.map(function(i) { return i[0]; }),
    INTERNALS.map(function(i) { return i[0]; }),
    COMMODITIES.map(function(i) { return i[0]; }),
    FUTURES.map(function(i) { return i[0]; })
  );
  var seen = {};
  var uniqueCore = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < coreSymbols.length; i++) {
    if (!seen[coreSymbols[i]]) {
      seen[coreSymbols[i]] = true;
      uniqueCore.push(coreSymbols[i]);
    }
  }
  
  // Single API call for all ~40 symbols
  var coreQuotes = tsQuotes(uniqueCore);
  
  var mktMap = {};
  for (var i = 0; i < coreQuotes.length; i++) mktMap[coreQuotes[i].Symbol] = coreQuotes[i];
  
  var breadthQuotes = coreQuotes.filter(function(q) { return BREADTH_SYMBOLS.indexOf(q.Symbol) >= 0; });
  var allSectors = GROWTH_SECTORS.concat(DEFENSIVE_SECTORS);
  var sectorQuotes = coreQuotes.filter(function(q) { return allSectors.indexOf(q.Symbol) >= 0; });
  var spyQuote = mktMap[BENCHMARK] || {};
  var inverseQuotes = coreQuotes.filter(function(q) { return INVERSE_ETFS.indexOf(q.Symbol) >= 0; });
  
  var breadth = scoreBreadth(breadthQuotes);
  var sectors = scoreSectors(sectorQuotes);
  var totalBreadth = breadth.score + sectors.sectorPts;
  var gameplan = getGameplan(totalBreadth);
  
  // Build Market sheet data (same format as main updateSheet)
  var marketData = [
    ['V9 CONFLUENCE SCANNER', '', '', new Date()],
    ['', '', '', ''],
    ['GAMEPLAN', 'Score', 'Adj %', 'Action'],
    ['GP-' + gameplan.gp, totalBreadth.toFixed(1), gameplan.adjPct + '%', gameplan.action + ' | ' + gameplan.sizing],
    ['', '', '', ''],
    ['BENCHMARKS', 'Last', 'Change %', 'Description'],
  ];
  
  for (var i = 0; i < BENCHMARKS.length; i++) {
    var sym = BENCHMARKS[i][0];
    var q = mktMap[sym];
    if (q) {
      var pct = parseFloat(q.NetChangePct || 0);
      marketData.push([sym, q.Last, pct.toFixed(2) + '%', BENCHMARKS[i][1]]);
    } else {
      marketData.push([sym, 'N/A', '', BENCHMARKS[i][1]]);
    }
  }
  
  marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
  marketData.push(['FUTURES', 'Last', 'Change %', 'Description']);
  for (var i = 0; i < FUTURES.length; i++) {
    var sym = FUTURES[i][0];
    var q = mktMap[sym];
    if (q) {
      var pct = parseFloat(q.NetChangePct || 0);
      marketData.push([sym, q.Last, pct.toFixed(2) + '%', FUTURES[i][1]]);
    } else {
      marketData.push([sym, 'N/A', '', FUTURES[i][1]]);
    }
  }
  
  marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
  marketData.push(['BREADTH DETAIL', 'Value', 'Points', 'Description']);
  marketData.push(['$TICK', breadth.tick, '', 'NYSE tick — net upticks vs downticks, >+700 strong buying']);
  marketData.push(['$ADD', breadth.add, '', 'NYSE A/D — advancing vs declining issues, >+1000 broad strength']);
  marketData.push(['$ADQD', breadth.adqd, '', 'NASDAQ A/D — tech/growth breadth, >+1000 strong']);
  marketData.push(['$VOLD (scaled)', breadth.vold.toFixed(0), '', 'NYSE up/down volume — confirms breadth with volume']);
  marketData.push(['$VOLQD (scaled)', breadth.volqd.toFixed(0), '', 'NASDAQ up/down volume — tech volume confirmation']);
  marketData.push(['$VIX', breadth.vix.toFixed(2), '', 'Fear gauge — <15 complacent, 15-18 normal, >25 elevated']);
  marketData.push(['Breadth Score', breadth.score, 'Sector Pts', sectors.sectorPts]);
  marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
  
  if (INTERNALS.length > 0) {
    marketData.push(['INTERNALS', 'Value', '', 'Description']);
    for (var i = 0; i < INTERNALS.length; i++) {
      var sym = INTERNALS[i][0];
      var q = mktMap[sym];
      marketData.push([sym, q ? q.Last : 'N/A', '', INTERNALS[i][1]]);
    }
    var addVal = parseFloat(breadth.add) || 0;
    var adqdVal = parseFloat(breadth.adqd) || 0;
    var addRatio = adqdVal !== 0 ? (addVal / adqdVal).toFixed(3) : 'N/A';
    marketData.push(['ADD/ADQD', addRatio, '', 'NYSE vs NASDAQ breadth — >1 NYSE leading, <1 NASDAQ leading, divergence = narrow leadership']);
    marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
  }
  
  if (RATIO_PAIRS.length > 0) {
    marketData.push(['INTERMARKET RATIOS', 'Ratio', 'Chg%', 'What It Tells You']);
    for (var i = 0; i < RATIO_PAIRS.length; i++) {
      var rp = RATIO_PAIRS[i];
      var numQ = mktMap[rp[1]];
      var denQ = mktMap[rp[2]];
      if (numQ && denQ) {
        var numLast = parseFloat(numQ.Last || 0);
        var denLast = parseFloat(denQ.Last || 1);
        var numPrev = parseFloat(numQ.PreviousClose || numLast);
        var denPrev = parseFloat(denQ.PreviousClose || denLast);
        var ratio = denLast > 0 ? (numLast / denLast) : 0;
        var prevRatio = denPrev > 0 ? (numPrev / denPrev) : 0;
        var ratioPctChg = prevRatio > 0 ? ((ratio - prevRatio) / prevRatio * 100) : 0;
        marketData.push([rp[0], ratio.toFixed(4), ratioPctChg.toFixed(2) + '%', rp[3] || '']);
      } else {
        marketData.push([rp[0], 'N/A', '', rp[3] || '']);
      }
    }
    marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
  }
  
  marketData.push(['COMMODITIES', 'Last', 'Change %', 'What It Tells You']);
  for (var i = 0; i < COMMODITIES.length; i++) {
    var sym = COMMODITIES[i][0];
    var q = mktMap[sym];
    if (q) {
      var pct = parseFloat(q.NetChangePct || 0);
      marketData.push([sym, q.Last, pct.toFixed(2) + '%', COMMODITIES[i][1]]);
    } else {
      marketData.push([sym, 'N/A', '', COMMODITIES[i][1]]);
    }
  }
  marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
  
  marketData.push(['GROWTH SECTORS', 'Change %', '', sectors.growthGreen + '/8 growth green']);
  for (var i = 0; i < GROWTH_SECTORS.length; i++) {
    var pct = sectors.sectorData[GROWTH_SECTORS[i]] || 0;
    marketData.push([GROWTH_SECTORS[i], pct.toFixed(2) + '%', pct > 0 ? 'UP' : 'DN', SECTOR_INFO[GROWTH_SECTORS[i]] || '']);
  }
  
  marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
  marketData.push(['DEFENSIVE SECTORS', 'Change %', '', sectors.defGreen + '/5 green']);
  for (var i = 0; i < DEFENSIVE_SECTORS.length; i++) {
    var pct = sectors.sectorData[DEFENSIVE_SECTORS[i]] || 0;
    marketData.push([DEFENSIVE_SECTORS[i], pct.toFixed(2) + '%', pct > 0 ? 'UP' : 'DN', SECTOR_INFO[DEFENSIVE_SECTORS[i]] || '']);
  }
  
  marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
  marketData.push(['Leader', sectors.leader, sectors.leaderPct.toFixed(2) + '%', '']);
  marketData.push(['Lagger', sectors.lagger, sectors.laggerPct.toFixed(2) + '%', '']);
  
  marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
  marketData.push(['INVERSE ETFs (GP-D)', 'Last', 'Change %', '']);
  for (var i = 0; i < inverseQuotes.length; i++) {
    marketData.push([inverseQuotes[i].Symbol, inverseQuotes[i].Last, (parseFloat(inverseQuotes[i].NetChangePct || 0)).toFixed(2) + '%', '']);
  }

  // ── INSTITUTIONAL PULSE (appended after Inverse ETFs) ──
  var _pulseStartRow = 0;
  var _pulseWrapIdxs = [];
  try {
    var pulseRows = _buildPulseRows();
    if (pulseRows && pulseRows.length > 0) {
      marketData.push(['', '', '', '']);
      // _pulseStartRow is 1-based sheet row of FIRST pulse row (after spacer)
      // marketData.length is now spacer row index, so +1 = next row = first pulse row
      _pulseStartRow = marketData.length + 1;
      _pulseWrapIdxs = pulseRows._wrapIdxs || [];
      for (var pi = 0; pi < pulseRows.length; pi++) {
        marketData.push(pulseRows[pi]);
      }
    }
  } catch(pe) {
    Logger.log('PULSE append error: ' + pe);
  }
  
  // Write ONLY columns A-D (preserve economic calendar in F-M)
  breadthSheet.getRange(1, 1, breadthSheet.getLastRow() || 1, 4).clearContent();
  // Clear formats only in A-D area
  breadthSheet.getRange(1, 1, breadthSheet.getLastRow() || 1, 4).setBackground(null).setFontColor(null).setFontWeight('normal').setFontSize(10);
  breadthSheet.getRange(1, 1, marketData.length, 4).setValues(marketData);
  formatMarketTab(breadthSheet, marketData.length, gameplan.gp);

  // Narrative rows: text in col D, wrap, fixed height
  if (_pulseWrapIdxs && _pulseWrapIdxs.length > 0) {
    for (var wi = 0; wi < _pulseWrapIdxs.length; wi++) {
      var wrapSheetRow = _pulseStartRow + _pulseWrapIdxs[wi];
      breadthSheet.getRange(wrapSheetRow, 4)
        .setWrap(true)
        .setWrapStrategy(SpreadsheetApp.WrapStrategy.WRAP)
        .setFontSize(9)
        .setFontColor('#000000')
        .setFontStyle('normal')
        .setVerticalAlignment('top');
      breadthSheet.setRowHeight(wrapSheetRow, 52);
    }
  }
  
  // Update market-specific timestamp (NOT lastUpdateTime which is for the 5-min scanner timer)
  var mktProps = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  mktProps.setProperty('lastMarketUpdateTime', Date.now().toString());
  
  // Record breadth & GP history for charts
  try {
    var histKey = 'BREADTH_GP_HISTORY';
    var histRaw = mktProps.getProperty(histKey) || '[]';
    var hist = JSON.parse(histRaw);
    // Clear if from a different day (AZ midnight = 07:00 UTC)
    var nowUtc = new Date();
    var azToday = new Date(nowUtc.getTime() - 7 * 3600000);
    var azDateStr = azToday.getFullYear() + '-' + String(azToday.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0') + '-' + String(azToday.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
    if (hist.length > 0 && hist[0].d !== azDateStr) hist = [];
    hist.push({ d: azDateStr, t: Date.now(), v: parseFloat(totalBreadth.toFixed(1)), gp: gameplan.gp });
    // Cap at 500 entries (~8 hrs at 1-min intervals)
    if (hist.length > 500) hist = hist.slice(hist.length - 500);
    mktProps.setProperty(histKey, JSON.stringify(hist));
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('History record error: ' + e.message);
  }
  
  // ── SPARKLINE CACHE ──
  try {
    _updateSparkCache(ss, azHour, azMinute);
    _updateVolToday(ss, azHour, azMinute);
  } catch(sparkErr) {
    Logger.log('Spark cache error: ' + sparkErr.message);
  }
}

// ═══════ SPARKLINE INTRADAY CACHE (_Spark tab) ═══════
// Layout: Row 1 = ['slot', ticker1, ticker2, ...]  (header)
//         Row 2 = [450, 316.50, 371.08, ...]       (7:30am = minute 450)
//         Row 3 = [455, 316.80, 371.20, ...]       (7:35am)
//         ...up to row 79 (2:00pm = minute 840, 78 slots at 5-min intervals)
// Cleared at market open each day. All watchlist tickers tracked.

var SPARK_INTERVAL = 5; // minutes between samples
var SPARK_START = 450 - _getMarketOffset(); // 7:30 (EST) or 6:30 (EDT) AZ
var SPARK_END = 840 - _getMarketOffset();   // 2:00 (EST) or 1:00 (EDT) AZ
var SPARK_SLOTS = Math.floor((SPARK_END - SPARK_START) / SPARK_INTERVAL) + 1; // 79 slots

function _updateSparkCache(ss, azHour, azMinute) {
  var azMin = azHour * 60 + azMinute;
  // Only during market window
  if (azMin < SPARK_START || azMin > SPARK_END) return;
  
  // Only on 5-min boundaries (±1 min tolerance for trigger drift)
  if (azMinute % SPARK_INTERVAL > 1 && azMinute % SPARK_INTERVAL < (SPARK_INTERVAL - 1)) return;
  
  var slotIdx = Math.round((azMin - SPARK_START) / SPARK_INTERVAL); // 0-based slot
  if (slotIdx < 0 || slotIdx >= SPARK_SLOTS) return;
  
  var sparkSheet = ss.getSheetByName('_Spark');
  
  // Read watchlist tickers and prices
  var wlSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
  if (!wlSheet) return;
  var wlData = wlSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  var startRow = -1;
  for (var i = 0; i < wlData.length; i++) {
    if (String(wlData[i][3]).trim() === 'Ticker') { startRow = i + 1; break; }
  }
  if (startRow < 0) return;
  
  // Collect all tickers and their current prices
  var tickers = [], prices = {};
  for (var i = startRow; i < wlData.length; i++) {
    var tk = String(wlData[i][3] || '').trim();
    if (!tk || !/^[A-Z]{1,5}$/.test(tk)) continue;
    var price = parseFloat(wlData[i][4]) || 0;
    if (price > 0 && tickers.indexOf(tk) < 0) {
      tickers.push(tk);
      prices[tk] = price;
    }
  }
  if (!tickers.length) return;
  tickers.sort(); // alphabetical for stable column order
  
  // Create or validate sheet
  if (!sparkSheet) {
    sparkSheet = ss.insertSheet('_Spark');
    sparkSheet.getRange(1, 1).setValue('__date__');
    // Will build header below
  }
  
  // Check if we need to reset for new day
  var dateCell = sparkSheet.getRange(1, 1).getValue();
  var today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  if (String(dateCell) !== today) {
    // New day — clear and rebuild header
    sparkSheet.clearContents();
    var header = ['slot'];
    for (var t = 0; t < tickers.length; t++) header.push(tickers[t]);
    sparkSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, header.length).setValues([header]);
    sparkSheet.getRange(1, 1).setValue(today); // overwrite 'slot' with date (row 1 col 1 = date marker)
    // Pre-fill slot column (rows 2 to SPARK_SLOTS+1)
    var slots = [];
    for (var s = 0; s < SPARK_SLOTS; s++) slots.push([SPARK_START + s * SPARK_INTERVAL]);
    sparkSheet.getRange(2, 1, SPARK_SLOTS, 1).setValues(slots);
  }
  
  // Read current header to get column mapping
  var headerRow = sparkSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sparkSheet.getLastColumn() || 1).getValues()[0];
  var colMap = {}; // ticker -> column index (1-based)
  for (var c = 1; c < headerRow.length; c++) {
    colMap[String(headerRow[c]).trim()] = c + 1; // +1 because getRange is 1-based
  }
  
  // Add any new tickers not in header
  var lastCol = headerRow.length;
  var newTickers = [];
  for (var t = 0; t < tickers.length; t++) {
    if (!colMap[tickers[t]]) {
      lastCol++;
      colMap[tickers[t]] = lastCol;
      newTickers.push(tickers[t]);
    }
  }
  if (newTickers.length) {
    var startCol = headerRow.length + 1;
    var vals = [newTickers];
    sparkSheet.getRange(1, startCol, 1, newTickers.length).setValues(vals);
  }
  
  // Write prices for this slot
  var row = slotIdx + 2; // row 2 = slot 0
  var writeData = [];
  var writeCols = [];
  for (var t = 0; t < tickers.length; t++) {
    var col = colMap[tickers[t]];
    if (col && prices[tickers[t]]) {
      writeCols.push(col);
      writeData.push(prices[tickers[t]]);
    }
  }
  // Write each price individually (scattered columns)
  for (var w = 0; w < writeCols.length; w++) {
    sparkSheet.getRange(row, writeCols[w]).setValue(writeData[w]);
  }
}

// ==================== MARKET TAB FORMATTING ====================
// Matches Watchlist GP banner colors: A=green, B=blue, C=orange, D=red
// Section headers get dark navy background, data rows get alternating subtle shading

function formatMarketTab(sheet, numRows, gpLetter) {
  // GP banner row (row 1) — matches Watchlist colors exactly
  var gpBg = '#1a1a2e'; var gpFont = '#ffffff';
  if (gpLetter === 'A') { gpBg = '#00C853'; gpFont = '#ffffff'; }
  else if (gpLetter === 'B') { gpBg = '#2196F3'; gpFont = '#ffffff'; }
  else if (gpLetter === 'C') { gpBg = '#FF9800'; gpFont = '#000000'; }
  else if (gpLetter === 'D') { gpBg = '#F44336'; gpFont = '#ffffff'; }
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 4).setBackground(gpBg).setFontColor(gpFont).setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(11);
  
  // Gameplan detail row (row 4: GP-X, score, adj%, action)
  sheet.getRange(4, 1, 1, 4).setBackground(gpBg).setFontColor(gpFont).setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(10);
  
  // GAMEPLAN header (row 3)
  sheet.getRange(3, 1, 1, 4).setBackground('#2a2a4a').setFontColor('#ffffff').setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(9);
  
  // Scan for section headers and format them
  // DATA_ROWS is the explicit whitelist of row values that must NEVER get header styling
  var DATA_ROW_PREFIXES = ['GLD/', 'QQQ/', 'IWM/', 'VUG/', 'TLT/', 'XLE/', 'XLF/', 'SMH/', 'SPY', 'QQQ', 'IWM',
    'SOXS', 'SQQQ', 'TECS', 'TSXD', 'UVXY', 'SMH', 'SOXX', 'XLK', 'XLY', 'XLF', 'XLI', 'XLC', 'XLU', 'XLP',
    'XLV', 'XLE', 'XLB', 'HYG', 'USO', 'GLD', 'SLV', 'CPER', 'BTCUSD', 'VIX', 'SPY IVR', 'QQQ IVR',
    'SPY IV 5d Δ',
    'Fear', 'NAAIM', '→ TODAY'];
  var data = sheet.getRange(1, 1, numRows, 1).getValues();
  var sectionHeaders = ['BENCHMARKS', 'FUTURES', 'BREADTH DETAIL', 'INTERNALS', 'INTERMARKET RATIOS', 'COMMODITIES',
    'GROWTH SECTORS', 'DEFENSIVE SECTORS', 'INVERSE ETFs (GP-D)', 'INSTITUTIONAL PULSE', 'VOL REGIME', 'TERM STRUCTURE', 'EXPECTED MOVE', 'SENTIMENT', 'COMBINED READ'];

  for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    var val = String(data[i][0]).trim();

    // Skip rows 1-4 (handled separately as GP banner)
    if (i < 4) continue;

    // Check if this is a known section header (exact match only)
    if (sectionHeaders.indexOf(val) >= 0) {
      sheet.getRange(i + 1, 1, 1, 4).setBackground('#2a2a4a').setFontColor('#ffffff').setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(9);
      continue;
    }

    // Explicitly clear background on data rows to prevent bleed
    // (catches tickers like GLD/SPY, SMH, SOXX, SQQQ, TECS that got dark bg erroneously)
    var isDataRow = false;
    for (var dp = 0; dp < DATA_ROW_PREFIXES.length; dp++) {
      if (val.indexOf(DATA_ROW_PREFIXES[dp]) === 0) { isDataRow = true; break; }
    }
    if (isDataRow || val === '') {
      sheet.getRange(i + 1, 1, 1, 4).setBackground(null).setFontColor(null);
    }

    // Leader/Lagger summary
    if (val === 'Leader' || val === 'Lagger') {
      sheet.getRange(i + 1, 1, 1, 4).setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(9);
    }
    // Breadth Score summary row
    if (val === 'Breadth Score') {
      sheet.getRange(i + 1, 1, 1, 4).setBackground('#1a1a2e').setFontColor('#ffffff').setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(9);
    }
  }
  
  // Color change% values green/red in data rows
  var chgCol = 3; // Column C has change %
  var chgData = sheet.getRange(1, chgCol, numRows, 1).getValues();
  for (var i = 0; i < chgData.length; i++) {
    var chgStr = String(chgData[i][0]);
    if (chgStr.indexOf('%') >= 0) {
      var chgNum = parseFloat(chgStr);
      if (!isNaN(chgNum)) {
        var cell = sheet.getRange(i + 1, chgCol);
        if (chgNum > 0) cell.setFontColor('#1b5e20');
        else if (chgNum < 0) cell.setFontColor('#b71c1c');
        else cell.setFontColor('#666666');
      }
    }
    // Also color UP/DN in column C for sectors
    if (chgStr === 'UP') sheet.getRange(i + 1, chgCol).setFontColor('#1b5e20').setFontWeight('bold');
    else if (chgStr === 'DN') sheet.getRange(i + 1, chgCol).setFontColor('#b71c1c').setFontWeight('bold');
  }
  
  // Freeze top rows
  sheet.setFrozenRows(4);
}

// ==================== ECONOMIC CALENDAR ====================

function fetchEconomicCalendar() {
  var TICKER_MAP = {
    'CPI': 'SPY, QQQ, TLT, GLD',
    'Core CPI': 'SPY, QQQ, TLT, GLD',
    'PPI': 'SPY, TLT, GLD',
    'Core PPI': 'SPY, TLT, GLD',
    'PCE': 'SPY, QQQ, TLT',
    'Core PCE': 'SPY, QQQ, TLT',
    'Nonfarm': 'SPY, QQQ, IWM, TLT',
    'Non-Farm': 'SPY, QQQ, IWM, TLT',
    'Unemployment': 'SPY, IWM, TLT',
    'Jobless Claims': 'SPY, IWM, TLT',
    'FOMC': 'SPY, QQQ, TLT, GLD, IWM',
    'Fed ': 'SPY, QQQ, TLT, GLD',
    'Interest Rate': 'SPY, QQQ, TLT, XLF',
    'GDP': 'SPY, QQQ, IWM, TLT',
    'Retail Sales': 'SPY, XLY, XRT, AMZN',
    'Consumer Confidence': 'SPY, XLY, XRT',
    'Consumer Sentiment': 'SPY, XLY, XRT',
    'Michigan': 'SPY, XLY, XRT',
    'ISM Manufacturing': 'SPY, XLI, SMH',
    'ISM Services': 'SPY, XLK, XLC',
    'PMI': 'SPY, XLI, IWM',
    'Manufacturing': 'SPY, XLI, IWM, SMH',
    'Empire State': 'SPY, XLI, IWM',
    'Philly Fed': 'SPY, XLI, IWM',
    'Philadelphia Fed': 'SPY, XLI, IWM',
    'Industrial Production': 'SPY, XLI, IWM',
    'Durable Goods': 'SPY, XLI, BA, CAT',
    'Housing': 'XHB, ITB, HD, LOW',
    'Home Sales': 'XHB, ITB, HD, LOW',
    'Building Permits': 'XHB, ITB, HD, LOW',
    'Housing Starts': 'XHB, ITB, HD, LOW',
    'NAHB': 'XHB, ITB, HD, LOW',
    'Crude Oil': 'XLE, USO, XOM, CVX',
    'EIA': 'XLE, USO, XOM, CVX',
    'Natural Gas': 'XLE, UNG',
    'Treasury': 'TLT, IEF, XLF',
    'Auction': 'TLT, IEF',
    'Trade Balance': 'SPY, UUP, EEM',
    'ADP': 'SPY, IWM, TLT',
    'Capacity Utilization': 'SPY, XLI',
    'Beige Book': 'SPY, QQQ, TLT',
    'Import': 'SPY, UUP',
    'Export': 'SPY, UUP',
    'Inflation': 'SPY, TLT, GLD, TIPS',
    'Personal Income': 'SPY, XLY, XRT',
    'Personal Spending': 'SPY, XLY, XRT',
    'Baker Hughes': 'XLE, USO',
    'Mortgage': 'XHB, ITB',
    'Pending Home': 'XHB, ITB, HD, LOW'
  };

  function getAffectedTickers(title) {
    var t = title.toUpperCase();
    for (var key in TICKER_MAP) {
      if (t.toUpperCase().indexOf(key.toUpperCase()) >= 0) return TICKER_MAP[key];
    }
    if (t.indexOf('SPEECH') >= 0 || t.indexOf('SPEAKS') >= 0) return 'SPY, TLT';
    return '';
  }

  function convertUTCtoAZ(isoDate) {
    var d = new Date(isoDate);
    var azMs = d.getTime() - (7 * 3600000);
    var az = new Date(azMs);
    var h = az.getUTCHours();
    var m = az.getUTCMinutes();
    var ampm = h >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
    var h12 = h % 12;
    if (h12 === 0) h12 = 12;
    return h12 + ':' + (m < 10 ? '0' : '') + m + ' ' + ampm;
  }

  var now = new Date();
  var todayStr = Utilities.formatDate(now, 'America/New_York', 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  var dayOfWeek = now.getDay();
  var daysToFri = (5 - dayOfWeek + 7) % 7;
  if (daysToFri === 0) daysToFri = 7;
  var friday = new Date(now.getTime() + daysToFri * 86400000 + 86400000);
  var toStr = Utilities.formatDate(friday, 'America/New_York', 'yyyy-MM-dd');

  var resp = trackedFetch(
    'https://economic-calendar.tradingview.com/events?from=' + todayStr + 'T00:00:00Z&to=' + toStr + 'T00:00:00Z&countries=US',
    {
      muteHttpExceptions: true,
      headers: { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0', 'Accept': 'application/json', 'Origin': 'https://www.tradingview.com' }
    },
    'econ-calendar'
  );

  if (resp.getResponseCode() !== 200) {
    Logger.log('TradingView economic calendar failed: ' + resp.getResponseCode());
    return [];
  }

  var data = JSON.parse(resp.getContentText());
  var events = data.result || [];

  var filtered = events.filter(function(e) { return (e.importance || 0) >= 0; });

  var today = [];
  var upcoming = [];

  for (var i = 0; i < filtered.length; i++) {
    var e = filtered[i];
    var dateStr = (e.date || '').substring(0, 10);
    var actualVal = (e.actual !== null && e.actual !== undefined) ? String(e.actual) + (e.scale ? e.scale : '') : '';
    var forecastVal = (e.forecast !== null && e.forecast !== undefined) ? String(e.forecast) + (e.scale ? e.scale : '') : '';
    var prevVal = (e.previous !== null && e.previous !== undefined) ? String(e.previous) + (e.scale ? e.scale : '') : '';

    var item = {
      title: e.title || '',
      time: convertUTCtoAZ(e.date),
      impact: e.importance >= 1 ? 'High' : e.importance === 0 ? 'Medium' : 'Low',
      date: dateStr,
      previous: prevVal,
      forecast: forecastVal,
      actual: actualVal,
      tickers: getAffectedTickers(e.title || ''),
      tvTicker: (e.ticker || '').replace('ECONOMICS:', ''),
      isSeparator: false
    };

    if (dateStr === todayStr) {
      today.push(item);
    } else {
      upcoming.push(item);
    }
  }

  var result = [];

  if (today.length > 0) {
    result.push({ title: '── TODAY ──', time: todayStr, impact: '', previous: '', forecast: '', actual: '', tickers: '', tvTicker: '', isSeparator: true });
    for (var i = 0; i < today.length; i++) result.push(today[i]);
  }

  if (upcoming.length > 0) {
    var currentDate = '';
    for (var i = 0; i < upcoming.length; i++) {
      if (upcoming[i].date !== currentDate) {
        currentDate = upcoming[i].date;
        var dayName = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(currentDate + 'T12:00:00'), 'America/New_York', 'EEEE');
        result.push({ title: '── ' + dayName.toUpperCase() + ' ──', time: currentDate, impact: '', previous: '', forecast: '', actual: '', tickers: '', tvTicker: '', isSeparator: true });
      }
      result.push(upcoming[i]);
    }
  }

  return result;
}

// ==================== CATALYST ANALYSIS ENGINE ====================
// Rule-based headline scanner — no API needed.
// Matches keywords in headlines to trading-relevant catalysts and maps to sectors/tickers.

var CATALYST_RULES = [
  // Trade/Tariffs
  { patterns: [/tariff/i, /trade war/i, /trade deal/i, /import dut/i, /export ban/i, /trade restrict/i, /trade tension/i, /sanction/i],
    emoji: '🔥', category: 'TARIFFS/TRADE', tickers: 'SOXX, SMH, AAPL, NVDA',
    bull: 'Trade deal/easing → tech rally, semis bid', bear: 'Tariff escalation → semis/tech vulnerable, watch inverse SOXS' },
  // Fed/Rates
  { patterns: [/\bfed\b/i, /federal reserve/i, /rate cut/i, /rate hike/i, /rate hold/i, /fomc/i, /powell/i, /hawkish/i, /dovish/i, /monetary policy/i, /rate decision/i],
    emoji: '🏦', category: 'FED/RATES', tickers: 'TLT, XLF, QQQ, IWM',
    bull: 'Dovish/cut → growth bid, QQQ+IWM up, TLT up', bear: 'Hawkish/hike → growth pressure, TLT down, XLF mixed' },
  // Inflation/CPI/PPI
  { patterns: [/\bcpi\b/i, /\bppi\b/i, /\bpce\b/i, /inflation/i, /consumer price/i, /producer price/i],
    emoji: '📊', category: 'INFLATION', tickers: 'SPY, QQQ, TLT, GLD',
    bull: 'Cool print → rate cut hopes, growth bid', bear: 'Hot print → rate fears, growth sells, TLT down' },
  // Jobs/Employment
  { patterns: [/nonfarm/i, /non-farm/i, /payroll/i, /unemployment/i, /jobless claim/i, /jobs report/i, /labor market/i, /hiring/i],
    emoji: '👷', category: 'JOBS', tickers: 'SPY, IWM, TLT',
    bull: 'Goldilocks jobs → soft landing, broad bid', bear: 'Too hot → rate fears; too cold → recession fears' },
  // GDP/Growth
  { patterns: [/\bgdp\b/i, /economic growth/i, /recession/i, /soft landing/i, /hard landing/i],
    emoji: '📈', category: 'GDP/GROWTH', tickers: 'SPY, QQQ, IWM',
    bull: 'Strong GDP → risk-on, supports higher GP', bear: 'Weak GDP/recession → risk-off, defensive rotation' },
  // Oil/Energy
  { patterns: [/\boil\b/i, /crude/i, /\bopec\b/i, /petroleum/i, /energy price/i, /oil price/i, /brent/i, /\bwti\b/i],
    emoji: '🛢️', category: 'OIL/ENERGY', tickers: 'XLE, COP, SLB, XOM',
    bull: 'Oil up → XLE bid, energy names run', bear: 'Oil crash → XLE weak, consumer benefit' },
  // China
  { patterns: [/china/i, /chinese/i, /beijing/i, /xi jinping/i, /yuan/i, /\bccp\b/i, /shanghai/i, /hang seng/i],
    emoji: '🇨🇳', category: 'CHINA', tickers: 'BABA, PDD, KWEB, FXI',
    bull: 'Stimulus/easing → China names bid, semis relief', bear: 'Crackdown/tensions → China names sell, tariff risk' },
  // Semis/Chips
  { patterns: [/semiconductor/i, /\bchip\b/i, /\bchips\b/i, /chip act/i, /\bnvda\b/i, /nvidia/i, /\bamd\b/i, /\btsmc\b/i, /\basml\b/i, /ai chip/i],
    emoji: '💾', category: 'SEMICONDUCTORS', tickers: 'NVDA, AMD, AVGO, SOXX, SMH',
    bull: 'Chip demand/AI boost → semis rally', bear: 'Export controls/demand miss → semis sell' },
  // AI
  { patterns: [/artificial intelligence/i, /\bai\b.*(?:model|launch|invest|race|boom|chip|spend)/i, /openai/i, /chatgpt/i, /deepseek/i, /generative ai/i, /\bllm\b/i],
    emoji: '🤖', category: 'AI', tickers: 'NVDA, MSFT, GOOG, META, PLTR',
    bull: 'AI investment/momentum → mega-cap tech bid', bear: 'AI regulation/slowdown → growth pressure' },
  // Earnings
  { patterns: [/earnings/i, /\beps\b/i, /revenue miss/i, /revenue beat/i, /guidance/i, /quarterly result/i, /profit warn/i, /beats estimate/i, /misses estimate/i],
    emoji: '💰', category: 'EARNINGS', tickers: '',
    bull: 'Beat + raise → stock runs, sector sympathy', bear: 'Miss + cut → stock gaps down, sector drag' },
  // Crypto
  { patterns: [/bitcoin/i, /\bbtc\b/i, /crypto/i, /ethereum/i, /\beth\b/i],
    emoji: '₿', category: 'CRYPTO', tickers: 'COIN, MARA, MSTR, RIOT',
    bull: 'BTC rally → crypto names bid', bear: 'BTC crash/regulation → crypto names sell' },

  { patterns: [/treasury/i, /bond yield/i, /10.year/i, /2.year/i, /yield curve/i, /bond market/i],

    bull: 'Yields down → growth/tech bid, TLT up', bear: 'Yields spike → growth sells, financials mixed' },
  // Dollar
  { patterns: [/\busd\b/i, /dollar strength/i, /dollar weak/i, /\bdxy\b/i, /dollar index/i],
    emoji: '💵', category: 'USD', tickers: 'GLD, EEM, UUP',
    bull: 'Dollar weak → commodities/EM bid, gold up', bear: 'Dollar strong → EM/commodities pressure' },
  // Gold
  { patterns: [/\bgold\b/i, /gold price/i, /precious metal/i, /safe.haven/i],
    emoji: '🥇', category: 'GOLD', tickers: 'GLD, GDX, NEM, GOLD',
    bull: 'Gold up → risk-off signal, uncertainty rising', bear: 'Gold down → risk-on, confidence' },
  // Geopolitical
  { patterns: [/war\b/i, /military/i, /missile/i, /invasion/i, /geopolit/i, /nato/i, /conflict/i, /attack/i, /iran/i, /russia/i, /ukraine/i, /israel/i, /gaza/i, /middle east/i],
    emoji: '⚠️', category: 'GEOPOLITICAL', tickers: 'XLE, GLD, TLT, VIX',
    bull: 'De-escalation → risk-on, VIX down', bear: 'Escalation → oil/gold bid, risk-off, VIX spike' },
  // Tech Regulation
  { patterns: [/antitrust/i, /regulat.*tech/i, /big tech.*regulat/i, /monopoly/i, /breakup/i, /doj.*google/i, /ftc.*meta/i],
    emoji: '⚖️', category: 'TECH REGULATION', tickers: 'GOOG, META, AAPL, AMZN, MSFT',
    bull: 'Regulation eases → mega-cap relief', bear: 'Crackdown → mega-cap pressure, QQQ drag' },
  // IPO/Market Structure
  { patterns: [/\bipo\b/i, /goes public/i, /public offering/i, /spac/i, /direct listing/i],
    emoji: '🔔', category: 'IPO', tickers: '',
    bull: 'Hot IPO market → risk appetite high', bear: 'IPO pulled → sentiment cooling' }
];

function generateCatalystBrief(news, gpLetter, breadthScore) {
  if (!news || news.length === 0) return '';
  
  var matched = [];
  var seenCategories = {};
  
  for (var i = 0; i < news.length; i++) {
    var headline = news[i].headline || '';
    var related = news[i].related || '';
    var combined = headline + ' ' + related;
    
    for (var r = 0; r < CATALYST_RULES.length; r++) {
      var rule = CATALYST_RULES[r];
      if (seenCategories[rule.category]) continue; // one match per category
      
      var hit = false;
      for (var p = 0; p < rule.patterns.length; p++) {
        if (rule.patterns[p].test(combined)) { hit = true; break; }
      }
      
      if (hit) {
        // Determine if headline leans bullish or bearish
        var sentiment = 'neutral';
        if (/surge|rally|jump|soar|rise|gain|up|boost|beat|strong|deal|ease|cut|stimulus|dovish|cool/i.test(headline)) sentiment = 'bull';
        if (/fall|drop|plunge|crash|sell|down|miss|weak|fear|hike|hot|restrict|ban|escalat|warn|hawk|crackdown/i.test(headline)) sentiment = 'bear';
        
        var line = rule.emoji + ' ' + rule.category;
        if (rule.tickers) line += ' → ' + rule.tickers;
        line += '\n';
        if (sentiment === 'bull') line += '   ↑ ' + rule.bull;
        else if (sentiment === 'bear') line += '   ↓ ' + rule.bear;
        else line += '   ↑ ' + rule.bull + '\n   ↓ ' + rule.bear;
        
        matched.push(line);
        seenCategories[rule.category] = true;
      }
    }
  }
  
  if (matched.length === 0) return '✅ No major catalysts detected in recent headlines';
  return matched.join('\n');
}

function getTimerState() {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var ws = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
  var enabled = isScannerEnabled();
  var fullEnabled = isFullScanEnabled();
  var quotaCount = _getRolling24hCount().count;
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  
  // Determine current phase for display (using reliable Utilities.formatDate)
  var now = new Date();
  var _tH = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'H'), 10);
  var _tM = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'm'), 10);
  var azMin = _tH * 60 + _tM;
  var phase = 'OFF';
  var fullScanIn = -1; // -1 = no periodic full scans in this phase
  
  if (azMin >= PHASE_CONFIG.PRE_MARKET.start && azMin < PHASE_CONFIG.PRE_MARKET.end) {
    phase = 'PM';
  } else if (azMin >= PHASE_CONFIG.MARKET_OPEN.start && azMin < PHASE_CONFIG.MARKET_OPEN.end) {
    phase = 'OPEN';
    if (fullEnabled) {
      var counter = parseInt(props.getProperty('PHASE_COUNTER_MARKETOPEN') || '0');
      fullScanIn = (PHASE_CONFIG.MARKET_OPEN.fullInterval - counter) * 5;
    }
  } else if (azMin >= PHASE_CONFIG.CORE_SESSION.start && azMin < PHASE_CONFIG.CORE_SESSION.end) {
    phase = 'CORE';
    if (fullEnabled) {
      var counter = parseInt(props.getProperty('PHASE_COUNTER_CORESESSION') || '0');
      fullScanIn = (PHASE_CONFIG.CORE_SESSION.fullInterval - counter) * 5;
    }
  } else if (azMin >= PHASE_CONFIG.AFTER_HOURS.start && azMin < PHASE_CONFIG.AFTER_HOURS.end) {
    phase = 'AH';
  }
  
  // Hourly quota breakdown for dashboard chart (last 120 hours = 5 days)
  var quotaHourly = [];
  var quotaByCat = {quotes:0,bars:0,market:0,bridge:0,claude:0,news:0,positions:0,other:0};
  var CATS = ['quotes','bars','market','bridge','claude','news','positions','other'];
  for (var qh = 119; qh >= 0; qh--) {
    var bucketTime = new Date(now.getTime() - qh * 3600000);
    var bucketKey = _getQuotaBucketKey(bucketTime);
    var bucketHour = Utilities.formatDate(bucketTime, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'M/d ha');
    var bucketVal = parseInt(props.getProperty(bucketKey) || '0');
    if (bucketVal === 0 && qh > 24) continue;  // Skip empty old hours to keep payload small
    var cats = {};
    for (var ci = 0; ci < CATS.length; ci++) {
      var cv = parseInt(props.getProperty(bucketKey + '_' + CATS[ci]) || '0');
      cats[CATS[ci]] = cv;
      quotaByCat[CATS[ci]] += cv;
    }
    quotaHourly.push({ h: bucketHour, v: bucketVal, c: cats });
  }
  var quotaLog = props.getProperty('QUOTA_LOG') || '';

  // API cost hourly data for dashboard chart
  var apiCostHourly = [];
  var apiCostTotal = parseFloat(props.getProperty('DASHBOARD_COST_CUM') || '0');
  try {
    for (var ah = 119; ah >= 0; ah--) {
      var aTime = new Date(now.getTime() - ah * 3600000);
      var aHour = Utilities.formatDate(aTime, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'ha');
      var aKey = 'APICOST_' + Utilities.formatDate(aTime, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd_HH');
      var aCost = parseFloat(props.getProperty(aKey) || '0');
      var tKey = 'APITOK_' + Utilities.formatDate(aTime, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd_HH');
      var aTok = {};
      try { aTok = JSON.parse(props.getProperty(tKey) || '{}'); } catch(te) {}
      apiCostHourly.push({ h: aHour, cost: Math.round(aCost * 10000) / 10000, tok: aTok });
    }
  } catch(ache) {}

  var breadthAlertsRaw = props.getProperty('BREADTH_ALERTS') || '[]'; var breadthAlerts = []; try { breadthAlerts = JSON.parse(breadthAlertsRaw); } catch(e) {}
  var internalsHistRaw = props.getProperty('INTERNALS_HIST') || '[]'; var internalsHist = []; try { internalsHist = JSON.parse(internalsHistRaw); } catch(e) {}
  var base = { enabled: enabled, fullEnabled: fullEnabled, marketEnabled: isMarketRefreshEnabled(), quotaCount: quotaCount, quotaHourly: quotaHourly, quotaByCat: quotaByCat, quotaLog: quotaLog, apiCostHourly: apiCostHourly, apiCostTotal: apiCostTotal, phase: phase, fullScanIn: fullScanIn, breadthAlerts: breadthAlerts, internalsHist: internalsHist };
  
  if (!ws) { base.updated = Date.now().toString(); base.gp = ''; base.gpLetter = 'C'; return base; }
  
  var gpText = String(ws.getRange(1, 1).getValue());
  var gpLetter = 'C';
  if (gpText.indexOf('GP-A') >= 0) gpLetter = 'A';
  else if (gpText.indexOf('GP-B') >= 0) gpLetter = 'B';
  else if (gpText.indexOf('GP-C') >= 0) gpLetter = 'C';
  else if (gpText.indexOf('GP-D') >= 0) gpLetter = 'D';
  
  base.gp = gpText;
  base.gpLetter = gpLetter;
  base.updated = props.getProperty('lastUpdateTime') || Date.now().toString();
  
  // Read Market tab data for sidebar display
  try {
    var mkt = ss.getSheetByName('Market');
    if (mkt) {
      var mktData = mkt.getDataRange().getValues();
      var sections = {};
      var currentSection = '';
      for (var i = 0; i < mktData.length; i++) {
        var label = String(mktData[i][0]).trim();
        if (!label) continue;
        // Detect section headers
        if (['BENCHMARKS','FUTURES','BREADTH DETAIL','INTERNALS','INTERMARKET RATIOS','COMMODITIES','GROWTH SECTORS','DEFENSIVE SECTORS','INVERSE ETFs (GP-D)','INSTITUTIONAL PULSE'].indexOf(label) >= 0) {
          currentSection = label;
          sections[currentSection] = [];
          continue;
        }
        if (label === 'V9 CONFLUENCE SCANNER' || label === 'GAMEPLAN' || label === '' || label === 'Leader' || label === 'Lagger' || label === 'Breadth Score' || label === 'ADD/ADQD') {
          // Special rows
          if (label === 'Breadth Score') {
            base.breadthScore = mktData[i][1];
            base.sectorPts = mktData[i][3];
          }
          if (label === 'Leader') { base.leader = String(mktData[i][1]) + ' ' + String(mktData[i][2]); }
          if (label === 'Lagger') { base.lagger = String(mktData[i][1]) + ' ' + String(mktData[i][2]); }
          continue;
        }
        if (currentSection && sections[currentSection] && label.indexOf('GP-') < 0) {
          sections[currentSection].push({
            sym: label,
            val: String(mktData[i][1] || ''),
            chg: String(mktData[i][2] || ''),
            desc: String(mktData[i][3] || '')
          });
        }
      }
      base.market = sections;
      // Build heatmap data from sectors
      var hm = [];
      var sectorSections = ['GROWTH SECTORS','DEFENSIVE SECTORS'];
      for (var si = 0; si < sectorSections.length; si++) {
        var sArr = sections[sectorSections[si]] || [];
        for (var sj = 0; sj < sArr.length; sj++) {
          var valStr = String(sArr[sj].val || '').replace('%','').trim();
          var chgVal = parseFloat(valStr);
          if (!isNaN(chgVal) && Math.abs(chgVal) < 0.5) chgVal = chgVal * 100; // Sheets % fix
          hm.push({ sym: sArr[sj].sym, chg: isNaN(chgVal) ? 0 : chgVal, name: sArr[sj].desc || sArr[sj].sym, type: si === 0 ? 'G' : 'D' });
        }
      }
      base.sectorHeatmap = hm;
    }
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('Timer market read error: ' + e.message);
  }
  
  // Fetch market news (cached 5 min to avoid quota burn)
  try {
    var newsCacheStr = props.getProperty('NEWS_CACHE') || '';
    var newsCacheTime = parseInt(props.getProperty('NEWS_CACHE_TIME') || '0');
    var newsAge = Date.now() - newsCacheTime;
    
    if (newsCacheStr && newsAge < 1800000) {  // 30-min cache
      // Use cached news (< 5 min old)
      base.news = JSON.parse(newsCacheStr);
    } else {
      // Fetch fresh news from Finnhub
      var fhKey = getFinnhubKey();
      if (fhKey) {
        var newsUrl = 'https://finnhub.io/api/v1/news?category=general&token=' + fhKey;
        var resp = trackedFetch(newsUrl, { muteHttpExceptions: true }, 'finnhub-news');
        if (resp.getResponseCode() === 200) {
          var allNews = JSON.parse(resp.getContentText());
          var recentNews = [];
          var srcBlacklist = {'MarketWatch': 1, 'marketwatch': 1};
          for (var n = 0; n < allNews.length && recentNews.length < 15; n++) {
            if (allNews[n].headline && !srcBlacklist[allNews[n].source]) {
              recentNews.push({
                headline: allNews[n].headline || '',
                source: allNews[n].source || '',
                url: allNews[n].url || '',
                time: allNews[n].datetime || 0,
                related: allNews[n].related || '',
                category: allNews[n].category || ''
              });
            }
          }
          props.setProperty('NEWS_CACHE', JSON.stringify(recentNews));
          props.setProperty('NEWS_CACHE_TIME', Date.now().toString());
          base.news = recentNews;
        }
      }
    }
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('News fetch error: ' + e.message);
  }
  
  // Fetch RSS feeds: Investing.com, CNBC, Yahoo Finance (shared cache, 10-min)
  // Also fetch per-ticker Yahoo feeds for My Positions (separate cache, 10-min)
  try {
    // Read My Positions tickers from ScriptProperties (set by refreshMyPositions)
    var posTickers = [];
    try {
      var ptRaw = props.getProperty('MY_POSITION_TICKERS');
      if (ptRaw) posTickers = JSON.parse(ptRaw);
    } catch(e) { Logger.log('Position tickers read: ' + e.message); }
    base.positionTickers = posTickers;
    
    var rssCacheStr = props.getProperty('RSS_NEWS_CACHE') || '';
    var rssCacheTime = parseInt(props.getProperty('RSS_NEWS_CACHE_TIME') || '0');
    var rssAge = Date.now() - rssCacheTime;
    var rssNews = [];
    
    if (rssCacheStr && rssAge < 1800000) {  // 30-min cache
      rssNews = JSON.parse(rssCacheStr);
    } else {
      var rssFeeds = [
        { url: 'https://www.investing.com/rss/news_25.rss', src: 'Investing.com', tag: 'IC', ua: true },
        { url: 'https://search.cnbc.com/rs/search/combinedcms/view.xml?partnerId=wrss01&id=100003114', src: 'CNBC', tag: 'CN', ua: false },
        { url: 'https://finance.yahoo.com/news/rssindex', src: 'Yahoo Finance', tag: 'YF', ua: false }
      ];
      // Reduced from 5+N feeds to 3 fixed feeds. Saves ~12+ fetches per refresh cycle.
      // Per-ticker Yahoo feeds REMOVED — burned N fetches per cycle for minimal value.
      // General Yahoo + CNBC + Investing.com cover market-moving news adequately.
      var rssSrcBlacklist = {'MarketWatch': 1, 'marketwatch': 1};
      for (var fi = 0; fi < rssFeeds.length; fi++) {
        try {
          var fetchOpts = { muteHttpExceptions: true };
          if (rssFeeds[fi].ua) fetchOpts.headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0' };
          var rssResp = trackedFetch(rssFeeds[fi].url, fetchOpts, 'rss-' + rssFeeds[fi].tag);
          if (rssResp.getResponseCode() === 200) {
            var xml = XmlService.parse(rssResp.getContentText());
            var root = xml.getRootElement();
            var channel = root.getChild('channel');
            if (channel) {
              var items = channel.getChildren('item');
              for (var ii = 0; ii < items.length && ii < 15; ii++) {
                var title = items[ii].getChildText('title') || '';
                var link = items[ii].getChildText('link') || '';
                var pubDate = items[ii].getChildText('pubDate') || '';
                var pubTime = 0;
                if (pubDate) {
                  try { pubTime = Math.floor(new Date(pubDate).getTime() / 1000); } catch(e) {}
                }
                if (!title) continue;
                // Skip blacklisted sources embedded in RSS item
                var itemSrc = items[ii].getChildText('source') || '';
                if (rssSrcBlacklist[itemSrc]) continue;
                // Dedupe within rssNews by first 40 chars
                var prefix40 = title.substring(0, 40).toLowerCase();
                var isDupe = false;
                for (var dd = 0; dd < rssNews.length; dd++) {
                  if (rssNews[dd].headline.substring(0, 40).toLowerCase() === prefix40) { isDupe = true; break; }
                }
                if (!isDupe) {
                  rssNews.push({
                    headline: title,
                    source: rssFeeds[fi].src,
                    url: link,
                    time: pubTime,
                    related: '',
                    category: '',
                    feed: rssFeeds[fi].tag
                  });
                }
              }
            }
          }
        } catch(e) {
          Logger.log('RSS feed error (' + rssFeeds[fi].tag + '): ' + e.message);
        }
      }
      if (rssNews.length > 0) {
        props.setProperty('RSS_NEWS_CACHE', JSON.stringify(rssNews));
        props.setProperty('RSS_NEWS_CACHE_TIME', Date.now().toString());
      }
    }
    
    // Merge Finnhub + RSS feeds, tag sources
    if (base.news) {
      for (var fn = 0; fn < base.news.length; fn++) {
        if (!base.news[fn].feed) base.news[fn].feed = 'FH';
      }
    } else {
      base.news = [];
    }
    
    // Dedupe RSS vs Finnhub by headline similarity (first 40 chars)
    for (var ri = 0; ri < rssNews.length; ri++) {
      var rPrefix = rssNews[ri].headline.substring(0, 40).toLowerCase();
      var exists = false;
      for (var ef = 0; ef < base.news.length; ef++) {
        if (base.news[ef].headline.substring(0, 40).toLowerCase() === rPrefix) {
          exists = true; break;
        }
      }
      if (!exists) base.news.push(rssNews[ri]);
    }
    
    // Sort all news by time descending
    base.news.sort(function(a, b) { return (b.time || 0) - (a.time || 0); });
