    // Cap at 30 total (more sources = higher cap)
    if (base.news.length > 30) base.news = base.news.slice(0, 30);
    
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('IC RSS error: ' + e.message);
  }
  
  // Rule-based Catalyst Analysis (no API needed)
  try {
    if (base.news && base.news.length > 0) {
      base.aiBrief = generateCatalystBrief(base.news, base.gpLetter, base.breadthScore);
    }
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('Catalyst brief error: ' + e.message);
  }
  
  // Send persisted breadth/GP history
  try {
    var histRaw = props.getProperty('BREADTH_GP_HISTORY') || '[]';
    base.history = JSON.parse(histRaw);
  } catch(e) { base.history = []; }
  
  // ── Weekend Pulse state (for dashboard pulse layout) ──
  base.pulseMode = props.getProperty('PULSE_MODE') === 'true';
  base.pulseEnabled = props.getProperty('WEEKEND_PULSE_ENABLED') === 'ON';
  base.pulseLastUpdate = props.getProperty('PULSE_LAST_UPDATE') || '';
  if (base.pulseMode) {
    try {
      var _pulseSessionsRaw = props.getProperty('PULSE_ACTIVE_SESSIONS');
      base.activeSessions = _pulseSessionsRaw ? JSON.parse(_pulseSessionsRaw) : {};
    } catch(e) { base.activeSessions = {}; }
    try {
      var _pulseNewsRaw = props.getProperty('PULSE_NEWS_CACHE');
      base.pulseNews = _pulseNewsRaw ? JSON.parse(_pulseNewsRaw) : [];
    } catch(e) { base.pulseNews = []; }
    // Read Weekend tab data for sidebar display
    try {
      var wkSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Weekend');
      if (wkSheet) {
        var wkData = wkSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
        var pulseSections = {};
        var currentPulseSection = '';
        for (var wi = 0; wi < wkData.length; wi++) {
          var wLabel = String(wkData[wi][0]).trim();
          if (!wLabel) continue;
          // Detect section headers by checking PULSE_SECTIONS labels
          var isHeader = false;
          for (var ps = 0; ps < PULSE_SECTIONS.length; ps++) {
            if (wLabel === PULSE_SECTIONS[ps].label) {
              currentPulseSection = PULSE_SECTIONS[ps].key;
              pulseSections[currentPulseSection] = { label: wLabel, items: [] };
              isHeader = true;
              break;
            }
          }
          if (isHeader || wLabel === '📡 WEEKEND PULSE') continue;
          if (currentPulseSection && pulseSections[currentPulseSection] && wLabel.indexOf('Last') < 0) {
            pulseSections[currentPulseSection].items.push({
              sym: wLabel,
              val: String(wkData[wi][1] || ''),
              chg: String(wkData[wi][2] || ''),
              status: String(wkData[wi][3] || '')
            });
          }
        }
        base.pulseData = pulseSections;
      }
    } catch(e) { Logger.log('Pulse tab read: ' + e.message); }
  }
  
  return base;
}

function testConnection() {
  try {
    const token = getAccessToken();
    const quotes = tsQuotes(['AAPL']);
    if (quotes.length > 0) {
      SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Connection successful!\n\nAAPL: $' + quotes[0].Last + '\nVWAP: $' + quotes[0].VWAP);
    } else {
      SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Connected but no data returned. Market may be closed.');
    }
  } catch (e) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Connection failed: ' + e.message);
  }
}

// ==================== TRADESTATION POSITIONS API (MULTI-ACCOUNT) ====================

// Discover all TS accounts
function tsGetAllAccounts() {
  var token = getAccessToken();
  var response = trackedFetch('https://api.tradestation.com/v3/brokerage/accounts', {
    method: 'get',
    headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  }, 'ts-accounts');
  var data = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
  return data.Accounts || [];
}

// Get configured account IDs from ScriptProperties
// Format: JSON array of {id: "12345", label: "Day Trade", type: "DT"} objects
// type: "DT" = Day Trade, "SW" = Swing, "ALL" = single account mode
function getTSAccountConfig() {
  var raw = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('TS_ACCOUNTS');
  if (raw) {
    try { return JSON.parse(raw); } catch(e) {}
  }
  return [];
}

// Setup: discover accounts and let user label them
function setupTSAccounts() {
  try {
    var accounts = tsGetAllAccounts();
    if (!accounts || accounts.length === 0) {
      SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('No TradeStation accounts found. Check API credentials.');
      return;
    }
    
    var msg = 'Found ' + accounts.length + ' TradeStation account(s):\n\n';
    for (var i = 0; i < accounts.length; i++) {
      var a = accounts[i];
      msg += (i + 1) + '. ' + a.AccountID + ' — ' + (a.AccountType || 'Unknown') + '\n';
    }
    
    if (accounts.length === 1) {
      var config = [{ id: accounts[0].AccountID, label: 'Trading', type: 'ALL' }];
      PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('TS_ACCOUNTS', JSON.stringify(config));
      SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(msg + '\nAuto-configured single account for all positions.');
      return;
    }
    
    var ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
    msg += '\nWhich account is your DAY TRADE account?\nEnter the account ID (number only):';
    var dtResponse = ui.prompt('Day Trade Account', msg, ui.ButtonSet.OK_CANCEL);
    if (dtResponse.getSelectedButton() !== ui.Button.OK) return;
    var dtId = dtResponse.getResponseText().trim();
    
    var swResponse = ui.prompt('Swing Account', 'Which account is your SWING account?\nEnter the account ID:', ui.ButtonSet.OK_CANCEL);
    if (swResponse.getSelectedButton() !== ui.Button.OK) return;
    var swId = swResponse.getResponseText().trim();
    
    var config = [];
    for (var i = 0; i < accounts.length; i++) {
      var a = accounts[i];
      if (a.AccountID === dtId) {
        config.push({ id: a.AccountID, label: 'Day Trade', type: 'DT' });
      } else if (a.AccountID === swId) {
        config.push({ id: a.AccountID, label: 'Swing', type: 'SW' });
      } else {
        config.push({ id: a.AccountID, label: 'Cash Reserve', type: 'CASH' });
      }
    }
    
    PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('TS_ACCOUNTS', JSON.stringify(config));
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Accounts configured!\n\nDay Trade: ' + dtId + '\nSwing: ' + swId + '\nRemaining accounts set as Cash Reserve.\n\nRun "Refresh My Positions" to pull data.');
  } catch(e) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Error: ' + e.message);
  }
}

function tsGetPositions(accountId) {
  var token = getAccessToken();
  var response = trackedFetch('https://api.tradestation.com/v3/brokerage/accounts/' + accountId + '/positions', {
    method: 'get',
    headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  }, 'ts-positions');
  var data = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
  return data.Positions || [];
}

function tsGetBalances(accountId) {
  var token = getAccessToken();
  var response = trackedFetch('https://api.tradestation.com/v3/brokerage/accounts/' + accountId + '/balances', {
    method: 'get',
    headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  }, 'ts-balances');
  var data = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
  return data.Balances && data.Balances.length > 0 ? data.Balances[0] : {};
}

// Build position rows from raw API positions
function _buildPositionRows(positions) {
  var rows = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < positions.length; i++) {
    var p = positions[i];
    if (p.AssetType && p.AssetType !== 'EQ' && p.AssetType !== 'STOCK') continue;
    var sym = p.Symbol || '';
    var side = p.LongShort || (parseFloat(p.Quantity || 0) >= 0 ? 'Long' : 'Short');
    var qty = Math.abs(parseFloat(p.Quantity || 0));
    var avgCost = parseFloat(p.AveragePrice || 0);
    var last = parseFloat(p.Last || p.MarkToMarketPrice || 0);
    var mktVal = parseFloat(p.MarketValue || (qty * last));
    var dayPL = parseFloat(p.TodaysProfitLoss || 0);
    var unrealPL = parseFloat(p.UnrealizedProfitLoss || 0);
    var costBasis = qty * avgCost;
    var dayPLPct = costBasis > 0 ? (dayPL / costBasis) : 0;
    var totalPLPct = costBasis > 0 ? (unrealPL / costBasis) : 0;
    rows.push({ sym: sym, side: side, qty: qty, avgCost: avgCost, last: last, mktVal: mktVal,
                dayPL: dayPL, dayPLPct: dayPLPct, unrealPL: unrealPL, totalPLPct: totalPLPct, costBasis: costBasis });
  }
  rows.sort(function(a, b) { return b.mktVal - a.mktVal; });
  return rows;
}

// Build account summary
function _buildAcctSummary(balances, rows) {
  var totalMktVal = 0, totalDayPL = 0, totalUnrealPL = 0, totalCostBasis = 0;
  for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
    totalMktVal += rows[i].mktVal;
    totalDayPL += rows[i].dayPL;
    totalUnrealPL += rows[i].unrealPL;
    totalCostBasis += rows[i].costBasis;
  }
  var nlv = parseFloat(balances.Equity || balances.NetLiquidatingValue || balances.CashBalance || 0);
  var bp = parseFloat(balances.BuyingPower || balances.DayTradingBuyingPower || 0);
  return { nlv: nlv, bp: bp, totalMktVal: totalMktVal, totalDayPL: totalDayPL,
           totalUnrealPL: totalUnrealPL, totalCostBasis: totalCostBasis, count: rows.length };
}

// Format a position row as sheet array
function _posRowToArray(r, acctLabel, tag) {
  return [r.sym, acctLabel, r.side, r.qty, r.avgCost, r.last, r.mktVal,
          r.dayPL, r.dayPLPct, r.unrealPL, r.totalPLPct, r.costBasis, tag || ''];
}

// ==================== ALPACA PAPER TRADING API ====================
// Pulls paper trading positions from Alpaca alongside live TradeStation positions.
// Auth: static API key + secret in headers (no OAuth/token refresh needed).
// Keys stored in ScriptProperties: ALPACA_KEY_ID, ALPACA_SECRET_KEY
// Endpoint: https://paper-api.alpaca.markets/v2

function alpacaGetPositions() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var keyId = props.getProperty('ALPACA_KEY_ID');
  var secretKey = props.getProperty('ALPACA_SECRET_KEY');
  if (!keyId || !secretKey) return [];
  
  var response = trackedFetch('https://paper-api.alpaca.markets/v2/positions', {
    method: 'get',
    headers: {
      'APCA-API-KEY-ID': keyId,
      'APCA-API-SECRET-KEY': secretKey,
      'accept': 'application/json'
    },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  }, 'alpaca-positions');
  
  var code = response.getResponseCode();
  if (code !== 200) {
    Logger.log('Alpaca positions error (' + code + '): ' + response.getContentText());
    return [];
  }
  return JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
}

function alpacaGetAccount() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var keyId = props.getProperty('ALPACA_KEY_ID');
  var secretKey = props.getProperty('ALPACA_SECRET_KEY');
  if (!keyId || !secretKey) return {};
  
  var response = trackedFetch('https://paper-api.alpaca.markets/v2/account', {
    method: 'get',
    headers: {
      'APCA-API-KEY-ID': keyId,
      'APCA-API-SECRET-KEY': secretKey,
      'accept': 'application/json'
    },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  }, 'alpaca-account');
  
  var code = response.getResponseCode();
  if (code !== 200) {
    Logger.log('Alpaca account error (' + code + '): ' + response.getContentText());
    return {};
  }
  return JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
}

// Map Alpaca position JSON to same format as _buildPositionRows output
function _buildAlpacaPositionRows(positions) {
  var rows = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < positions.length; i++) {
    var p = positions[i];
    // Alpaca fields: symbol, qty, side, avg_entry_price, current_price, market_value,
    //                unrealized_pl, unrealized_plpc, change_today
    var sym = p.symbol || '';
    var side = p.side === 'long' ? 'Long' : 'Short';
    var qty = Math.abs(parseFloat(p.qty || 0));
    var avgCost = parseFloat(p.avg_entry_price || 0);
    var last = parseFloat(p.current_price || 0);
    var mktVal = Math.abs(parseFloat(p.market_value || (qty * last)));
    var unrealPL = parseFloat(p.unrealized_pl || 0);
    var costBasis = qty * avgCost;
    // Alpaca gives change_today as decimal (0.01 = 1%), use for day P&L estimate
    var changeToday = parseFloat(p.change_today || 0);
    var dayPL = costBasis * changeToday;
    var dayPLPct = changeToday;
    var totalPLPct = costBasis > 0 ? (unrealPL / costBasis) : 0;
    rows.push({ sym: sym, side: side, qty: qty, avgCost: avgCost, last: last, mktVal: mktVal,
                dayPL: dayPL, dayPLPct: dayPLPct, unrealPL: unrealPL, totalPLPct: totalPLPct, costBasis: costBasis });
  }
  rows.sort(function(a, b) { return b.mktVal - a.mktVal; });
  return rows;
}

// Map Alpaca account JSON to same format as _buildAcctSummary output
function _buildAlpacaSummary(account, rows) {
  var totalMktVal = 0, totalDayPL = 0, totalUnrealPL = 0, totalCostBasis = 0;
  for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
    totalMktVal += rows[i].mktVal;
    totalDayPL += rows[i].dayPL;
    totalUnrealPL += rows[i].unrealPL;
    totalCostBasis += rows[i].costBasis;
  }
  var nlv = parseFloat(account.equity || account.portfolio_value || 0);
  var bp = parseFloat(account.buying_power || account.daytrading_buying_power || 0);
  return { nlv: nlv, bp: bp, totalMktVal: totalMktVal, totalDayPL: totalDayPL,
           totalUnrealPL: totalUnrealPL, totalCostBasis: totalCostBasis, count: rows.length };
}

// Check if Alpaca paper trading is configured
function isAlpacaConfigured() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  return !!(props.getProperty('ALPACA_KEY_ID') && props.getProperty('ALPACA_SECRET_KEY'));
}

// Force re-discover TS accounts (run once after adding/removing accounts)
function resetTSAccounts() {
  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().deleteProperty('TS_ACCOUNTS');
  Logger.log('TS_ACCOUNTS cleared. Next Refresh My Positions will auto-discover all accounts.');
}


// Refresh My Positions tab from TradeStation API (multi-account) + Alpaca Paper
function refreshMyPositions() {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sheet = ss.getSheetByName('My Positions');
    if (!sheet) { sheet = ss.insertSheet('My Positions'); }
    
    // ── Preserve existing tags before clearing ──
    var tagMap = {};
    try {
      var existingData = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      for (var i = 0; i < existingData.length; i++) {
        var ticker = String(existingData[i][0] || '').trim();
        var acct = String(existingData[i][1] || '').trim();
        var tag = String(existingData[i][12] || '').trim();
        if (ticker && tag && ticker !== 'Ticker' && ticker !== 'TOTAL' && ticker.indexOf('━') < 0) {
          tagMap[ticker + '|' + acct] = tag;
        }
      }
    } catch(e) {}
    
    var acctConfig = getTSAccountConfig();
    
    if (acctConfig.length === 0) {
      var accounts = tsGetAllAccounts();
      if (accounts.length === 0) { Logger.log('No TS accounts found'); return -1; }
      if (accounts.length === 1) {
        acctConfig = [{ id: accounts[0].AccountID, label: 'Trading', type: 'ALL' }];
      } else {
        for (var i = 0; i < accounts.length; i++) {
          if (i === 0) acctConfig.push({ id: accounts[i].AccountID, label: 'Day Trade', type: 'DT' });
          else if (i === 1) acctConfig.push({ id: accounts[i].AccountID, label: 'Swing', type: 'SW' });
          else acctConfig.push({ id: accounts[i].AccountID, label: 'Cash Reserve', type: 'CASH' });
        }
      }
      PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('TS_ACCOUNTS', JSON.stringify(acctConfig));
    }
    
    var headers = ['Ticker', 'Account', 'Side', 'Shares', 'Avg Cost', 'Last', 'Mkt Value', 'Day P&L $', 'Day P&L %', 'Total P&L $', 'Total P&L %', 'Cost Basis', 'Tag'];
    var now = new Date();
    var azTime = Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'h:mm:ss a');
    
    var allSections = [];
    var allPosTickers = [];
    var liveMkt = 0, liveDayPL = 0, liveUnrealPL = 0, liveCost = 0, liveNLV = 0, liveBP = 0, liveCount = 0;
    
    for (var a = 0; a < acctConfig.length; a++) {
      var acct = acctConfig[a];
      try {
        var positions = tsGetPositions(acct.id);
        var balances = tsGetBalances(acct.id);
        var rows = _buildPositionRows(positions);
        var summary = _buildAcctSummary(balances, rows);
        allSections.push({ label: acct.label, type: acct.type, id: acct.id, summary: summary, rows: rows });
        for (var r = 0; r < rows.length; r++) {
          if (allPosTickers.indexOf(rows[r].sym) < 0) allPosTickers.push(rows[r].sym);
        }
        liveMkt += summary.totalMktVal; liveDayPL += summary.totalDayPL;
        liveUnrealPL += summary.totalUnrealPL; liveCost += summary.totalCostBasis;
        liveNLV += summary.nlv; liveBP += summary.bp; liveCount += summary.count;
      } catch(e) {
        Logger.log('Error pulling account ' + acct.id + ': ' + e.message);
        allSections.push({ label: acct.label, type: acct.type, id: acct.id, summary: null, rows: [], error: e.message });
      }
    }
    
    if (isAlpacaConfigured()) {
      try {
        var alpPos = alpacaGetPositions();
        var alpAcct = alpacaGetAccount();
        var alpRows = _buildAlpacaPositionRows(alpPos);
        var alpSum = _buildAlpacaSummary(alpAcct, alpRows);
        allSections.push({ label: 'Paper', type: 'PAPER', id: 'ALPACA', summary: alpSum, rows: alpRows });
        for (var r = 0; r < alpRows.length; r++) {
          if (allPosTickers.indexOf(alpRows[r].sym) < 0) allPosTickers.push(alpRows[r].sym);
        }
      } catch(e) {
        Logger.log('Alpaca error: ' + e.message);
        allSections.push({ label: 'Paper', type: 'PAPER', id: 'ALPACA', summary: null, rows: [], error: e.message });
      }
    }
    
    sheet.clearContents();
    sheet.clearFormats();
    var sheetRows = [];
    var rowMeta = [];
    
    var fmtK = function(v) { return v > 0 ? '$' + (v/1000).toFixed(1) + 'K' : '$0'; };
    sheetRows.push([
      'LIVE TOTAL (' + liveCount + ' positions)  |  Updated: ' + azTime, '', '', '',
      'NLV: ' + fmtK(liveNLV), 'BP: ' + fmtK(liveBP),
      liveMkt, liveDayPL,
      liveCost > 0 ? liveDayPL / liveCost : 0,
      liveUnrealPL,
      liveCost > 0 ? liveUnrealPL / liveCost : 0,
      liveCost, ''
    ]);
    rowMeta.push('grand');
    
    for (var s = 0; s < allSections.length; s++) {
      var sec = allSections[s];
      
      sheetRows.push(new Array(headers.length).fill(''));
      rowMeta.push('spacer');
      
      var label = sec.label.toUpperCase();
      if (sec.type === 'DT') label += ' (DAY TRADE)';
      else if (sec.type === 'SW') label += ' (SWING)';
      else if (sec.type === 'PAPER') label += ' (PAPER TRADING)';
      else if (sec.type === 'CASH') label += ' (CASH RESERVE)';
      label = '━━ ' + label + ' ━━  #' + sec.id;
      
      if (sec.summary) {
        sheetRows.push([
          label, '', 'Positions: ' + sec.summary.count, '',
          'NLV: ' + fmtK(sec.summary.nlv), 'BP: ' + fmtK(sec.summary.bp),
          sec.summary.totalMktVal, sec.summary.totalDayPL,
          sec.summary.totalCostBasis > 0 ? sec.summary.totalDayPL / sec.summary.totalCostBasis : 0,
          sec.summary.totalUnrealPL,
          sec.summary.totalCostBasis > 0 ? sec.summary.totalUnrealPL / sec.summary.totalCostBasis : 0,
          azTime, ''
        ]);
      } else {
        sheetRows.push([label, '', 'ERROR: ' + (sec.error || 'Unknown'), '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', azTime, '']);
      }
      rowMeta.push('acct');
      
      sheetRows.push(headers);
      rowMeta.push('header');
      
      for (var r = 0; r < sec.rows.length; r++) {
        var posTag = tagMap[sec.rows[r].sym + '|' + sec.label] || '';
        sheetRows.push(_posRowToArray(sec.rows[r], sec.label, posTag));
        rowMeta.push('data');
      }
      if (sec.rows.length === 0 && !sec.error) {
        sheetRows.push(['(no open positions)', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '']);
        rowMeta.push('data');
      }
    }
    
    // ── Tag Summary Sections (separate Live vs Paper) ──
    var liveTagStats = {};
    var paperTagStats = {};
    for (var s = 0; s < allSections.length; s++) {
      var sec = allSections[s];
      var targetStats = (sec.type === 'PAPER') ? paperTagStats : liveTagStats;
      for (var r = 0; r < sec.rows.length; r++) {
        var posTag = tagMap[sec.rows[r].sym + '|' + sec.label] || '';
        if (posTag) {
          if (!targetStats[posTag]) targetStats[posTag] = { count: 0, mktVal: 0, dayPL: 0, unrealPL: 0, costBasis: 0, tickers: [] };
          targetStats[posTag].count++;
          targetStats[posTag].mktVal += sec.rows[r].mktVal;
          targetStats[posTag].dayPL += sec.rows[r].dayPL;
          targetStats[posTag].unrealPL += sec.rows[r].unrealPL;
          targetStats[posTag].costBasis += sec.rows[r].costBasis;
          targetStats[posTag].tickers.push(sec.rows[r].sym);
        }
      }
    }
    
    // Live Tag Performance
    var liveTagKeys = Object.keys(liveTagStats);
    if (liveTagKeys.length > 0) {
      sheetRows.push(new Array(headers.length).fill(''));
      rowMeta.push('spacer');
      sheetRows.push(['━━ LIVE TAG PERFORMANCE ━━', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '']);
      rowMeta.push('taghdr');
      sheetRows.push(['Tag', 'Tickers', 'Count', '', '', '', 'Mkt Value', 'Day P&L $', 'Day P&L %', 'Total P&L $', 'Total P&L %', 'Cost Basis', '']);
      rowMeta.push('header');
      for (var t = 0; t < liveTagKeys.length; t++) {
        var tag = liveTagKeys[t];
        var ts = liveTagStats[tag];
        sheetRows.push([
          tag, ts.tickers.join(', '), ts.count, '', '', '',
          ts.mktVal, ts.dayPL,
          ts.costBasis > 0 ? ts.dayPL / ts.costBasis : 0,
          ts.unrealPL,
          ts.costBasis > 0 ? ts.unrealPL / ts.costBasis : 0,
          ts.costBasis, ''
        ]);
        rowMeta.push('tagrow');
      }
    }
    
    // Paper Tag Performance
    var paperTagKeys = Object.keys(paperTagStats);
    if (paperTagKeys.length > 0) {
      sheetRows.push(new Array(headers.length).fill(''));
      rowMeta.push('spacer');
      sheetRows.push(['━━ PAPER TAG PERFORMANCE ━━', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '']);
      rowMeta.push('papertaghdr');
      sheetRows.push(['Tag', 'Tickers', 'Count', '', '', '', 'Mkt Value', 'Day P&L $', 'Day P&L %', 'Total P&L $', 'Total P&L %', 'Cost Basis', '']);
      rowMeta.push('header');
      for (var t = 0; t < paperTagKeys.length; t++) {
        var tag = paperTagKeys[t];
        var ts = paperTagStats[tag];
        sheetRows.push([
          tag, ts.tickers.join(', '), ts.count, '', '', '',
          ts.mktVal, ts.dayPL,
          ts.costBasis > 0 ? ts.dayPL / ts.costBasis : 0,
          ts.unrealPL,
          ts.costBasis > 0 ? ts.unrealPL / ts.costBasis : 0,
          ts.costBasis, ''
        ]);
        rowMeta.push('tagrow');
      }
    }
    
    if (sheetRows.length > 0) {
      sheet.getRange(1, 1, sheetRows.length, headers.length).setValues(sheetRows);
    }
    
    for (var i = 0; i < rowMeta.length; i++) {
      var rn = i + 1;
      var range = sheet.getRange(rn, 1, 1, headers.length);
      var meta = rowMeta[i];
      
      if (meta === 'grand') {
        range.setBackground('#0d47a1').setFontColor('#fff').setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(11);
        sheet.getRange(rn, 7, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('$#,##0');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 8, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('+$#,##0.00;-$#,##0.00');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 9, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('+0.00%;-0.00%');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 10, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('+$#,##0.00;-$#,##0.00');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 11, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('+0.00%;-0.00%');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 12, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('$#,##0');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 8, 1, 2).setFontColor(liveDayPL >= 0 ? '#81c784' : '#ef9a9a');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 10, 1, 2).setFontColor(liveUnrealPL >= 0 ? '#81c784' : '#ef9a9a');
      } else if (meta === 'acct') {
        var secType = '';
        for (var si = 0; si < allSections.length; si++) {
          if (String(sheetRows[i][0]).indexOf(allSections[si].id) >= 0) { secType = allSections[si].type; break; }
        }
        var bg = secType === 'DT' ? '#1b5e20' : secType === 'SW' ? '#4a148c' : secType === 'PAPER' ? '#e65100' : secType === 'CASH' ? '#004d40' : '#37474f';
        range.setBackground(bg).setFontColor('#fff').setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(10);
        sheet.getRange(rn, 7, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('$#,##0');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 8, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('+$#,##0.00;-$#,##0.00');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 9, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('+0.00%;-0.00%');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 10, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('+$#,##0.00;-$#,##0.00');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 11, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('+0.00%;-0.00%');
      } else if (meta === 'header') {
        range.setBackground('#333').setFontColor('#aaa').setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(9);
      } else if (meta === 'taghdr') {
        range.setBackground('#1a237e').setFontColor('#fff').setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(11);
      } else if (meta === 'papertaghdr') {
        range.setBackground('#bf360c').setFontColor('#fff').setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(11);
      } else if (meta === 'tagrow') {
        range.setBackground('#1a1a3e').setFontColor('#e0e0e0').setFontSize(10);
        sheet.getRange(rn, 7, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('$#,##0');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 8, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('+$#,##0.00;-$#,##0.00');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 9, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('+0.00%;-0.00%');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 10, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('+$#,##0.00;-$#,##0.00');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 11, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('+0.00%;-0.00%');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 12, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('$#,##0');
        var tdv = sheetRows[i][7];
        if (typeof tdv === 'number') sheet.getRange(rn, 8, 1, 2).setFontColor(tdv >= 0 ? '#4caf50' : '#f44336');
        var ttv = sheetRows[i][9];
        if (typeof ttv === 'number') sheet.getRange(rn, 10, 1, 2).setFontColor(ttv >= 0 ? '#4caf50' : '#f44336');
      } else if (meta === 'data') {
        range.setBackground(i % 2 === 0 ? '#1a1a2e' : '#12121f').setFontColor('#e0e0e0').setFontSize(10);
        sheet.getRange(rn, 5, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('$#,##0.00');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 6, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('$#,##0.00');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 7, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('$#,##0.00');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 8, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('+$#,##0.00;-$#,##0.00');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 9, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('+0.00%;-0.00%');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 10, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('+$#,##0.00;-$#,##0.00');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 11, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('+0.00%;-0.00%');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 12, 1, 1).setNumberFormat('$#,##0.00');
        sheet.getRange(rn, 13, 1, 1).setBackground('#0a2a2a').setFontColor('#4dd0e1').setFontWeight('bold');
        var dv = sheetRows[i][7];
        if (typeof dv === 'number') sheet.getRange(rn, 8, 1, 2).setFontColor(dv >= 0 ? '#4caf50' : '#f44336');
        var tv = sheetRows[i][9];
        if (typeof tv === 'number') sheet.getRange(rn, 10, 1, 2).setFontColor(tv >= 0 ? '#4caf50' : '#f44336');
      } else if (meta === 'spacer') {
        range.setBackground('#0a0a14').setFontSize(4);
      }
    }
    
    for (var c = 1; c <= headers.length; c++) { sheet.autoResizeColumn(c); }
    // Force Tag column wider for easy editing
    sheet.setColumnWidth(13, 120);
    
    // Cache all position tickers (live + paper combined)
    PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('MY_POSITION_TICKERS', JSON.stringify(allPosTickers));
    
    // Cache paper-only tickers separately for Watchlist Doc sync
    var paperOnlyTickers = [];
    for (var ps = 0; ps < allSections.length; ps++) {
      if (allSections[ps].type === 'PAPER') {
        for (var pr = 0; pr < allSections[ps].rows.length; pr++) {
          if (paperOnlyTickers.indexOf(allSections[ps].rows[pr].sym) < 0) {
            paperOnlyTickers.push(allSections[ps].rows[pr].sym);
          }
        }
      }
    }
    PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('PAPER_POSITION_TICKERS', JSON.stringify(paperOnlyTickers));
    
    // ── Auto-populate Config tab: MY POSITIONS and PAPER TRADES sections ──
    try {
      var configSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Config');
      if (configSheet) {
        var cfgLastRow = configSheet.getLastRow();
        var cfgData = cfgLastRow > 0 ? configSheet.getRange(1, 1, cfgLastRow, 2).getValues() : [];
        var myPosHeaderRow = -1, paperHeaderRow = -1, myPosEndRow = -1, paperEndRow = -1;
        
        // Find section header rows (column A non-empty = section name)
        for (var ci = 0; ci < cfgData.length; ci++) {
          var secName = String(cfgData[ci][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
          if (secName === '' || secName === 'SECTION') continue;
          if (secName === 'MY POSITIONS') { myPosHeaderRow = ci; continue; }
          if (secName === 'PAPER TRADES') { paperHeaderRow = ci; continue; }
          // Any other section header marks end of previous open section
          if (myPosHeaderRow >= 0 && myPosEndRow < 0) myPosEndRow = ci;
          if (paperHeaderRow >= 0 && paperEndRow < 0) paperEndRow = ci;
        }
        if (myPosHeaderRow >= 0 && myPosEndRow < 0) myPosEndRow = cfgLastRow;
        if (paperHeaderRow >= 0 && paperEndRow < 0) paperEndRow = cfgLastRow;
        
        // Helper: rewrite tickers in column B under a section header
        var _rewriteConfigSection = function(headerRow, endRow, tickers) {
          if (headerRow < 0) return;
          var startRow = headerRow + 2; // 0-idx to 1-idx + skip header row
          var clearCount = endRow - headerRow - 1;
          if (clearCount > 0) {
            configSheet.getRange(startRow, 2, clearCount, 1).clearContent();
          }
          for (var ti = 0; ti < tickers.length; ti++) {
            configSheet.getRange(startRow + ti, 2).setValue(tickers[ti]);
          }
        };
        
        // Live tickers = allPosTickers minus paper
        var liveTickers = [];
        for (var lt = 0; lt < allPosTickers.length; lt++) {
          if (paperOnlyTickers.indexOf(allPosTickers[lt]) < 0) {
            liveTickers.push(allPosTickers[lt]);
          }
        }
        
        if (myPosHeaderRow >= 0) _rewriteConfigSection(myPosHeaderRow, myPosEndRow, liveTickers);
        if (paperHeaderRow >= 0) _rewriteConfigSection(paperHeaderRow, paperEndRow, paperOnlyTickers);
      }
    } catch(cfgErr) {
      Logger.log('Config auto-populate error (non-fatal): ' + cfgErr.message);
    }
    
    Logger.log('My Positions refreshed: ' + liveCount + ' live + paper across ' + allSections.length + ' accounts, Live NLV: $' + liveNLV + ', Paper tickers: ' + paperOnlyTickers.length);
    return liveCount;
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('refreshMyPositions error: ' + e.message);
    return -1;
  }
}

// Manual menu trigger
function refreshMyPositionsManual() {
  var count = refreshMyPositions();
  if (count >= 0) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('My Positions refreshed: ' + count + ' positions');
  } else {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Error refreshing positions. Check API credentials.\nRun "Setup TS Accounts" first if needed.');
  }
}

function getMyPositionTickers() {
  // Try ScriptProperties cache first (fastest)
  var cached = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('MY_POSITION_TICKERS');
  if (cached) {
    try { return JSON.parse(cached); } catch(e) {}
  }
  // Fallback: read from My Positions sheet
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var sheet = ss.getSheetByName('My Positions');
  if (!sheet) return [];
  var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  var tickers = [];
  for (var i = 3; i < data.length; i++) { // Skip acct row, summary row, header row
    var t = String(data[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (t && t !== '' && t !== 'ACCOUNT' && t !== 'TICKER' && t.indexOf('NLV') < 0) {
      tickers.push(t);
    }
  }
  return tickers;
}

// Returns only Alpaca paper trading tickers (subset of allPosTickers)
// Cache-only — populated by refreshMyPositions(). Returns [] if no cache yet.
function getPaperPositionTickers() {
  var cached = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('PAPER_POSITION_TICKERS');
  if (cached) {
    try { return JSON.parse(cached); } catch(e) {}
  }
  return [];
}

// ==================== POSITION SCANNER VIEW ====================
function buildPositionScannerView(ss, rows, headers, gameplan, totalBreadth, sectors) {
  var sheetName = 'Position Scanner';
  var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet(sheetName);
  }

  var activeRows = [];
  for (var i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
    var sec = String(rows[i][0]).trim().toUpperCase();
    if (sec === 'MY POSITIONS') {
      activeRows.push(rows[i]);
    }
  }

  if (activeRows.length === 0) {
    sheet.clearContents();
    sheet.clearFormats();
    sheet.getRange(1, 1).setValue('No position tickers found in scanner');
    return;
  }

  var gpRow = new Array(headers.length).fill('');
  gpRow[0] = 'GP-' + gameplan.gp + '  |  ' + gameplan.action + '  |  Score: ' + totalBreadth.toFixed(1) + ' (' + gameplan.adjPct + '%)  |  Sizing: ' + gameplan.sizing + '  |  Growth: ' + sectors.growthGreen + '/8  |  Defensive: ' + sectors.defGreen + '/5  |  Updated: ' + new Date().toLocaleTimeString() + '  |  Next: ' + new Date(Date.now() + 5 * 60000).toLocaleTimeString();

  var groupRow = new Array(headers.length).fill('');
  groupRow[0] = 'IDENTITY + PRICE';
  groupRow[6] = 'CONFLUENCE';
  groupRow[9] = 'CORE SCORES (0-5)';
  groupRow[15] = 'MODIFIERS (±2)';
  groupRow[19] = 'FLAGS';
  groupRow[23] = 'TECHNICALS';
  groupRow[33] = 'EXECUTION';
  groupRow[37] = 'REFERENCE';
  groupRow[46] = 'EARNINGS / NOTES';

  var allRows = [gpRow, groupRow, headers, ...activeRows];

  sheet.clearContents();
  sheet.clearFormats();
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, allRows.length, headers.length).setValues(allRows);

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).merge();

  var merges = [
    [2, 1, 1, 6], [2, 7, 1, 9], [2, 10, 1, 15], [2, 16, 1, 19],
    [2, 20, 1, 23], [2, 24, 1, 33], [2, 34, 1, 37], [2, 38, 1, 46], [2, 47, 1, 49]
  ];
  for (var m = 0; m < merges.length; m++) {
    var mg = merges[m];
    sheet.getRange(mg[0], mg[1], 1, mg[3] - mg[1] + 1).merge().setHorizontalAlignment('center');
  }
  var groupEnds = [6, 9, 15, 19, 23, 33, 37, 46, 49];
  for (var g = 0; g < groupEnds.length - 1; g++) {
    sheet.getRange(2, groupEnds[g], 2, 1)
      .setBorder(null, null, null, true, null, null, '#ffffff', SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID_THICK);
    sheet.getRange(2, groupEnds[g] + 1, 2, 1)
      .setBorder(null, true, null, null, null, null, '#ffffff', SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID_THICK);
  }

  formatWatchlist(sheet, allRows.length, headers.length, 4);

  sheet.getRange(allRows.length + 1, 1).setValue('Last Updated: ' + new Date().toLocaleString());
}

// ==================== PRE-MARKET TAB ====================

function buildPreMarketTab(ss, watchlistItems, gfDaily, quoteMap, earningsMap, spyQuote) {
  var sheetName = 'Pre-Market';
  var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet(sheetName);
  }

  var spyPct = parseFloat((spyQuote || {}).NetChangePct || 0);

  var headers = ['Section', 'Ticker', 'Name', 'Last', 'Gap%', 'RelStr%', 'Vol', 'AvgVol', 'RVOL',
                 'Mkt Cap', '52w%', 'Earnings', 'PM Score', 'Notes'];

  var rows = [];

  for (var i = 0; i < watchlistItems.length; i++) {
    var item = watchlistItems[i];
    var q = quoteMap[item.symbol] || {};
    var gf = gfDaily[item.symbol] || {};
    var earn = earningsMap[item.symbol] || {};

    var last = q.Last || 0;
    var prevClose = q.PreviousClose || last;
    var open = q.Open || last;
    var vol = q.Volume || 0;
    var avgVol = q.AverageVolume || q.PreviousVolume || 1;
    var rvol = avgVol > 0 ? (vol / avgVol) : 0;
    var gapPct = prevClose > 0 ? ((open - prevClose) / prevClose * 100) : 0;
    var netPct = q.NetChangePct ? parseFloat(q.NetChangePct) : 0;
    var relStr = netPct - spyPct;
    var mktCap = q.MarketCap ? formatMarketCap(parseFloat(q.MarketCap)) : (gf.marketcap ? formatMarketCap(gf.marketcap) : '');
    var h52 = gf.high52 || q.High52Week || 0;
    var l52 = gf.low52 || q.Low52Week || 0;
    var range52 = h52 - l52;
    var pct52 = (range52 > 0 && last > 0) ? ((last - l52) / range52 * 100).toFixed(1) : '';
    var name = q.Name || gf.name || '';

    // PM Score: gap + relstr + rvol + earnings proximity
    var pmScore = 0;
    if (Math.abs(gapPct) >= 2) pmScore += 3;
    else if (Math.abs(gapPct) >= 1) pmScore += 2;
    else if (Math.abs(gapPct) >= 0.5) pmScore += 1;

    if (relStr >= 2) pmScore += 3;
    else if (relStr >= 1) pmScore += 2;
    else if (relStr >= 0.5) pmScore += 1;

    if (rvol >= 3) pmScore += 3;
    else if (rvol >= 2) pmScore += 2;
    else if (rvol >= 1) pmScore += 1;

    if (earn.daysUntil !== undefined && earn.daysUntil <= 1) pmScore += 2;
    else if (earn.daysUntil !== undefined && earn.daysUntil <= 7) pmScore += 1;

    rows.push([
      item.section, item.symbol, name, last,
      gapPct.toFixed(2), relStr.toFixed(2),
      vol, avgVol, rvol.toFixed(2),
      mktCap, pct52,
      earn.display || '', pmScore, ''
    ]);
  }

  // Sort by PM Score descending
  rows.sort(function(a, b) { return (b[12] || 0) - (a[12] || 0); });

  sheet.clearContents();
  sheet.clearFormats();

  var headerRow = [headers];
  var allRows = [headers, ...rows];

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, allRows.length, headers.length).setValues(allRows);

  // Format header
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setBackground('#1a1a2e').setFontColor('#ffffff')
    .setFontWeight('bold').setFontSize(9);
  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);

  // Color PM Score
  if (rows.length > 0) {
    var scoreRange = sheet.getRange(2, 13, rows.length, 1);
    var scoreVals = scoreRange.getValues();
    var scoreBgs = [], scoreFonts = [];
    for (var i = 0; i < scoreVals.length; i++) {
      var s = parseFloat(scoreVals[i][0]) || 0;
      if (s >= 8) { scoreBgs.push(['#c6efce']); scoreFonts.push(['#006100']); }
      else if (s >= 5) { scoreBgs.push(['#d5f5d5']); scoreFonts.push(['#006100']); }
      else if (s >= 3) { scoreBgs.push(['#ffeb9c']); scoreFonts.push(['#9c6500']); }
      else { scoreBgs.push(['#ffffff']); scoreFonts.push(['#666666']); }
    }
    scoreRange.setBackgrounds(scoreBgs).setFontColors(scoreFonts).setFontWeight('bold');

    // Color gap and relstr
    colorBySign(sheet, 2, 5, rows.length);
    colorBySign(sheet, 2, 6, rows.length);

    // Section highlighting
    var sectionVals = sheet.getRange(2, 1, rows.length, 1).getValues();
    for (var i = 0; i < sectionVals.length; i++) {
      var sec = String(sectionVals[i][0]).trim().toUpperCase();
      var row = i + 2;
      if (sec === 'MY POSITIONS') {
        sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, headers.length).setBackground('#d0e2f7').setFontWeight('bold');
      } else if (sec === 'ARETE' || sec === 'ARETE RESEARCH') {
        sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, headers.length).setBackground('#d4edda').setFontWeight('bold');
      } else if (sec === 'WATCHING') {
        sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, headers.length).setBackground('#fde8d0').setFontWeight('bold');
      }
    }
  }

  sheet.getRange(rows.length + 2, 1).setValue('Last Updated: ' + new Date().toLocaleString());
}

// ==================== V9 TRADING DASHBOARD ====================
// Auto-generates "The Story" narrative using Claude Opus API.
// Runs every 30 min during market hours via trigger.
// Bundles: breadth, positions, sectors, catalysts, Arete email, journal history.
// Writes response to "Dashboard" sheet tab + serves via doGet for live HTML page.

// ── Dashboard Trigger Control ──

function startDashboard() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  props.setProperty('DASHBOARD_ENABLED', 'ON');
  
  // Create 30-min trigger if not exists
  var triggers = ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers();
  var hasTrigger = false;
  for (var i = 0; i < triggers.length; i++) {
    if (triggers[i].getHandlerFunction() === 'updateDashboard') {
      hasTrigger = true;
      break;
    }
  }
  if (!hasTrigger) {
    ScriptApp.newTrigger('updateDashboard')
      .timeBased()
      .everyMinutes(30)
      .create();
  }
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('✅ V9 Trading Dashboard ON — Claude Opus narrative every 30 min during market hours.');
}

function stopDashboard() {
  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('DASHBOARD_ENABLED', 'OFF');
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('🛑 V9 Trading Dashboard OFF — trigger still exists but updateDashboard() will skip.');
}

function isDashboardEnabled() {
  return PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('DASHBOARD_ENABLED') === 'ON';
}

function forceDashboard() {
  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('DASHBOARD_FORCE', 'true');
  updateDashboard();
}

// ── Core Dashboard Function ──

function updateDashboard() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  
  // Force flag check
  var force = props.getProperty('DASHBOARD_FORCE') === 'true';
  if (force) props.deleteProperty('DASHBOARD_FORCE');
  
  // Enabled check
  if (!force && !isDashboardEnabled()) return;
  
  // Market hours + weekend gate
  var now = new Date();
  var azHour = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'H'), 10);
  var azMin  = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'm'), 10);
  var azTime = azHour * 60 + azMin;
  var azDow  = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'u'), 10);
  
  if (!force && azDow >= 6) return; // Weekend
  var _off = _getMarketOffset();
  if (!force && (azTime < (390 - _off) || azTime > (960 - _off))) return; // dynamic market hours
  
  // Determine session label
  var session = 'PRE';
  if (azTime >= (450 - _off) && azTime < (540 - _off)) session = 'OPEN';
  else if (azTime >= (540 - _off) && azTime < (780 - _off)) session = 'CORE';
  else if (azTime >= (780 - _off) && azTime < (840 - _off)) session = 'POWER';
  else if (azTime >= (840 - _off)) session = 'AH';
  
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // PHASE 1: Collect all data for the prompt
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  
  var promptData = {};
  
  // 1A. Breadth & Gameplan from Market tab
  try {
    var mkt = ss.getSheetByName('Market');
    if (mkt) {
      var mktVals = mkt.getDataRange().getValues();
      var breadthLines = [];
      var currentSec = '';
      for (var i = 0; i < mktVals.length; i++) {
        var label = String(mktVals[i][0]).trim();
        if (!label) continue;
        if (label === 'GAMEPLAN') {
          // Next row has GP data
          if (i + 1 < mktVals.length) {
            promptData.gameplan = String(mktVals[i+1][0]) + ' | Score: ' + String(mktVals[i+1][1]) + ' | Adj: ' + String(mktVals[i+1][2]) + ' | ' + String(mktVals[i+1][3]);
          }
          continue;
        }
        if (['BENCHMARKS','FUTURES','BREADTH DETAIL','INTERNALS','INTERMARKET RATIOS','GROWTH SECTORS','DEFENSIVE SECTORS','INVERSE ETFs (GP-D)','COMMODITIES'].indexOf(label) >= 0) {
          currentSec = label;
          breadthLines.push('\n[' + label + ']');
          continue;
        }
        if (currentSec && label !== 'V9 CONFLUENCE SCANNER' && label.indexOf('GP-') < 0) {
          breadthLines.push(label + ': ' + String(mktVals[i][1] || '') + ' (' + String(mktVals[i][2] || '') + ')');
        }
        if (label === 'Breadth Score') {
          promptData.breadthScore = String(mktVals[i][1]);
          promptData.sectorPts = String(mktVals[i][3]);
        }
      }
      promptData.marketSnapshot = breadthLines.join('\n');
    }
  } catch(e) { Logger.log('Dashboard mkt read: ' + e.message); }
  
  // 1B. Positions from My Positions tab
  try {
    var posSheet = ss.getSheetByName('My Positions');
    if (posSheet) {
      var posVals = posSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      var posLines = [];
      for (var i = 0; i < posVals.length; i++) {
        var ticker = String(posVals[i][0]).trim();
        if (!ticker || ticker === 'Ticker' || ticker.indexOf('━') >= 0 || ticker === 'TOTAL') continue;
        // Account headers start with ═ or contain account label
        if (ticker.indexOf('═') >= 0 || ticker.indexOf('Account') >= 0) {
          posLines.push(ticker);
          continue;
        }
        var side = String(posVals[i][2] || '');
        var shares = String(posVals[i][3] || '');
        var avgCost = String(posVals[i][4] || '');
        var last = String(posVals[i][5] || '');
        var dayPL = String(posVals[i][7] || '');
        var dayPLPct = String(posVals[i][8] || '');
        var totalPL = String(posVals[i][9] || '');
        var totalPLPct = String(posVals[i][10] || '');
        var tag = String(posVals[i][12] || '');
        posLines.push(ticker + ' [' + tag + '] ' + side + ' ' + shares + 'sh @ ' + avgCost + ' → ' + last + ' | Day: ' + dayPL + ' (' + dayPLPct + ') | Total: ' + totalPL + ' (' + totalPLPct + ')');
      }
      promptData.positions = posLines.join('\n');
    }
  } catch(e) { Logger.log('Dashboard pos read: ' + e.message); }
  
  // 1C. Top confluence picks from Watchlist tab
  try {
    var wl = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
    if (wl) {
      var wlVals = wl.getDataRange().getValues();
      var topPicks = [];
      // Find confluence column (usually col with score)
      for (var i = 1; i < Math.min(wlVals.length, 50); i++) {
        var sym = String(wlVals[i][0] || '').trim();
        if (!sym) continue;
        // Cols: A=ticker, B=last, C=chg%, D=RVOL, E=sector, ... varies
        // Just grab first 15 rows which are sorted by confluence
        var rowStr = '';
        for (var c = 0; c < Math.min(wlVals[i].length, 10); c++) {
          if (c > 0) rowStr += ' | ';
          rowStr += String(wlVals[i][c] || '');
        }
        topPicks.push(rowStr);
        if (topPicks.length >= 15) break;
      }
      promptData.watchlistTop15 = topPicks.join('\n');
    }
  } catch(e) { Logger.log('Dashboard wl read: ' + e.message); }
  
  // 1D. News/RSS catalysts (from cache)
  try {
    var newsCache = props.getProperty('NEWS_CACHE') || '[]';
    var rssCache = props.getProperty('RSS_NEWS_CACHE') || '[]';
    var allNews = JSON.parse(newsCache).concat(JSON.parse(rssCache));
    // Sort by time, take top 20
    allNews.sort(function(a,b) { return (b.time||0) - (a.time||0); });
    var newsLines = [];
    var seen = {};
    for (var i = 0; i < allNews.length && newsLines.length < 20; i++) {
      var h = String(allNews[i].headline || '').substring(0, 60);
      if (seen[h]) continue;
      seen[h] = true;
      newsLines.push('[' + (allNews[i].source || allNews[i].feed || '') + '] ' + allNews[i].headline);
    }
    promptData.catalysts = newsLines.join('\n');
  } catch(e) { Logger.log('Dashboard news read: ' + e.message); }
  
  // 1E. Arete morning call from Gmail
  try {
    var areteText = getAreteFromGmail_();
    if (areteText) {
      promptData.arete = areteText;
    }
  } catch(e) { Logger.log('Dashboard Arete: ' + e.message); }
  
  // 1F. Breadth history (last 6 readings for trajectory)
  try {
    var histRaw = props.getProperty('BREADTH_GP_HISTORY') || '[]';
    var hist = JSON.parse(histRaw);
    if (hist.length > 0) {
      var histLines = [];
      var start = Math.max(0, hist.length - 6);
      for (var i = start; i < hist.length; i++) {
        histLines.push(hist[i].time + ': GP-' + hist[i].gp + ' (' + hist[i].score + ')');
      }
      promptData.breadthTrajectory = histLines.join(' → ');
    }
  } catch(e) {}
  
  // 1G. Journal context (last 3 session summaries for behavioral coaching)
  try {
    var journalSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Journal');
    if (journalSheet) {
      var jVals = journalSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      var journalLines = [];
      // Read last 3 non-empty rows
      for (var i = jVals.length - 1; i >= 1 && journalLines.length < 3; i--) {
        var jDate = String(jVals[i][0] || '').trim();
        if (jDate) {
          var jLine = jDate;
          for (var c = 1; c < Math.min(jVals[i].length, 6); c++) {
            jLine += ' | ' + String(jVals[i][c] || '');
          }
          journalLines.push(jLine);
        }
      }
      if (journalLines.length > 0) {
        promptData.recentJournal = journalLines.join('\n');
      }
    }
  } catch(e) {}
  
  // 1G. Watching tickers from Config tab
  try {
    var cfgSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Config');
    if (cfgSheet) {
      var cfgData = cfgSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      var wSection = '', myW = [], arW = [];
      for (var i = 0; i < cfgData.length; i++) {
        var cA = String(cfgData[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        var cB = String(cfgData[i][1] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        if (cA === 'WATCHING' || cA === 'MY WATCHING') { wSection = 'my'; continue; }
        if (cA === 'ARETE WATCHING' || cA === 'ARETE_WATCHING') { wSection = 'ar'; continue; }
        if (cA && cA !== cB && (cA.indexOf('POSITION') >= 0 || cA.indexOf('PAPER') >= 0 || cA.indexOf('ARETE SWING') >= 0 || cA.indexOf('ARETE DAY') >= 0 || cA.indexOf('CARRY') >= 0 || cA.indexOf('TIER') >= 0)) { wSection = ''; continue; }
        if (!cB) continue;
        if (cB === 'TICKER' || cB === 'STOCK TICKER') continue;
        if (wSection === 'my') myW.push(cB);
        else if (wSection === 'ar') arW.push(cB);
      }
      var wLines = [];
      if (myW.length) wLines.push('My Watching: ' + myW.join(', '));
      if (arW.length) wLines.push('Arete Watching: ' + arW.join(', '));
      if (wLines.length) promptData.watching = wLines.join('\n');
    }
  } catch(e) {}

  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // PHASE 2: Build the prompt
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  
  var timestamp = Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'h:mm a') + ' AZ';
  
  var systemPrompt = [
    'You are a trading desk analyst. Produce a market brief with ALL 10 sections below.',
    'V9 system: GP-A(≥+9.5,$15-20K) GP-B(+3to+9.5,$8-12K) GP-C(-3to+3,no trades) GP-D(≤-3,inverse).',
    'Max 5 positions, $36K/sector, $60K total. Confluence ≥24/38 to trade. Stop 1.5×ATR, target 3×ATR.',
    '',
    'YOU MUST PRODUCE ALL 9 SECTIONS. Use these EXACT ## headers. Skipping any = broken dashboard.',
    '',
    '## THE STORY',
    '5-8 sentences. What + why. Connect breadth→sectors→catalysts. Reference data. End with GP implication.',
    '',
    '## GAMEPLAN STATUS',
    'GP letter, score, trajectory (building/fading/stable). Distance to next threshold.',
    '',
    '## SESSION ANALYSIS',
    'One line per asset, format "TICKER: what it means" (not what it is):',
    'SPY: [meaning] | QQQ: [meaning] | VIX: [meaning] | DXY: [meaning]',
    'USO: [meaning] | SLV: [meaning] | BTCUSD: [meaning]',
    '',
    '## POSITION ALERTS',
    'Every position, pipe format: | TICKER | P&L context | HOLD/TRIM/EXIT/REVIEW — reason |',
    '',
    '## PORTFOLIO RISK',
    'Sector clusters, exposure vs limits, correlation risk, specific recommendations.',
    '',
    '## TOP SETUPS',
    '1-3 names from watchlist: ticker, score/38, setup, entry, why now. Or "None meet ≥24."',
    '',
    '## INTERMARKET READ',
    '3-4 sentences tying ratios into one narrative. Use description first, ticker in parens: e.g. "credit risk appetite (HYG/TLT)" not "HYG/TLT". Ratio descriptions: HYG/TLT=credit risk appetite, GLD/SPY=gold vs equities, QQQ/SPY=tech vs broad, VUG/VTV=growth vs value, IWM/SPY=small cap vs large, XLK/XLU=tech vs utilities, TLT/SHY=long vs short bonds, XLE/SPY=energy vs broad, XLF/SPY=financials vs broad, SMH/QQQ=semis vs Nasdaq.',
    '',
    '## WATCHING NOTES',
    'For each My Watching ticker: TICKER — LONG/SHORT/NEUTRAL | key level | 1-line thesis.',
    'Use market context, sector flows, and Arete alignment to determine bias and levels.',
    'Format: one line per ticker. Skip Arete Watching (too many).',
    '',
    '## BOTTOM LINE',
    '4-5 sentences. Accountability. Reference this session. Specific tickers + numbers. One action item.',
    '',
    '## DAILY EDGE',
    "CONCEPT: [name]. 4-6 sentences teaching one concept using today's data. End with V9 rule.",
    '',
    'Dense. Specific. Actionable. All 10 sections required.'
  ].join('\n');
  
  var userMessage = [
    'TIMESTAMP: ' + timestamp + ' | SESSION: ' + session,
    '',
    '=== GAMEPLAN ===',
    promptData.gameplan || 'No data',
    '',
    '=== BREADTH TRAJECTORY ===',
    promptData.breadthTrajectory || 'No history yet',
    '',
    '=== MARKET SNAPSHOT ===',
    promptData.marketSnapshot || 'No market data',
    '',
    '=== ACTIVE POSITIONS ===',
    promptData.positions || 'No positions',
    '',
    '=== WATCHLIST TOP 15 (by confluence) ===',
    promptData.watchlistTop15 || 'No watchlist data',
    '',
    '=== CATALYSTS & NEWS ===',
    promptData.catalysts || 'No news available',
    '',
    '=== ARETE MORNING CALL ===',
    promptData.arete || 'No Arete email found today',
    '',
    '=== RECENT JOURNAL (last 3 sessions) ===',
    promptData.recentJournal || 'No journal entries yet',
    '',
    '=== WATCHING TICKERS ===',
    promptData.watching || 'No watching tickers'
  ].join('\n');
  
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // PHASE 3: Call Claude Opus API
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  
  var apiKey = props.getProperty('ANTHROPIC_API_KEY');
  if (!apiKey) {
    Logger.log('Dashboard: No ANTHROPIC_API_KEY in Script Properties. Add via Project Settings.');
    return;
  }
  
  var payload = {
    model: 'claude-opus-4-5-20251101',
    max_tokens: 3500,
    system: systemPrompt,
    messages: [
      { role: 'user', content: userMessage }
    ]
  };
  
  var options = {
    method: 'post',
    contentType: 'application/json',
    headers: {
      'x-api-key': apiKey,
      'anthropic-version': '2023-06-01'
    },
    payload: JSON.stringify(payload),
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  };
  
  var modelUsed = 'claude-opus-4-5-20251101';
  var response;
  try {
    response = trackedFetch('https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', options, 'claude-dashboard');
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('Dashboard API error: ' + e.message);
    return;
  }
  
  var code = response.getResponseCode();
  var body = response.getContentText();
  
  // Fallback to Sonnet on 529 (overloaded) or 529-like errors
  if (code === 529 || code === 503) {
    Logger.log('Dashboard: Opus overloaded (' + code + '), falling back to Sonnet...');
    modelUsed = 'claude-sonnet-4-5-20250929';
    payload.model = modelUsed;
    options.payload = JSON.stringify(payload);
    try {
      response = trackedFetch('https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', options, 'claude-dashboard-fallback');
      code = response.getResponseCode();
      body = response.getContentText();
    } catch(e2) {
      Logger.log('Dashboard Sonnet fallback error: ' + e2.message);
      writeDashboard_(ss, timestamp, session, promptData.gameplan || '', 'API ERROR: Opus overloaded, Sonnet fallback also failed', props);
      return;
    }
  }
  
  if (code !== 200) {
    Logger.log('Dashboard API ' + code + ': ' + body.substring(0, 500));
    writeDashboard_(ss, timestamp, session, promptData.gameplan || '', 'API ERROR (' + code + '): ' + body.substring(0, 200), props);
    return;
  }
  
  var result = JSON.parse(body);
  var narrative = '';
  for (var i = 0; i < result.content.length; i++) {
    if (result.content[i].type === 'text') {
      narrative += result.content[i].text;
    }
  }
  
  // Tag narrative with model used so dashboard can show it
  if (modelUsed.indexOf('sonnet') >= 0) {
    narrative = '<!-- model:sonnet -->\n' + narrative;
  }
  
  // Log usage for cost tracking
  var usage = result.usage || {};
  var inputTok = usage.input_tokens || 0;
  var outputTok = usage.output_tokens || 0;
  var opusCost = (inputTok / 1000000 * 5) + (outputTok / 1000000 * 25);
  var sonnetCost = (inputTok / 1000000 * 3) + (outputTok / 1000000 * 15);
  var costEst = modelUsed.indexOf('sonnet') >= 0 ? sonnetCost : opusCost;
  Logger.log('Dashboard API (' + modelUsed + '): ' + inputTok + ' in / ' + outputTok + ' out | ~$' + costEst.toFixed(4));
  
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // PHASE 4: Write to Dashboard tab + cache for doGet
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  
  writeDashboard_(ss, timestamp, session, promptData.gameplan || '', narrative, props);
  
  // Cache for live page polling
  props.setProperty('DASHBOARD_NARRATIVE', narrative);
  props.setProperty('DASHBOARD_TIMESTAMP', timestamp);
  props.setProperty('DASHBOARD_SESSION', session);
  props.setProperty('DASHBOARD_GAMEPLAN', promptData.gameplan || '');
  props.setProperty('DASHBOARD_COST', '$' + costEst.toFixed(4));
  props.setProperty('DASHBOARD_TOKENS', inputTok + ' in / ' + outputTok + ' out');
  // Cumulative session cost
  var prevCum = parseFloat(props.getProperty('DASHBOARD_COST_CUM') || '0');
  var newCum = prevCum + costEst;
  props.setProperty('DASHBOARD_COST_CUM', newCum.toFixed(4));

  // Hourly cost bucket (mirrors quota hourly tracking)
  var costBucketKey = 'APICOST_' + Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd_HH');
  var prevBucket = parseFloat(props.getProperty(costBucketKey) || '0');
  props.setProperty(costBucketKey, (prevBucket + costEst).toFixed(4));
  // Token tracking per hour
  var tokBucketKey = 'APITOK_' + Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd_HH');
  var prevTokBucket = JSON.parse(props.getProperty(tokBucketKey) || '{"in":0,"out":0,"calls":0}');
  prevTokBucket['in'] += inputTok; prevTokBucket['out'] += outputTok; prevTokBucket.calls += 1;
  props.setProperty(tokBucketKey, JSON.stringify(prevTokBucket));
  
  // ── First narrative of day (for retrospective) ──
  var azToday = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), 'America/Phoenix', 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  var firstNarDate = props.getProperty('FIRST_NARRATIVE_DATE') || '';
  if (firstNarDate !== azToday) {
    // New day — store this as the first narrative
    props.setProperty('FIRST_NARRATIVE_OF_DAY', narrative);
    props.setProperty('FIRST_NARRATIVE_DATE', azToday);
    props.setProperty('FIRST_NARRATIVE_TS', timestamp);
    props.setProperty('FIRST_NARRATIVE_SESSION', session);
    Logger.log('First narrative of day saved for ' + azToday);
  }
}

// ── Write narrative to Dashboard sheet tab ──

function writeDashboard_(ss, timestamp, session, gameplan, narrative, props) {
  var sheet = ss.getSheetByName('Dashboard');
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet('Dashboard');
    sheet.setTabColor('#0f3460');
    // Headers
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 4).setValues([['Timestamp', 'Session', 'Gameplan', 'Narrative']]);
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 4).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#0f3460').setFontColor('#00e5ff');
    sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 100);
    sheet.setColumnWidth(2, 70);
    sheet.setColumnWidth(3, 250);
    sheet.setColumnWidth(4, 800);
    sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  }
  
  // Append new row (newest at top, below header)
  sheet.insertRowAfter(1);
  sheet.getRange(2, 1, 1, 4).setValues([[timestamp, session, gameplan, narrative]]);
  sheet.getRange(2, 1, 1, 4)
    .setBackground('#1a1a2e')
    .setFontColor('#e0e0e0')
    .setFontFamily('Roboto Mono')
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment('top')
    .setWrapStrategy(SpreadsheetApp.WrapStrategy.WRAP);
  
  // Keep only last 50 narratives to prevent tab bloat
  var lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow > 51) {
    sheet.deleteRows(52, lastRow - 51);
  }
}

// ── Gmail Arete Email Pull (full week, stored by day) ──

function getAreteFromGmail_() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  
  // Cache for 2 hours
  var cacheTime = parseInt(props.getProperty('ARETE_GMAIL_CACHE_TIME') || '0');
  var cacheText = props.getProperty('ARETE_GMAIL_CACHE') || '';
  var age = Date.now() - cacheTime;
  
  if (cacheText && age < 7200000) {
    return cacheText; // Return most recent for Opus prompt (backward compat)
  }
  
  try {
    // Pull up to 7 emails from this week — Arete sends from ccsend.com, shows as Alpha Chasers
    // Search for Arete emails — forwarded body always contains arete@aretetrading.ccsend.com
    var threads = GmailApp.search('aretetrading.ccsend.com newer_than:7d', 0, 10);
    if (threads.length === 0) return null;
    
    var weekEmails = [];
    var latestText = '';
    
    for (var t = 0; t < threads.length; t++) {
      var messages = threads[t].getMessages();
      for (var m = 0; m < messages.length; m++) {
        var msg = messages[m];
        var subject = msg.getSubject() || '';
        var body = msg.getPlainBody() || '';
        var date = msg.getDate();
        var dateStr = Utilities.formatDate(date, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
        var dayName = Utilities.formatDate(date, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'EEEE');
        var timeStr = Utilities.formatDate(date, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'h:mm a');
        
        weekEmails.push({
          date: dateStr,
          day: dayName,
          time: timeStr,
          subject: subject,
          body: body, // full body — no truncation for dashboard
          bodyTrunc: body.length > 2000 ? body.substring(0, 2000) + '\n... [truncated]' : body
        });
      }
    }
    
    // Sort newest first
    weekEmails.sort(function(a, b) { return b.date.localeCompare(a.date) || b.time.localeCompare(a.time); });
    
    // Dedupe by date+subject (same email in thread)
    var seen = {};
    var deduped = [];
    for (var d = 0; d < weekEmails.length; d++) {
      var key = weekEmails[d].date + '|' + weekEmails[d].subject;
      if (!seen[key]) { seen[key] = true; deduped.push(weekEmails[d]); }
    }
    
    // Store full week for dashboard
    props.setProperty('ARETE_EMAILS_WEEK', JSON.stringify(deduped));
    props.setProperty('ARETE_EMAILS_WEEK_TIME', Date.now().toString());
    
    // Most recent email for Opus prompt (backward compat)
    if (deduped.length > 0) {
      latestText = 'Subject: ' + deduped[0].subject + '\n\n' + deduped[0].bodyTrunc;
    }
    
    // Cache latest for backward compat
    props.setProperty('ARETE_GMAIL_CACHE', latestText);
    props.setProperty('ARETE_GMAIL_CACHE_TIME', Date.now().toString());
    
    return latestText;
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('Arete Gmail error: ' + e.message);
    return null;
  }
}

// ── Dashboard data endpoint (for live HTML page polling) ──

function getDashboardData() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var t0 = Date.now();
  var state = getTimerState();
  var t1 = Date.now(); // Existing scanner data (market, sectors, news, breadth, history)
  
  // ── Dashboard Narrative (from Claude Opus API) ──
  state.dashboardNarrative = props.getProperty('DASHBOARD_NARRATIVE') || '';
  state.dashboardTimestamp = props.getProperty('DASHBOARD_TIMESTAMP') || '';
  state.dashboardSession = props.getProperty('DASHBOARD_SESSION') || '';
  state.dashboardGameplan = props.getProperty('DASHBOARD_GAMEPLAN') || '';
  state.dashboardCost = props.getProperty('DASHBOARD_COST') || '';
  state.dashboardTokens = props.getProperty('DASHBOARD_TOKENS') || '';
  state.dashboardCostCum = props.getProperty('DASHBOARD_COST_CUM') || '';
  state.dashboardTokens = props.getProperty('DASHBOARD_TOKENS') || '';
  
  // ── Arete Emails (full week for dashboard display) ──
  // Refresh independently of Opus narrative — 2hr cache
  try {
    var areteWeekTime = parseInt(props.getProperty('ARETE_EMAILS_WEEK_TIME') || '0');
    var areteAge = Date.now() - areteWeekTime;
    if (areteAge > 7200000 || !props.getProperty('ARETE_EMAILS_WEEK')) {
      Logger.log('Arete emails: refreshing (age=' + Math.round(areteAge/60000) + 'min, hasCache=' + !!props.getProperty('ARETE_EMAILS_WEEK') + ')');
      try { 
        getAreteFromGmail_();
        Logger.log('Arete emails: refresh complete, count=' + (JSON.parse(props.getProperty('ARETE_EMAILS_WEEK') || '[]')).length);
      } catch(ag) { 
        Logger.log('Arete emails ERROR: ' + ag.message + ' | stack: ' + ag.stack);
        state.areteEmailError = ag.message;
      }
    }
    var areteWeekRaw = props.getProperty('ARETE_EMAILS_WEEK');
    if (areteWeekRaw) {
      state.areteEmails = JSON.parse(areteWeekRaw);
      Logger.log('Arete emails: sending ' + state.areteEmails.length + ' to dashboard');
    } else {
      state.areteEmails = [];
      Logger.log('Arete emails: EMPTY — no ARETE_EMAILS_WEEK in properties');
    }
  } catch(ae) { 
    state.areteEmails = []; 
    state.areteEmailError = ae.message;
    Logger.log('Arete emails OUTER ERROR: ' + ae.message);
  }
  
  // ── First narrative of day (for retrospective) ──
  var azToday = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), 'America/Phoenix', 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  var firstNarDate = props.getProperty('FIRST_NARRATIVE_DATE') || '';
  if (firstNarDate === azToday) {
    state.firstNarrativeOfDay = props.getProperty('FIRST_NARRATIVE_OF_DAY') || '';
    state.firstNarrativeTs = props.getProperty('FIRST_NARRATIVE_TS') || '';
    state.firstNarrativeSession = props.getProperty('FIRST_NARRATIVE_SESSION') || '';
  }
  
  // ── Institutional Pulse (from Market tab pulse module) ──
  try {
    var pulseRaw = props.getProperty(PULSE_CACHE_PROP);
    if (pulseRaw) {
      var pulse = JSON.parse(pulseRaw);
      state.instPulse = {
        data:      pulse.data      || {},
        narrative: pulse.narrative || {},
        ts:        pulse.ts        || 0
      };
      // Previous day snapshot for change indicators
      var prevSnapRaw = props.getProperty('PULSE_PREV_SNAP');
      if (prevSnapRaw) {
        try { state.instPulsePrev = JSON.parse(prevSnapRaw); } catch(epp) {}
      }
    }
  } catch(ep) {
    Logger.log('getDashboardData pulse parse error: ' + ep);
  }
  
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  
  // ── Positions from My Positions tab ──
  // Structure: Row 0 = LIVE TOTAL, then per-account sections with ━━ LABEL ━━ headers,
  // then headers row, then data rows. Tag summary sections at bottom.
  // We separate MY live/paper positions from Arete/carry sections by account type.
  try {
    var posSheet = ss.getSheetByName('My Positions');
    if (posSheet) {
      var posVals = posSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      var myPositions = [];  // User's actual positions
      var currentAccount = '';
      var currentType = '';   // DT, SW, PAPER, CASH
      var inTagSection = false;
      var fmtNum = function(v) {
        var n = parseFloat(String(v).replace(/[,$]/g, ''));
        if (isNaN(n)) return '—';
        return n.toFixed(2);
      };
      var fmtPct = function(v) {
        var n = parseFloat(v);
        if (isNaN(n)) return '—';
        return (n >= 0 ? '+' : '') + (n * 100).toFixed(2) + '%';
      };
      var fmtDollar = function(v) {
        var n = parseFloat(String(v).replace(/[,$]/g, ''));
        if (isNaN(n)) return '—';
        return (n >= 0 ? '+$' : '-$') + Math.abs(n).toFixed(2);
      };
      
      for (var i = 0; i < posVals.length; i++) {
        var col0 = String(posVals[i][0]).trim();
        if (!col0) continue;
        
        // Skip LIVE TOTAL header
        if (col0.indexOf('LIVE TOTAL') >= 0) continue;
        
        // Detect Tag Summary sections — stop processing
        if (col0.indexOf('TAG PERFORMANCE') >= 0 || col0.indexOf('PAPER TAG') >= 0) {
          inTagSection = true;
          continue;
        }
        if (inTagSection) continue;
        
        // Detect account section headers: ━━ SWING (SW) ━━  #12345
        if (col0.indexOf('━━') >= 0) {
          currentAccount = col0.replace(/━/g, '').replace(/#\d+/g, '').trim();
          // Determine type from label
          if (col0.indexOf('DAY TRADE') >= 0 && col0.indexOf('CARRY') >= 0) currentType = 'ARETE_DT';
          else if (col0.indexOf('ARETE') >= 0 && col0.indexOf('SWING') >= 0) currentType = 'ARETE_SW';
          else if (col0.indexOf('ARETE') >= 0 && col0.indexOf('WATCH') >= 0) currentType = 'ARETE_WATCH';
          else if (col0.indexOf('DAY TRADE') >= 0) currentType = 'DT';
          else if (col0.indexOf('SWING') >= 0) currentType = 'SW';
          else if (col0.indexOf('PAPER') >= 0) currentType = 'PAPER';
          else if (col0.indexOf('CASH') >= 0) currentType = 'CASH';
          else currentType = 'LIVE';
          continue;
        }
        
        // Skip header rows and empty markers
        if (col0 === 'Ticker' || col0 === 'Tag' || col0 === '(no open positions)') continue;
        if (col0.indexOf('Updated') >= 0 || col0.indexOf('NLV') >= 0) continue;
        
        // This should be a data row: Ticker, Account, Side, Shares, Avg Cost, Last, Mkt Value, Day P&L $, Day P&L %, Total P&L $, Total P&L %, Cost Basis, Tag
        var ticker = col0;
        // Validate it looks like a ticker (1-5 uppercase letters)
        if (!/^[A-Z]{1,5}$/.test(ticker)) continue;
        
        var side = String(posVals[i][2] || '');
        if (side !== 'Long' && side !== 'Short') continue; // Skip non-position rows
        
        myPositions.push({
          ticker: ticker,
          account: currentAccount,
          accountType: currentType,
          side: side,
          shares: String(posVals[i][3] || '0'),
          avgCost: fmtNum(posVals[i][4]),
          last: fmtNum(posVals[i][5]),
          mktValue: fmtDollar(posVals[i][6]),
          dayPL: fmtDollar(posVals[i][7]),
          dayPLPct: fmtPct(posVals[i][8]),
          totalPL: fmtDollar(posVals[i][9]),
          totalPLPct: fmtPct(posVals[i][10]),
          costBasis: fmtNum(posVals[i][11]),
          tag: String(posVals[i][12] || '')
        });
      }
      // Split into: live positions and paper trades
      var livePos = [], paperPos = [];
      for (var p = 0; p < myPositions.length; p++) {
        var at = myPositions[p].accountType;
        if (at === 'PAPER') paperPos.push(myPositions[p]);
        else if (at === 'DT' || at === 'SW' || at === 'CASH' || at === 'LIVE') livePos.push(myPositions[p]);
        // Skip ARETE_SW, ARETE_DT, ARETE_WATCH — those come from Arete Trades tab
      }
      state.positions = livePos;
      state.paperPositions = paperPos;
    }
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('Dashboard positions read: ' + e.message);
    state.positions = [];
  }
  
  // ── Top Confluence from Watchlist tab ──
  // Columns: A=Section, B=Sector, C=Name, D=Ticker, E=Last, F=Chg%,
  // G=Confluence, H=Quality, I=Setup, J-N=sub-scores, O-R=mods, S-V=flags, ...
  try {
    var wl = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
    if (wl) {
      var wlVals = wl.getDataRange().getValues();
      var watchTop = [];
      // Row 0 = GP banner (merged), Row 1 = group headers, Row 2 = column headers, Row 3+ = data
      var startRow = 3; // Skip GP banner + group headers + column headers
      // Verify by finding 'Section' in col A
      for (var i = 0; i < Math.min(wlVals.length, 5); i++) {
        if (String(wlVals[i][0]).trim() === 'Section') { startRow = i + 1; break; }
      }
      for (var i = startRow; i < wlVals.length; i++) {
        var section = String(wlVals[i][0] || '').trim();
        var ticker = String(wlVals[i][3] || '').trim();
        if (!ticker || !/^[A-Z]{1,5}$/.test(ticker)) continue;
        var confluence = parseFloat(wlVals[i][6]) || 0;
        var quality = String(wlVals[i][7] || '');
        var setup = String(wlVals[i][8] || '');
        watchTop.push({
          ticker: ticker,
          name: String(wlVals[i][2] || ''),
          section: section,
          sector: String(wlVals[i][1] || ''),
          last: String(wlVals[i][4] || ''),
          chg: String(wlVals[i][5] || ''),
          confluence: confluence,
          quality: quality,
          setup: setup
        });
      }
      // Sort by confluence descending
      watchTop.sort(function(a, b) { return b.confluence - a.confluence; });
      state.watchlistTop = watchTop;
      
      // Build tickerQuotes from watchlist data (price + change for all tickers)
      var tq = {};
      for (var i = startRow; i < wlVals.length; i++) {
        var tk = String(wlVals[i][3] || '').trim();
        if (!tk || !/^[A-Z]{1,5}$/.test(tk)) continue;
        var last = String(wlVals[i][4] || '');
        var chg = String(wlVals[i][5] || '');
        if (!last) continue;
        tq[tk] = {
          last: last,
          chg: chg,
          rs: String(wlVals[i][24] || ''),       // RelStr%
          rvol: String(wlVals[i][26] || ''),      // RVOL
          rsi: String(wlVals[i][25] || ''),       // RSI(5m)
          atr: String(wlVals[i][29] || ''),       // ATR
          gap: String(wlVals[i][30] || ''),       // Gap%
          w52: String(wlVals[i][42] || ''),       // 52w %
          ema50d: String(wlVals[i][44] || ''),    // EMA50 Dist%
          vwapF: String(wlVals[i][19] || ''),     // VWAP Flag
          rsF: String(wlVals[i][20] || ''),       // RS Flag
          rsiF: String(wlVals[i][21] || ''),      // RSI Flag
          rvolF: String(wlVals[i][22] || ''),     // RVOL Flag
          vwap: String(wlVals[i][23] || ''),      // VWAP price
          ema9: String(wlVals[i][27] || ''),      // EMA9
          ema20: String(wlVals[i][28] || ''),     // EMA20
          vol: String(wlVals[i][36] || ''),       // Volume
          avgVol: String(wlVals[i][45] || ''),    // AvgVol
          conf: String(wlVals[i][6] || ''),       // Confluence score
          setup: String(wlVals[i][8] || ''),      // Setup name
          orHi: String(wlVals[i][31] || ''),      // Opening Range Hi
          orLo: String(wlVals[i][32] || '')       // Opening Range Lo
        };
      }
      state.tickerQuotes = tq;
    }
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('Dashboard watchlist read: ' + e.message);
    state.watchlistTop = [];
  }
  
  // ── Economic Calendar (from Market tab cols F-M, written by fetchEconomicCalendar) ──
  try {
    var breadthSheet2 = ss.getSheetByName('Market');
    if (breadthSheet2) {
      var lastEcoRow = breadthSheet2.getLastRow();
      if (lastEcoRow >= 4) {
        var ecoRange = breadthSheet2.getRange(3, 6, lastEcoRow - 2, 8).getValues();
        var ecoEvents = [];
        for (var i = 1; i < ecoRange.length; i++) {
          var title = String(ecoRange[i][0] || '').trim();
          if (!title) continue;
          if (title.indexOf('\u2500') >= 0 || title.indexOf('\u2501') >= 0 || title.match(/^[A-Z]+DAY$/)) {
            ecoEvents.push({ isSep: true, title: title.replace(/[\u2500\u2501\u2014]/g, '').trim() });
            continue;
          }
          ecoEvents.push({
            title: title,
            time: String(ecoRange[i][1] || '').trim(),
            impact: String(ecoRange[i][2] || '').trim(),
            previous: String(ecoRange[i][3] || '').trim(),
            forecast: String(ecoRange[i][4] || '').trim(),
            actual: String(ecoRange[i][5] || '').trim(),
            tickers: String(ecoRange[i][7] || '').trim()
          });
        }
        if (ecoEvents.length > 0) state.ecoEvents = ecoEvents;
      }
    }
  } catch(ecoErr) {
    Logger.log('Dashboard ecoEvents read: ' + ecoErr.message);
  }


  // ── Earnings This Week (Finnhub, 3-tier filter) ──
  // Tier 1 (green): positions + arete + watching = always show
  // Tier 2 (blue):  Watchlist tab col AU = always show
  // Tier 3 (fallback): if T1+T2 = 0, show top 20 by revenue estimate
  try {
    // Tier 1: positions + arete + watching
    var t1 = {};
    if (state.positions) { for (var i = 0; i < state.positions.length; i++) t1[state.positions[i].ticker] = 1; }
    if (state.paperPositions) { for (var i = 0; i < state.paperPositions.length; i++) t1[state.paperPositions[i].ticker] = 1; }
    if (state.aretePositions) { for (var i = 0; i < state.aretePositions.length; i++) t1[state.aretePositions[i].ticker] = 1; }
    if (state.myWatching) { for (var i = 0; i < state.myWatching.length; i++) t1[state.myWatching[i]] = 1; }
    if (state.areteWatching) { for (var i = 0; i < state.areteWatching.length; i++) t1[state.areteWatching[i]] = 1; }
    if (state.watchlistTop) { for (var i = 0; i < state.watchlistTop.length; i++) { if (state.watchlistTop[i].ticker) t1[state.watchlistTop[i].ticker] = 1; } }

    // Tier 2: Watchlist tab col AU (unfiltered master list 440+)
    var t2 = {};
    var wlSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
    if (wlSheet) {
      var wlLastRow = wlSheet.getLastRow();
      if (wlLastRow > 1) {
        var wlTickers = wlSheet.getRange(2, 47, wlLastRow - 1, 1).getValues();
        for (var i = 0; i < wlTickers.length; i++) {
          var tk = String(wlTickers[i][0] || '').trim();
          if (tk && tk.length <= 6 && tk === tk.toUpperCase()) t2[tk] = 1;
        }
      }
    }
    Logger.log('Earnings filter: T1=' + Object.keys(t1).length + ' T2=' + Object.keys(t2).length);

    // Merge for watchlistSymbols (dashboard highlighting)
    var allKnown = {};
    var t1k = Object.keys(t1); for (var i = 0; i < t1k.length; i++) allKnown[t1k[i]] = 1;
    var t2k = Object.keys(t2); for (var i = 0; i < t2k.length; i++) allKnown[t2k[i]] = 1;
    state.watchlistSymbols = { all: Object.keys(allKnown), autoPass: Object.keys(t1) };

    var earningsRaw = props.getProperty('EARNINGS_WEEK_CACHE') || '';
    var earningsCacheAge = parseInt(props.getProperty('EARNINGS_WEEK_TS') || '0');
    var cacheMaxAge = 4 * 60 * 60 * 1000;

    if (earningsRaw && (Date.now() - earningsCacheAge) < cacheMaxAge) {
      state.earnings = JSON.parse(earningsRaw);
    } else {
      var key = getFinnhubKey();
      if (key) {
        var now2 = new Date();
        var monday = new Date(now2);
        monday.setDate(now2.getDate() - ((now2.getDay() + 6) % 7));
        var friday = new Date(monday);
        friday.setDate(monday.getDate() + 4);
        var fromStr = Utilities.formatDate(monday, 'America/Phoenix', 'yyyy-MM-dd');
        var toStr = Utilities.formatDate(friday, 'America/Phoenix', 'yyyy-MM-dd');

        var resp = UrlFetchApp.fetch(
          'https://finnhub.io/api/v1/calendar/earnings?from=' + fromStr + '&to=' + toStr + '&token=' + key,
          { muteHttpExceptions: true }
        );

        if (resp.getResponseCode() === 200) {
          var data = JSON.parse(resp.getContentText());
          var ec = data.earningsCalendar || [];
          var dayNames = ['Sunday','Monday','Tuesday','Wednesday','Thursday','Friday','Saturday'];

          ec.sort(function(a,b) {
            if (a.date !== b.date) return a.date < b.date ? -1 : 1;
            return (a.hour || 0) - (b.hour || 0);
          });

          function buildEarnEntry(er, tier) {
            var sym = er.symbol || '';
            var dateObj = new Date(er.date + 'T12:00:00');
            var dayName = dayNames[dateObj.getDay()];
            var timeLabel = '';
            if (er.hour === 0 || er.hour === 'bmo') timeLabel = 'Pre-Market';
            else if (er.hour === 1 || er.hour === 'amc') timeLabel = 'Post-Market';
            else timeLabel = String(er.hour || '\u2014');
            var note = '';
            if (er.epsEstimate != null) note = 'Est: $' + er.epsEstimate;
            if (er.revenueEstimate != null) {
              var revB = (er.revenueEstimate / 1e9).toFixed(1);
              note += (note ? ' | ' : '') + 'Rev: $' + revB + 'B';
            }
            var entry = { symbol: sym, day: dayName, time: timeLabel, note: note, date: er.date, tier: tier };
            if (er.epsActual != null) entry.epsActual = er.epsActual;
            if (er.revenueActual != null) entry.revenueActual = er.revenueActual;
            return entry;
          }

          // Pass 1: filter T1 + T2
          var filtered = [];
          var allEntries = [];
          for (var i = 0; i < ec.length; i++) {
            var sym = ec[i].symbol || '';
            if (!sym) continue;
            if (t1[sym]) {
              filtered.push(buildEarnEntry(ec[i], 'mine'));
            } else if (t2[sym]) {
              filtered.push(buildEarnEntry(ec[i], 'watchlist'));
            }
            allEntries.push(ec[i]);
