          }

          // Fallback: if T1+T2 = 0, top 20 by revenue estimate
          // Enhancement v90.5: ALWAYS add top 20 (deduped) so there's always market context
          var earnings = filtered;
          var seenSyms = {};
          for (var s = 0; s < filtered.length; s++) seenSyms[filtered[s].symbol] = 1;
          
          if (allEntries.length > 0) {
            allEntries.sort(function(a,b) {
              return (b.revenueEstimate || 0) - (a.revenueEstimate || 0);
            });
            var top20 = allEntries.slice(0, 20);
            top20.sort(function(a,b) {
              if (a.date !== b.date) return a.date < b.date ? -1 : 1;
              return (a.hour || 0) - (b.hour || 0);
            });
            for (var i = 0; i < top20.length; i++) {
              var topSym = top20[i].symbol || '';
              if (!seenSyms[topSym]) {
                earnings.push(buildEarnEntry(top20[i], filtered.length === 0 ? 'top20' : 'market'));
                seenSyms[topSym] = 1;
              }
            }
          }

          Logger.log('Earnings: ' + ec.length + ' total, ' + filtered.length + ' matched, ' + earnings.length + ' final');

          if (earnings.length > 0) {
            props.setProperty('EARNINGS_WEEK_CACHE', JSON.stringify(earnings));
            props.setProperty('EARNINGS_WEEK_TS', String(Date.now()));
            state.earnings = earnings;
          }
        }
      }
    }

    if (!state.earnings) {
      var oldCache = props.getProperty('EARNINGS_CACHE') || '';
      if (oldCache) state.earnings = JSON.parse(oldCache);
    }
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('Dashboard earnings fetch: ' + e.message);
  }

  // ── IC Slugs (from IC Slugs tab, cached in script property) ──
  try {
    var slugCache = props.getProperty('IC_SLUGS_CACHE') || '';
    if (slugCache) {
      state.icSlugs = JSON.parse(slugCache);
    } else {
      var slugSheet = ss.getSheetByName('IC Slugs');
      if (slugSheet && slugSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
        var slugData = slugSheet.getRange(2, 1, slugSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 2).getValues();
        var slugMap = {};
        for (var i = 0; i < slugData.length; i++) {
          var tk = String(slugData[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
          var path = String(slugData[i][1] || '').trim();
          if (tk && path) slugMap[tk] = path;
        }
        if (Object.keys(slugMap).length > 0) {
          state.icSlugs = slugMap;
          props.setProperty('IC_SLUGS_CACHE', JSON.stringify(slugMap));
        }
      }
    }
  } catch(slugErr) {
    Logger.log('IC Slugs read: ' + slugErr.message);
  }

  // ── Watching from Config tab ──
  // Config format: Col A = section headers, Col B = tickers, Col C = notes/tags
  try {
    var myWatching = [], areteWatching = [];
    var config = ss.getSheetByName('Config');
    if (config) {
      var cfgVals = config.getDataRange().getValues();
      var section = '';
      var CONFIG_SECTIONS = {'WATCHING':1,'MY WATCHING':1,'MY_WATCHING':1,'ARETE_WATCHING':1,'ARETE WATCHING':1,
        'ARETE SWING':1,'ARETE_SWINGS':1,'ARETE SWINGS':1,'SWING TRADES':1,
        'DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS':1,'DAYTRADE CARRY OVERS':1,'DT CARRY OVERS':1,'ARETE_CARRIES':1,'ARETE CARRIES':1,
        'ARETE DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS':1,'ARETE DAYTRADE CARRY OVERS':1,
        'MY POSITIONS':1,'PAPER TRADES':1,'PAPER':1,'SECTION':1};
      for (var i = 0; i < cfgVals.length; i++) {
        var colA = String(cfgVals[i][0] || '').trim();
        var colAUC = colA.toUpperCase();
        var colB = String(cfgVals[i][1] || '').trim();
        if (colAUC.indexOf('===') >= 0 || colAUC.indexOf('───') >= 0) { section = ''; continue; }
        // Check if Col A is a section header
        if (colA && CONFIG_SECTIONS[colAUC]) {
          if (colAUC === 'WATCHING' || colAUC === 'MY WATCHING' || colAUC === 'MY_WATCHING') section = 'mywatch';
          else if (colAUC === 'ARETE_WATCHING' || colAUC === 'ARETE WATCHING') section = 'aretewatch';
          else section = '';
          continue;
        }
        // Ticker is in Col B
        if (!colB) continue;
        var ticker = colB.toUpperCase();
        if (ticker === 'TICKER' || ticker === 'STOCK TICKER') continue;
        if (section === 'mywatch') myWatching.push(ticker);
        else if (section === 'aretewatch') areteWatching.push(ticker);
      }
    }
    state.myWatching = myWatching;
    state.areteWatching = areteWatching;
  } catch(e) { Logger.log('Dashboard watching: ' + e.message); }
  
  // ── Arete Book from ARETE TRADES tab ──
  // One book: Swing, DTC, Option, Long (skip Special Situations)
  // A=flags/headers, B=ticker, C=entry date, D=entry price, E=target, F=price, G=trim, H=stop, I=stop2, J=risk, K=notes, L=thesis
  try {
    var aretePositions = [];
    var areteSheet = ss.getSheetByName('ARETE TRADES');
    if (areteSheet && areteSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var lastCol = Math.max(areteSheet.getLastColumn(), 12);
      var arVals = areteSheet.getRange(1, 1, areteSheet.getLastRow(), lastCol).getValues();
      var arTag = '';
      var FLAG_WORDS = {'NEW':1,'UPDATE':1,'UPDATED':1,'REMOVED':1,'CLOSED':1};
      var SECTION_MAP = {
        'SWING TRADES': 'Swing',
        'DAYTRADE CARRY OVERS': 'DTC', 'DAYTRADE CARRYOVERS': 'DTC',
        'DAY TRADE CARRY OVERS': 'DTC', 'DT CARRY OVERS': 'DTC',
        'OPTIONS': 'Option',
        'LONG TERM POSITIONS': 'Long', 'LONG TERM': 'Long'
      };
      var SKIP_SECTIONS = {'SPECIAL SITUATIONS':1, 'LEGEND':1, 'LAST UPDATED':1};
      for (var i = 0; i < arVals.length; i++) {
        var colA = String(arVals[i][0] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        var colB = String(arVals[i][1] || '').trim();
        if (!colA && !colB) continue;
        var foundSection = false;
        var sKeys = Object.keys(SECTION_MAP);
        for (var sk = 0; sk < sKeys.length; sk++) {
          if (colA === sKeys[sk] || colA.indexOf(sKeys[sk]) === 0) { arTag = SECTION_MAP[sKeys[sk]]; foundSection = true; break; }
        }
        if (foundSection) continue;
        var skipKeys = Object.keys(SKIP_SECTIONS);
        for (var sk2 = 0; sk2 < skipKeys.length; sk2++) {
          if (colA === skipKeys[sk2] || colA.indexOf(skipKeys[sk2]) === 0) { arTag = ''; foundSection = true; break; }
        }
        if (foundSection) continue;
        if (colA && !FLAG_WORDS[colA] && colA.charAt(0) !== '(') { arTag = ''; continue; }
        if (arTag && colB) {
          var ticker = colB.replace(/\s*\(.*?\)\s*/g, '').trim().toUpperCase();
          if (!ticker || ticker === 'STOCK TICKER' || ticker === 'TICKER' || ticker === 'BUT WE NEED') continue;
          var displayName = ticker;
          if (arTag === 'Option') {
            displayName = colB.trim().toUpperCase();
            var rootMatch = colB.match(/^([A-Z]{1,5})\b/i);
            if (rootMatch) ticker = rootMatch[1].toUpperCase();
          }
          var anno = colB.match(/\(([^)]+)\)/);
          var entryDate = '';
          var entryDateObj = null;
          if (arVals[i][2] instanceof Date) { 
            entryDateObj = arVals[i][2];
            entryDate = (arVals[i][2].getMonth()+1) + '/' + arVals[i][2].getDate(); 
          } else if (arVals[i][2]) { entryDate = String(arVals[i][2]).trim(); }
          var entryPrice = '';
          if (typeof arVals[i][3] === 'number' && arVals[i][3] > 0) entryPrice = '$' + arVals[i][3].toFixed(2);
          else if (arVals[i][3]) { var ep = String(arVals[i][3]).trim(); if (ep && ep !== '0') entryPrice = ep; }
          var stopLoss = '';
          if (typeof arVals[i][7] === 'number' && arVals[i][7] > 0) stopLoss = '$' + arVals[i][7].toFixed(2);
          else if (arVals[i][7]) { var sl = String(arVals[i][7]).trim(); if (sl && sl !== '0') stopLoss = sl; }
          var note = String(arVals[i][10] || '').trim();
          var thesis = arVals[i].length > 11 ? String(arVals[i][11] || '').trim() : '';
          var flag = FLAG_WORDS[colA] ? colA : '';
          // Col F (index 5) = current price from Arete sheet
          var curPrice = '';
          if (typeof arVals[i][5] === 'number' && arVals[i][5] > 0) curPrice = arVals[i][5].toFixed(2);
          else if (arVals[i][5]) { var cp = String(arVals[i][5]).trim(); if (cp && cp !== '0' && cp !== '$0.00') curPrice = cp.replace('$',''); }
          aretePositions.push({ ticker: ticker, displayName: displayName || ticker, side: anno ? anno[1] : '', entry: entryPrice, date: entryDate, dateObj: entryDateObj ? entryDateObj.getTime() : 0, stop: stopLoss, note: note, thesis: thesis, flag: flag, tag: arTag, curPrice: curPrice });
        }
      }
      aretePositions.sort(function(a, b) { return (b.dateObj || 0) - (a.dateObj || 0); });
    }
    state.aretePositions = aretePositions;
    
    // ── Merge Arete position tickers into tickerQuotes (for dashboard enrichment) ──
    if (state.tickerQuotes && aretePositions.length) {
      for (var ai = 0; ai < aretePositions.length; ai++) {
        var atk = aretePositions[ai].ticker;
        if (atk && !state.tickerQuotes[atk] && aretePositions[ai].curPrice) {
          state.tickerQuotes[atk] = { last: aretePositions[ai].curPrice, chg: '' };
        }
      }
    }
  } catch(e) { Logger.log('Dashboard arete trades: ' + e.message); }
  
  // ── Section timestamps ──
  state.positionsUpdated = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), 'America/Phoenix', 'h:mm a');
  state.areteUpdated = state.positionsUpdated;
  
  // ── Sparkline data from _Spark tab ──
  try {
    var sparkSheet = ss.getSheetByName('_Spark');
    if (sparkSheet && sparkSheet.getLastRow() > 1 && sparkSheet.getLastColumn() > 1) {
      var sparkAll = sparkSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      var sparkData = {};
      // Row 0 = header: [date, ticker1, ticker2, ...]
      // Row 1+ = [slot_minute, price1, price2, ...]
      var hdr = sparkAll[0];
      for (var c = 1; c < hdr.length; c++) {
        var tk = String(hdr[c]).trim();
        if (!tk) continue;
        var pts = [];
        for (var r = 1; r < sparkAll.length; r++) {
          var v = sparkAll[r][c];
          if (v && typeof v === 'number' && v > 0) {
            pts.push(v);
          } else {
            pts.push(null);
          }
        }
        // Only include if there's at least one data point
        var hasData = false;
        for (var p = 0; p < pts.length; p++) { if (pts[p]) { hasData = true; break; } }
        if (hasData) sparkData[tk] = pts;
      }
      state.sparkData = sparkData;
    }
  } catch(sparkE) { Logger.log('Spark read: ' + sparkE.message); }
  
  state._timing = 'getTimerState:' + (t1-t0) + 'ms, getDashboardData total:' + (Date.now()-t0) + 'ms';
  
  // ── GP Trajectory & Sub-Mode (v90.5) ──
  try {
    var trajRaw = props.getProperty('GP_TRAJECTORY');
    if (trajRaw) state.gpTrajectory = JSON.parse(trajRaw);
    var subModeRaw = props.getProperty('GP_SUB_MODE');
    if (subModeRaw) state.gpSubMode = JSON.parse(subModeRaw);
  } catch(trajE) { Logger.log('Dashboard trajectory read: ' + trajE.message); }
  
  // ── In Play Today (v90.5) ──
  try {
    var inPlayRaw = props.getProperty('IN_PLAY_TODAY');
    if (inPlayRaw) state.inPlayToday = JSON.parse(inPlayRaw);
    // Hot sectors (from last refresh)
    var hotRaw = props.getProperty('HOT_SECTORS');
    if (hotRaw) state.hotSectors = JSON.parse(hotRaw);
    // Dynamic watchlist tickers for dashboard ⚡ badges
    try {
      var dynItems = _readDynamic(ss);
      var dynMap = {};
      for (var dmi = 0; dmi < dynItems.length; dmi++) {
        dynMap[dynItems[dmi].symbol] = { source: dynItems[dmi].source, reason: dynItems[dmi].reason };
      }
      state.dynamicTickers = dynMap;
    } catch(dte) { state.dynamicTickers = {}; }
  } catch(ipE) { Logger.log('Dashboard inPlay read: ' + ipE.message); }
  
  return state;
}

// ==================== NOTES TAB BUILDER v4 ====================
// Batch data write + efficient merge/height pass. 

function buildNotesTab() {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var ex = ss.getSheetByName('Notes');
  if (ex) ss.deleteSheet(ex);
  var sh = ss.insertSheet('Notes');
  sh.setTabColor('#1a1a2e');

  var D='#1a1a2e',S='#16213e',H='#0f3460';
  var G='#00e676',R='#ff5252',Y='#ffd740',C='#00e5ff',W='#e0e0e0';
  var DM='#9e9e9e',O='#ff9100',P='#bb86fc';

  var vals=[],bgs=[],fcs=[],wts=[],htArr=[],mergeRows=[];

  function add(v,bg,fc,wt,ht,merge){
    vals.push([v[0]||'',v[1]||'',v[2]||'',v[3]||'']);
    bgs.push(bg||[D,D,D,D]);
    fcs.push(fc||[W,W,W,W]);
    wts.push(wt||['bold','normal','normal','normal']);
    htArr.push(ht||24);
    if(merge) mergeRows.push(vals.length); // 1-indexed row
  }
  function sec(t){add([t,'','',''],[H,H,H,H],[C,C,C,C],['bold','bold','bold','bold'],36,true)}
  function sub(t){add([t,'','',''],[S,S,S,S],[Y,Y,Y,Y],['bold','bold','bold','bold'],28,true)}
  function hdr(a,b,c,d){add([a,b,c,d],[S,S,S,S],[C,C,C,C],['bold','bold','bold','bold'],22)}
  function row(v,fc){var bg=(vals.length%2===0)?[S,S,S,S]:[D,D,D,D];add(v,bg,fc||[W,W,W,W],['bold','normal','normal','normal'],24)}
  function note(t,c){add([t,'','',''],[D,D,D,D],[c||DM,c||DM,c||DM,c||DM],['normal','normal','normal','normal'],34,true)}
  function gap(){add(['','','',''],[D,D,D,D],[D,D,D,D],['normal','normal','normal','normal'],10)}

  // ═══ TITLE ═══
  add(['V9 TRADING SYSTEM — QUICK REFERENCE','','',''],[D,D,D,D],[G,G,G,G],['bold','bold','bold','bold'],44,true);
  add(['The System Protects You. Follow It.','','',''],[D,D,D,D],[R,R,R,R],['bold','bold','bold','bold'],30,true);
  gap();

  // ═══ 1. GAMEPLAN ═══
  sec('① GAMEPLAN QUICK REFERENCE');
  hdr('Gameplan','Score / Threshold','Size / Risk','Action');
  row(['A — HUNT MODE','≥ +9.5 pts (≥67%)','$15K–$20K / $150–200','LONG — all setups valid'],[G,W,W,G]);
  row(['B — SNIPER MODE','+3 to +9.5 (45–67%)','$8K–$12K / $100–150','LONG — high confluence only'],[Y,W,W,Y]);
  row(['C — SELECTIVE','−3 to +3 (24–45%)','$0–$6K (sub-mode)','Check trajectory: Recovery/Flat/Deteriorating'],[O,W,O,O]);
  row(['D — SHORT MODE','≤ −3 pts (<24%)','$8K–$12K / $100–150','Inverse ETFs or sit out'],[R,W,W,R]);
  gap();

  // ═══ 2. SETUPS ═══
  sec('② SETUP RULES (6 Setups)');
  sub('VWAP-Hold');
  hdr('Criteria','Value','Stop','Target');
  row(['Price','Above VWAP, close (<0.5%)','1.5× ATR below entry','3.0× ATR above entry']);
  row(['EMA / RSI','Above EMA9 · RSI 40–60','','']);
  row(['Idea','VWAP as institutional support — price respecting it','','']);
  gap();
  sub('OR-Break');
  row(['Price','Breaks above Opening Range High','Below OR High','3.0× ATR above']);
  row(['Filters','RVOL ≥ 1.5× · RSI < 75','','']);
  row(['Idea','First 15-min range resolved upside with volume','','']);
  gap();
  sub('Pullback-EMA');
  row(['Price','Pulled back to EMA 9/20 zone','Below EMA20','3.0× ATR above']);
  row(['Filters','EMA9 > EMA20 stacked · RSI 35–55','','']);
  row(['Idea','Trend intact, healthy pullback to MA support','','']);
  gap();
  sub('Momentum');
  row(['Price','Above EMA9, EMA9 > EMA20','1.5× ATR below','3.0× ATR above']);
  row(['Filters','RSI 55–75 · RVOL ≥1.5× · RelStr ≥1%','','']);
  row(['Idea','Strong name getting stronger — ride institutional wave','','']);
  gap();
  sub('Failed-Breakdown');
  row(['Price','Broke below OR Low, reclaimed it + VWAP','Below OR Low re-break','VWAP → OR High']);
  row(['Idea','Bears trapped — forced covering drives price up','','']);
  gap();
  sub('RS Override (Lone Wolf) — ALL 6 Required');
  hdr('Criteria','Required Value','','');
  row(['① Gameplan','C or D (otherwise no need)','',''],[Y,W,W,W]);
  row(['② RelStr vs SPY','≥ +5%','',''],[Y,W,W,W]);
  row(['③ Confluence','≥ 30/38','',''],[Y,W,W,W]);
  row(['④ RVOL','≥ 3.0×','',''],[Y,W,W,W]);
  row(['⑤ Sector','GREEN','',''],[Y,W,W,W]);
  row(['⑥ ATR Move','< 3× (not overextended)','',''],[Y,W,W,W]);
  note('ALL 6 required. GP-B sizing ($8K–$12K). Max 1 override/day.',O);
  gap();

  // ═══ 3. CONFLUENCE ═══
  sec('③ CONFLUENCE SCORING (38-Point Scale)');
  sub('Thresholds');
  hdr('Rating','Score','Action','');
  row(['A+ Setup','≥ 28/38','EXECUTE with confidence — full size',''],[G,W,G,W]);
  row(['Solid Setup','24–27/38','EXECUTE — standard size',''],[Y,W,Y,W]);
  row(['Playbook','20–23/38','EXECUTE if setup checklist passes — Tier 1-2',''],[O,W,O,W]);
  row(['Watch','16–19/38','On radar — not tradeable yet',''],[R,W,O,W]);
  row(['Skip','< 16/38','SKIP',''],[R,W,R,W]);
  gap();
  sub('Core Categories (0–30 pts)');
  hdr('Category','Max','What It Measures','');
  row(['Market Context','0–5','Maps from breadth score (GP sets ceiling)','']);
  row(['Price Structure','0–5','VWAP, EMA 9/20/50 alignment, OR position','']);
  row(['Momentum','0–5','RSI sweet spot, trend score, direction','']);
  row(['Volume','0–5','RVOL: 3×=5, 2×=4, 1.5×=3, 1×=2, 0.75×=1','']);
  row(['Key Level Proximity','0–5','Distance to VWAP / OR / yesterday levels','']);
  row(['Execution Quality','0–5','Spread, liquidity, entry zone, time bonus','']);
  gap();
  sub('Modifiers (±8 pts)');
  hdr('Modifier','Range','Logic','');
  row(['ATR Multiple','+2 to −2','Penalizes extended (>2.5× ATR = −2)','']);
  row(['Gap Analysis','+2 to −2','Small gap + holds = +2, large = −2','']);
  row(['Relative Strength','+2 to −2','≥3% = +2, ≤−3% = −2','']);
  row(['News/Catalyst','+2 to −2','NOT AUTOMATED (always 0) — add mentally',''],[O,O,O,W]);
  gap();

  // ═══ 4. BREADTH ═══
  sec('④ BREADTH SCORING CHEAT SHEET');
  note('Score range: −10 to +19 pts · Adj% = (Score + 10) / 29 × 100%',C);
  gap();
  sub('Primary Drivers (−6 to +6 pts)');
  hdr('Indicator','+2 pts','+1 pt','−1 / −2 pts');
  row(['$TICK (NYSE)','≥ +700','+300 to +700','≤−300 / ≤−700']);
  row(['$ADD (NYSE)','≥ +1,000','+400 to +1,000','≤−400 / ≤−1K']);
  row(['$ADQD (NASDAQ)','≥ +1,000','+500 to +1,000','≤−500 / ≤−1K']);
  row(['$VOLD (NYSE scaled)','≥ +700K','+150K to +700K','≤−150K / ≤−700K']);
  row(['$VOLQD (NQ scaled)','≥ +3,500K','+1.5M to +3.5M','≤−1.5M / ≤−3.5M']);
  gap();
  sub('Regime Modifiers (0 to +4 pts)');
  hdr('Indicator','Bullish','Neutral','No Bonus');
  row(['VIX','< 15 → +1','15–18 → +0.5','> 18 → 0']);
  row(['HYG/TLT','≥ 0.95 → +1','0.90–0.95 → +0.5','< 0.90 → 0']);
  row(['BTC','≥ 95K → +1','90–95K → +0.5','< 90K → 0']);
  row(['ES/NQ Futures','Both green + aligned → +0.5','','Otherwise → 0']);
  gap();
  sub('Sector Participation (0 to +2 pts)');
  hdr('Growth Green','Base Pts','Rotation Adj','');
  row(['7–8 / 8','+1.5','+0.5 if Def ≥3 green too','']);
  row(['6 / 8','+1.25','','']);
  row(['5 / 8','+1.0','','']);
  row(['4 / 8','+0.75','','']);
  row(['3 / 8','+0.5','','']);
  row(['2 / 8','+0.25','−0.5 if Def ≥4 & Growth ≤2','']);
  row(['0–1 / 8','0','','']);
  note('Growth: XLK SOXX SMH XLY XLF XLI XLC IWM  |  Def: XLU XLP XLV XLE XLB',DM);
  gap();

  // ═══ 5. GP-D ═══
  sec('⑤ GP-D INSTRUMENT MENU');
  sub('Sector-Wide Inverse ETFs');
  hdr('Ticker','Leverage','What It Shorts','Use When');
  row(['SOXS','3× Inverse','PHLX Semis (SOXX)','Semis leading decline — your edge'],[C,W,W,W]);
  row(['TSXD','2× Inverse','Top 5 Semis','Concentrated semi weakness, less decay'],[C,W,W,W]);
  row(['TECS','3× Inverse','Technology Sector','Broad tech selloff beyond semis'],[C,W,W,W]);
  row(['SQQQ','3× Inverse','Nasdaq-100','Full risk-off unwind'],[C,W,W,W]);
  row(['SPXU','3× Inverse','S&P 500','Market-wide selloff'],[C,W,W,W]);
  row(['TZA','3× Inverse','Russell 2000','Small-cap leading weakness'],[C,W,W,W]);
  gap();
  sub('Single-Stock Inverse ETFs');
  hdr('Ticker','Leverage','Underlying','Provider');
  row(['DAMD','2× Inverse','AMD','Defiance']);
  row(['STSM','2× Inverse','TSM','Defiance']);
  row(['SMCZ','2× Inverse','SMCI','Defiance']);
  row(['NVDD','1× Inverse','NVDA','Direxion']);
  row(['PLTZ','2× Inverse','PLTR','Defiance']);
  row(['SMST','2× Inverse','MSTR','Defiance']);
  note('Others: IONZ(IONQ) QBTZ(QBTS) RGTZ(RGTI) HOOZ(HOOD) RKLZ(RKLB) OKLS(OKLO)',DM);
  gap();
  sub('GP-D Decision Tree');
  row(['1. Broad selling, all red','→ SOXS (3×) or SQQQ (3×)','',''],[W,G,W,W]);
  row(['2. Semis leading decline','→ TSXD (2×) or SOXS (3×)','',''],[W,G,W,W]);
  row(['3. Specific name breaking','→ Defiance single-stock','',''],[W,G,W,W]);
  row(['4. Bearish but uncertain','→ 1× products (NVDD, QQQD)','',''],[W,Y,W,W]);
  row(['5. Unsure / choppy','→ SIT OUT ENTIRELY','',''],[W,R,W,W]);
  note('⚠ Intraday/single-day holds only. Never swing leveraged inverse ETFs.',R);
  gap();

  // ═══ 6. SIZING ═══
  sec('⑥ POSITION SIZING TABLE');
  hdr('Gameplan','$50 Stock','$100 Stock','$200 Stock');
  row(['A ($15K)','300 shares','150 shares','75 shares'],[G,W,W,W]);
  row(['A ($20K)','400 shares','200 shares','100 shares'],[G,W,W,W]);
  row(['B ($8K)','160 shares','80 shares','40 shares'],[Y,W,W,W]);
  row(['B ($12K)','240 shares','120 shares','60 shares'],[Y,W,W,W]);
  row(['C','—','—','—'],[O,W,W,W]);
  row(['D / RS Override ($8K)','160 shares','80 shares','40 shares'],[R,W,W,W]);
  row(['D / RS Override ($12K)','240 shares','120 shares','60 shares'],[R,W,W,W]);
  gap();

  // ═══ 7. CORRELATION ═══
  sec('⑦ CORRELATION & MAX EXPOSURE');
  sub('Correlation Clusters (update weekly)');
  hdr('Cluster','Tickers (edit)','Correlation','Notes');
  row(['Semis / AI','','HIGH','All move with NVDA / AI narrative']);
  row(['Software / SaaS','','HIGH','CRM/WDAY/APP read through together']);
  row(['Uncorrelated','','LOW','UEC/RKLB — independent catalysts']);
  note('⚠ Update tickers weekly. 3+ correlated = one trade, not three.',O);
  gap();
  sub('Max Exposure Rules');
  row(['Max per sector cluster','$36K (3 × GP-B max)','',''],[W,Y,W,W]);
  row(['Max correlated exposure','$36K total across cluster','',''],[W,Y,W,W]);
  row(['Max total DT capital','$60K at any time','',''],[W,Y,W,W]);
  row(['Max positions at once','5 active day trades','',''],[W,Y,W,W]);
  note('Hit max? Close weakest before adding. No exceptions.',R);
  gap();

  // ═══ 8. STOPS ═══
  sec('⑧ STOP LOSS PROTOCOL');
  hdr('Rule','Detail','','');
  row(['Default Stop','1.5× ATR below entry','','']);
  row(['Default Target','3.0× ATR above entry (2:1 R:R)','','']);
  row(['Stop Type','HARD stop in system — not mental','',''],[W,R,W,W]);
  row(['Never widen a stop','NEVER. If wrong, take the loss.','',''],[R,R,W,W]);
  row(['Trail stop when','+1R profit → move stop to breakeven','','']);
  row(['Trail method','Below each higher swing low (5m chart)','','']);
  row(['Time stop','No movement after 30 min → reassess/exit','','']);
  row(['Max loss per trade','GP-A: $200 | GP-B: $150 | GP-D: $150','',''],[O,O,W,W]);
  row(['Daily loss limit','3 consecutive losses → stop trading for day','',''],[R,R,W,W]);
  gap();

  // ═══ 9. TRANSITIONS ═══
  sec('⑨ GAMEPLAN TRANSITION RULES');
  hdr('Transition','Action','','');
  row(['A → B (breadth fading)','Tighten stops to breakeven, reduce targets','','']);
  row(['B → C (breadth weak)','No new entries. Trail existing tight.','',''],[W,O,W,W]);
  row(['B → D (breadth flips)','Exit all longs. Evaluate GP-D inverses.','',''],[W,R,W,W]);
  row(['C → B (improving)','Wait 15 min to confirm. Then GP-B rules.','','']);
  row(['D → C (recovering)','Exit inverses. Go flat. Wait for B.','','']);
  note('GP shifts mid-session are the hardest. These rules remove the decision.',P);
  gap();

  // ═══ 10. RE-ENTRY ═══
  sec('⑩ RE-ENTRY RULES');
  hdr('Rule','Detail','','');
  row(['After stop-out','Wait minimum 15 minutes','','']);
  row(['Same ticker re-entry','Requires DIFFERENT setup type','',''],[W,Y,W,W]);
  row(['Same setup re-entry','Requires higher confluence than first','',''],[W,Y,W,W]);
  row(['After 2 stops same name','Done with that ticker for the day','',''],[W,R,W,W]);
  row(['After daily loss limit','No re-entry. Session is over.','',''],[R,R,W,W]);
  note('"I\'ll just try one more time" = revenge trading in disguise.',R);
  gap();

  // ═══ 11. TIMING ═══
  sec('⑪ SESSION TIMING (Arizona — No DST)');
  hdr('Session','AZ Time','ET Time','Notes');
  row(['Pre-Market Data','6:00 AM','8:00 AM','Scanner starts, PMW sync']);
  row(['Econ Releases','6:30 AM','8:30 AM','Most economic data']);
  row(['Market Open','7:30 AM','9:30 AM','Opening Range starts (15 min)']);
  row(['OR Complete','7:45 AM','9:45 AM','OR-Break setups active']);
  row(['First 90 Min End','9:00 AM','11:00 AM','Best volume window closes']);
  row(['Midday Chop','9:00–11:00','11:00–1:00 PM','Avoid new entries']);
  row(['Power Hour','1:00 PM','3:00 PM','Volume resumes']);
  row(['Market Close','2:00 PM','4:00 PM','Flatten day trades']);
  row(['After Hours End','4:00 PM','6:00 PM','Scanner auto-disables']);
  note('Best windows: 7:30–9:00 (open) + 1:00–2:00 (power hour). Avoid 9–11 chop.',C);
  gap();

  // ═══ 12. EOD ═══
  sec('⑫ END-OF-DAY CHECKLIST (2:00 PM AZ)');
  hdr('#','Task','Done?','');
  row(['1','Flatten all day trades','☐','']);
  row(['2','Set/verify swing position stops','☐','']);
  row(['3','Check overnight catalyst calendar','☐','']);
  row(['4','Screenshot final dashboard state','☐','']);
  row(['5','Run EOD analysis with Claude (TradesViz)','☐','']);
  row(['6','Log trades in journal tab','☐','']);
  gap();

  // ═══ 13. WEEKLY ═══
  sec('⑬ WEEKLY PREP CHECKLIST (Sunday Night)');
  hdr('#','Task','Done?','');
  row(['1','Review Arete weekly themes','☐','']);
  row(['2','Review all open position theses','☐','']);
  row(['3','Update correlation clusters (⑦)','☐','']);
  row(['4','Set key levels for Monday','☐','']);
  row(['5','Check econ calendar (FOMC/CPI/jobs)','☐','']);
  row(['6','Review last week in journal tab','☐','']);
  gap();

  // ═══ 14. REMINDERS ═══
  sec('⑭ DAILY REMINDERS');
  note('◆ Breadth determines bias. Not your gut. Not the chart. Breadth.',G);
  note('◆ No longs in GP-D. One break costs more than 10 good trades.',R);
  note('◆ Don\'t chase gaps. Wait for pullback or find next setup.',Y);
  note('◆ Patience after GP-D IS the edge. Survive to trade GP-A days.',C);
  note('◆ Confluence ≥ 24 or skip. Marginal setups = marginal results.',Y);
  note('◆ If emotional, you\'re wrong. Close the platform. Come back tomorrow.',R);
  note('◆ Position sizing IS risk management. Never exceed GP limits.',O);
  note('◆ First 90 minutes have the volume. After that, be patient or be done.',DM);
  note('◆ One good trade > three mediocre trades. Quality always.',G);
  note('◆ You are not fighting the market. You are reading it.',P);
  gap();

  // ═══ FOOTER ═══
  note('V9 Trading System — The System Protects You. Follow It.',DM);

  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // PHASE 1: Bulk data write (single chained call)
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  var n = vals.length;
  var rng = sh.getRange(1, 2, n, 4);
  rng.setValues(vals);
  rng.setBackgrounds(bgs);
  rng.setFontColors(fcs);
  rng.setFontWeights(wts);
  rng.setVerticalAlignment('middle');
  rng.setWrapStrategy(SpreadsheetApp.WrapStrategy.WRAP);
  rng.setFontFamily('Roboto Mono');
  rng.setFontSize(10);
  
  // Spacer columns
  sh.getRange(1, 1, n, 1).setBackground(D);
  sh.getRange(1, 6, n, 1).setBackground(D);
  
  // Column widths
  sh.setColumnWidth(1, 20);
  sh.setColumnWidth(2, 200);
  sh.setColumnWidth(3, 180);
  sh.setColumnWidth(4, 180);
  sh.setColumnWidth(5, 220);
  sh.setColumnWidth(6, 20);
  
  // Flush to prevent timeout on subsequent calls
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // PHASE 2: Merges + row heights (batched in groups of 50)
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  
  // Set all row heights at once using setRowHeights where possible
  // Group consecutive rows with same height
  var i = 0;
  while (i < n) {
    var h = htArr[i];
    var j = i;
    while (j < n && htArr[j] === h) j++;
    sh.setRowHeightsForced(i + 1, j - i, h);
    i = j;
  }
  
  // Merges in batches
  for (var m = 0; m < mergeRows.length; m++) {
    sh.getRange(mergeRows[m], 2, 1, 4).merge();
    // Flush every 50 merges to avoid timeout
    if (m > 0 && m % 50 === 0) SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  }

  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  // PHASE 3: Font size overrides for headers
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  for (var r = 0; r < n; r++) {
    var h = htArr[r];
    if (h === 44) sh.getRange(r+1, 2, 1, 4).setFontSize(16);      // title
    else if (h === 30) sh.getRange(r+1, 2, 1, 4).setFontSize(12);  // subtitle
    else if (h === 36) sh.getRange(r+1, 2, 1, 4).setFontSize(13);  // section
    else if (h === 28) sh.getRange(r+1, 2, 1, 4).setFontSize(11);  // sub
    else if (h === 22) sh.getRange(r+1, 2, 1, 4).setFontSize(9);   // colhdr
  }

  sh.setFrozenRows(3);
  sh.setHiddenGridlines(true);
  ss.setActiveSheet(sh);
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('✅ Notes tab built — 14 sections.');
}

function cleanDashboardCache() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  props.deleteProperty('DASH_CACHE');
  props.deleteProperty('DASH_CACHE_TIME');
  props.deleteProperty('IC_SLUGS_CACHE');
  props.deleteProperty('WA_CACHE');
  props.deleteProperty('WA_CACHE_TIME');
  props.deleteProperty('W_CACHE');
  props.deleteProperty('W_CACHE_TIME');
  props.deleteProperty('A_CACHE');
  props.deleteProperty('A_CACHE_TIME');
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Done');
}


// ============================================================
// INSTITUTIONAL PULSE MODULE — v90.0
// ============================================================
// 5 data lenses pulled from the Python bridge (v9_pulse_bridge_v3.py):
//   1. VOL REGIME    — VIX level + regime, SPY/QQQ/IWM IV Rank & IV%
//   2. FEAR & GREED  — alternative.me index (0–100)
//   3. NAAIM         — Active manager equity exposure (-200 to +200)
//   4. SPY P/C RATIO — Put/call ratio from options chain (yfinance)
//   5. CLAUDE NARRATIVE — Opus (→Sonnet fallback) explains what the
//                         combined readings mean for V9 trade sizing
//
// SETUP (run once from script editor):
//   1. setAnthropicKey()  — paste your Anthropic API key
//   2. setBridgeUrl()     — confirms static ngrok domain is stored
//   3. testInstitutionalPulse() — verify all 5 lenses working
//
// The bridge (v9_pulse_bridge_v3.py) must be running on your Desktop.
// Static ngrok domain: ecclesiastically-ratio-lauran.ngrok-free.dev
// ============================================================

// ── PULSE CONFIGURATION ────────────────────────────────────

var BRIDGE_URL_PROP     = 'PULSE_BRIDGE_URL';
var PULSE_CACHE_PROP    = 'PULSE_DATA_CACHE';
var PULSE_CACHE_TIME    = 'PULSE_CACHE_TIME';
var PULSE_CACHE_TTL     = 300; // 5 minutes — matches bridge cache
var BRIDGE_DEFAULT_URL  = 'https://ecclesiastically-ratio-lauran.ngrok-free.dev';

var ANTHROPIC_KEY_PROP  = 'ANTHROPIC_API_KEY';
var CLAUDE_MODEL_OPUS   = 'claude-opus-4-6';
var CLAUDE_MODEL_SONNET = 'claude-sonnet-4-6';

// ── INTERNAL: BUILD ROWS FOR MARKET TAB ───────────────────

/**
 * Called from updateMarketTab() to get the pulse rows to append.
 * Returns array of [colA, colB, colC, colD] rows, or [] on failure.
 */
function _buildPulseRows() {
  var pulse = _fetchInstitutionalPulse();
  if (!pulse) return [];

  var d   = pulse.data       || {};
  var vol = d.vol_regime     || {};
  var fg  = d.fear_greed     || {};
  var pc  = (d.put_call && d.put_call.cboe) ? d.put_call.cboe : {};
  var nm  = d.aaii           || {};
  var nar = pulse.narrative  || {};
  var ts  = _pulseFmt(vol.vix ? ('Updated ' + _pulseTimestamp(d.timestamp)) : '');

  var rows     = [];
  var wrapIdxs = [];  // 0-based row indices within pulse block that need text wrap

  // ── INSTITUTIONAL PULSE header ──
  rows.push(['INSTITUTIONAL PULSE', '', '', ts]);

  // ── VOL REGIME ──
  rows.push(['VOL REGIME', 'Value', '', 'What It Means']);
  rows.push(['VIX',         _pulseFmt(vol.vix),        vol.regime || '',  'Fear gauge: <15 complacent, 15-20 normal, >25 elevated fear']);
  rows.push(['SPY IVR',     _pulseP(vol.spy_ivr),      'SPY IV%',         _pulseP(vol.spy_iv_pct)]);
  rows.push(['QQQ IVR',     _pulseP(vol.qqq_ivr),      'IWM IVR',         _pulseP(vol.iwm_ivr)]);
  // IV 5-day change
  if (vol.spy_iv_5d_chg != null) {
    rows.push(['SPY IV 5d Δ',  _pulseP(vol.spy_iv_5d_chg), 'QQQ IV 5d Δ', _pulseP(vol.qqq_iv_5d_chg)]);
  }
  if (nar.vol_context) {
    wrapIdxs.push(rows.length);
    rows.push(['', '', '', _pulseClip(nar.vol_context, 400)]);
  }
  rows.push(['', '', '', '']);

  // ── VIX TERM STRUCTURE ──
  var term = d.term_structure || {};
  if (term.vix9d || term.vix3m) {
    rows.push(['TERM STRUCTURE', 'Value', 'Ratio', 'Signal']);
    rows.push(['VIX9D',  _pulseFmt(term.vix9d),  'VIX9D/VIX',   _pulseFmt(term.vix9d_vix_ratio)]);
    rows.push(['VIX3M',  _pulseFmt(term.vix3m),  'VIX/VIX3M',   _pulseFmt(term.vix_vix3m_ratio)]);
    if (term.vix6m) rows.push(['VIX6M',  _pulseFmt(term.vix6m),  'VIX/VIX6M',   _pulseFmt(term.vix_vix6m_ratio)]);
    if (term.vvix)  rows.push(['VVIX',   _pulseFmt(term.vvix),   term.vvix_warning || '', 'Vol of VIX — >120 elevated, >140 extreme']);
    rows.push(['State',  term.state || '', term.signal || '', '>1.0 = backwardation (fear), <0.92 = contango (calm)']);
    if (nar.term_structure_context) {
      wrapIdxs.push(rows.length);
      rows.push(['', '', '', _pulseClip(nar.term_structure_context, 400)]);
    }
    rows.push(['', '', '', '']);
  }

  // ── EXPECTED MOVE ──
  var em = d.expected_move || {};
  if (em.status === 'ok') {
    rows.push(['EXPECTED MOVE', 'Daily', 'Weekly', 'Source']);
    rows.push(['SPY', '±$' + _pulseFmt(em.daily_pts) + ' (' + _pulseFmt(em.daily_pct) + '%)',
               '±$' + _pulseFmt(em.weekly_pts) + ' (' + _pulseFmt(em.weekly_pct) + '%)',
               'IV-derived @ $' + _pulseFmt(em.spy_price)]);
    rows.push(['', '', '', '']);
  }

  // ── SENTIMENT ──
  rows.push(['SENTIMENT', 'Value', 'Signal', 'Source / Notes']);
  rows.push(['Fear & Greed',   _pulseFmt(fg.score),    fg.zone || '',     (fg.rating || '') + ' — alternative.me']);
  rows.push(['NAAIM Exposure', _pulseP(nm.exposure),   nm.sentiment || '', 'Mgr equity % as of ' + (nm.date || 'recent') + ' — naaim.org']);
  rows.push(['SPY Put/Call',   _pulseFmt(pc.total_pc), pc.sentiment || '', 'Calls:' + _pulseFmt(pc.call_vol) + ' Puts:' + _pulseFmt(pc.put_vol)]);
  if (nar.sentiment_context) {
    wrapIdxs.push(rows.length);
    rows.push(['', '', '', _pulseClip(nar.sentiment_context, 400)]);
  }
  rows.push(['', '', '', '']);

  // ── COMBINED READ ──
  rows.push(['COMBINED READ', '', '', '']);
  if (nar.combined_read) {
    wrapIdxs.push(rows.length);
    rows.push(['', '', '', _pulseClip(nar.combined_read, 400)]);
  }
  if (nar.trading_implication) {
    wrapIdxs.push(rows.length);
    rows.push(['→ TODAY', '', '', _pulseClip(nar.trading_implication, 400)]);
  }
  rows.push(['', '', '', '']);

  // Attach wrap indices as a property for the caller to use
  rows._wrapIdxs = wrapIdxs;
  return rows;
}

// Truncate narrative text for sheet cells — keeps rows readable, not a novel
function _pulseClip(text, maxLen) {
  if (!text) return '';
  maxLen = maxLen || 220;
  if (text.length <= maxLen) return text;
  return text.substring(0, maxLen - 1) + '…';
}

// ── FETCH + CACHE ──────────────────────────────────────────

function _fetchInstitutionalPulse() {
  try {
    var cached = _getPulseCache();
    if (cached) return cached;

    var raw = _fetchBridgeData();
    if (!raw) { Logger.log('PULSE: bridge unreachable'); return null; }

    var narrative = _buildClauseNarrative(raw);
    var pulse = { data: raw, narrative: narrative, ts: Date.now() };
    _setPulseCache(pulse);
    return pulse;

  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('PULSE _fetchInstitutionalPulse error: ' + e);
    return null;
  }
}

function _fetchBridgeData() {
  var baseUrl = _getBridgeUrl();
  var endpoints = [baseUrl + '/pulse', baseUrl + '/pulse/refresh'];

  for (var i = 0; i < endpoints.length; i++) {
    try {
      var resp = UrlFetchApp.fetch(endpoints[i], {
        method:             'get',
        muteHttpExceptions: true,
        headers: {
          'ngrok-skip-browser-warning': 'true',
          'User-Agent': 'V9-Scanner/1.0'
        },
        followRedirects: true
      });
      if (resp.getResponseCode() === 200) {
        Logger.log('PULSE: data from ' + endpoints[i]);
        return JSON.parse(resp.getContentText());
      }
    } catch(e) {
      Logger.log('PULSE endpoint error ' + endpoints[i] + ': ' + e);
    }
  }
  return null;
}

function _getBridgeUrl() {
  var stored = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty(BRIDGE_URL_PROP);
  return (stored && stored !== '') ? stored : BRIDGE_DEFAULT_URL;
}

function _getPulseCache() {
  try {
    var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var ts    = parseInt(props.getProperty(PULSE_CACHE_TIME) || '0', 10);
    if ((Date.now() - ts) / 1000 > PULSE_CACHE_TTL) return null;
    var raw = props.getProperty(PULSE_CACHE_PROP);
    return raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : null;
  } catch(e) { return null; }
}

function _setPulseCache(pulse) {
  try {
    var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    
    // ── Save previous day snapshot (once per day) ──
    var azToday = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), 'America/Phoenix', 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    var prevPulseDate = props.getProperty('PULSE_PREV_DATE') || '';
    if (prevPulseDate !== azToday && pulse && pulse.data) {
      // First pulse fetch of the new day — snapshot yesterday's last values as prev
      var existingRaw = props.getProperty(PULSE_CACHE_PROP);
      if (existingRaw) {
        try {
          var existing = JSON.parse(existingRaw);
          if (existing.data) {
            // Store just the key numeric values we want deltas for
            var prevSnap = {};
            var ev = existing.data.vol_regime || {};
            if (ev.vix != null) prevSnap.vix = ev.vix;
            if (ev.spy_ivr != null) prevSnap.spy_ivr = ev.spy_ivr;
            if (ev.qqq_ivr != null) prevSnap.qqq_ivr = ev.qqq_ivr;
            if (ev.iwm_ivr != null) prevSnap.iwm_ivr = ev.iwm_ivr;
            var efg = existing.data.fear_greed || {};
            if (efg.score != null) prevSnap.fg_score = parseFloat(efg.score);
            var epc = (existing.data.put_call && existing.data.put_call.cboe) ? existing.data.put_call.cboe : {};
            if (epc.total_pc != null) prevSnap.put_call = parseFloat(epc.total_pc);
            var enm = existing.data.aaii || {};
            if (enm.exposure != null) prevSnap.naaim = parseFloat(enm.exposure);
            props.setProperty('PULSE_PREV_SNAP', JSON.stringify(prevSnap));
            props.setProperty('PULSE_PREV_DATE', azToday);
            Logger.log('Pulse prev-day snapshot saved for ' + azToday);
          }
        } catch(ep) { /* ignore parse errors on existing cache */ }
      }
    }
    
    // Script properties max 9KB per value — trim narrative if needed
    var str = JSON.stringify(pulse);
    if (str.length > 8000) {
      pulse.narrative = { trading_implication: pulse.narrative.trading_implication || '' };
      str = JSON.stringify(pulse);
    }
    props.setProperty(PULSE_CACHE_PROP, str);
    props.setProperty(PULSE_CACHE_TIME, Date.now().toString());
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('PULSE cache write error: ' + e);
  }
}

// ── CLAUDE NARRATIVE ───────────────────────────────────────

function _buildClauseNarrative(data) {
  var apiKey = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty(ANTHROPIC_KEY_PROP) || '';
  if (!apiKey || apiKey === '') {
    Logger.log('PULSE: no Anthropic key — using rule-based fallback');
    return _pulseFallbackNarrative(data);
  }

  var vol = data.vol_regime  || {};
  var fg  = data.fear_greed  || {};
  var pc  = (data.put_call && data.put_call.cboe) ? data.put_call.cboe : {};
  var nm  = data.aaii        || {};
  var term = data.term_structure || {};
  var em   = data.expected_move  || {};

  var prompt = [
    'You are a trading coach for a systematic intraday trader using the V9 breadth-confirmed scalping system.',
    'The trader takes day trades in SPY, QQQ, NVDA, TSLA, SMCI and other liquid tech/growth names.',
    'Trade duration: minutes to hours. Position sizing is driven by a breadth score (Gameplan A/B/C/D):',
    '  A (≥+9.5) = Hunt, full size $15-20K',
    '  B (+3/+9.5) = Sniper, reduced size $8-12K', 
    '  C (-3/+3) = Bench — very selective or sit out',
    '  D (≤-3) = Inverse ETFs (SQQQ/SOXS) or sit out entirely',
    '',
    'Current institutional pulse data:',
    '  VIX: ' + (vol.vix || 'N/A') + ' | Regime: ' + (vol.regime || 'N/A'),
    '  SPY IV Rank: ' + (vol.spy_ivr || 'N/A') + '% | IV Percentile: ' + (vol.spy_iv_pct || 'N/A') + '%',
    '  QQQ IVR: ' + (vol.qqq_ivr || 'N/A') + '% | IWM IVR: ' + (vol.iwm_ivr || 'N/A') + '%',
    '  SPY IV 5-day change: ' + (vol.spy_iv_5d_chg || 'N/A') + '% | QQQ: ' + (vol.qqq_iv_5d_chg || 'N/A') + '%',
    '',
    'VIX term structure:',
    '  VIX1D: ' + (term.vix1d || 'N/A') + ' | VIX9D: ' + (term.vix9d || 'N/A') + ' | VIX(30d): ' + (term.vix || 'N/A'),
    '  VIX3M: ' + (term.vix3m || 'N/A') + ' | VIX6M: ' + (term.vix6m || 'N/A'),
    '  VIX/VIX3M ratio: ' + (term.vix_vix3m_ratio || 'N/A') + ' | VIX9D/VIX: ' + (term.vix9d_vix_ratio || 'N/A'),
    '  State: ' + (term.state || 'N/A') + ' | VVIX: ' + (term.vvix || 'N/A') + ' (' + (term.vvix_warning || '') + ')',
    '',
    'Expected move (IV-derived):',
    '  SPY daily: ±$' + (em.daily_pts || 'N/A') + ' (' + (em.daily_pct || 'N/A') + '%) | weekly: ±$' + (em.weekly_pts || 'N/A') + ' (' + (em.weekly_pct || 'N/A') + '%)',
    '',
    'Sentiment:',
    '  Fear & Greed: ' + (fg.score || 'N/A') + ' — ' + (fg.rating || fg.zone || 'N/A'),
    '  NAAIM Exposure: ' + (nm.exposure || 'N/A') + '% (active mgr equity exposure, -200 to +200 scale, as of ' + (nm.date || 'recent') + ')',
    '  SPY Put/Call Ratio: ' + (pc.total_pc || 'N/A') + ' | Sentiment: ' + (pc.sentiment || 'N/A'),
    '',
    'Definitions for context:',
    '  IV Rank (IVR): Where current IV sits vs its 52-week range. 0% = lowest ever, 100% = highest ever.',
    '  IV 5-day change: Positive = IV expanding (expect bigger moves), negative = IV contracting (ranges tightening).',
    '  VIX term structure: When VIX > VIX3M (ratio >1.0), it is in BACKWARDATION — near-term fear exceeds longer-term. This is a danger signal.',
    '    Normal = CONTANGO (ratio <0.92). When VIX9D > VIX AND VIX > VIX3M = FULLY INVERTED, historically precedes major selloffs.',
    '  VVIX: Volatility of VIX itself. >120 = VIX could spike violently. >140 = extreme regime change risk.',
    '  Expected move: How much SPY is expected to move today/this week based on current IV. Use for stop/target calibration.',
    '  NAAIM: Active investment managers survey. >75% = bullish exposure. <25% = defensive. Updates weekly.',
    '  Put/Call >1.1 = more puts than calls = bearish hedging. <0.7 = call-heavy = bullish speculation.',
    '',
    'Respond ONLY with valid JSON — no markdown fences, no preamble, no trailing text. Structure:',
    '{',
    '  "vol_context": "2-3 sentences. What do the VIX level, IVR, and IV 5-day change mean RIGHT NOW for intraday range expectations? Is vol expanding or contracting? What does this mean for stop placement?",',
    '  "term_structure_context": "2-3 sentences. Interpret the VIX term structure state. Is it contango (normal/healthy), flat, backwardation (caution), or inverted (danger)? What does the VVIX level add? How should this affect the trader aggression today?",',
    '  "expected_move_context": "1-2 sentences. Given SPY expected daily move, what are reasonable intraday target/stop expectations? Is the expected move unusually large or small vs typical?",',
    '  "sentiment_context": "2-3 sentences. Analyze the RELATIONSHIP between Fear & Greed (retail), NAAIM (professionals), and Put/Call ratio. Divergence or alignment? Contrarian or confirming signal?",',
    '  "combined_read": "1-2 sentences. One clear market environment description synthesizing all lenses including term structure.",',
    '  "trading_implication": "1 sentence. Specific actionable implication for V9 trade sizing and execution today."',
    '}'
  ].join('\n');

  var models = [CLAUDE_MODEL_OPUS, CLAUDE_MODEL_SONNET];
  for (var m = 0; m < models.length; m++) {
    try {
      var resp = UrlFetchApp.fetch('https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', {
        method:      'post',
        contentType: 'application/json',
        headers: {
          'x-api-key':         apiKey,
          'anthropic-version': '2023-06-01'
        },
        payload: JSON.stringify({
          model:      models[m],
          max_tokens: 900,
          messages:   [{ role: 'user', content: prompt }]
        }),
        muteHttpExceptions: true
      });

      if (resp.getResponseCode() === 200) {
        var result = JSON.parse(resp.getContentText());
        var text   = result.content[0].text.trim()
          .replace(/^```json\s*/i, '').replace(/^```\s*/i, '').replace(/```\s*$/i, '').trim();
        var narrative = JSON.parse(text);
        Logger.log('PULSE: narrative via ' + models[m]);
        return narrative;
      } else {
        Logger.log('PULSE Claude ' + models[m] + ' HTTP ' + resp.getResponseCode() + ': ' + resp.getContentText().substring(0, 200));
      }
    } catch(e) {
      Logger.log('PULSE Claude ' + models[m] + ' error: ' + e);
    }
  }

  return _pulseFallbackNarrative(data);
}

function _pulseFallbackNarrative(data) {
  var vol      = data.vol_regime || {};
  var fg       = data.fear_greed || {};
  var pc       = (data.put_call && data.put_call.cboe) ? data.put_call.cboe : {};
  var nm       = data.aaii      || {};
  var term     = data.term_structure || {};
  var em       = data.expected_move  || {};
  var vix      = parseFloat(vol.vix    || 20);
  var fgScore  = parseFloat(fg.score   || 50);
  var naaim    = parseFloat(nm.exposure || 60);
  var pcRatio  = parseFloat(pc.total_pc || 1.0);

  var volText = vix >= 28
    ? 'VIX at ' + vix + ' — elevated fear. Wider intraday ranges expected, bigger whips. Reduce size, widen stops.'
    : vix <= 14
    ? 'VIX at ' + vix + ' — compressed vol. Tight ranges, smaller moves. Normal sizing applies.'
    : 'VIX at ' + vix + ' — normal regime. Standard range expectations and sizing.';
  if (vol.spy_iv_5d_chg != null) {
    var chg = parseFloat(vol.spy_iv_5d_chg);
    volText += chg > 3 ? ' IV expanding (+' + chg + '% 5-day) — expect widening ranges.'
             : chg < -3 ? ' IV contracting (' + chg + '% 5-day) — ranges tightening.'
             : '';
  }

  // Term structure narrative
  var termText = '';
  if (term.state) {
    if (term.state === 'INVERTED') {
      termText = 'DANGER: VIX term structure is fully inverted — near-term fear exceeds long-term across all tenors. Historically precedes significant selloffs. Maximum caution regardless of breadth score.';
    } else if (term.state === 'BACKWARDATION') {
      termText = 'Caution: VIX in backwardation (VIX/VIX3M: ' + (term.vix_vix3m_ratio || '?') + '). Near-term vol elevated vs longer-term — market pricing in imminent risk. Consider reducing aggression.';
    } else if (term.state === 'FLAT') {
      termText = 'VIX term structure is flat — low conviction from options market. No strong directional signal from volatility curve.';
    } else {
      termText = 'VIX term structure in healthy contango — near-term calm, longer-term normal. Standard vol environment for day trading.';
    }
    if (term.vvix && parseFloat(term.vvix) > 120) {
      termText += ' VVIX at ' + term.vvix + ' — elevated. VIX itself could spike violently today.';
    }
  }

  // Expected move narrative
  var emText = '';
  if (em.status === 'ok') {
    emText = 'SPY expected daily move: ±$' + em.daily_pts + ' (' + em.daily_pct + '%). ';
    if (em.daily_pct > 1.5) emText += 'Unusually wide — use wider stops and bigger targets.';
    else if (em.daily_pct < 0.6) emText += 'Very tight — expect choppy, low-range price action. Smaller targets.';
    else emText += 'Normal range — standard stop/target calibration applies.';
  }

  var sentText;
  if (fgScore < 25 && naaim > 70) {
    sentText = 'Classic divergence: retail at Extreme Fear (' + fgScore + ') while pros are ' + naaim + '% long. Historically this is a contrarian bullish setup — institutions are not selling despite the fear.';
  } else if (fgScore < 25 && naaim < 40) {
    sentText = 'Fear confirmed on both sides: F&G at ' + fgScore + ' and NAAIM only ' + naaim + '% long. Pros and retail aligned cautiously — risk-off environment.';
  } else if (fgScore > 75 && naaim > 90) {
    sentText = 'Euphoria warning: F&G at ' + fgScore + ' with NAAIM at ' + naaim + '% — both retail and pros are heavily loaded. Watch for distribution and mean reversion.';
  } else {
    sentText = 'F&G at ' + fgScore + ' (' + (fg.zone || 'neutral') + ') with NAAIM at ' + naaim + '%. P/C ratio of ' + pcRatio + ' shows ' + (pc.sentiment || 'neutral') + ' options positioning.';
  }

  var combined = (vol.regime || 'NORMAL') + ' volatility regime (' + (term.state || 'unknown') + ' term structure) with ' + (fg.zone || 'neutral') + ' sentiment and ' + naaim + '% professional equity exposure.';

  var implication = pcRatio > 1.2
    ? 'Heavy put hedging in market — respect downside momentum and let breadth score confirm before adding size.'
    : pcRatio < 0.7
    ? 'Call-heavy positioning — bullish bias but watch for complacency reversals; breadth confirmation still required.'
    : 'Balanced options flow — breadth score is your primary sizing signal today.';

  return {
    vol_context:              volText,
    term_structure_context:   termText,
    expected_move_context:    emText,
    sentiment_context:        sentText,
    combined_read:            combined,
    trading_implication:      implication
  };
}

// ── FORMAT HELPERS ─────────────────────────────────────────

function _pulseFmt(v) {
  if (v === null || v === undefined) return 'N/A';
  return String(v);
}

function _pulseP(v) {
  if (v === null || v === undefined) return 'N/A';
  return v + '%';
}

function _pulseTimestamp(iso) {
  if (!iso) return '';
  try {
    return Utilities.formatDate(new Date(iso), 'America/Phoenix', 'h:mm a');
  } catch(e) { return ''; }
}

}

// ==================== END INSTITUTIONAL PULSE MODULE ====================


// ============================================================
// ==================== WEEKEND PULSE MODULE ====================
// ============================================================
// Lightweight off-hours scanner: 25 tickers, hourly on the hour.
// Covers futures, macro, crypto, and global equity ETFs across
// 6 regions with session indicators and RSS news.
// Writes to separate "Weekend" tab. Dashboard reads PULSE_MODE
// flag to switch between market and pulse layouts.
// ============================================================


// ── WEEKEND PULSE: ENABLED CHECK ──

function isWeekendPulseEnabled() {
  return PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('WEEKEND_PULSE_ENABLED') === 'ON';
}


// ── WEEKEND PULSE: CORE FUNCTION ──

function weekendPulse() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  
  // 0. Enabled check
  if (props.getProperty('WEEKEND_PULSE_ENABLED') !== 'ON') return;
  
  // 1. Gate — skip if main scanner is in any active phase
  var now = new Date();
  var azH = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'H'), 10);
  var azM = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'm'), 10);
  var azDow = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'u'), 10); // 1=Mon...7=Sun
  var azMin = azH * 60 + azM;
  
  var isWeekday = azDow >= 1 && azDow <= 5;
  var inMainWindow = azMin >= PHASE_CONFIG.PRE_MARKET.start 
                     && azMin < PHASE_CONFIG.AFTER_HOURS.end;
  var isHoliday = isMarketHoliday(now);
  
  // Run if: weekend OR (weekday but outside main window) OR holiday
  if (isWeekday && inMainWindow && !isHoliday) {
    Logger.log('Weekend Pulse: main scanner active, skipping.');
    return;
  }
  
  Logger.log('📡 Weekend Pulse running — ' + Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'EEE MMM d, h:mm a') + ' AZ');
  
  // 2. Fetch quotes — single API call, 25 tickers
  var quotes = [];
  try {
    quotes = tsQuotes(PULSE_ALL_SYMBOLS);
    Logger.log('Weekend Pulse: fetched ' + quotes.length + ' quotes');
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('Weekend Pulse: quote fetch error — ' + e.message);
    return;
  }
  
  // Build quote lookup map
  var quoteMap = {};
  for (var i = 0; i < quotes.length; i++) {
    quoteMap[quotes[i].Symbol] = quotes[i];
  }
  
  // 3. Determine which global sessions are live
  var sessions = getActiveSessions(azMin, azDow);
  
  // 4. Detect futures halt — flag stale
  flagHaltedFutures(quoteMap, azMin);
  
  // 5. Fetch RSS news (60-min cache)
  var news = fetchPulseNews(props);
  
  // 6. Write to Weekend tab
  writeWeekendTab(quoteMap, news, sessions, now);
  
  // 7. Cache state for dashboard
  cachePulseForDashboard(props, quoteMap, news, sessions, now);
  
  Logger.log('📡 Weekend Pulse complete — ' + Object.keys(quoteMap).length + ' quotes, ' + news.length + ' headlines');
}


// Force run — bypasses gate check for manual testing
function forceWeekendPulse() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  
  var now = new Date();
  Logger.log('📡 Force Weekend Pulse — ' + Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'EEE MMM d, h:mm a') + ' AZ');
  
  // Fetch quotes
  var quotes = [];
  try {
    quotes = tsQuotes(PULSE_ALL_SYMBOLS);
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('Force Weekend Pulse: quote error — ' + e.message);
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('❌ Weekend Pulse failed: ' + e.message);
    return;
  }
  
  var quoteMap = {};
  for (var i = 0; i < quotes.length; i++) {
    quoteMap[quotes[i].Symbol] = quotes[i];
  }
  
  var azH = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'H'), 10);
  var azM = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'm'), 10);
  var azDow = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'u'), 10);
  var azMin = azH * 60 + azM;
  
  var sessions = getActiveSessions(azMin, azDow);
  flagHaltedFutures(quoteMap, azMin);
  var news = fetchPulseNews(props);
  
  writeWeekendTab(quoteMap, news, sessions, now);
  cachePulseForDashboard(props, quoteMap, news, sessions, now);
  
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('📡 Weekend Pulse complete.\n' + Object.keys(quoteMap).length + ' quotes, ' + news.length + ' headlines.\nCheck Weekend tab.');
}


// ── WEEKEND PULSE: SESSION DETECTION ──

function getActiveSessions(azMin, azDow) {
  var result = {};
  var isWeekend = azDow >= 6;
  
  // Equity session detection
  for (var region in GLOBAL_SESSIONS) {
    var s = GLOBAL_SESSIONS[region];
    var live = false;
    
    if (isWeekend) {
      // Most equity markets closed on weekends
      live = false;
    } else if (s.start > s.end) {
      // Wraps midnight (e.g. Asia 5PM-11PM = 1020-1380 doesn't actually wrap,
      // but if start > end it would mean wrap)
      live = azMin >= s.start || azMin < s.end;
    } else {
      live = azMin >= s.start && azMin < s.end;
    }
    result[region] = { live: live, label: s.label, emoji: s.emoji };
  }
  
  // Futures: Sun ~4PM AZ through Fri ~4PM AZ, except daily halt
  // On weekends: only Sunday after ~4PM (futures reopen)
  var futuresLive = false;
  if (isWeekend) {
    if (azDow === 7 && azMin >= 960) {
      // Sunday 4:00 PM AZ = futures reopen (~6:00 PM ET during EST)
      futuresLive = true;
    }
    // Saturday: futures closed
  } else {
    // Weekdays: futures trade except during daily halt
    futuresLive = true;
  }
  result.futures = { live: futuresLive, label: 'FUTURES', emoji: '📊' };
  
  // Crypto: always live
  result.crypto = { live: true, label: 'CRYPTO', emoji: '₿' };
  
  return result;
}


// ── WEEKEND PULSE: HOLIDAY DETECTION ──

function isMarketHoliday(date) {
  var dateStr = Utilities.formatDate(date, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  for (var i = 0; i < MARKET_HOLIDAYS_2026.length; i++) {
    if (dateStr === MARKET_HOLIDAYS_2026[i]) return true;
  }
  return false;
}


// ── WEEKEND PULSE: FUTURES HALT DETECTION ──

function flagHaltedFutures(quoteMap, azMin) {
  // Daily futures halt window
  // EST period (Nov-Mar): halt 5:00-6:00 PM ET = 3:00-4:00 PM AZ (900-960)
  // EDT period (Mar-Nov): halt 5:00-6:00 PM ET = 2:00-3:00 PM AZ (840-900)
  // For simplicity, flag both windows — the gate logic means pulse only runs
  // outside main scanner hours anyway, so the 2-3 PM window is inside main scanner.
  // The 3-4 PM window (900-960) is at the tail of AFTER_HOURS.
  var haltStart = 900;  // 3:00 PM AZ
  var haltEnd   = 960;  // 4:00 PM AZ
  
  var inHalt = azMin >= haltStart && azMin < haltEnd;
  var futuresTickers = ['@ES', '@NQ', '@RTY', '@CL', '@GC'];
  
  if (inHalt) {
    for (var i = 0; i < futuresTickers.length; i++) {
      var sym = futuresTickers[i];
      if (quoteMap[sym]) {
        quoteMap[sym]._halted = true;
      }
    }
  }
}


// ── WEEKEND PULSE: NEWS FETCH ──
// Reuses same RSS feeds as main scanner, with 60-min cache TTL

function fetchPulseNews(props) {
  var cacheStr = props.getProperty('PULSE_NEWS_CACHE') || '';
  var cacheTime = parseInt(props.getProperty('PULSE_NEWS_CACHE_TIME') || '0');
  var age = Date.now() - cacheTime;
  
  // Return cached if fresh
  if (cacheStr && age < PULSE_NEWS_CACHE_TTL) {
    try {
      return JSON.parse(cacheStr);
    } catch(e) { /* fall through to fetch */ }
  }
  
  var rssNews = [];
  var rssFeeds = [
    { url: 'https://www.investing.com/rss/news_25.rss', src: 'Investing.com', tag: 'IC', ua: true },
    { url: 'https://www.investing.com/rss/news_14.rss', src: 'Investing.com', tag: 'IC', ua: true },
    { url: 'https://search.cnbc.com/rs/search/combinedcms/view.xml?partnerId=wrss01&id=100003114', src: 'CNBC', tag: 'CN', ua: false },
    { url: 'https://www.cnbc.com/id/15839069/device/rss/rss.html', src: 'CNBC', tag: 'CN', ua: false },
    { url: 'https://finance.yahoo.com/news/rssindex', src: 'Yahoo Finance', tag: 'YF', ua: false }
  ];
  
  var rssSrcBlacklist = {'MarketWatch': 1, 'marketwatch': 1};
  
  for (var fi = 0; fi < rssFeeds.length; fi++) {
    try {
      var fetchOpts = { muteHttpExceptions: true };
      if (rssFeeds[fi].ua) fetchOpts.headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0' };
      var rssResp = trackedFetch(rssFeeds[fi].url, fetchOpts, 'pulse-rss-' + rssFeeds[fi].tag);
      if (rssResp.getResponseCode() === 200) {
        var xml = XmlService.parse(rssResp.getContentText());
        var root = xml.getRootElement();
        var channel = root.getChild('channel');
        if (channel) {
          var items = channel.getChildren('item');
          for (var ii = 0; ii < items.length && ii < 15; ii++) {
            var title = items[ii].getChildText('title') || '';
            var link = items[ii].getChildText('link') || '';
            var pubDate = items[ii].getChildText('pubDate') || '';
            var pubTime = 0;
            if (pubDate) {
              try { pubTime = Math.floor(new Date(pubDate).getTime() / 1000); } catch(e) {}
            }
            if (!title) continue;
            // Skip blacklisted sources
            var itemSrc = items[ii].getChildText('source') || '';
            if (rssSrcBlacklist[itemSrc]) continue;
            // Dedupe by first 40 chars
            var prefix40 = title.substring(0, 40).toLowerCase();
            var isDupe = false;
            for (var dd = 0; dd < rssNews.length; dd++) {
              if (rssNews[dd].headline.substring(0, 40).toLowerCase() === prefix40) { isDupe = true; break; }
            }
            if (!isDupe) {
              rssNews.push({
                headline: title,
                source: rssFeeds[fi].src,
                url: link,
                time: pubTime,
                feed: rssFeeds[fi].tag
              });
            }
          }
        }
      }
    } catch(e) {
      Logger.log('Pulse RSS error (' + rssFeeds[fi].tag + '): ' + e.message);
    }
  }
  
  // Sort by time descending (newest first)
  rssNews.sort(function(a, b) { return (b.time || 0) - (a.time || 0); });
  
  // Cache
  if (rssNews.length > 0) {
    // Keep only last 50 headlines to avoid property size limits
    var toCache = rssNews.slice(0, 50);
    props.setProperty('PULSE_NEWS_CACHE', JSON.stringify(toCache));
    props.setProperty('PULSE_NEWS_CACHE_TIME', Date.now().toString());
  }
  
  return rssNews;
}


// ── WEEKEND PULSE: WRITE WEEKEND TAB ──

function writeWeekendTab(quoteMap, news, sessions, now) {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var sheet = ss.getSheetByName('Weekend');
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet('Weekend');
  }
  
  var timeStr = Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'EEE MMM d, h:mm a') + ' AZ';
  
  // Build data rows
  var data = [];
  data.push(['📡 WEEKEND PULSE', '', '', 'Last update: ' + timeStr]);
  data.push(['', '', '', '']);
  
  // Each section
  for (var si = 0; si < PULSE_SECTIONS.length; si++) {
    var section = PULSE_SECTIONS[si];
    
    // Section header with session status
    var sessionStatus = '';
    if (section.session && sessions[section.session]) {
      sessionStatus = sessions[section.session].live ? section.session.toUpperCase() + ' LIVE' : section.session.toUpperCase() + ' CLOSED';
    } else if (section.key === 'futures') {
      sessionStatus = sessions.futures && sessions.futures.live ? 'FUTURES LIVE' : 'FUTURES CLOSED';
    } else if (section.key === 'commodities') {
      // Mixed: futures + crypto
      sessionStatus = sessions.crypto && sessions.crypto.live ? 'CRYPTO 24/7' : '';
    }
    
    data.push([section.label, 'Last', 'Chg %', sessionStatus]);
    
    // Ticker rows
    for (var ti = 0; ti < section.symbols.length; ti++) {
      var sym = section.symbols[ti];
      var q = quoteMap[sym];
      
      if (q) {
        var last = q.Last || q.LastPrice || '';
        var pct = parseFloat(q.NetChangePct || 0);
        var pctStr = pct !== 0 ? pct.toFixed(2) + '%' : '';
        var status = '';
        
        if (q._halted) {
          status = 'HALTED';
        } else if (sym === 'BTCUSD') {
          status = '24/7';
        } else if (['$VIX', '$TNX', 'CPER'].indexOf(sym) >= 0) {
          // These only update during US market hours
          status = 'LAST CLOSE';
        } else if (section.session && sessions[section.session]) {
          status = sessions[section.session].live ? 'LIVE' : 'LAST CLOSE';
        } else if (['@ES', '@NQ', '@RTY', '@CL', '@GC'].indexOf(sym) >= 0) {
          status = (sessions.futures && sessions.futures.live && !q._halted) ? 'LIVE' : 'CLOSED';
        } else if (sym === '$DXY') {
          status = sessions.futures && sessions.futures.live ? 'LIVE' : 'LAST CLOSE';
        }
        
        data.push([sym, last, pctStr, status]);
      } else {
        // No data returned
        data.push([sym, 'N/A', '', 'NO DATA']);
      }
    }
    
    data.push(['', '', '', '']); // blank row between sections
  }
  
  // News section
  data.push(['📰 HEADLINES', '', '', '']);
  var newsLimit = Math.min(news.length, 20);
  for (var ni = 0; ni < newsLimit; ni++) {
    var h = news[ni];
    var timeAgo = '';
    if (h.time) {
      var ageSec = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000) - h.time;
      if (ageSec < 3600) timeAgo = Math.floor(ageSec / 60) + 'm ago';
      else if (ageSec < 86400) timeAgo = Math.floor(ageSec / 3600) + 'h ago';
      else timeAgo = Math.floor(ageSec / 86400) + 'd ago';
    }
    data.push([h.headline, h.source, timeAgo, h.url || '']);
  }
  
  // Write all data
  sheet.clearContents();
  if (data.length > 0) {
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, data.length, 4).setValues(data);
  }
  
  // Basic formatting
  sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 280);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(2, 120);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(3, 80);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(4, 200);
  
  // Bold section headers
  for (var ri = 0; ri < data.length; ri++) {
    var cellVal = String(data[ri][0]);
    if (cellVal === '📡 WEEKEND PULSE' || cellVal === '📰 HEADLINES') {
      sheet.getRange(ri + 1, 1, 1, 4).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#1a1a2e').setFontColor('#FF9800');
    } else {
      for (var psi = 0; psi < PULSE_SECTIONS.length; psi++) {
        if (cellVal === PULSE_SECTIONS[psi].label) {
          sheet.getRange(ri + 1, 1, 1, 4).setFontWeight('bold').setBackground('#1a1a2e').setFontColor('#c8cdd8');
          break;
        }
      }
    }
  }
  
  Logger.log('Weekend tab written: ' + data.length + ' rows');
}


// ── WEEKEND PULSE: CACHE FOR DASHBOARD ──

function cachePulseForDashboard(props, quoteMap, news, sessions, now) {
  // Set pulse mode flag
  props.setProperty('PULSE_MODE', 'true');
  props.setProperty('PULSE_LAST_UPDATE', Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'h:mm a') + ' AZ');
  
  // Cache sessions for dashboard
  try {
    props.setProperty('PULSE_ACTIVE_SESSIONS', JSON.stringify(sessions));
  } catch(e) { Logger.log('Pulse session cache error: ' + e.message); }
  
  // News is already cached by fetchPulseNews — PULSE_NEWS_CACHE property
}


// ── WEEKEND PULSE: TRIGGER MANAGEMENT ──

function startWeekendPulse() {
  var triggers = ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers();
  var hasTrigger = false;
  for (var i = 0; i < triggers.length; i++) {
    if (triggers[i].getHandlerFunction() === 'weekendPulse') {
      hasTrigger = true;
      break;
    }
  }
  if (!hasTrigger) {
    ScriptApp.newTrigger('weekendPulse')
      .timeBased()
      .everyHours(1)
      .create();
  }
  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('WEEKEND_PULSE_ENABLED', 'ON');
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('📡 Weekend Pulse ON — hourly refresh active.\n\nRuns automatically outside market hours (4PM-6:30AM weekdays, all weekend, holidays).\nUse "Weekend Pulse Now" to force a manual run.');
}

function stopWeekendPulse() {
  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('WEEKEND_PULSE_ENABLED', 'OFF');
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('🛑 Weekend Pulse OFF — trigger still exists but weekendPulse() will skip.\nUse "Start Weekend Pulse" to re-enable.');
}


// ── WEEKEND PULSE: CLEANUP ──
// Call from removeTrigger() or manually to fully remove

function removeWeekendPulseTrigger() {
  var triggers = ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers();
  for (var i = 0; i < triggers.length; i++) {
    if (triggers[i].getHandlerFunction() === 'weekendPulse') {
      ScriptApp.deleteTrigger(triggers[i]);
      Logger.log('Weekend Pulse trigger removed.');
    }
  }
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  props.setProperty('WEEKEND_PULSE_ENABLED', 'OFF');
  props.setProperty('PULSE_MODE', 'false');
  props.deleteProperty('PULSE_LAST_UPDATE');
  props.deleteProperty('PULSE_ACTIVE_SESSIONS');
  props.deleteProperty('PULSE_NEWS_CACHE');
  props.deleteProperty('PULSE_NEWS_CACHE_TIME');
}

function clearWeekendPulseCache() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  props.deleteProperty('PULSE_NEWS_CACHE');
  props.deleteProperty('PULSE_NEWS_CACHE_TIME');
  props.deleteProperty('PULSE_ACTIVE_SESSIONS');
  props.deleteProperty('PULSE_LAST_UPDATE');
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Weekend Pulse caches cleared.');
}


// ── Manual Arete test — run from Script Editor to diagnose ──
function testAreteEmails() {
  try {
    Logger.log('Testing Arete email search...');
    
    // Test 1: Direct search
    var threads1 = GmailApp.search('aretetrading.ccsend.com newer_than:7d', 0, 10);
    Logger.log('Search (aretetrading.ccsend.com): ' + threads1.length + ' threads');
    
    for (var ti = 0; ti < Math.min(threads1.length, 5); ti++) {
      var msg = threads1[ti].getMessages()[0];
      Logger.log('  Thread ' + ti + ': subject=' + msg.getSubject().substring(0,80) + ' date=' + msg.getDate());
    }
    
    // Test 5: Check stored data
    var stored = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('ARETE_EMAILS_WEEK');
    Logger.log('Stored ARETE_EMAILS_WEEK: ' + (stored ? stored.length + ' chars, ' + JSON.parse(stored).length + ' emails' : 'NULL'));
    
    // Test 6: Force refresh
    Logger.log('Force refreshing...');
    PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().deleteProperty('ARETE_GMAIL_CACHE_TIME');
    PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().deleteProperty('ARETE_EMAILS_WEEK_TIME');
    var result = getAreteFromGmail_();
    Logger.log('Refresh result: ' + (result ? result.substring(0, 100) + '...' : 'null'));
    
    var afterStore = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('ARETE_EMAILS_WEEK');
    Logger.log('After refresh: ' + (afterStore ? JSON.parse(afterStore).length + ' emails' : 'NULL'));
    
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Check Execution Log for results');
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('testAreteEmails ERROR: ' + e.message + '\n' + e.stack);
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Error: ' + e.message);
  }
}

// PHASE 1A: ACCOUNTS TAB

/**
 * Creates the Accounts tab with headers. If it already exists, does nothing.
 * Called from buildTradeManagementTabs() or menu.
 */
function _ensureAccountsTab() {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(TM_TAB_ACCOUNTS);
  if (!sheet) sheet = ss.insertSheet(TM_TAB_ACCOUNTS);
  if (String(sheet.getRange(1,1).getValue()).trim() !== TM_ACCOUNTS_HEADERS[0]) {
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, TM_ACCOUNTS_HEADERS.length).setValues([TM_ACCOUNTS_HEADERS]);
    sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
    Logger.log('Trade Management: Accounts tab created');
  }
  return sheet;
}

/**
 * Seeds the Accounts tab from existing TS_ACCOUNTS config + live balance data.
 * Preserves user-edited risk config fields if rows already exist.
 * Called manually or on first setup.
 */
function seedAccountsTab() {
  var sheet = _ensureAccountsTab();
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  
  // Get existing rows (skip header)
  var existingData = sheet.getLastRow() > 1 ? sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, TM_ACCOUNTS_HEADERS.length).getValues() : [];
  var existingMap = {};
  for (var i = 0; i < existingData.length; i++) {
    var id = String(existingData[i][0]).trim();
    if (id) existingMap[id] = { row: i + 2, data: existingData[i] };
  }
  
  // Gather accounts from TS config
  var tsConfig = getTSAccountConfig();
  var accounts = [];
  
  for (var t = 0; t < tsConfig.length; t++) {
    var c = tsConfig[t];
    var acctId = 'TS-' + (c.type || 'UNK');
    // Try to get live balance
    var nlv = 0;
    try {
      var bal = tsGetBalances(c.id);
      nlv = parseFloat(bal.Equity || bal.NetLiquidatingValue || bal.CashBalance || 0);
    } catch(e) {
      Logger.log('seedAccountsTab: Could not fetch balance for ' + acctId + ': ' + e.message);
    }
    
    accounts.push({
      account_id: acctId,
      label: c.label || acctId,
      broker: 'tradestation',
      type: c.type || 'DT',
      equity: nlv,
      ts_raw_id: c.id
    });
  }
  
  // Include Alpaca paper account if credentials are configured
  var hasPaper = false;
  for (var k in existingMap) {
    if (String(existingMap[k].data[3]).trim() === 'PAPER') { hasPaper = true; break; }
  }
  if (!hasPaper) {
    var alpacaEquity = 0;
    try {
      var alpAcct = alpacaGetAccount();
      alpacaEquity = parseFloat(alpAcct.equity || alpAcct.portfolio_value || 0);
    } catch(e) {
      Logger.log('seedAccountsTab: Alpaca balance fetch failed: ' + e.message);
    }
    if (alpacaEquity > 0) {
      accounts.push({
        account_id: 'ALPACA-PAPER',
        label: 'Alpaca Paper Trading',
        broker: 'alpaca',
        type: 'PAPER',
        equity: alpacaEquity,
        ts_raw_id: null
      });
    }
  }
  
  // Write/update each account row
  var now = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss');
  var writeRow = 2;
  
  for (var a = 0; a < accounts.length; a++) {
    var acct = accounts[a];
    var defaults = TM_RISK_DEFAULTS[acct.type] || TM_RISK_DEFAULTS.DT;
    
    if (existingMap[acct.account_id]) {
      // Row exists — update equity fields, preserve risk config
      var existing = existingMap[acct.account_id];
      var r = existing.row;
      // Update equity columns (5-8) and last_updated (14) only
      if (acct.equity > 0) {
        var bodEquity = existing.data[4] || acct.equity; // Keep BOD if already set
        var currentEquity = acct.equity;
        var dailyPnl = currentEquity - bodEquity;
        var dailyPnlPct = bodEquity > 0 ? (dailyPnl / bodEquity * 100) : 0;
        
        sheet.getRange(r, 5).setValue(bodEquity);
        sheet.getRange(r, 6).setValue(currentEquity);
        sheet.getRange(r, 7).setValue(Math.round(dailyPnl * 100) / 100);
        sheet.getRange(r, 8).setValue(Math.round(dailyPnlPct * 100) / 100);
      }
      sheet.getRange(r, 14).setValue(now);
      Logger.log('seedAccountsTab: Updated ' + acct.account_id + ' (equity: ' + acct.equity + ')');
    } else {
      // New row — write full row with default risk config
      var row = [
        acct.account_id,
        acct.label,
        acct.broker,
        acct.type,
        acct.equity,         // bod_equity (first time = current)
        acct.equity,         // current_equity
        0,                   // daily_pnl
        0,                   // daily_pnl_pct
        defaults.daily_loss_limit,
        defaults.max_risk_per_trade,
        defaults.max_risk_pct,
        defaults.max_positions,
        0,                   // open_positions
        now
      ];
      sheet.getRange(sheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, 1, row.length).setValues([row]);
      Logger.log('seedAccountsTab: Created ' + acct.account_id + ' (equity: ' + acct.equity + ')');
    }
  }
  
  // Store TS raw IDs mapping in ScriptProperties for future sync
  var idMap = {};
  for (var a = 0; a < accounts.length; a++) {
    if (accounts[a].ts_raw_id) idMap[accounts[a].account_id] = accounts[a].ts_raw_id;
  }
  PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('TM_ACCT_ID_MAP', JSON.stringify(idMap));
  
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  Logger.log('seedAccountsTab: Complete — ' + accounts.length + ' accounts');
  return accounts.length;
}

/**
 * Refreshes equity on all Accounts rows. Called on first scanner trigger each day
 * to set BOD equity, and intraday to update current equity.
 * @param {boolean} setBOD - if true, also overwrites bod_equity (first run of day)
 */
function refreshAccountEquity(setBOD) {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(TM_TAB_ACCOUNTS);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) return;
  
  var data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, TM_ACCOUNTS_HEADERS.length).getValues();
  var idMap = {};
  try { idMap = JSON.parse(PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('TM_ACCT_ID_MAP') || '{}'); } catch(e) {}
  
  var now = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss');
  
  for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    var acctId = String(data[i][0]).trim();
    var broker = String(data[i][2]).trim();
    var r = i + 2; // sheet row (1-indexed, skip header)
    
    var equity = 0;
    
    if (broker === 'tradestation' && idMap[acctId]) {
      try {
        var bal = tsGetBalances(idMap[acctId]);
        equity = parseFloat(bal.Equity || bal.NetLiquidatingValue || bal.CashBalance || 0);
      } catch(e) {
        Logger.log('refreshAccountEquity: TS balance fail for ' + acctId + ': ' + e.message);
        continue;
      }
    } else if (broker === 'alpaca') {
      try {
        var alpAcct = alpacaGetAccount();
        equity = parseFloat(alpAcct.equity || alpAcct.portfolio_value || 0);
      } catch(e) {
        Logger.log('refreshAccountEquity: Alpaca fail: ' + e.message);
        continue;
      }
    } else {
      continue;
    }
    
    if (equity <= 0) continue;
    
    var bodEquity = data[i][4]; // existing BOD
    
    if (setBOD || !bodEquity || bodEquity === 0) {
      // Set BOD (first run of day or first time)
      sheet.getRange(r, 5).setValue(equity); // bod_equity
      bodEquity = equity;
    }
    
    // Always update current equity + derived fields
    var dailyPnl = equity - bodEquity;
    var dailyPnlPct = bodEquity > 0 ? (dailyPnl / bodEquity * 100) : 0;
    
    sheet.getRange(r, 6).setValue(equity);                              // current_equity
    sheet.getRange(r, 7).setValue(Math.round(dailyPnl * 100) / 100);   // daily_pnl
    sheet.getRange(r, 8).setValue(Math.round(dailyPnlPct * 100) / 100);// daily_pnl_pct
    sheet.getRange(r, 14).setValue(now);                                // last_updated
  }
  
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  Logger.log('refreshAccountEquity: Done (setBOD=' + setBOD + ')');
}

/**
 * Returns account data as an object map keyed by account_id.
 * Used by pre-trade card, scorecard, and dashboard.
 */
function getAccountsMap() {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(TM_TAB_ACCOUNTS);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) return {};
  
  var data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, TM_ACCOUNTS_HEADERS.length).getValues();
  var map = {};
  
  for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    var id = String(data[i][0]).trim();
    if (!id) continue;
    map[id] = {
      account_id:         id,
      label:              String(data[i][1]),
      broker:             String(data[i][2]),
      type:               String(data[i][3]),
      bod_equity:         parseFloat(data[i][4]) || 0,
      current_equity:     parseFloat(data[i][5]) || 0,
      daily_pnl:          parseFloat(data[i][6]) || 0,
      daily_pnl_pct:      parseFloat(data[i][7]) || 0,
      daily_loss_limit:   parseFloat(data[i][8]) || 0,
      max_risk_per_trade: parseFloat(data[i][9]) || 0,
      max_risk_pct:       parseFloat(data[i][10]) || 0,
      max_positions:      parseInt(data[i][11]) || 0,
      open_positions:     parseInt(data[i][12]) || 0,
      last_updated:       String(data[i][13])
    };
  }
  return map;
}

/**
 * Returns the daily loss limit status for a given account.
 * Used by scorecard (sc_daily_limit) and dashboard banner.
 * @returns {string} GREEN / YELLOW / RED
 */
function getDailyLimitStatus(accountId) {
  var accounts = getAccountsMap();
  var acct = accounts[accountId];
  if (!acct || acct.daily_loss_limit === 0) return 'GREEN';
  
  var limit = Math.abs(acct.daily_loss_limit);
  var pnl = acct.daily_pnl;
  
  if (pnl >= -(limit * 0.5)) return 'GREEN';
  if (pnl >= -limit) return 'YELLOW';
  return 'RED';
}

// ============================================================
// PHASE 1B: EXECUTIONS TAB
// ============================================================

/**
 * Creates the Executions tab with headers.
 */
function _ensureExecutionsTab() {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(TM_TAB_EXECUTIONS);
  if (!sheet) sheet = ss.insertSheet(TM_TAB_EXECUTIONS);
  if (String(sheet.getRange(1,1).getValue()).trim() !== TM_EXECUTIONS_HEADERS[0]) {
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, TM_EXECUTIONS_HEADERS.length).setValues([TM_EXECUTIONS_HEADERS]);
    sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
    Logger.log('Trade Management: Executions tab created');
  }
  return sheet;
}

    sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
    Logger.log('Trade Management: Trades tab created (65 columns)');
  }
  return sheet;
}
