// ============================================================
// MASTER SETUP: Build All Trade Management Tabs
// ============================================================

/**
 * Creates all 5 trade management tabs (headers only, no API calls).
 * Fast - should complete in <5 seconds. Safe to run multiple times.
 */
function buildTradeManagementTabs() {
  var t0 = Date.now();
  
  _ensureAccountsTab();
  _ensureExecutionsTab();
  _ensureTradesTab();
  _ensureDailyLogTab();
  _ensureSnapshotsTab();
  
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  var elapsed = ((Date.now() - t0) / 1000).toFixed(1);
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(
    'Trade Management tabs created! (' + elapsed + 's)\n\n' +
    'Accounts (14 columns)\n' +
    'Executions (12 columns)\n' +
    'Trades (65 columns)\n' +
    'DailyLog (31 columns)\n' +
    'Snapshots (25 columns)\n\n' +
    'Next: Run "Seed Accounts from TS" to populate account rows,\n' +
    'then review risk config on the Accounts tab.'
  );
  Logger.log('buildTradeManagementTabs: Complete in ' + elapsed + 's');
}

/**
 * Seeds Accounts tab from TS config + live balances.
 * Separate from tab creation to avoid Sheets timeout on API calls.
 */
function seedAccountsFromMenu() {
  try {
    var count = seedAccountsTab();
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Accounts seeded!\n\n' + count + ' account(s) from TradeStation config.\nReview risk limits on the Accounts tab.');
  } catch(e) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Seed failed: ' + e.message + '\n\nMake sure TS credentials are configured.');
    Logger.log('seedAccountsFromMenu error: ' + e.message);
  }
}

/**
 * Returns the next trade number (auto-increment).
 * Reads the max trade_num from Trades tab and adds 1.
 */
function _nextTradeNum() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var current = parseInt(props.getProperty('TM_TRADE_NUM_SEQ') || '0');
  
  // On first call or if counter is behind sheet, sync from sheet
  if (current === 0) {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(TM_TAB_TRADES);
    if (sheet && sheet.getLastRow() >= 2) {
      var nums = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getValues();
      for (var i = 0; i < nums.length; i++) {
        var n = parseInt(nums[i][0]) || 0;
        if (n > current) current = n;
      }
    }
  }
  
  var next = current + 1;
  props.setProperty('TM_TRADE_NUM_SEQ', String(next));
  return next;
}

/**
 * Takes a market context snapshot and writes to Snapshots tab.
 * @param {string} trigger - TRADE_ENTRY / TRADE_EXIT / GP_FLIP / ALERT
 * @param {number|null} tradeNum - FK to Trades tab (null for GP_FLIP/ALERT)
 * @param {string|null} tickerForContext - ticker symbol for IVR/beta/sector lookup
 * @returns {string} snap_id
 */
function snapshotContext(trigger, tradeNum, tickerForContext) {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(TM_TAB_SNAPSHOTS);
  if (!sheet) sheet = _ensureSnapshotsTab();
  
  var now = new Date();
  var snapId = 'SNAP-' + (tradeNum || Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyyMMddHHmmss')) + '-' + trigger;
  var ts = Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss');
  
  // Read current market state from Market tab
  var mkt = ss.getSheetByName('Market');
  var breadthScore = '', gameplan = '', vix = '', vixRegime = '', termStructure = '';
  var vixVix3m = '', vvix = '', spyIvr = '', tickerIvr = '', tickerBeta = '';
  var spyEm = '', fgScore = '', naaim = '', sectorLeader = '', tickerSector = '';
  var spyPrice = '', qqqPrice = '', tick = '', add = '', confluence = '';
  
  if (mkt) {
    var mktData = mkt.getDataRange().getValues();
    for (var i = 0; i < mktData.length; i++) {
      var label = String(mktData[i][0]).trim();
      var val = mktData[i][1];
      if (label === 'Breadth Score') breadthScore = val;
      if (label === 'VIX' || label === '$VIX.X') { vix = val; }
      if (label === 'SPY') spyPrice = val;
      if (label === 'QQQ') qqqPrice = val;
      if (label === '$TICK') tick = val;
      if (label === '$ADD') add = val;
    }
    // Gameplan from Watchlist tab A1
    var ws = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
    if (ws) {
      var gpText = String(ws.getRange(1, 1).getValue());
      if (gpText.indexOf('GP-A') >= 0) gameplan = 'A';
      else if (gpText.indexOf('GP-B') >= 0) gameplan = 'B';
      else if (gpText.indexOf('GP-C') >= 0) gameplan = 'C';
      else if (gpText.indexOf('GP-D') >= 0) gameplan = 'D';
    }
  }
  
  // Session phase
  var _tH = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'H'), 10);
  var _tM = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'm'), 10);
  var azMin = _tH * 60 + _tM;
  var sessionPhase = 'OFF';
  var _gpOff = _getMarketOffset();
  if (azMin >= (360 - _gpOff) && azMin < (450 - _gpOff)) sessionPhase = 'PM';
  else if (azMin >= (450 - _gpOff) && azMin < (540 - _gpOff)) sessionPhase = 'OPEN';
  else if (azMin >= (540 - _gpOff) && azMin < (780 - _gpOff)) sessionPhase = 'CORE';
  else if (azMin >= (780 - _gpOff) && azMin < (840 - _gpOff)) sessionPhase = 'POWER';
  else if (azMin >= (840 - _gpOff) && azMin < (960 - _gpOff)) sessionPhase = 'AH';
  
  // Bridge data (IVR, F&G, NAAIM, etc.) from cached properties
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  try {
    var pulseRaw = props.getProperty('PULSE_CACHE');
    if (pulseRaw) {
      var pulse = JSON.parse(pulseRaw);
      if (pulse.data) {
        spyIvr = pulse.data.spy_ivr || '';
        vvix = pulse.data.vvix || '';
        fgScore = pulse.data.fear_greed || '';
        naaim = pulse.data.naaim || '';
        spyEm = pulse.data.spy_em || '';
        var vixVal = parseFloat(vix) || 0;
        var vix3m = parseFloat(pulse.data.vix3m || 0);
        if (vixVal > 0 && vix3m > 0) vixVix3m = (vixVal / vix3m).toFixed(3);
        // Term structure
        if (vixVix3m) {
          var ratio = parseFloat(vixVix3m);
          if (ratio >= 1.05) termStructure = 'INVERTED';
          else if (ratio >= 0.95) termStructure = 'FLAT';
          else termStructure = 'CONTANGO';
        }
        // VIX regime
        if (vixVal < 15) vixRegime = 'Low';
        else if (vixVal < 18) vixRegime = 'Normal';
        else if (vixVal < 25) vixRegime = 'Elevated';
        else vixRegime = 'High';
      }
    }
  } catch(e) {}
  
  // Ticker-specific data (IVR, beta, sector, confluence) from Watchlist
  if (tickerForContext) {
    var ws2 = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
    if (ws2 && ws2.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var wsData = ws2.getDataRange().getValues();
      for (var w = 0; w < wsData.length; w++) {
        if (String(wsData[w][0]).trim().toUpperCase() === tickerForContext.toUpperCase()) {
          // Column positions depend on Watchlist layout — adjust as needed
          confluence = wsData[w][7] || ''; // confluence score column
          break;
        }
      }
    }
  }
  
  var row = [
    snapId, ts, trigger, tradeNum || '',
    breadthScore, gameplan, sessionPhase,
    vix, vixRegime, termStructure, vixVix3m, vvix,
    spyIvr, tickerIvr, tickerBeta, spyEm,
    fgScore, naaim, sectorLeader, tickerSector,
    spyPrice, qqqPrice, tick, add, confluence
  ];
  
  sheet.getRange(sheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, 1, row.length).setValues([row]);
  Logger.log('snapshotContext: ' + snapId);
  return snapId;
}


// ============================================================
// PHASE 2-3: TRADE SYNC ENGINE
// ============================================================
// _fetchTSFilledOrders  - pulls filled orders from TradeStation
// _fetchAlpacaFilledOrders - pulls filled orders from Alpaca
// logExecution - writes single row to Executions tab (dedup)
// groupToTrade - creates/updates parent Trade from execution
// syncTrades - master sync called every scanner tick
// ============================================================

function _fetchTSFilledOrders(tsRawAccountId, sinceDate) {
  var token = getAccessToken();
  var url = 'https://api.tradestation.com/v3/brokerage/accounts/' + tsRawAccountId + '/orders?since=' + sinceDate + '&pageSize=600';
  var response = trackedFetch(url, { method: 'get', headers: { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + token }, muteHttpExceptions: true }, 'ts-orders');
  if (response.getResponseCode() !== 200) { Logger.log('_fetchTSFilledOrders: HTTP ' + response.getResponseCode()); return []; }
  var orders = (JSON.parse(response.getContentText())).Orders || [];
  var fills = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < orders.length; i++) {
    var o = orders[i];
    var status = String(o.Status || o.StatusDescription || '').toUpperCase();
    if (status.indexOf('FLL') < 0 && status.indexOf('FILL') < 0) continue;
    var assetType = String(o.AssetType || '').toUpperCase();
    if (assetType && assetType !== 'EQ' && assetType !== 'STOCK' && assetType !== '') continue;
    var sym = String(o.Symbol || '').replace(/\s+/g, '');
    if (!sym) continue;
    var buyOrSell = String(o.BuyOrSell || o.Side || '').toUpperCase();
    var action = 'BUY';
    if (buyOrSell === 'SELL') action = 'SELL';
    if (buyOrSell === 'SELLSHORT' || buyOrSell === 'SHORT') action = 'SHORT';
    if (buyOrSell === 'BUYTOCOVER' || buyOrSell === 'COVER') action = 'COVER';
    var legs = o.Legs || [];
    if (legs.length > 0) {
      for (var l = 0; l < legs.length; l++) {
        var leg = legs[l];
        fills.push({
          exec_id: 'TS-' + String(o.OrderID || '') + '-' + l,
          timestamp: leg.ExecutionTimestamp || o.ClosedDateTime || o.OpenedDateTime || '',
          symbol: sym, action: action,
          quantity: Math.abs(parseFloat(leg.ExecQuantity || leg.QuantityOrdered || o.FilledQuantity || 0)),
          fill_price: parseFloat(leg.ExecPrice || leg.ExecutionPrice || o.FilledPrice || 0),
          commission: parseFloat(leg.Commission || 0),
          order_type: String(o.OrderType || o.Type || 'MARKET').toUpperCase()
        });
      }
    } else {
      fills.push({
        exec_id: 'TS-' + String(o.OrderID || ''),
        timestamp: o.ClosedDateTime || o.OpenedDateTime || '',
        symbol: sym, action: action,
        quantity: Math.abs(parseFloat(o.FilledQuantity || o.Quantity || o.QuantityOrdered || 0)),
        fill_price: parseFloat(o.FilledPrice || o.AvgFillPrice || o.AverageFillPrice || 0),
        commission: parseFloat(o.CommissionFee || o.Commission || 0),
        order_type: String(o.OrderType || o.Type || 'MARKET').toUpperCase()
      });
    }
  }
  Logger.log('_fetchTSFilledOrders: ' + fills.length + ' fills from ' + tsRawAccountId);
  return fills;
}

function _fetchAlpacaFilledOrders(sinceISO) {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var keyId = props.getProperty('ALPACA_KEY_ID');
  var secretKey = props.getProperty('ALPACA_SECRET_KEY');
  if (!keyId || !secretKey) return [];
  var url = 'https://paper-api.alpaca.markets/v2/orders?status=filled&limit=500&direction=asc';
  if (sinceISO) url += '&after=' + sinceISO;
  var response = trackedFetch(url, {
    method: 'get',
    headers: { 'APCA-API-KEY-ID': keyId, 'APCA-API-SECRET-KEY': secretKey, 'accept': 'application/json' },
    muteHttpExceptions: true
  }, 'alpaca-orders');
  if (response.getResponseCode() !== 200) { Logger.log('_fetchAlpacaFilledOrders: HTTP ' + response.getResponseCode()); return []; }
  var orders = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
  var fills = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < orders.length; i++) {
    var o = orders[i];
    if (String(o.status) !== 'filled') continue;
    if (String(o.asset_class || 'us_equity') !== 'us_equity') continue;
    var sym = String(o.symbol || '');
    if (!sym) continue;
    var side = String(o.side || '').toUpperCase();
    var action = (side === 'BUY') ? 'BUY' : 'SELL';
    fills.push({
      exec_id: 'ALP-' + String(o.id || ''),
      timestamp: o.filled_at || o.updated_at || '',
      symbol: sym, action: action,
      quantity: Math.abs(parseFloat(o.filled_qty || o.qty || 0)),
      fill_price: parseFloat(o.filled_avg_price || 0),
      commission: 0,
      order_type: String(o.type || 'market').toUpperCase()
    });
  }
  Logger.log('_fetchAlpacaFilledOrders: ' + fills.length + ' fills');
  return fills;
}

function logExecution(fill, accountId, source) {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(TM_TAB_EXECUTIONS);
  if (!sheet) sheet = _ensureExecutionsTab();
  var lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow > 1) {
    var existingIds = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 1).getValues();
    for (var i = 0; i < existingIds.length; i++) {
      if (String(existingIds[i][0]).trim() === fill.exec_id) return false;
    }
  }
  var azTimestamp = '';
  if (fill.timestamp) {
    try { azTimestamp = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(fill.timestamp), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss'); }
    catch(e) { azTimestamp = String(fill.timestamp); }
  }
  var row = [fill.exec_id, '', azTimestamp, accountId, fill.symbol, fill.action,
             fill.quantity, fill.fill_price, fill.commission || 0, '',
             fill.order_type || '', source];
  sheet.getRange(lastRow + 1, 1, 1, row.length).setValues([row]);
  return true;
}

function _currentGameplan(ws) {
  if (!ws) return 'C';
  var gpText = String(ws.getRange(1, 1).getValue());
  if (gpText.indexOf('GP-A') >= 0) return 'A';
  if (gpText.indexOf('GP-B') >= 0) return 'B';
  if (gpText.indexOf('GP-D') >= 0) return 'D';
  return 'C';
}

function groupToTrade(fill, accountId, execRow) {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var tradesSheet = ss.getSheetByName(TM_TAB_TRADES);
  var execSheet = ss.getSheetByName(TM_TAB_EXECUTIONS);
  if (!tradesSheet || !execSheet) return;
  // Guard: skip if already grouped
  var existingTN = execSheet.getRange(execRow, 2).getValue();
  if (existingTN && String(existingTN).trim() !== '') {
    Logger.log('groupToTrade: row ' + execRow + ' already trade #' + existingTN);
    return parseInt(existingTN);
  }

  // Find matching OPEN or PLANNED trade: same symbol + same account
  var tradesData = tradesSheet.getLastRow() > 1
    ? tradesSheet.getRange(2, 1, tradesSheet.getLastRow() - 1, TM_TRADES_HEADERS.length).getValues()
    : [];

  var matchIdx = -1;
  for (var i = 0; i < tradesData.length; i++) {
    var tSym = String(tradesData[i][1]).trim().toUpperCase();
    var tAcct = String(tradesData[i][2]).trim();
    var tStatus = String(tradesData[i][5]).trim().toUpperCase();
    if (tSym === fill.symbol.toUpperCase() && tAcct === accountId &&
        (tStatus === 'OPEN' || tStatus === 'PLANNED')) {
      matchIdx = i;
      break;
    }
  }

  var isAdditive = (fill.action === 'BUY' || fill.action === 'SHORT');
  var tradeNum;

  if (matchIdx >= 0) {
    // ---- EXISTING TRADE ----
    tradeNum = parseInt(tradesData[matchIdx][0]);
    var tradeRow = matchIdx + 2;
    var currentStatus = String(tradesData[matchIdx][5]).trim().toUpperCase();
    var wasPlanned = (currentStatus === 'PLANNED');
    var currentSide = String(tradesData[matchIdx][3]).trim().toUpperCase();

    // Column indices (0-based in tradesData array)
    // [0]=trade_num [1]=symbol [2]=account_id [3]=side [4]=trade_type [5]=status [6]=was_planned
    // [13]=dollar_risk [32]=gameplan_at_entry
    // [36]=entry_time [37]=entry_price [38]=total_shares [39]=position_dollars [40]=entry_legs
    // [41]=exit_time [42]=exit_price [43]=exit_legs
    // [44]=gross_pnl [45]=net_pnl [46]=pnl_pct [47]=r_multiple
    // [50]=entry_snap_id [51]=exit_snap_id
    // [63]=hold_minutes [64]=hold_days

    var curEntryPrice = parseFloat(tradesData[matchIdx][37]) || 0;
    var curShares = parseFloat(tradesData[matchIdx][38]) || 0;
    var curEntryLegs = parseInt(tradesData[matchIdx][40]) || 0;
    var curExitLegs = parseInt(tradesData[matchIdx][43]) || 0;

    if (isAdditive) {
      // ---- SCALE-IN ----
      var newTotalCost = (curEntryPrice * curShares) + (fill.fill_price * fill.quantity);
      var newShares = curShares + fill.quantity;
      var newAvg = newShares > 0 ? (newTotalCost / newShares) : fill.fill_price;

      tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 38).setValue(Math.round(newAvg * 10000) / 10000);
      tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 39).setValue(newShares);
      tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 40).setValue(Math.round(newShares * newAvg * 100) / 100);
      tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 41).setValue(curEntryLegs + 1);

      if (wasPlanned) {
        tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 6).setValue('OPEN');
        try {
          tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 37).setValue(
            Utilities.formatDate(new Date(fill.timestamp), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss'));
        } catch(e) {}
        var snapId = snapshotContext('TRADE_ENTRY', tradeNum, fill.symbol);
        tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 51).setValue(snapId);
        var ws = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
        tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 33).setValue(_currentGameplan(ws));
      }
      execSheet.getRange(execRow, 10).setValue(newShares);

    } else {
      // ---- SCALE-OUT / CLOSE ----
      var remaining = curShares - fill.quantity;
      tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 44).setValue(curExitLegs + 1);

      if (remaining <= 0) {
        remaining = 0;
        tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 6).setValue('CLOSED');
        try {
          tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 42).setValue(
            Utilities.formatDate(new Date(fill.timestamp), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss'));
        } catch(e) {}
        tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 43).setValue(fill.fill_price);

        // P&L calculation
        var entryP = curEntryPrice;
        var exitP = fill.fill_price;
        var grossPnl = (currentSide === 'LONG') ? (exitP - entryP) * curShares : (entryP - exitP) * curShares;
        var netPnl = grossPnl - (fill.commission || 0);
        var posDollars = parseFloat(tradesData[matchIdx][39]) || (entryP * curShares);
        var pnlPct = posDollars > 0 ? (netPnl / posDollars * 100) : 0;
        var dollarRisk = parseFloat(tradesData[matchIdx][13]) || 0;
        var rMult = dollarRisk > 0 ? (netPnl / dollarRisk) : 0;

        tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 45).setValue(Math.round(grossPnl * 100) / 100);
        tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 46).setValue(Math.round(netPnl * 100) / 100);
        tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 47).setValue(Math.round(pnlPct * 100) / 100);
        tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 48).setValue(Math.round(rMult * 100) / 100);

        // Hold time
        var entryTime = tradesData[matchIdx][36];
        if (entryTime) {
          try {
            var holdMs = new Date(fill.timestamp) - new Date(entryTime);
            tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 64).setValue(Math.round(holdMs / 60000));
            tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 65).setValue(Math.round(holdMs / 86400000));
          } catch(e) {}
        }

        // Exit snapshot
        var exitSnapId = snapshotContext('TRADE_EXIT', tradeNum, fill.symbol);
        tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 52).setValue(exitSnapId);
      }
      execSheet.getRange(execRow, 10).setValue(remaining);
    }
    execSheet.getRange(execRow, 2).setValue(tradeNum);

  } else {
    // ---- NEW UNPLANNED TRADE ----
    tradeNum = _nextTradeNum();
    var side = (fill.action === 'BUY' || fill.action === 'COVER') ? 'LONG' : 'SHORT';
    var accounts = getAccountsMap();
    var acct = accounts[accountId];
    var tradeType = acct ? acct.type : 'DT';

    var newRow = new Array(TM_TRADES_HEADERS.length).fill('');
    newRow[0] = tradeNum;
    newRow[1] = fill.symbol;
    newRow[2] = accountId;
    newRow[3] = side;
    newRow[4] = tradeType;
    newRow[5] = 'OPEN';
    newRow[6] = false;

    try {
      newRow[36] = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(fill.timestamp), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss');
    } catch(e) { newRow[36] = String(fill.timestamp); }
    newRow[37] = fill.fill_price;
    newRow[38] = fill.quantity;
    newRow[39] = Math.round(fill.fill_price * fill.quantity * 100) / 100;
    newRow[40] = 1;

    var ws = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
    newRow[32] = _currentGameplan(ws);

    var snapId = snapshotContext('TRADE_ENTRY', tradeNum, fill.symbol);
    newRow[50] = snapId;

    tradesSheet.getRange(tradesSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, 1, newRow.length).setValues([newRow]);
    execSheet.getRange(execRow, 2).setValue(tradeNum);
    execSheet.getRange(execRow, 10).setValue(fill.quantity);
    Logger.log('groupToTrade: NEW #' + tradeNum + ' ' + fill.symbol + ' ' + side);
  }
  return tradeNum;
}

function syncTrades() {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  var lastAlpacaSync = props.getProperty('TM_LAST_ALPACA_SYNC') || '';
  var totalNew = 0;

  // TradeStation accounts
  var tsConfig = getTSAccountConfig();
  for (var t = 0; t < tsConfig.length; t++) {
    var cfg = tsConfig[t];
    if (cfg.type === 'CASH') continue;
    var ourAcctId = 'TS-' + (cfg.type || 'UNK');
    try {
      var fills = _fetchTSFilledOrders(cfg.id, today);
      for (var f = 0; f < fills.length; f++) {
        var isNew = logExecution(fills[f], ourAcctId, 'tradestation');
        if (isNew) {
          var execRow = ss.getSheetByName(TM_TAB_EXECUTIONS).getLastRow();
          groupToTrade(fills[f], ourAcctId, execRow);
          totalNew++;
        }
      }
    } catch(e) { Logger.log('syncTrades: TS error ' + ourAcctId + ': ' + e.message); }
  }
  props.setProperty('TM_LAST_TS_SYNC', new Date().toISOString());

  // Alpaca paper
  try {
    var alpacaSince = lastAlpacaSync || (today + 'T00:00:00Z');
    var alpacaFills = _fetchAlpacaFilledOrders(alpacaSince);
    for (var a = 0; a < alpacaFills.length; a++) {
      var isNew = logExecution(alpacaFills[a], 'ALPACA-PAPER', 'alpaca');
      if (isNew) {
        var execRow = ss.getSheetByName(TM_TAB_EXECUTIONS).getLastRow();
        groupToTrade(alpacaFills[a], 'ALPACA-PAPER', execRow);
        totalNew++;
      }
    }
  } catch(e) { Logger.log('syncTrades: Alpaca error: ' + e.message); }
  props.setProperty('TM_LAST_ALPACA_SYNC', new Date().toISOString());

  if (totalNew > 0) {
    Logger.log('syncTrades: ' + totalNew + ' new executions');
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  }
  return totalNew;
}

function syncTradesManual() {
  var count = syncTrades();
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Trade sync complete!\n\n' + count + ' new execution(s) logged.');
}



// ============================================================
// RECONCILE: Sync Trades tab to actual broker positions
// ============================================================

/**
 * Reads current positions from all brokers and reconciles with Trades tab.
 * - If OPEN trade exists for symbol+account: updates total_shares, entry_price, position_dollars
 * - If no trade exists: creates new OPEN trade from position data
 * - If OPEN trade has no matching position: marks as CLOSED (position was closed outside sync)
 * Run once to bootstrap existing positions, then syncTrades handles ongoing.
 */
function reconcilePositions() {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var tradesSheet = ss.getSheetByName(TM_TAB_TRADES);
  if (!tradesSheet) tradesSheet = _ensureTradesTab();
  
  var now = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss');
  var ws = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
  var gp = _currentGameplan(ws);
  
  // Gather all positions from all brokers
  var allPositions = []; // { symbol, side, qty, avgCost, accountId, broker }
  
  // TradeStation positions
  var tsConfig = getTSAccountConfig();
  for (var t = 0; t < tsConfig.length; t++) {
    var cfg = tsConfig[t];
    if (cfg.type === 'CASH') continue;
    var ourAcctId = 'TS-' + (cfg.type || 'UNK');
    try {
      var rawPositions = tsGetPositions(cfg.id);
      var rows = _buildPositionRows(rawPositions);
      for (var r = 0; r < rows.length; r++) {
        allPositions.push({
          symbol: rows[r].sym,
          side: rows[r].side === 'Long' ? 'LONG' : 'SHORT',
          qty: rows[r].qty,
          avgCost: rows[r].avgCost,
          accountId: ourAcctId,
          broker: 'tradestation'
        });
      }
    } catch(e) {
      Logger.log('reconcilePositions: TS error ' + ourAcctId + ': ' + e.message);
    }
  }
  
  // Alpaca positions
  try {
    var alpacaRaw = alpacaGetPositions();
    var alpacaRows = _buildAlpacaPositionRows(alpacaRaw);
    for (var a = 0; a < alpacaRows.length; a++) {
      allPositions.push({
        symbol: alpacaRows[a].sym,
        side: alpacaRows[a].side === 'Long' ? 'LONG' : 'SHORT',
        qty: alpacaRows[a].qty,
        avgCost: alpacaRows[a].avgCost,
        accountId: 'ALPACA-PAPER',
        broker: 'alpaca'
      });
    }
  } catch(e) {
    Logger.log('reconcilePositions: Alpaca error: ' + e.message);
  }
  
  Logger.log('reconcilePositions: ' + allPositions.length + ' positions found across all accounts');
  
  // Read existing trades
  var tradesData = tradesSheet.getLastRow() > 1
    ? tradesSheet.getRange(2, 1, tradesSheet.getLastRow() - 1, TM_TRADES_HEADERS.length).getValues()
    : [];
  
  // Build lookup: key = SYMBOL|ACCOUNT_ID, value = { rowIndex, data }
  var tradeMap = {};
  for (var i = 0; i < tradesData.length; i++) {
    var tStatus = String(tradesData[i][5]).trim().toUpperCase();
    if (tStatus !== 'OPEN' && tStatus !== 'PLANNED') continue;
    var key = String(tradesData[i][1]).trim().toUpperCase() + '|' + String(tradesData[i][2]).trim();
    tradeMap[key] = { rowIndex: i, row: i + 2, data: tradesData[i] };
  }
  
  var updated = 0;
  var created = 0;
  var matched = {}; // track which trade keys were matched to a position
  
  for (var p = 0; p < allPositions.length; p++) {
    var pos = allPositions[p];
    var key = pos.symbol.toUpperCase() + '|' + pos.accountId;
    matched[key] = true;
    
    if (tradeMap[key]) {
      // ---- UPDATE EXISTING TRADE ----
      var tr = tradeMap[key];
      var tradeRow = tr.row;
      
      tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 4).setValue(pos.side);                                       // side
      tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 38).setValue(pos.avgCost);                                    // entry_price
      tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 39).setValue(pos.qty);                                        // total_shares
      tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 40).setValue(Math.round(pos.qty * pos.avgCost * 100) / 100);  // position_dollars
      
      // If status was PLANNED, promote to OPEN
      if (String(tr.data[5]).trim().toUpperCase() === 'PLANNED') {
        tradesSheet.getRange(tradeRow, 6).setValue('OPEN');
      }
      
      updated++;
      Logger.log('reconcilePositions: UPDATED ' + pos.symbol + ' @ ' + pos.accountId + ' -> ' + pos.qty + ' shares @ $' + pos.avgCost);
      
    } else {
      // ---- CREATE NEW TRADE FROM POSITION ----
      var tradeNum = _nextTradeNum();
      var accounts = getAccountsMap();
      var acct = accounts[pos.accountId];
      var tradeType = acct ? acct.type : 'DT';
      
      var newRow = new Array(TM_TRADES_HEADERS.length).fill('');
      newRow[0] = tradeNum;              // trade_num
      newRow[1] = pos.symbol;            // symbol
      newRow[2] = pos.accountId;         // account_id
      newRow[3] = pos.side;              // side
      newRow[4] = tradeType;             // trade_type
      newRow[5] = 'OPEN';               // status
      newRow[6] = false;                 // was_planned
      newRow[32] = gp;                   // gameplan_at_entry
      newRow[36] = now;                  // entry_time (approximate - we don't know actual)
      newRow[37] = pos.avgCost;          // entry_price
      newRow[38] = pos.qty;              // total_shares
      newRow[39] = Math.round(pos.qty * pos.avgCost * 100) / 100; // position_dollars
      newRow[40] = 1;                    // entry_legs (unknown, default 1)
      
      tradesSheet.getRange(tradesSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, 1, newRow.length).setValues([newRow]);
      
      // Update tradeMap so subsequent positions don't duplicate
      var newIdx = tradesSheet.getLastRow() - 2;
      tradeMap[key] = { rowIndex: newIdx, row: tradesSheet.getLastRow(), data: newRow };
      
      created++;
      Logger.log('reconcilePositions: CREATED trade #' + tradeNum + ' ' + pos.symbol + ' ' + pos.side + ' ' + pos.qty + ' @ $' + pos.avgCost);
    }
  }
  
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  
  var msg = 'Position reconciliation complete!\n\n' +
            allPositions.length + ' broker position(s) found\n' +
            updated + ' existing trade(s) updated\n' +
            created + ' new trade(s) created\n\n' +
            'Review the Trades tab to verify.';
  
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(msg);
  Logger.log('reconcilePositions: ' + updated + ' updated, ' + created + ' created');
}


// ============================================================
// PHASE 1D: DAILY LOG + EOD FLOW
// ============================================================

function generateDailyLog() {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(TM_TAB_DAILYLOG);
  if (!sheet) sheet = _ensureDailyLogTab();
  var today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  var now = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss');
  var lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow > 1) {
    var dates = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 1).getValues();
    for (var i = 0; i < dates.length; i++) {
      var existing = '';
      try { existing = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(dates[i][0]), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd'); } catch(e) { existing = String(dates[i][0]).substring(0, 10); }
      if (existing === today) {
        _writeDailyLogRow(sheet, i + 2, today, now, ss);
        Logger.log('generateDailyLog: Updated existing entry for ' + today);
        return;
      }
    }
  }
  _writeDailyLogRow(sheet, lastRow + 1, today, now, ss);
  Logger.log('generateDailyLog: New entry for ' + today);
}

function _writeDailyLogRow(sheet, rowNum, today, now, ss) {
  var accounts = getAccountsMap();
  var totalDayPnl = 0;
  var totalEquity = 0;
  var bodEquity = 0;
  for (var id in accounts) {
    totalDayPnl += parseFloat(accounts[id].daily_pnl) || 0;
    totalEquity += parseFloat(accounts[id].current_equity) || 0;
    bodEquity += parseFloat(accounts[id].bod_equity) || 0;
  }
  var dayPnlPct = bodEquity > 0 ? (totalDayPnl / bodEquity * 100) : 0;

  var tradesSheet = ss.getSheetByName(TM_TAB_TRADES);
  var tradesData = tradesSheet && tradesSheet.getLastRow() > 1
    ? tradesSheet.getRange(2, 1, tradesSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 65).getValues() : [];

  var todayOpened = 0;
  var todayWins = 0;
  var todayLosses = 0;
  var todayGrossPnl = 0;
  var todayCommissions = 0;
  var todayRMultiples = [];
  var biggestWin = 0;
  var biggestLoss = 0;
  var openPositions = 0;

  for (var i = 0; i < tradesData.length; i++) {
    var entryTime = String(tradesData[i][36]).substring(0, 10);
    var exitTime = String(tradesData[i][41]).substring(0, 10);
    var status = String(tradesData[i][5]).trim().toUpperCase();
    if (entryTime === today) todayOpened++;
    if (status === 'OPEN') openPositions++;
    if (status === 'CLOSED' && exitTime === today) {
      var grossPnl = parseFloat(tradesData[i][44]) || 0;
      var netPnl = parseFloat(tradesData[i][45]) || 0;
      var rMult = parseFloat(tradesData[i][47]) || 0;
      todayGrossPnl += grossPnl;
      todayCommissions += grossPnl - netPnl;
      todayRMultiples.push(rMult);
      if (netPnl > 0) { todayWins++; if (netPnl > biggestWin) biggestWin = netPnl; }
      else if (netPnl < 0) { todayLosses++; if (netPnl < biggestLoss) biggestLoss = netPnl; }
    }
  }

  var todayClosed = todayWins + todayLosses;
  var winRate = todayClosed > 0 ? (todayWins / todayClosed * 100) : 0;
  var avgR = todayRMultiples.length > 0
    ? todayRMultiples.reduce(function(a,b){return a+b;}, 0) / todayRMultiples.length : 0;

  var marketSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Market');
  var breadthScore = 0;
  if (marketSheet) { try { breadthScore = parseFloat(marketSheet.getRange('B2').getValue()) || 0; } catch(e) {} }

  var ws = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
  var gp = _currentGameplan(ws);
  var dayOfWeek = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'EEEE');

  // 31 columns matching TM_DAILYLOG_HEADERS
  var row = [
    today, dayOfWeek, gp, breadthScore, 0, 0,
    todayOpened, todayClosed, todayWins, todayLosses,
    Math.round(winRate * 10) / 10,
    Math.round(todayGrossPnl * 100) / 100,
    Math.round((todayGrossPnl - todayCommissions) * 100) / 100,
    Math.round(todayCommissions * 100) / 100,
    Math.round(biggestWin * 100) / 100,
    Math.round(biggestLoss * 100) / 100,
    Math.round(avgR * 100) / 100,
    Math.round(totalDayPnl * 100) / 100,
    Math.round(dayPnlPct * 100) / 100,
    Math.round(bodEquity * 100) / 100,
    Math.round(totalEquity * 100) / 100,
    openPositions,
    '', '', '', '', '', '', '', '', now
  ];
  sheet.getRange(rowNum, 1, 1, row.length).setValues([row]);
}

function runEOD() {
  var t0 = Date.now();
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var newExecs = 0;
  try { newExecs = syncTrades(); } catch(e) { Logger.log('EOD syncTrades: ' + e.message); }
  try { refreshAccountEquity(false); } catch(e) { Logger.log('EOD equity: ' + e.message); }
  try { generateDailyLog(); } catch(e) { Logger.log('EOD dailyLog: ' + e.message); }
  // Dynamic watchlist EOD cleanup
  try { cleanupDynamic(ss); } catch(e) { Logger.log('EOD dynamic cleanup: ' + e.message); }
  // Decay CONF_PEAK_5D for low-signal deprioritization
  try { _decayConfPeaks(); } catch(e) { Logger.log('EOD confPeak decay: ' + e.message); }
  // Merge today's volume into rolling profile for RVOL-TOD
  try { _mergeVolProfile(ss); } catch(e) { Logger.log('EOD volProfile merge: ' + e.message); }
  var elapsed = ((Date.now() - t0) / 1000).toFixed(1);
  var accounts = getAccountsMap();
  var totalPnl = 0;
  for (var id in accounts) { totalPnl += parseFloat(accounts[id].daily_pnl) || 0; }
  var pnlSign = totalPnl >= 0 ? '+' : '';
  var msg = 'EOD Complete (' + elapsed + 's)\n\n' +
    'New executions: ' + newExecs + '\n' +
    'Day P&L: ' + pnlSign + '$' + (Math.round(totalPnl * 100) / 100) + '\n\n' +
    'DailyLog updated. Fill in:\n' +
    '- rules_followed\n- emotional_state\n- lessons\n- plan_for_tomorrow';
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(msg);
  Logger.log('runEOD: Complete in ' + elapsed + 's');
}

function runEODManual() {
  runEOD();
}

/**
 * Triggered version of EOD — skips weekends and holidays.
 * Called by the time-based trigger installed via installEODTrigger().
 */
function runEODTriggered() {
  var dayOfWeek = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'EEEE');
  if (dayOfWeek === 'Saturday' || dayOfWeek === 'Sunday') {
    Logger.log('runEODTriggered: Weekend (' + dayOfWeek + '), skipping');
    return;
  }
  Logger.log('runEODTriggered: ' + dayOfWeek + ', running EOD');
  runEOD();
}

/**
 * Installs a daily trigger for EOD at ~2:05 PM AZ time.
 * Run once from the menu. The trigger fires M-F only (weekend gate in runEODTriggered).
 */
function installEODTrigger() {
  var triggers = ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers();
  for (var i = 0; i < triggers.length; i++) {
    if (triggers[i].getHandlerFunction() === 'runEODTriggered') {
      ScriptApp.deleteTrigger(triggers[i]);
    }
  }
  ScriptApp.newTrigger('runEODTriggered')
    .timeBased()
    .atHour(14)
    .nearMinute(5)
    .everyDays(1)
    .inTimezone('America/Phoenix')
    .create();
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('EOD trigger installed!' + '\n' + 'Fires daily ~2:05 PM AZ (M-F only).' + '\n' + 'Weekends are auto-skipped.');
}

/**
 * Removes the EOD trigger.
 */
function removeEODTrigger() {
  var removed = 0;
  var triggers = ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers();
  for (var i = 0; i < triggers.length; i++) {
    if (triggers[i].getHandlerFunction() === 'runEODTriggered') {
      ScriptApp.deleteTrigger(triggers[i]);
      removed++;
    }
  }
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(removed + ' EOD trigger(s) removed.');
}

// PHASE 2: PRE-TRADE CARD — SCANNER BACKEND (v90.8)
// ============================================================
// getPreTradeData(symbol)      → returns all scanner data for card
// evaluateScorecard(params)    → 8 traffic-light checks
// computePositionSize(params)  → gameplan-adjusted sizing w/ IVR+beta
// logPlannedTrade(params)      → writes PLANNED row + snapshot
// getActiveSetups()            → surfaces high-confluence actionable tickers

// ── Gameplan position sizing — PERCENT OF CURRENT LIVE EQUITY ──
// All sizing is now % based. Dollar amounts computed at runtime by
// multiplying % × current equity from Accounts tab.
// Equity reference: current_equity (live, updates intraday).
var GP_SIZING_PCT = {
  'A': { posLo: 0.20, posHi: 0.25, riskLo: 0.0075, riskHi: 0.010 },
  'B': { posLo: 0.12, posHi: 0.18, riskLo: 0.0050, riskHi: 0.0075 },
  'C': { posLo: 0,    posHi: 0,    riskLo: 0,       riskHi: 0 },
  'D': { posLo: 0.12, posHi: 0.18, riskLo: 0.0050, riskHi: 0.0075 }
};

// ── Sub-mode sizing overrides (sizingAdj → % of equity) ──
// Authoritative sizing source. GP_SIZING_PCT is legacy fallback.
// posLo/posHi = position size as fraction of equity (0.20 = 20%)
// riskLo/riskHi = max risk per trade as fraction of equity (0.01 = 1%)
var SUBMODE_SIZING_PCT = {
  'full':     { posLo: 0.20, posHi: 0.25, riskLo: 0.0075, riskHi: 0.010 },   // A-Surge, A-Steady
  'standard': { posLo: 0.12, posHi: 0.18, riskLo: 0.0050, riskHi: 0.0075 },  // B-Building, B-Steady, D-Persistent
  'reduce':   { posLo: 0.08, posHi: 0.12, riskLo: 0.0035, riskHi: 0.005 },   // A-Cooling, A-Choppy, B-Weakening, B-Choppy, D-Bottoming
  'caution':  { posLo: 0.08, posHi: 0.12, riskLo: 0.0035, riskHi: 0.005 },   // alias for reduce
  'small':    { posLo: 0.04, posHi: 0.07, riskLo: 0.0020, riskHi: 0.0035 },  // C-Recovery — Tier 1-3 max
  'bench':    { posLo: 0,    posHi: 0,    riskLo: 0,       riskHi: 0 },       // C-Flat, C-Choppy, C-Deteriorating
  'inverse':  { posLo: 0.12, posHi: 0.18, riskLo: 0.0050, riskHi: 0.0075 }   // D-Persistent, D-Capitulation, D-Choppy
};

// ── Helper: read current sub-mode from ScriptProperties ──
function _getCurrentSubMode() {
  try {
    var raw = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('GP_SUB_MODE');
    if (raw) return JSON.parse(raw);
  } catch(e) {}
  return null;
}

// ── Helper: check if setup is allowed for current GP sub-mode ──
// Returns { allowed:bool, caution:bool, reason:string }
function _checkSetupGP(setupType, subModeLabel, gpLetter) {
  var reg = SETUP_REGISTRY[setupType];
  if (!reg || !reg.validGP) return { allowed: true, caution: false, reason: '' };
  var validGP = reg.validGP;

  // 1. Exact sub-mode label match (e.g. 'C-Recovery')
  if (validGP.indexOf(subModeLabel) >= 0) {
    return { allowed: true, caution: false, reason: subModeLabel + ' supports ' + setupType };
  }

  // 2. Base GP letter match (e.g. 'A' matches A-Surge, A-Cooling, etc.)
  if (validGP.indexOf(gpLetter) >= 0) {
    // Check for caution: sub-mode suggests weakness within an allowed GP
    var cautionModes = {
      'A-Cooling': ['Momentum','GapGo'],
      'A-Choppy':  ['Momentum','GapGo','BigDog'],
      'B-Weakening': ['OR-Break','DailyBreakout','BigDog','SecondDay','OpeningDrive'],
      'B-Choppy':  ['OR-Break','DailyBreakout','BigDog']
    };
    var cautionSetups = cautionModes[subModeLabel] || [];
    if (cautionSetups.indexOf(setupType) >= 0) {
      return { allowed: true, caution: true, reason: subModeLabel + ': breadth weakening, ' + setupType + ' higher risk' };
    }
    return { allowed: true, caution: false, reason: 'GP-' + gpLetter + ' supports ' + setupType };
  }

  // 3. Not allowed
  return { allowed: false, caution: false, reason: subModeLabel + ' does not support ' + setupType };
}

// ── Helper: get effective sizing percentages for current sub-mode ──
// Returns { posLo, posHi, riskLo, riskHi } as fractions (0.20 = 20%)
function _getEffectiveSizingPct(subMode, gpLetter) {
  if (subMode && subMode.sizingAdj && SUBMODE_SIZING_PCT[subMode.sizingAdj]) {
    return SUBMODE_SIZING_PCT[subMode.sizingAdj];
  }
  return GP_SIZING_PCT[gpLetter] || GP_SIZING_PCT['C'];
}

// ── Helper: resolve current live equity from Accounts tab ──
function _getCurrentEquity(accountId) {
  try {
    var accounts = getAccountsMap();
    if (accountId && accounts[accountId]) {
      return parseFloat(accounts[accountId].current_equity) || 0;
    }
    var total = 0;
    for (var id in accounts) {
      total += parseFloat(accounts[id].current_equity) || 0;
    }
    return total;
  } catch(e) {
    return 0;
  }
}

// ── Helper: convert sizing percentages to dollar amounts given equity ──
// Returns baseLo/baseHi/riskLo/riskHi in dollars PLUS pct fields + equity ref.
// Same return shape as old _getEffectiveSizing so all callers work unchanged.
function _getEffectiveSizing(subMode, gpLetter, accountId) {
  var pct = _getEffectiveSizingPct(subMode, gpLetter);
  var equity = _getCurrentEquity(accountId);
  if (equity <= 0) {
    return { baseLo: 0, baseHi: 0, riskLo: 0, riskHi: 0,
             posLoPct: pct.posLo, posHiPct: pct.posHi,
             riskLoPct: pct.riskLo, riskHiPct: pct.riskHi,
             equity: 0, pctBased: true };
  }
  return {
    baseLo: Math.round(equity * pct.posLo),
    baseHi: Math.round(equity * pct.posHi),
    riskLo: Math.round(equity * pct.riskLo),
    riskHi: Math.round(equity * pct.riskHi),
    posLoPct: pct.posLo,
    posHiPct: pct.posHi,
    riskLoPct: pct.riskLo,
    riskHiPct: pct.riskHi,
    equity: equity,
    pctBased: true
  };
}

/**
 * Returns current session phase string for scorecard/sizing.
 */
function _currentSessionPhase() {
  var now = new Date();
  var h = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'H'), 10);
  var m = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(now, SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'm'), 10);
  var azMin = h * 60 + m;
  var off = _getMarketOffset();
  if (azMin >= (360 - off) && azMin < (450 - off)) return 'PM';
  if (azMin >= (450 - off) && azMin < (540 - off)) return 'OPEN';
  if (azMin >= (540 - off) && azMin < (780 - off)) return 'CORE';
  if (azMin >= (780 - off) && azMin < (840 - off)) return 'POWER';
  if (azMin >= (840 - off) && azMin < (960 - off)) return 'AH';
  return 'OFF';
}


// ====================================================================
// getPreTradeData(symbol) — returns everything the dashboard card needs
// ====================================================================
function getPreTradeData(symbol) {
  if (!symbol) return { error: 'No symbol provided' };
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  symbol = String(symbol).toUpperCase().trim();

  // ── Read Watchlist row for this ticker ──
  var wlSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
  var tData = {};
  if (wlSheet && wlSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    var wlVals = wlSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    for (var i = 1; i < wlVals.length; i++) {
      var tk = String(wlVals[i][3] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      if (tk === symbol) {
        tData = {
          last:    parseFloat(wlVals[i][4]) || 0,
          chg:     String(wlVals[i][5] || ''),
          conf:    parseInt(wlVals[i][6]) || 0,
          setup:   String(wlVals[i][8] || ''),
          vwap:    parseFloat(wlVals[i][23]) || 0,
          rs:      String(wlVals[i][24] || ''),
          rsi:     String(wlVals[i][25] || ''),
          rvol:    String(wlVals[i][26] || ''),
          ema9:    parseFloat(wlVals[i][27]) || 0,
          ema20:   parseFloat(wlVals[i][28]) || 0,
          atr:     parseFloat(wlVals[i][29]) || 0,
          gap:     String(wlVals[i][30] || ''),
          orHi:    parseFloat(wlVals[i][31]) || 0,
          orLo:    parseFloat(wlVals[i][32]) || 0,
          vol:     String(wlVals[i][36] || ''),
          avgVol:  String(wlVals[i][45] || ''),
          w52:     String(wlVals[i][42] || ''),
          ema50d:  String(wlVals[i][44] || '')
        };
        break;
      }
    }
  }
  if (!tData.last) return { error: 'Ticker not found in watchlist: ' + symbol };

  // ── VWAP distance ──
  var vwapDist = tData.vwap > 0 ? ((tData.last - tData.vwap) / tData.vwap * 100) : 0;

  // ── Market state from Market tab ──
  var mkt = ss.getSheetByName('Market');
  var breadthScore = 0, vix = 0;
  if (mkt) {
    var mktData = mkt.getDataRange().getValues();
    for (var m = 0; m < mktData.length; m++) {
      var lbl = String(mktData[m][0]).trim();
      if (lbl === 'Breadth Score') breadthScore = parseFloat(mktData[m][1]) || 0;
      if (lbl === 'VIX' || lbl === '$VIX.X') vix = parseFloat(mktData[m][1]) || 0;
    }
  }

  // ── Gameplan ──
  var ws = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
  var gameplan = _currentGameplan(ws);
  var sessionPhase = _currentSessionPhase();

  // ── Pulse data (cached from bridge) ──
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var pulseData = {};
  try {
    var pulseRaw = props.getProperty('PULSE_CACHE');
    if (pulseRaw) {
      var pc = JSON.parse(pulseRaw);
      if (pc.data) pulseData = pc.data;
    }
  } catch(e) {}

  var spyIvr = parseFloat(pulseData.spy_ivr) || 0;
  var spyEM = parseFloat(pulseData.spy_em) || 0;
  var vvix = parseFloat(pulseData.vvix) || 0;
  var vix3m = parseFloat(pulseData.vix3m) || 0;
  var fgScore = parseFloat(pulseData.fear_greed) || 0;
  var naaimVal = parseFloat(pulseData.naaim) || 0;

  // VIX regime + term structure
  var vixRegime = vix < 15 ? 'Low' : vix < 18 ? 'Normal' : vix < 25 ? 'Elevated' : 'High';
  var vixVix3mRatio = (vix > 0 && vix3m > 0) ? (vix / vix3m) : 0;
  var termStructure = 'CONTANGO';
  if (vixVix3mRatio >= 1.05) termStructure = 'INVERTED';
  else if (vixVix3mRatio >= 0.95) termStructure = 'FLAT';

  // Ticker IVR (from TastyTrade via bridge, if cached)
  var tickerIvr = parseFloat(pulseData[symbol + '_ivr']) || 0;

  // Beta + sector
  var beta = 1.0;
  var sector = getSector(symbol);
  // Estimate beta from RS if available, otherwise default
  var rsNum = parseFloat(String(tData.rs).replace('%', '')) || 0;
  if (Math.abs(rsNum) > 3) beta = 1.0 + Math.abs(rsNum) / 10; // rough estimate
  if (beta > 2.5) beta = 2.5; // cap

  // ── Accounts ──
  var accounts = {};
  try { accounts = getAccountsMap(); } catch(e) {}

  // ── Open trades for correlation check ──
  var openTrades = [];
  try {
    var tSheet = ss.getSheetByName(TM_TAB_TRADES);
    if (tSheet && tSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
      var tVals = tSheet.getRange(2, 1, tSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 6).getValues();
      for (var t = 0; t < tVals.length; t++) {
        if (String(tVals[t][5]).trim().toUpperCase() === 'OPEN') {
          openTrades.push({ symbol: String(tVals[t][1]).trim(), sector: getSector(String(tVals[t][1]).trim()), account: String(tVals[t][2]).trim() });
        }
      }
    }
  } catch(e) {}

  // ── Sub-mode data for dashboard ──
  var subMode = _getCurrentSubMode();
  var subModeLabel = (subMode && subMode.subMode) ? subMode.subMode : '';
  var sizingAdj = (subMode && subMode.sizingAdj) ? subMode.sizingAdj : '';
  var subModeDesc = (subMode && subMode.desc) ? subMode.desc : '';
  var effectiveSizing = _getEffectiveSizing(subMode, gameplan, '');

  return {
    symbol: symbol,
    // Price + technicals
    last: tData.last, chg: tData.chg, vwap: tData.vwap, vwapDist: Math.round(vwapDist * 100) / 100,
    ema9: tData.ema9, ema20: tData.ema20, atr: tData.atr,
    orHi: tData.orHi, orLo: tData.orLo, vol: tData.vol, avgVol: tData.avgVol,
    rs: tData.rs, rsi: tData.rsi, rvol: tData.rvol, gap: tData.gap,
    w52: tData.w52, ema50d: tData.ema50d,
    // Scanner signals
    conf: tData.conf, setup: tData.setup, sector: sector, beta: Math.round(beta * 100) / 100,
    ivr: tickerIvr,
    // Market context
    gameplan: gameplan, breadthScore: breadthScore, sessionPhase: sessionPhase,
    vix: vix, vixRegime: vixRegime, termStructure: termStructure,
    vixVix3mRatio: Math.round(vixVix3mRatio * 1000) / 1000,
    spyIvr: spyIvr, spyEM: spyEM, vvix: vvix, fgScore: fgScore, naaim: naaimVal,
    // Sub-mode (NEW — for Phase 3 dashboard pre-trade card)
    gpSubMode: subModeLabel,
    gpSizingAdj: sizingAdj,
    gpSubModeDesc: subModeDesc,
    // Sizing reference (now uses sub-mode-aware effective sizing)
    gpSizing: effectiveSizing,
    // Open book (for correlation/sector checks)
    openTrades: openTrades,
    // Accounts
    accounts: accounts,
    // Setup type options (now includes validGP, minRVOL, nature)
    setupTypes: Object.keys(SETUP_REGISTRY).map(function(k) {
      var r = SETUP_REGISTRY[k];
      return { key: k, label: r.label, sessions: r.sessions, validGP: r.validGP, minRVOL: r.minRVOL, nature: r.nature };
    }),
    // Timestamp
    asOf: Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss')
  };
}


// ====================================================================
// computePositionSize(params) — sub-mode aware sizing
// ====================================================================
// params: { gameplan, currentPrice, stop, target, accountId, ivr, beta, side, setupType, spyEM }
// Returns: { baseDollars, ivrAdj, betaAdj, finalDollars, shares, dollarRisk,
//            riskPctAccount, r1, r2, r3, tickerEM, targetVsEM, stopVsEM, scalePlan,
//            subMode, sizingAdj, blocked, reason }

function computePositionSize(params) {
  var gp = params.gameplan || 'C';
  var price = parseFloat(params.currentPrice) || 0;
  var stop = parseFloat(params.stop) || 0;
  var target = parseFloat(params.target) || 0;
  var ivr = parseFloat(params.ivr) || 0;
  var beta = parseFloat(params.beta) || 1.0;
  var side = (params.side || 'LONG').toUpperCase();
  var accountId = params.accountId || '';
  var setupType = params.setupType || 'Momentum';
  var spyEM = parseFloat(params.spyEM) || 0;

  if (price <= 0) return { error: 'Invalid price' };
  if (stop <= 0) return { error: 'Stop price required' };

  // ── Read current sub-mode for sizing + GP validation ──
  var subMode = _getCurrentSubMode();
  var subModeLabel = (subMode && subMode.subMode) ? subMode.subMode : '';
  var sizingAdj = (subMode && subMode.sizingAdj) ? subMode.sizingAdj : '';
  var effectiveSizing = _getEffectiveSizing(subMode, gp, accountId);

  // ── GP + sub-mode gate: check if setup is allowed ──
  var gpCheck = _checkSetupGP(setupType, subModeLabel, gp);
  if (!gpCheck.allowed) {
    return { baseDollars: 0, finalDollars: 0, shares: 0, dollarRisk: 0,
             riskPctAccount: 0, blocked: true,
             reason: gpCheck.reason || (subModeLabel + ': ' + setupType + ' not valid.'),
             subMode: subModeLabel, sizingAdj: sizingAdj };
  }

  // ── Bench sizing = blocked (C-Flat, C-Choppy, C-Deteriorating) ──
  if (sizingAdj === 'bench' && setupType !== 'RS-Override') {
    return { baseDollars: 0, finalDollars: 0, shares: 0, dollarRisk: 0,
             riskPctAccount: 0, blocked: true,
             reason: subModeLabel + ': Bench mode. No live capital. RS Override or SIM only.',
             subMode: subModeLabel, sizingAdj: sizingAdj };
  }

  // Base = midpoint of effective sizing range
  var baseDollars = Math.round((effectiveSizing.baseLo + effectiveSizing.baseHi) / 2);

  // ── IVR adjustment: high IVR = reduce size ──
  // IVR 0-30: no adj | 30-50: -10% | 50-70: -20% | 70+: -30%
  var ivrAdj = 1.0;
  if (ivr >= 70) ivrAdj = 0.70;
  else if (ivr >= 50) ivrAdj = 0.80;
  else if (ivr >= 30) ivrAdj = 0.90;

  // ── Beta adjustment: high beta = reduce size ──
  // Beta 0-1.2: no adj | 1.2-1.5: -10% | 1.5-2.0: -20% | 2.0+: -30%
  var betaAdj = 1.0;
  if (beta >= 2.0) betaAdj = 0.70;
  else if (beta >= 1.5) betaAdj = 0.80;
  else if (beta >= 1.2) betaAdj = 0.90;

  var finalDollars = Math.round(baseDollars * ivrAdj * betaAdj);
  var shares = Math.floor(finalDollars / price);
  if (shares < 1 && finalDollars > 0) shares = 1;
  if (finalDollars <= 0) shares = 0;

  // Risk calculation
  var stopDist = Math.abs(price - stop);
  var dollarRisk = Math.round(shares * stopDist * 100) / 100;

  // ── Risk cap: if dollarRisk exceeds max risk %, reduce shares ──
  var maxRiskDollars = effectiveSizing.riskHi || 0;
  if (maxRiskDollars > 0 && dollarRisk > maxRiskDollars && stopDist > 0) {
    shares = Math.floor(maxRiskDollars / stopDist);
    if (shares < 1) shares = 1;
    finalDollars = Math.round(shares * price);
    dollarRisk = Math.round(shares * stopDist * 100) / 100;
  }

  // Account risk %
  var riskPctAccount = 0;
  var equity = effectiveSizing.equity || 0;
  if (equity > 0) {
    riskPctAccount = Math.round(dollarRisk / equity * 10000) / 100;
  } else if (accountId) {
    try {
      var accounts = getAccountsMap();
      var acct = accounts[accountId];
      if (acct && acct.current_equity > 0) {
        equity = parseFloat(acct.current_equity);
        riskPctAccount = Math.round(dollarRisk / equity * 10000) / 100;
      }
    } catch(e) {}
  }

  // R-multiple levels
  var rDist = stopDist; // 1R = stop distance
  var r1, r2, r3;
  if (side === 'LONG') {
    r1 = Math.round((price + rDist) * 100) / 100;
    r2 = Math.round((price + 2 * rDist) * 100) / 100;
    r3 = Math.round((price + 3 * rDist) * 100) / 100;
  } else {
    r1 = Math.round((price - rDist) * 100) / 100;
    r2 = Math.round((price - 2 * rDist) * 100) / 100;
    r3 = Math.round((price - 3 * rDist) * 100) / 100;
  }

  // Expected move context
  var tickerEM = Math.round(spyEM * beta * 100) / 100;
  var targetDist = target > 0 ? Math.abs(target - price) : 0;
  var targetVsEM = tickerEM > 0 ? Math.round(targetDist / tickerEM * 100) / 100 : 0;
  var stopVsEM = tickerEM > 0 ? Math.round(stopDist / tickerEM * 100) / 100 : 0;

  // Default scale plan from setup registry
  var reg = SETUP_REGISTRY[setupType] || {};
  var scalePlan = reg.scalePlan || '50% at 1R, trail rest';

  return {
    baseDollars: baseDollars,
    ivrAdj: ivrAdj,
    betaAdj: betaAdj,
    finalDollars: finalDollars,
    shares: shares,
    dollarRisk: dollarRisk,
    riskPctAccount: riskPctAccount,
    r1: r1, r2: r2, r3: r3,
    tickerEM: tickerEM,
    targetVsEM: targetVsEM,
    stopVsEM: stopVsEM,
    scalePlan: scalePlan,
    subMode: subModeLabel,
    sizingAdj: sizingAdj,
    caution: gpCheck.caution,
    cautionReason: gpCheck.caution ? gpCheck.reason : '',
    blocked: false
  };
}


// ====================================================================
// evaluateScorecard(params) — 8 traffic-light checks
// ====================================================================
// params: { symbol, side, setupType, stop, target, accountId }
// Returns: { checks: [{name, status, reason}], score, pass }

function evaluateScorecard(params) {
  var symbol = String(params.symbol || '').toUpperCase().trim();
  var side = (params.side || 'LONG').toUpperCase();
  var setupType = params.setupType || 'Momentum';
  var stop = parseFloat(params.stop) || 0;
  var target = parseFloat(params.target) || 0;
  var accountId = params.accountId || '';

  var preData = getPreTradeData(symbol);
  if (preData.error) return { error: preData.error, checks: [], score: 0, pass: false };

  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var checks = [];
  var reg = SETUP_REGISTRY[setupType] || {};

  // ── CHECK 1: Breadth confirms side (sub-mode aware) ──
  var gp = preData.gameplan;
  var subMode = _getCurrentSubMode();
  var subModeLabel = (subMode && subMode.subMode) ? subMode.subMode : '';
  var gpCheck = _checkSetupGP(setupType, subModeLabel, gp);

  var c1 = { name: 'Breadth Confirms Side', status: 'RED', reason: '' };
  if (side === 'LONG') {
    if (!gpCheck.allowed) {
      c1.status = 'RED';
      c1.reason = gpCheck.reason || (subModeLabel || ('GP-' + gp)) + ': ' + setupType + ' not valid for longs';
    } else if (gpCheck.caution) {
      c1.status = 'YELLOW';
      c1.reason = gpCheck.reason;
    } else if (gp === 'D') {
      c1.status = 'RED';
      c1.reason = 'GP-D: Short mode — no longs';
    } else if (gp === 'C' && subModeLabel === 'C-Recovery') {
      c1.status = 'YELLOW';
      c1.reason = 'C-Recovery: reduced size ($3-5K), structure setups only';
    } else if (gp === 'C') {
      c1.status = 'RED';
      c1.reason = (subModeLabel || 'GP-C') + ': No longs — bench mode';
    } else {
      c1.status = 'GREEN';
      c1.reason = (subModeLabel || ('GP-' + gp)) + ': Longs confirmed';
    }
  } else { // SHORT
    if (gp === 'D') { c1.status = 'GREEN'; c1.reason = (subModeLabel || 'GP-D') + ': Short mode confirmed'; }
    else if (gp === 'C') { c1.status = 'YELLOW'; c1.reason = (subModeLabel || 'GP-C') + ': Weak — shorts with caution'; }
    else { c1.status = 'RED'; c1.reason = (subModeLabel || ('GP-' + gp)) + ': Bullish — avoid shorts'; }
  }
  checks.push(c1);

  // ── CHECK 2: Session phase matches setup ──
  var phase = preData.sessionPhase;
  var c2 = { name: 'Session Phase Match', status: 'RED', reason: '' };
  var validSessions = reg.sessions || ['OPEN','CORE','POWER'];
  if (phase === 'OFF' || phase === 'AH') {
    c2.status = 'RED'; c2.reason = 'Market closed — ' + phase;
  } else if (phase === 'PM') {
    c2.status = 'YELLOW'; c2.reason = 'Pre-market — limited setups';
  } else if (validSessions.indexOf(phase) >= 0) {
    c2.status = 'GREEN'; c2.reason = setupType + ' valid in ' + phase + ' session';
  } else {
    c2.status = 'YELLOW'; c2.reason = setupType + ' typically runs in ' + validSessions.join('/') + ', currently ' + phase;
  }
  checks.push(c2);

  // ── CHECK 3: IVR supports target distance ──
  var c3 = { name: 'IVR Target Support', status: 'GREEN', reason: '' };
  var ivr = preData.ivr || preData.spyIvr || 0;
  if (ivr >= 70) {
    c3.status = 'RED'; c3.reason = 'IVR ' + ivr + '% — extreme. Targets may compress, reduce size';
  } else if (ivr >= 50) {
    c3.status = 'YELLOW'; c3.reason = 'IVR ' + ivr + '% — elevated. Wide ranges but expect mean reversion';
  } else {
    c3.status = 'GREEN'; c3.reason = 'IVR ' + ivr + '% — normal range';
  }
  checks.push(c3);

  // ── CHECK 4: Term structure safe ──
  var c4 = { name: 'Term Structure', status: 'GREEN', reason: '' };
  var ts = preData.termStructure;
  if (ts === 'INVERTED') {
    if (side === 'LONG') { c4.status = 'RED'; c4.reason = 'VIX inverted — fear spike, dangerous for longs'; }
    else { c4.status = 'GREEN'; c4.reason = 'VIX inverted — supports short thesis'; }
  } else if (ts === 'FLAT') {
    c4.status = 'YELLOW'; c4.reason = 'VIX term structure flat — transition zone, be cautious';
  } else {
    if (side === 'LONG') { c4.status = 'GREEN'; c4.reason = 'VIX contango — normal, supports longs'; }
    else { c4.status = 'YELLOW'; c4.reason = 'VIX contango — vol calm, shorts harder'; }
  }
  checks.push(c4);

  // ── CHECK 5: Not adding correlated exposure ──
  var c5 = { name: 'Correlation Check', status: 'GREEN', reason: '' };
  var mySector = preData.sector;
  var sameSectorCount = 0;
  var sameSymbolOpen = false;
  for (var i = 0; i < preData.openTrades.length; i++) {
    var ot = preData.openTrades[i];
    if (ot.symbol === symbol && ot.account === accountId) sameSymbolOpen = true;
    if (ot.sector === mySector && mySector !== '') sameSectorCount++;
  }
  if (sameSymbolOpen) {
    c5.status = 'RED'; c5.reason = 'Already have OPEN position in ' + symbol + ' on this account';
  } else if (sameSectorCount >= 2) {
    c5.status = 'RED'; c5.reason = sameSectorCount + ' open positions in ' + mySector + ' sector — concentrated';
  } else if (sameSectorCount === 1) {
    c5.status = 'YELLOW'; c5.reason = '1 existing ' + mySector + ' position — adding sector exposure';
  } else {
    c5.status = 'GREEN'; c5.reason = 'No sector overlap with current book';
  }
  checks.push(c5);

  // ── CHECK 6: Within daily loss limit ──
  var c6 = { name: 'Daily Loss Limit', status: 'GREEN', reason: '' };
  try {
    var accounts = preData.accounts;
    var acct = accounts[accountId];
    if (acct) {
      var pnl = parseFloat(acct.daily_pnl) || 0;
      var limit = parseFloat(acct.daily_loss_limit) || -500;
      var pctUsed = limit < 0 ? (pnl / limit * 100) : 0;
      if (pctUsed >= 100) {
        c6.status = 'RED'; c6.reason = 'DAILY LIMIT HIT: $' + pnl + ' (limit: $' + limit + ')';
      } else if (pctUsed >= 50) {
        c6.status = 'YELLOW'; c6.reason = 'Day P&L $' + pnl + ' — ' + Math.round(pctUsed) + '% of daily limit used';
      } else {
        c6.status = 'GREEN'; c6.reason = 'Day P&L $' + pnl + ' — within limits';
      }
    } else {
      c6.status = 'YELLOW'; c6.reason = 'Account not found — cannot verify limit';
    }
  } catch(e) {
    c6.status = 'YELLOW'; c6.reason = 'Could not read account data';
  }
  checks.push(c6);

  // ── CHECK 7: Sector concentration ──
  var c7 = { name: 'Sector Concentration', status: 'GREEN', reason: '' };
  // Re-use data from check 5
  if (sameSectorCount >= 2) {
    c7.status = 'RED'; c7.reason = 'Would be ' + (sameSectorCount + 1) + ' positions in ' + mySector;
  } else if (sameSectorCount === 1) {
    c7.status = 'YELLOW'; c7.reason = 'Would be 2 positions in ' + mySector + ' — manageable';
  } else {
    c7.status = 'GREEN'; c7.reason = 'New sector exposure — diversified';
  }
  checks.push(c7);

  // ── CHECK 8: Risk per trade within limits ──
  var c8 = { name: 'Risk Per Trade', status: 'GREEN', reason: '' };
  if (stop > 0 && preData.last > 0) {
    var sizing = computePositionSize({
      gameplan: gp, currentPrice: preData.last, stop: stop, target: target,
      ivr: ivr, beta: preData.beta, side: side, accountId: accountId,
      setupType: setupType, spyEM: preData.spyEM
    });
    if (sizing.blocked) {
      c8.status = 'RED'; c8.reason = sizing.reason;
    } else {
      try {
        var acctData = preData.accounts[accountId];
        var maxRisk = parseFloat(acctData.max_risk_per_trade) || 250;
        if (sizing.dollarRisk > maxRisk) {
          c8.status = 'RED'; c8.reason = 'Dollar risk $' + sizing.dollarRisk + ' exceeds max $' + maxRisk;
        } else if (sizing.dollarRisk > maxRisk * 0.8) {
          c8.status = 'YELLOW'; c8.reason = 'Dollar risk $' + sizing.dollarRisk + ' — approaching max $' + maxRisk;
        } else {
          c8.status = 'GREEN'; c8.reason = 'Dollar risk $' + sizing.dollarRisk + ' within limits';
        }
      } catch(e) {
        c8.status = 'GREEN'; c8.reason = 'Risk calc OK — $' + (sizing.dollarRisk || '?');
      }
    }
  } else {
    c8.status = 'YELLOW'; c8.reason = 'Need stop price to evaluate risk';
  }
  checks.push(c8);

  // ── Score ──
  var greenCount = 0;
  for (var j = 0; j < checks.length; j++) {
    if (checks[j].status === 'GREEN') greenCount++;
  }

  return {
    checks: checks,
    score: greenCount,
    total: 8,
    pass: greenCount >= 6,
    gameplan: gp,
    sessionPhase: phase
  };
}


// ====================================================================
// logPlannedTrade(params) — writes PLANNED row to Trades tab + snapshot
// ====================================================================
// params: { symbol, side, setupType, stop, target, accountId, catalyst, scalePlan }
// Returns: { tradeNum, scorecard, sizing, snapId } or { error }

function logPlannedTrade(params) {
  var symbol = String(params.symbol || '').toUpperCase().trim();
  var side = (params.side || 'LONG').toUpperCase();
  var setupType = params.setupType || 'Momentum';
  var stop = parseFloat(params.stop) || 0;
  var target = parseFloat(params.target) || 0;
  var accountId = params.accountId || '';
  var catalyst = params.catalyst || '';
  var scalePlanOverride = params.scalePlan || '';

  if (!symbol) return { error: 'Symbol required' };
  if (!stop) return { error: 'Stop price required' };
  if (!accountId) return { error: 'Account ID required' };

  // ── Check for existing OPEN/PLANNED trade in same symbol+account ──
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var tradesSheet = ss.getSheetByName(TM_TAB_TRADES);
  if (!tradesSheet) tradesSheet = _ensureTradesTab();
  if (tradesSheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
    var existing = tradesSheet.getRange(2, 1, tradesSheet.getLastRow() - 1, 6).getValues();
    for (var e = 0; e < existing.length; e++) {
      var eSym = String(existing[e][1]).trim().toUpperCase();
      var eAcct = String(existing[e][2]).trim();
      var eStat = String(existing[e][5]).trim().toUpperCase();
      if (eSym === symbol && eAcct === accountId && (eStat === 'OPEN' || eStat === 'PLANNED')) {
        return { error: 'Already have ' + eStat + ' trade for ' + symbol + ' in ' + accountId + ' (Trade #' + existing[e][0] + ')' };
      }
    }
  }

  // ── Get pre-trade data + scorecard + sizing ──
  var preData = getPreTradeData(symbol);
  if (preData.error) return { error: preData.error };

  var scorecard = evaluateScorecard({
    symbol: symbol, side: side, setupType: setupType,
    stop: stop, target: target, accountId: accountId
  });

  var sizing = computePositionSize({
    gameplan: preData.gameplan, currentPrice: preData.last, stop: stop, target: target,
    ivr: preData.ivr || preData.spyIvr, beta: preData.beta, side: side,
    accountId: accountId, setupType: setupType, spyEM: preData.spyEM
  });

  if (sizing.blocked) return { error: sizing.reason, scorecard: scorecard, sizing: sizing };

  // ── Determine account type ──
  var tradeType = 'DT';
  try {
    var accounts = getAccountsMap();
    var acct = accounts[accountId];
    if (acct) tradeType = acct.type || 'DT';
  } catch(e) {}

  // ── Build TRADES row (65 columns) ──
  var tradeNum = _nextTradeNum();
  var now = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), SCANNER_TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss');
  var scalePlan = scalePlanOverride || sizing.scalePlan || '';

  var newRow = new Array(TM_TRADES_HEADERS.length).fill('');

  // 3A Identification (cols 0-6)
  newRow[0] = tradeNum;
  newRow[1] = symbol;
  newRow[2] = accountId;
  newRow[3] = side;
  newRow[4] = tradeType;
  newRow[5] = 'PLANNED';
  newRow[6] = true; // was_planned

  // 3B Plan (cols 7-21)
  newRow[7]  = setupType;
  newRow[8]  = preData.last;     // planned_entry (current price as reference)
  newRow[9]  = stop;             // planned_stop
  newRow[10] = target;           // planned_target
  newRow[11] = sizing.finalDollars;  // planned_size_dollars
  newRow[12] = sizing.shares;    // planned_shares
  newRow[13] = sizing.dollarRisk;  // dollar_risk
  newRow[14] = sizing.riskPctAccount; // risk_pct_account
  newRow[15] = scalePlan;        // scale_plan
  newRow[16] = catalyst;         // catalyst
  newRow[17] = sizing.r1;        // r1_price
  newRow[18] = sizing.r2;        // r2_price
  newRow[19] = sizing.r3;        // r3_price
  newRow[20] = sizing.targetVsEM;  // target_vs_em_ratio
  newRow[21] = sizing.stopVsEM;  // stop_vs_em_ratio

  // 3C Scorecard (cols 22-31)
  for (var s = 0; s < scorecard.checks.length && s < 8; s++) {
    newRow[22 + s] = scorecard.checks[s].status;
  }
  newRow[30] = scorecard.score;  // sc_score
  newRow[31] = scorecard.pass;   // sc_pass

  // 3D Key Context denormalized (cols 32-35)
  newRow[32] = preData.gameplan;
  newRow[33] = preData.conf;
  newRow[34] = preData.sessionPhase;
  newRow[35] = preData.vix;

  // 3E-3J: Entry, Exit, P&L, Snap links, Review, Timing — all blank for PLANNED

  // Write to sheet
  tradesSheet.getRange(tradesSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, 1, newRow.length).setValues([newRow]);

  // ── Snapshot context ──
  var snapId = snapshotContext('TRADE_PLAN', tradeNum, symbol);
  // Write snap_id to entry_snap_id (col 51)
  var lastRow = tradesSheet.getLastRow();
  tradesSheet.getRange(lastRow, 51).setValue(snapId);

  Logger.log('logPlannedTrade: #' + tradeNum + ' ' + symbol + ' ' + side + ' ' + setupType +
             ' | SC: ' + scorecard.score + '/8 | Size: $' + sizing.finalDollars + ' | Risk: $' + sizing.dollarRisk);

  return {
    tradeNum: tradeNum,
    scorecard: scorecard,
    sizing: sizing,
    snapId: snapId,
    preData: { last: preData.last, conf: preData.conf, vwap: preData.vwap, gameplan: preData.gameplan }
  };
}


// ====================================================================
// getActiveSetups() — surfaces high-confluence actionable tickers
// ====================================================================
// Scans watchlist for tickers that meet minimum confluence for their
// detected setup type + current gameplan permits trading.
// Returns sorted array (highest confluence first) for dashboard surfacing.

function getActiveSetups() {
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  var wlSheet = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
  if (!wlSheet || wlSheet.getLastRow() < 2) return [];

  var ws = ss.getSheetByName('Watchlist');
  var gameplan = _currentGameplan(ws);
  var sessionPhase = _currentSessionPhase();

  // ── Read sub-mode for validGP filtering ──
  var subMode = _getCurrentSubMode();
  var subModeLabel = (subMode && subMode.subMode) ? subMode.subMode : '';

  var wlVals = wlSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  var actionable = [];

  for (var i = 1; i < wlVals.length; i++) {
    var tk = String(wlVals[i][3] || '').trim();
    if (!tk || !/^[A-Z]{1,5}$/.test(tk)) continue;

    var conf = parseInt(wlVals[i][6]) || 0;
    var setupRaw = String(wlVals[i][8] || '').trim();
    var last = parseFloat(wlVals[i][4]) || 0;
    var chg = String(wlVals[i][5] || '');
    var rs = String(wlVals[i][24] || '');
    var rvol = String(wlVals[i][26] || '');
    var vwap = parseFloat(wlVals[i][23]) || 0;

    if (conf < 12 || !last) continue; // floor: skip low-signal tickers

    // Map scanner setup flags to registry keys
    var matchedSetup = _matchSetupType(setupRaw, last, vwap, parseFloat(wlVals[i][31]) || 0, parseFloat(wlVals[i][32]) || 0);
    if (!matchedSetup) continue;

    var reg = SETUP_REGISTRY[matchedSetup];
    if (!reg) continue;

    // Check minimum confluence for this setup
    if (conf < reg.minConf) continue;

    // Check session validity
    if (sessionPhase !== 'OFF' && reg.sessions.indexOf(sessionPhase) < 0) continue;

    // ── Check GP validity using validGP + sub-mode (replaces hardcoded letter checks) ──
    var gpCheck = _checkSetupGP(matchedSetup, subModeLabel, gameplan);
    var sideOk = gpCheck.allowed;

    // Side direction check
    if (sideOk) {
      if (reg.side === 'LONG' && gameplan === 'D') sideOk = false;
      else if (reg.side === 'SHORT' && (gameplan === 'A' || gameplan === 'B')) sideOk = false;
    }

    // Determine if this is a reduced-size C-Recovery trade
    var isReducedSize = (gameplan === 'C' && subModeLabel === 'C-Recovery' && sideOk);

    var sector = getSector(tk);

    actionable.push({
      symbol: tk,
      conf: conf,
      setup: matchedSetup,
      setupLabel: reg.label,
      last: last,
      chg: chg,
      rs: rs,
      rvol: rvol,
      vwapDist: vwap > 0 ? Math.round((last - vwap) / vwap * 10000) / 100 : 0,
      sector: sector,
      side: reg.side === 'ANY' ? (gameplan === 'D' ? 'SHORT' : 'LONG') : reg.side,
      gpAllowed: sideOk,
      caution: gpCheck.caution,
      cautionReason: gpCheck.caution ? gpCheck.reason : '',
      reducedSize: isReducedSize,
      subMode: subModeLabel,
      minConf: reg.minConf,
      minRVOL: reg.minRVOL || 0,
      nature: reg.nature || '',
      sessions: reg.sessions
    });
  }

  // Sort by confluence descending
  actionable.sort(function(a, b) { return b.conf - a.conf; });

  return actionable;
}

/**
 * Maps raw scanner setup flag text to SETUP_REGISTRY key.
 * Scanner flags are like "VWAP", "OR-Break", "Momentum", etc.
 */
function _matchSetupType(setupRaw, price, vwap, orHi, orLo) {
  if (!setupRaw) return null;
  var s = setupRaw.toUpperCase();

  if (s.indexOf('VWAP') >= 0 && s.indexOf('HOLD') >= 0) return 'VWAP-Hold';
  if (s.indexOf('VWAP') >= 0) {
    // Check if price is near VWAP (within 0.5%)
    if (vwap > 0 && Math.abs(price - vwap) / vwap < 0.005) return 'VWAP-Hold';
  }
  if (s.indexOf('OR') >= 0 && s.indexOf('BREAK') >= 0) return 'OR-Break';
  if (s.indexOf('OPENING') >= 0 && s.indexOf('RANGE') >= 0) return 'OR-Break';
  if (s.indexOf('PULLBACK') >= 0 || s.indexOf('PB') >= 0) return 'Pullback-EMA';
  if (s.indexOf('MOMENTUM') >= 0 || s.indexOf('MOM') >= 0) return 'Momentum';
  if (s.indexOf('FAILED') >= 0 || s.indexOf('FAIL') >= 0) return 'Failed-BD';
  if (s.indexOf('RS') >= 0 && s.indexOf('OVERRIDE') >= 0) return 'RS-Override';
  if (s.indexOf('LONE') >= 0) return 'RS-Override';
  if (s.indexOf('ROTATION') >= 0 || s.indexOf('ETF') >= 0) return 'Rotation-ETF';
  if (s.indexOf('BIG DOG') >= 0 || s.indexOf('BIGDOG') >= 0 || s.indexOf('CONSOL') >= 0) {
    // Distinguish bounce variant: if price is below VWAP, it's a bounce play
    if (vwap > 0 && price < vwap) return 'BigDogBounce';
    return 'BigDog';
  }
  if (s.indexOf('BOUNCE') >= 0 || s.indexOf('REVERSAL') >= 0) return 'BigDogBounce';
  if (s.indexOf('GAP') >= 0) return 'GapGo';
  if (s.indexOf('DAILY') >= 0 && s.indexOf('BREAK') >= 0) return 'DailyBreakout';
  if (s.indexOf('OPENING DRIVE') >= 0 || s.indexOf('FIRST MOVE') >= 0) return 'OpeningDrive';
  if (s.indexOf('MARKET PLAY') >= 0 || s.indexOf('SPY') >= 0 || s.indexOf('QQQ') >= 0) return 'MarketPlay';
  if (s.indexOf('SECOND DAY') >= 0 || s.indexOf('2ND DAY') >= 0) return 'SecondDay';
  if (s.indexOf('RETURN') >= 0 || s.indexOf('RTN') >= 0) return 'ReturnPullback';
  if (s.indexOf('SCALP') >= 0) return 'Scalping';

  // Fallback: if conf is high and we have price context, try to infer
  if (orHi > 0 && price > orHi) return 'OR-Break';
  if (vwap > 0 && Math.abs(price - vwap) / vwap < 0.005) return 'VWAP-Hold';

  return 'Momentum'; // default fallback for high-conf untagged tickers
}




function showActiveSetups() {
  var setups = getActiveSetups();
  var msg = setups.length + ' actionable setups found:\n\n';
  for (var i = 0; i < Math.min(setups.length, 10); i++) {
    var s = setups[i];
    msg += (i+1) + '. ' + s.symbol + ' — ' + s.setupLabel + ' (Conf: ' + s.conf + ', ' + s.side + ')\n';
  }
  if (setups.length > 10) msg += '\n... and ' + (setups.length - 10) + ' more.';
  if (setups.length === 0) msg = 'No actionable setups right now. Check gameplan and session phase.';
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(msg);
}

function showPlannedTradeDialog() {
  var ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  var resp = ui.prompt('Plan Trade', 'Enter: SYMBOL, SIDE, SETUP_TYPE, STOP, TARGET, ACCOUNT_ID\n' +
    'Example: NVDA, LONG, VWAP-Hold, 141.20, 145.00, TS-DT', ui.ButtonSet.OK_CANCEL);
  if (resp.getSelectedButton() !== ui.Button.OK) return;
  var parts = resp.getResponseText().split(',').map(function(p) { return p.trim(); });
  if (parts.length < 6) { ui.alert('Need 6 fields: symbol, side, setup, stop, target, account'); return; }
  var result = logPlannedTrade({
    symbol: parts[0], side: parts[1], setupType: parts[2],
    stop: parseFloat(parts[3]), target: parseFloat(parts[4]),
    accountId: parts[5], catalyst: parts[6] || ''
  });
  if (result.error) { ui.alert('Error: ' + result.error); return; }
  ui.alert('Trade #' + result.tradeNum + ' PLANNED\n\n' +
    'Scorecard: ' + result.scorecard.score + '/8 (' + (result.scorecard.pass ? 'PASS' : 'FAIL') + ')\n' +
    'Size: $' + result.sizing.finalDollars + ' (' + result.sizing.shares + ' shares)\n' +
    'Risk: $' + result.sizing.dollarRisk + ' (' + result.sizing.riskPctAccount + '% of account)\n' +
    'R1: $' + result.sizing.r1 + ' | R2: $' + result.sizing.r2 + ' | R3: $' + result.sizing.r3);
}

// ==================== END TRADE MANAGEMENT MODULE ====================

/**
 * Manual menu trigger for equity refresh (always current, not BOD).
 */
function refreshAccountEquityManual() {
  refreshAccountEquity(false);
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Account equity refreshed!');
}
